PVSV_1,1–1,7	om namaḥ buddhāya vidhūta kalpanā jāla gambhīraḥ udāra mūrtaye namaḥ samantabhadrāya samanta spharaṇa tviṣe prāyas prākṛta saktiḥ apratibala prajñaḥ janaḥ kevalam na anarthī eva su bhāṣitaiḥ parigataḥ vidveṣṭi api īrṣyā malaiḥ tena ayam na paraḥ upakāraḥ iti naḥ cintā api cetas ciram sūktaḥ abhyāsa vivardhita vyasanam iti atra anubaddha spṛham 
PVSV_1,8–2,1	 artha anartha vivecanasya anumānaḥ āśraya tvāt tat vipratipatteḥ tat vyavasthāpanāya āha pakṣa dharmaḥ tat aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ tridhā eva saḥ avinābhāva niyamāt hetu ābhāsāḥ tatas apare pakṣaḥ dharmī avayave samudāyaḥ upacārāt prayojana abhāvāt anupacāraḥ iti ced na sarva dharmi dharma pratiṣedha artha tvāt tat eka deśa tvāt tat upacāra yogya dharmi dharma pratipatti artham tathā ca cākṣuṣa tve ādi parihāraḥ dharma vacanena api dharmī āśraya siddhau dharmi grahaṇa sāmarthyāt pratyāsattyā sādhya dharmi siddhiḥ 
PVSV_2,2–2,6	 iti ced na dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇaḥ api pratyāsatteḥ tat aṃśa vyāptyā dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattva siddheḥ dharmi vacanāt sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ siddhe punar vacanam niyama artham āśaṅkyeta sajātīyaḥ eva sattvam iti siddhe api vijātīya vyatireke sādhya abhāve asattva vacana vat sāmarthyāt artha gatau pratipatti 
PVSV_2,7–2,11	 gaurava parihāra artham ca pakṣa vacanam pakṣasya dharma tve tat viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā iti ced na ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt yathā caitraḥ dhanurdharaḥ na anya yoga vyavacchedena yathā pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ iti ākṣepsyāmaḥ tat aṃśaḥ tat dharmaḥ vaktuḥ abhiprāya vaśāt na tat eka deśaḥ 
PVSV_2,12–2,16	 pakṣa śabdena samudāya avacanāt vyāptiḥ vyāpakasya tatra bhāvaḥ eva vyāpyasya vā tatra eva bhāvaḥ etena avayava vyatirekau yathāsvam pramāṇena niścitau uktau pakṣa dharmaḥ ca te ete kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi lakṣaṇāḥ trayaḥ hetavaḥ yathā agniḥ atra dhūmāt vṛkṣaḥ ayam śiṃśapā tvāt pradeśa viśeṣe kvacid na ghaṭaḥ upalabdhi 
PVSV_2,17–2,21	 lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdheḥ yadi syāt upalabdhi asattvaḥ eva syāt na anyathā tena upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta sattvasya iti uktam bhavati tatra dvau vastu sādhanau ekaḥ pratiṣedha hetuḥ svabhāva pratibandhe hi sati arthaḥ artham na vyabhicarati sa ca tad ātma tvāt tad ātma tve sādhya sādhana bhedaḥ abhāvaḥ iti ced 
PVSV_2,22–3,3	 na dharma bheda parikalpanāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ tathā ca āha sarve eva ayam anumāna anumeya vyavahāraḥ buddhi ārūḍhena dharma dharmi bhedena iti bhedaḥ dharma dharmi tayā buddhi ākāra kṛtaḥ na arthaḥ api vikalpa bhedānām sva tantrāṇām anarthaḥ āśraya tvāt tat kalpita viṣayāt artha pratītau anartha pratilambhaḥ eva syāt kāryasya 
PVSV_3,4–3,8	 api svabhāva pratibandhaḥ tat svabhāvasya tad utpatteḥ iti etau dvau anumeya pratyayau sākṣāt anutpatteḥ atat pratibhāsi tve api tad utpatteḥ tat vyabhicāriṇau iti pramāṇam pratyakṣa vat pratyakṣasya api hi artha avyabhicāraḥ eva prāmāṇyam tat abhāve bhāvinaḥ tat vipralambhāt avyabhicāraḥ ca anyasya kaḥ anyaḥ tad utpatteḥ 
PVSV_3,9–4,1	 anāyatta rūpāṇām sahabhāva niyama abhāvāt yadi tad utpatteḥ kāryam gamakam sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ sarvathā janya janaka bhāvāt na tat abhāve bhavataḥ tad utpatti niyama abhāvāt tasmāt kāryam svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ avinābhāvi kāraṇe teṣām hetuḥ tat kāryatva niyamāt taiḥ eva dharmaiḥ ye taiḥ vinā na bhavati aṃśena janya janakatva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na tat janya viśeṣa grahaṇe abhimata tvāt liṅga viśeṣaḥ upādhīnām ca sāmānyānām aviśiṣṭa sāmānya vivakṣāyām vyabhicārāt naḥ iṣyate svabhāve bhāvaḥ api bhāva mā atra anurodhini 
PVSV_4,2–4,13	 hetuḥ iti vartate tādātmyam hi arthasya tat mā atra anurodhini eva na anyāḥ āyatte tat bhāve abhūtasya paścāt bhāva niyama abhāvāt kāraṇānām kārya vyabhicārāt apravṛttiḥ pramāṇānām anupalabdhiḥ apravṛtti phalāḥ asati sat jñāna śabda vyavahāra pratiṣedha phalāḥ upalabdhi pūrvaka tvāt teṣām iti idam sat asat pratiṣedha vidhi hetvoḥ tulyam rūpam tathā hi sattvam upalabdhiḥ eva vastu yogyatā lakṣaṇā tat āśrayā vā jñāna pravṛttiḥ tatas sat jñāna śabda vyavahāra vṛtteḥ asatām ca asattvam anupalabdhiḥ asat jñāna phalā kācid hetu bheda vyapekṣayā 
PVSV_4,14–4,18	 hetuḥ anupalabdhiḥ bhedaḥ asyāḥ viśeṣaṇam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta sattvam atra anupalabdheḥ liṅgāt asattāyām upalabdheḥ abhāvaḥ api anyayā anupalabdhyā sādhyaḥ iti anavasthānāt apratipattiḥ syāt atha upalabdhi abhāvaḥ vinā anupalabdhyā syāt tathā sattā abhāvaḥ api syāt apārthika anupalabdhiḥ atha anyaḥ upalabdhyā 
PVSV_4,19–4,23	 anupalabdhi siddhiḥ iti pratyakṣa siddhāḥ anupalabdhiḥ tathā anye sat tayā asattā kim na sidhyati iti yadā punar evaṃvidhāḥ anupalabdhiḥ eva asatām asattā tadā siddhe api viṣaye mohāt viṣayiṇo asat jñāna śabda vyavahārān apratipadyamānaḥ viṣaya pradarśanena samaye pravartyate yathā gauḥ ayam sāsnā ādi samudāyaḥ ātmaka tvāt 
PVSV_4,24–5,8	 iti tathā ca dṛṣṭānta asiddhi codanāḥ api prativyūḍhā viṣaya pratipattau api apratipad na viṣayīṇām darśanāt evam anayoḥ anupalabdhyoḥ sva viparyaya hetu abhāva bhāvābhyām sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha phala tvam tulyam ekatra saṃśayāt anyatra viparyayāt tatra ādyā sat vyavahāra niṣedhaḥ upayogāt pramāṇam uktāḥ na tu vyatireka darśanaḥ ādau upayujyate saṃśayāt dvitīyā tu atra pramāṇam niścaya phala tvāt sā ca prayoga bhedāt viruddha kāryayoḥ siddhiḥ asiddhiḥ hetu bhāvayoḥ dṛśyaḥ ātmanoḥ abhāva arthaḥ anupalabdhiḥ caturvidhāḥ 
PVSV_5,9–5,13	 yāvān kaścid pratiṣedhaḥ sa sarvaḥ anupalabdheḥ tathā hi sa dvidhā kriyeta kasyacid vidhinā niṣedhena vā vidhau viruddhaḥ vā vidhīyeta aviruddhaḥ vā aviruddhasya vidhau sahabhāva virodha abhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ viruddhasya api anupalabdhi abhāvena virodha apratipattiḥ tathā hi aparyanta kāraṇasya bhavataḥ anyaḥ bhāve 
PVSV_5,14–5,18	 abhāvāt virodha gatiḥ sa ca anupalabdheḥ anyonyaḥ upalabdhi parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tā vā virodhaḥ nitya anitya tva vat tatra api ekaḥ upalabdhyā anyaḥ anupalabdhiḥ eva ucyate anyathā aniṣiddhaḥ upalabdheḥ abhāva asiddheḥ ekasya niṣedhena anyaḥ abhāva sādhane siddhāḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ niṣedhasya anupalabdhi rūpa tvāt tatra api artha antara niṣedhe 
PVSV_5,19–5,23	 kārya kāraṇayoḥ anubhavasya vā tatra anubhavasya apratibandhāt tat abhāve anyena na bhavitavyam iti kutas etat kārya anupalabdhau api na avaśyam kāraṇāḥ api tadvanti bhavanti iti tat abhāvaḥ kutas tasmāt kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ eva abhāvam gamayati iti svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ tu svayam asattāḥ eva tatra kevalam viṣayī sādhyate 
PVSV_5,24–6,3	 asyām api yadā vyāpaka dharma anupalabdhyā vyāpya abhāvam āha tadā abhāvaḥ api iti iyam pratiṣedha viṣaya anupalabdhiḥ prayoga bhedena caturdhā bhavati viruddha siddhyā yathā na śīta sparśaḥ atra agneḥ etena vyāpaka viruddha siddhiḥ uktāḥ veditavyā yathā na tuṣāra sparśaḥ atra agneḥ viruddha kārya siddhyā yathā na śīta 
PVSV_6,4–6,12	 sparśaḥ atra dhūmāt hetu asiddhyā yathā na atra dhūmaḥ anagneḥ svabhāva asiddhyā yathā na atra dhūmaḥ anupalabdheḥ etena vyāpaka svabhāva asiddheḥ uktāḥ yathā na atra śiṃśapā vṛkṣāḥ abhāvāt sarvatra ca asyām abhāva sādhanyām anupalabdhau dṛśyaḥ ātmanām eva teṣām tat viruddhānām ca siddhiḥ asiddhiḥ ca veditavyā anyeṣām abhāva virodha asiddheḥ yadi viruddha kāryaḥ upalabdhyā api abhāva siddhiḥ tat kāraṇaḥ upalabdhyā kim na sidhyati tat viruddha nimittasya yā upalabdhiḥ prayujyate nimittayoḥ viruddha tva abhāve sā vyabhicāriṇī 
PVSV_6,13–6,21	 yathā na śīta sparśaḥ atra kāṣṭhāt iti nimittayoḥ punar virodhe gamikāḥ eva yathā na asya roma harṣaḥ ādi viśeṣāḥ santi saṃnihita dahana viśeṣa tvāt etena tat kāryāt api tat viruddha kārya abhāva gatiḥ uktā veditavyā yathā na roma harṣaḥ ādi viśeṣa yukta puruṣavān ayam pradeśaḥ dhūmāt iyam ca hetu asiddhyā eva tat viruddha siddhiḥ prāk eva nirdiṣṭāḥ iti iyam prayoga bhedāt aṣṭadhā anupalabdhiḥ tatra yā iyam viruddha kāryaḥ upalabdhiḥ uktā tatra iṣṭam viruddha kārye api deśa kāle ādi apekṣaṇam anyathā vyabhicāri syāt bhasmāḥ iva aśīta sādhane 
PVSV_6,22–7,4	 yaḥ tarhi samagreṇa hetunā kāryaḥ utpādaḥ anumīyate sa katham trividhe hetau antarbhavati hetunā yaḥ samagreṇa kāryaḥ utpādaḥ anumīyate artha antara anapekṣa tvāt sa svabhāvaḥ anuvarṇitaḥ asau api yathā asaṃnihitāt na anyam apekṣate iti tat mā atra anubandhī svabhāvaḥ bhāvasya tatra hi kevalam samagrāt kāraṇāt kāryaḥ utpatti sambhavaḥ anumīyate samagrāṇām kāryaḥ utpādana yogyatā anumānāt yogyatā ca sāmagrī mā atra anubandhinī iti svabhāva bhūtāḥ eva anumīyate kim punar kāraṇam sāmagryāḥ kāryam eva na anumīyate sāmagrī phala śaktīnām pariṇāma anubandhini anaikāntika tā kārye pratibandhasya sambhavāt 
PVSV_7,5–7,9	 na hi samagrāṇi iti eva kāraṇa dravyāṇi sva kāryam janayanti sāmagrī janmanām śaktīnām pariṇāma apekṣa tvāt kāryaḥ utpādasya atra antare ca pratibandha sambhavāt na kārya anumānam yogyatāyāḥ tu dravya antara anapekṣa tvāt na virudhyate anumānam uttarottara śakti pariṇāmena kāryaḥ utpādana samarthāḥ iyam kāraṇa sāmagrī 
PVSV_7,10–7,15	 śakti pariṇāma pratyayasya anyasya apekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt iti pūrva sajāti mā atra hetu tvāt śakti prasūteḥ sāmagryā yogyatā ananya apekṣiṇī iti ucyate yā tarhi akārya kāraṇa bhūtena anyena rasaḥ ādinā rūpa ādi gatiḥ sā katham sā api eka sāmagrī adhīnasya rūpaḥ ādeḥ asataḥ gatiḥ hetu dharma anumānena dhūmaḥ indhana vikāra vat 
PVSV_7,16–8,11	 tatra hetuḥ eva tathābhūtaḥ anumīyate pravṛtta śakti rūpaḥ upādāna kāraṇa sahakāri pratyayaḥ hi rasa hetuḥ rasam janayati indhana vikāra viśeṣaḥ upādāna hetu sahakāri pratyaya agni dhūma janana vat tathā hi śakti pravṛttyā sva kāraṇasya phalaḥ utpādanam prati ābhi mukhyena na vinā rasaḥ saḥ eva anya kāraṇam rūpaḥ upādāna hetūnām pravṛtti kāraṇam sā api rasaḥ upādāna kāraṇa pravṛttiḥ rūpaḥ upādāna kāraṇa pravṛtti sahakāriṇī tasmāt yathābhūtāt hetoḥ rasaḥ utpannaḥ tathābhūtam anumāpayan rūpam anumāpayati iti tatra api atītaḥ ekaikālānām gatiḥ na anāgatānām vyabhicārāt tat tasmāt iyam kārya liṅga jāḥ 
PVSV_8,12–8,17	 tena na anyaḥ hetuḥ gamakaḥ asti apratibaddha svabhāvasya avinā abhāva niyama abhāvāt etena pipīlikaḥ utsaraṇa matsya vikāraḥ ādeḥ varṣaḥ ādi anumānam uktam tatra api bhūta pariṇāmaḥ eva varṣa hetuḥ pipīlikaḥ ādi saṃkṣobhaḥ ādi hetuḥ iti hetunā tu asamagreṇa yat kāryam anumīyate śeṣavat tat asāmarthyāt dehāt rāga anumāna vat 
PVSV_8,18–9,2	 samagrāṇi eva hi kāraṇāni yogyatām api anumāpayanti asamagrasya ekānta asāmarthyāt yathā dehaḥ indriya buddhibhyaḥ rāgaḥ ādi anumānam ātmaḥ ātmīya abhiniveśa pūrvakāḥ hi rāgaḥ ādayaḥ ayoniśaḥ manaskāra pūrvaka tvāt sarva doṣaḥ utpatteḥ dehaḥ ādīnām hetu tve api na kevalānām sāmarthyam asti iti vipakṣa vṛtteḥ adṛṣṭau api śeṣavat anumānāt saṃśayaḥ tathā vipakṣe adṛṣṭi mātreṇa kārya sāmānya darśanāt hetu jñānam pramāṇaḥ ābham vacanāt rāgitaḥ ādi vat 
PVSV_9,3–9,7	 na hi rāgaḥ ādīnām eva kāryam spandana vacanaḥ ādayaḥ vaktu kāma tā sāmānya hetu tvāt saḥ eva rāgaḥ iti ced iṣṭa tvāt na kiṃcid bādhitam syāt nitya sukhaḥ ātmaḥ ātmīya darśanaḥ ākṣiptam sa āsrava dharma viṣayam cetasaḥ abhiṣvaṅgam rāgam āhuḥ na evam karuṇāḥ ādayaḥ anyathā api sambhavāt iti nivedayiṣyāmaḥ atra yathā raktaḥ bravīti 
PVSV_9,8–9,12	 tathā viraktaḥ api iti vacana mātrāt apratipattiḥ na api viśeṣāt abhiprāyasya durbodha tvāt vyavahāra saṃkareṇa sarveṣām vyabhicārāt prayojana abhāvāt avyāhāraḥ iti ced na para artha tvāt na yuktaḥ vīta rāga tvāt iti ced na karuṇāḥ api vṛtteḥ saḥ eva rāgaḥ iti ced iṣṭam aviparyāsa samudbhavāt na doṣaḥ asati 
PVSV_9,13–9,17	 api ātma grahe duḥkha viśeṣa darśana mātreṇa abhyāsa balaḥ utpādinī bhavati eva karuṇā tathā hi sattva dharmaḥ ādi ālambanāḥ maitrī ādaye iṣyante etāḥ ca sajātīya abhyāsa vṛttayaḥ na rāga apekṣiṇyaḥ na evam rāgaḥ ādayaḥ viparyāsa abhāve abhāvāt kāruṇikasya api niṣphalaḥ ārambhaḥ aviparyāsāt iti ced na para arthasya eva 
PVSV_9,18–10,1	 phala tvena iṣṭa tvāt icchā lakṣaṇa tvāt phalasya sarvathā abhūta asamāropāt nirdoṣaḥ tat anyena doṣavat tva sādhane na kiṃcid aniṣṭam vaktari ātmani rāgaḥ ādi darśanena anyatra tat anumāne atiprasaṅgaḥ vyabhicārāt ananyaḥ anumāne iha avyabhicāraḥ iti kaḥ niścayaḥ karaṇa guṇa vaktu kāmate hi vacanam anumāpayet 
PVSV_10,2–10,6	 rāgaḥ utpādana yogyatā rahite vacanaḥ adarśanāt tat anumāne atiprasaṅgaḥ uktaḥ rāgasya anupayoge katham tat śaktiḥ upayujyate śakti upayoge hi saḥ eva upayuktaḥ syāt tat ca na asti iti uktam tasmāt na antarīyakam eva kāryam kāraṇam anumāpayati tat pratibandhāt na anyat vipakṣe adarśane api sarva darśinaḥ hi darśana 
PVSV_10,7–10,14	 vyāvṛttiḥ sarvatra abhāvam gamayet kvacid tathā dṛṣṭānām api deśa kāla saṃskāra bhedena anyathā adarśanāt yathā āmalakyaḥ kṣīra avasekena madhura phalāḥ bhavanti na ca evam bahulam dṛśyante tena evam syāt yuktam vaktum mādṛśaḥ vaktā rāgī iti rāgaḥ utpatti pratyaya viśeṣeṇa ātma darśana ayoniśaḥ manaskāreṇa yogāt tadā api apārthakaḥ vacanaḥ udāhāraḥ tasmāt vipakṣe adṛṣṭiḥ ahetuḥ na ca adarśana mātreṇa vipakṣe avyabhicāritā sambhāvya vyabhicāra tvāt sthālī taṇḍula pāka vat 
PVSV_10,15–10,20	 na hi bahulam pakva darśane api sthālī antargamana mātreṇa pākaḥ sidhyati vyabhicāra darśanāt evam tu syāt evam svabhāvāḥ etat samānaḥ pāka hetavaḥ pakvāḥ iti anyathā tu śeṣavat etat anumānam vyabhicāri kim punar etat śeṣavat yasya adarśana mātreṇa vyatirekaḥ pradarśyate tasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt śeṣavat tat udāhṛtam 
PVSV_10,21–10,27	 sa tasya vyatirekaḥ na niścitaḥ iti vipakṣe vṛttiḥ āśaṅkyeta vyatireka sādhanasya adarśana mātrasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt na sarve anupalabdhiḥ gamikā tasmāt eka nivṛttyā anya nivṛttim icchatā tayoḥ kaścid svabhāva pratibandhaḥ api eṣṭavyaḥ anyathā agamakaḥ hetuḥ syāt hetoḥ triṣu api rūpeṣu niścayaḥ tena varṇitaḥ asiddha viparīta artha vyabhicāri vipakṣataḥ 
PVSV_10,28–11,4	 na hi asati pratibandhe anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ asti tena tam eva darśayan niścayam āha tatra anvayasya niścayena viruddha tat pakṣyāṇām nirāsaḥ vyatirekasya anaikāntikasya tat pakṣasya ca śeṣavat ādeḥ dvayoḥ iti eka siddha pratiṣedhaḥ prasiddha vacanena sandigdhayoḥ śeṣavat asādhāraṇayoḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ 
PVSV_11,5–11,12	 api anyathā hi asati pratibandhe adarśana mātreṇa vyatireke vyabhicāri vipakṣeṇa vaidharmya vacanam ca yat yat āha eṣa tāvat nyāyaḥ yat ubhayam vaktavyam viruddha anaikāntika pratipakṣeṇa iti vaidharmya vacanam anaikāntika pratipakṣeṇa yadi adṛṣṭi phalam tat ca yadi tena vipakṣe adarśanam khyāpyate tat anukte api gamyate 
PVSV_11,13–12,7	 na hi tasya prāk darśana bhrāntiḥ yā vacanena nivartyeta smṛtiḥ vāca adarśane kriyate iti ced darśanam khalu apratīyamānam anaṅgam iti yuktam tatra smaraṇaḥ ādhānam adarśanam tu darśana abhāvaḥ sa darśanena bādhyate tat abhāve tu siddhaḥ eva iti apārthakam tat siddhaye vacanam na vai anupalambhamānasya tāvatā na asti iti bhavati tat artham vacanam iti ced na ca na asti iti vacanāt tat na asti eva yathā yadi na asti sa khyāpyate nyāyaḥ tadā na asti iti gamyate 
PVSV_12,8–12,12	 yadi anupalabhamānaḥ na asti iti na pratyeti vacanāt api naḥ eva pratyeṣyati tat api hi anupalambham eva khyāpayati na ca ekaḥ anupalambhaḥ anyaḥ abhāvam sādhayati atiprasaṅgāt na ca tena na asti iti vacanāt tathā bhavati atiprasaṅgāt tat katham vaidharmya vacanena anaikāntika parihāraḥ tasmāt vyāvṛttim icchatā 
PVSV_12,13–12,18	 tatra nyāyaḥ vaktavyaḥ yatas asya vyāvṛttam iti bhavati nanu tat abhāve anupalambhāt siddhā vyāvṛttiḥ yadi adṛṣṭyā nivṛttiḥ syāt śeṣavat vyabhicāri kim yathā pakvāni etāni phalāni evam rasāni vā rūpa aviśeṣāt eka śākhā prabhava tvāt vā upayukta vat iti atra api vivakṣita aśeṣa pakṣīkaraṇe hetoḥ sādhya abhāve anupalambhaḥ asti iti katham vyabhicāraḥ 
PVSV_12,19–12,23	 pratyakṣa bādhā āśaṅkā vyabhicāraḥ iti eke na pakṣīkṛta viṣaye abhāvāt kadācid bhavet iti ced tathā śaṅkāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ anyatra api abhāva niyama abhāvāt vṛttam pramāṇam bādhakam avṛtta bādhane sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ vyatirekaḥ tu siddhaḥ eva sādhanam iti tathā abhāva niścayam apekṣate anupalambhāt tu 
PVSV_12,24–13,4	 kvacid abhāva siddhau api apratibaddhasya tat abhāve sarvatra abhāva asiddheḥ saṃśayāt avyatirekaḥ vyabhicāraḥ śeṣavataḥ kim ca vyatireki api hetuḥ syāt na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram aprāṇaḥ ādimattva prasaṅgāt iti nirātmakeṣu ghaṭaḥ ādiṣu dṛṣṭeṣu prāṇaḥ ādi adarśanāt tat nivṛtti ātma gatiḥ syāt adṛśya anupalambhāt abhāva asiddhau ghaṭe ādīnām 
PVSV_13,5–13,14	 nairātmya asiddheḥ prāṇaḥ ādeḥ anivṛttiḥ abhyupagamāt siddham iti ced katham idānīm ātma siddhiḥ parasya api apramāṇikā katham nairātmya siddhiḥ abhyupagamena ca sa ātmaka anātmakau vibhajya tatra abhāvena gamaka tvam kathayatā āgamika tvam ātmani pratipannam syāt na anumeya tvam tasmāt adarśane api ātmanaḥ nivṛtti asiddheḥ tat nivṛttau kvacid nivṛttau api prāṇaḥ ādīnām apratibandhāt sarvatra nivṛtti asiddheḥ agamaka tvam yā api asiddhi yojanā tathā sa pakṣe san asan iti evam ādiṣu api yathāyogam udāharyam iti evam ādikāḥ sā api na vācyāḥ asiddhi yojanā 
PVSV_13,15–14,1	 anupalambhaḥ eva saṃśayāt upalambhe tat abhāvāt anupalambhāt ca vyatirekaḥ iti saṃśayitaḥ anivāryaḥ syāt yathāyoga vacanāt anivāritaḥ eva iti ced na yaḥ eva tu ubhaya niścita vācī iti ādi vacanāt tena anupalambhe api saṃśayāt anivṛttim manyamānaḥ tat pratiṣedham āha kim ca viśeṣasya vyavaccheda hetu tā syāt adarśanāt 
PVSV_14,2–14,10	 śrāvaṇa tvasya api nitya anityayoḥ adarśanāt vyāvṛttiḥ iti tat vyavaccheda hetu tā syāt na hi tat vyāvṛtteḥ anyat vyavacchedanam avyavacchedaḥ tu kutaścid vyāvṛtteḥ eva aniścayāt yaḥ hi yatra na asti iti niścitaḥ sa bhavan tat abhāvam katham na gamayet pramāṇa antara bādhā ced atha api syāt ubhaya vyavacchede pramāṇa antaram bādhakam asti anyonya vyavaccheda rūpāṇām eka vyavacchedena anya vidhānāt apratiṣedhaḥ vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ virodhāt na idānīm na astitāḥ adṛśaḥ 
PVSV_14,11–14,19	 na evam adarśanam pramāṇam bādhāḥ asambhavāt tathā anyatra api sambhāvyam pramāṇa antara bādhanam lakṣaṇa yukte bādhāḥ asambhave tat lakṣaṇam eva dūṣitam syāt iti sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ anumāna viṣaye api pratyakṣa anumāna virodha darśanāt anāśvāsa prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na yathā ukte asambhavāt sambhavinaḥ ca atat lakṣaṇa tvāt viruddha avyabhicārī avacanam iti ced anumāna viṣaye avacanāt iṣṭam viṣayam ca asya nivedayiṣyāmaḥ kim ca dṛṣṭā ayuktiḥ adṛṣṭeḥ ca syāt sparśasya avirodhinī 
PVSV_14,20–15,3	 yadi hi anupalambhena abhāvaḥ sidhyet yat āha yadi adarśana mātreṇa dṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na ca saḥ api yuktaḥ iti katham ayuktaḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddheḥ nanu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ sparśasya yuktaḥ eva pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ dṛśya tat svabhāva viṣaya mā atra apratiṣedhāt pṛthivī ādi sāmānyena 
PVSV_15,4–15,10	 gṛhītvā ayam pratiṣedham āha tatra ca tūlaḥ upala pallava ādiṣu tat bhāve api sparśa bheda darśanāt asya api kvacid viśeṣe sambhavaḥ āśaṅkayā bhavitavyam iti sarvatra adarśana mātreṇa ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti evam ācāryīyaḥ kaścid anupalambhāt abhāvam bruvāṇaḥ upālabdhaḥ api ca deśaḥ ādi bhedāt dṛśyante bhinnāḥ dravyeṣu śaktayaḥ tatra eka dṛṣṭyā na anyatra yuktaḥ tat bhāva niścayaḥ 
PVSV_15,11–15,15	 yadi kathaṃcid vipakṣe adarśana mātreṇa apratibaddhasya api tat avyabhicāraḥ kvacid deśe kānicid dravyāṇi kathaṃcid dṛṣṭāni punar anyathā anyatra dṛśyante yathā kāścid oṣadhayaḥ kṣetra viśeṣe viśiṣṭa rasa vīrya vipākāḥ bhavanti na anyatra tathā kāla saṃskāra bhedāt na ca tat deśaiḥ tathā dṛṣṭāḥ iti sarvāḥ tattvena 
PVSV_15,16–15,20	 tathābhūtāḥ sidhyanti guṇa antarāṇām kāraṇa antara apekṣa tvāt viśeṣa hetu abhāve tu syāt anumānam yathā adṛṣṭa kartṛkam api vākyam puruṣa saṃskāra pūrvakam iti vākyeṣu viśeṣa abhāvāt sarva prakārāṇām puruṣaiḥ karaṇasya darśanāt na evam asambhavat viśeṣa hetavaḥ puruṣāḥ yena vacanaḥ ādeḥ kiṃcid mā atra sādharmyāt 
PVSV_15,21–15,25	 sarve ākāra sāmyam anumīyeta sarva guṇeṣu viśeṣa darśanāt saṃskāra bhedena viśeṣa pratipatteḥ tadvat anyasya api sambhavāt asambhava anumāne ca bādhaka hetu abhāvāt vairāgya adṛṣṭeḥ adṛṣṭena ca bādhya bādhaka bhāva asiddheḥ rāgaḥ ādi avyabhicāri kārya abhāvāt sambhave api viśeṣāṇām draṣṭum aśakya tvāt 
PVSV_16,1–16,10	 tādṛśām ca apratikṣepa artha tvāt na evam vākyāni dṛśya viśeṣa tvāt adṛśya tve api adṛṣṭa viśeṣāṇām vijātīyatve upagama virodhāt tat viśeṣāṇām anyatra api śakya kriya tvāt pratyakṣāṇām śabdānām apratyakṣa svabhāva abhāvāt bhrānti nimitta abhāvāt bādhaka abhāvāt bhrānti asiddheḥ puruṣeṣu viśeṣa darśanasya bādhaka tvāt asamānam para bhāva bhūtasya ca vākya viśeṣasya atat viśeṣa tvāt tat abhinna svabhāvānām sarveṣām puruṣa kriyā na vā kasyacid kim ca ātma mṛd cetanā ādīnām yaḥ abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ saḥ eva anupalambhaḥ kim hetu abhāvasya sādhakaḥ 
PVSV_16,11–16,15	 anupalambham ca asya pramāṇayataḥ ātma vādaḥ nirālambaḥ syāt apratyakṣa tvāt ātmanaḥ tat kārya asiddheḥ indriyaḥ ādīnām tu vijñāna kāryasya kādācid ka tvāt sa apekṣya siddhyā prasiddhiḥ ucyate kim api asya kāraṇam asti iti ca tu evaṃbhūtam iti na evam sukhaḥ ādi kāryam prasādhitam kaṃcid artham puṣṇāti 
PVSV_16,16–16,20	 yena kenacid kāraṇavat tva abhyupagamāt tathā ca anupalambhaḥ eva ātmanaḥ syāt tam tena pratyācakṣāṇaḥ kim iti prativyūḍhaḥ anupalambhasya asādhana tvāt iti katham asādhanam vyatirekam sādhayet mṛdaḥ khalu api kaścid caitanyam anupalabhyamānam api icchan adarśanāt vacanaḥ ādeḥ vyāvṛttim āha dadhi ādikam 
PVSV_16,21–16,25	 ca aparaḥ kṣīraḥ ādiṣu apara artheṣu saṃghāta tva adarśanāt vyatirekam kaḥ hi atra niyamaḥ saṃhataiḥ avaśyam para arthaiḥ bhavitavyam iti asti eva upalambhaḥ dadhi ādīnām kṣīraḥ ādiṣu anumānam aśaktāt anutpatteḥ atha kā iyam śaktiḥ saḥ eva bhāvaḥ uta anyat eva kiṃcid saḥ eva ced tathā eva upalabhyeta viśeṣa abhāvāt 
PVSV_16,26–17,4	 anyat ced katham anyaḥ bhāve tat asti upacāra mātram tu syāt iti ayam eṣām paraspara vyāghātaḥ tasmāt tat mā atra sambandhaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvam eva vā nivartayet yathā vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapām śākhāḥ ādimat viśeṣasya eva kasyacid tathā prasiddheḥ sa tasya svabhāvaḥ svam ca svabhāvam parityajya katham bhāvaḥ bhavet svabhāvasya eva bhāva tvāt iti tasya svabhāva pratibandhāt avyabhicāraḥ kāraṇam vā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ 
PVSV_17,5–17,11	 kāraṇam nivartamānam kāryam nivartayati anyathā tat tasya kāryam eva na syāt siddhaḥ tu kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ svabhāvam niyamayati iti ubhayathā svabhāva pratibandhāt eva nivṛttiḥ anyathā eka nivṛttyā anya vinivṛttiḥ katham bhavet na aśvavān iti martyena na bhāvyam gamatā api kim saṃnidhānāt tathā ekasya katham anyasya saṃnidhiḥ gomān iti eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatāḥ api kim 
PVSV_17,12–17,23	 tasmāt svabhāva pratibandhāt eva hetuḥ sādhyam gamayati sa ca tat bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ vā saḥ eva avinā abhāvaḥ dṛṣṭāntābhyām pradarśyate tasmāt vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte na iṣṭaḥ avaśyam iha āśrayaḥ tat abhāve ca tat naḥ iti vacanāt api tat gateḥ yatas tat bhāva hetu bhāvau hi dṛṣṭānte tat avedinaḥ khyāpyete dṛṣṭānte hi sādhya dharmasya tat bhāvaḥ tat mā atra anubandhena tat svabhāvatayā khyāpyate yaḥ kṛtakam svabhāvam janayati saḥ anitya svabhāvam santam janayati iti pramāṇam dṛṣṭāntena upadarśyate anyathā eka dharma sat bhāvāt tat anyena api bhavitavyam 
PVSV_17,24–18,4	 iti niyama abhāvāt sādhanasya sādhya vyabhicāraḥ āśaṅkā syāt tena ca pramāṇena sādhya dharmasya tat mā atra anubandhaḥ khyāpyate sva kāraṇāt eva kṛtakaḥ tathābhūtaḥ jātaḥ yaḥ naśvaraḥ kṣaṇa sthitaḥ dharmāḥ anyatas tasya tat bhāva niṣedhāt hetu bhāvaḥ vā tasmin sati eva bhāvāt iti dṛṣṭāntena pradarśyate artha antarasya 
PVSV_18,5–18,11	 tathā prasiddhe tat bhāve hetu bhāve vā anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvam na bhavati dahana abhāve ca dhūmaḥ tathā hi sa tasya svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ vā katham svam svabhāvam hetum vā antareṇa bhavet iti āśrayam antareṇa api vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte prasidhyati vyatirekaḥ yeṣām punar prasiddhau eva tat bhāva hetu bhāvau teṣām viduṣām vācyaḥ hetuḥ eva hi kevalaḥ 
PVSV_18,12–18,21	 yat arthe dṛṣṭāntaḥ ucyate saḥ arthaḥ siddhaḥ iti kim tat vacanena tadā tat pradarśane api kim vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ āśrayeṇa iti manyamānaḥ āśrayam pratikṣipti sma tena eva jñāta sambandhe dvayoḥ anyataraḥ uktitaḥ arthāpattyā dvitīye api smṛtiḥ samupajāyate yat āha arthāpattyā vā anyatareṇa ubhaya pradarśanāt iti tatra api dṛṣṭāntena tat bhāva hetu bhāva pradarśanam manyamānaḥ arthāpattyai eka vacanena dvitīya siddhim āha tathā hi yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti ukte anartha antara bhāve vyaktam ayam asya svabhāvaḥ tat mātra anubandhī pramāṇa dṛṣṭaḥ tat bhāva niyamāt iti jñāta 
PVSV_18,22–18,26	 tat bhāvasya arthāpattyā anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvam na bhavati iti bhavati na hi svabhāvasya abhāve bhāvaḥ bhavati abhedāt anyathā tat bhāve bhavati iti eva na syāt tathā tat abhāve na bhavati iti ukte tatas eva tat bhāvatā vedinaḥ tathā hi ayam asya svabhāvaḥ yena tat abhāve na bhavati anyathā ayogāt iti tat 
PVSV_19,1–19,5	 tat svabhāva tā pratipattyā anvaya smṛtiḥ bhavati tathā yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti ukte kāryam dhūmaḥ dahanasya yena dhūme avaśyam agniḥ bhavati anyathā artha antarasya tat anubandha niyama abhāvāt svātantryam bhāvasya syāt atas tat abhāve api svabhāva avaikalyāt na abhāvaḥ kārye tu avaśyam kāraṇam 
PVSV_19,6–19,10	 bhavati idam eva hi kāraṇasya kāraṇa tvam yat artha antara bhāve svabhāvaḥ upadhānam kāryasya api tat bhāvaḥ eva bhāvaḥ tat ca asti dhūme tasmāt kāryam dhūmaḥ iti anvayena vidhita tat kāryatvasya dahana abhāve dhūmaḥ na bhavati iti arthāt vyatireka pratipattiḥ bhavati tathā asati agnau dhūmaḥ na asti iti 
PVSV_19,11–19,15	 ukte agniḥ dhūme bhavati avaśyam iti arthāt anvaya pratipattiḥ anyathā hi tat abhāve kim na bhavet iti nanu ca nitya anitya artha kāryatva abhāve api śravaṇa jñānam na bhavati tat abhāve na vai na bhavati tayoḥ eva tatas saṃśayāt anyathā abhāvena niścitāt katham tat bhāva parāmarśena saṃśayaḥ syāt 
PVSV_19,16–19,20	 kevalam tu bhāva niścaya abhāvāt na asti iti ucyate yadā punar dṛṣṭāntena na agni dhūmayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pradarśyate tadā yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti eva na syāt pratibandha abhāvāt kutas agni abhāve dhūmaḥ na asti iti arthāt vyatireka siddhiḥ tathā vaidharmyeṇa abhāva asiddheḥ anvaya smṛtiḥ tasmāt dṛṣṭāntena ayam 
PVSV_19,21–20,3	 eva yathā ukta svabhāva pratibandhaḥ pradarśyate eka sat bhāve anyasya prasiddhi artham tat abhāve asambhavāt hetu svabhāva abhāvaḥ atas pratiṣedhe ca kasyacid hetuḥ tau eva hi nivartamānau sva pratibaddham nivartayate iti kasyacid arthasya pratiṣedham api sādhayitu kāmena hetoḥ vyāpakasya vā svabhāvasya nivṛttiḥ hetu tvena ākhyeyāḥ apratibandhe hi katham ekasya nivṛttiḥ anyasya nivṛttim sādhayet yuktaḥ upalabhasya tasya ca anupalambhanam 
PVSV_20,4–20,15	 pratiṣedha hetuḥ pratiṣedha viṣaya vyavahāra hetuḥ tat hetuḥ iti uktaḥ svayam tathā abhūta anupalambhasya pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt hetu vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ ubhayasya api hetuḥ iti iyam trividhā api uktaḥ anupalabdhiḥ anekadhā tat tat viruddhaḥ ādi agati gati bheda prayogataḥ trividhaḥ eva hi pratiṣedha hetuḥ upalabhya sattvasya hetoḥ tathā abhāva niścaye vyāpakasya sva ātmanaḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ iti sa prayoga vaśena tat tat viruddhaḥ ādi agati gati bheda prayogataḥ aneka prakāraḥ uktaḥ tasya agatyā tat viruddha gatyā viruddha kārya gatyā iti ādi bheda prayogaiḥ yathoktam prāk kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinābhāva niyamaḥ adarśanāt na na darśanāt 
PVSV_20,16–20,23	 avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ kaḥ parasya anyathā paraiḥ artha antara nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga vat iti antara ślokau api ca artha antara nimittaḥ hi dharmaḥ syāt anyaḥ eva saḥ na hi tasmin niṣpanne aniṣpannaḥ bhinna hetukaḥ vā tat svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ ayam eva khalu bhedaḥ bheda hetuḥ vā bhāvānām viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ kāraṇa bhedaḥ ca tau ced na bhedakau tadā na kasyacid kutaścid bhedaḥ iti ekam dravyam viśvam syāt 
PVSV_20,24–21,4	 tatas ca saha utpatti vināśau sarvasya ca sarvatra upayogaḥ syāt anyathā ekam iti eva na syāt nāma antaram vā artha bhedam abhyupagamya tathā abhidhānāt nanu anartha antara hetu tve api bhāva kāle anitya tā aniṣpatteḥ tulyāḥ atat svabhāva tā na vai kācid anyā anitya tā nāma yā paścāt niṣpadyeta saḥ eva hi bhāvaḥ kṣaṇa 
PVSV_21,5–21,9	 sthiti dharmāḥ anitya tā vacana bhede api dharmi dharma tayā nimittam vakṣyāmaḥ tām punar asya kṣaṇa sthitaḥ dharma tām svabhāvam sva hetoḥ eva tathā utpatteḥ paśyan api manda buddhiḥ sattā upalambhena sarvadā tad bhāva śaṅkā vipralabdhaḥ na vyavasyati sadṛśā paraḥ utpatti vipralabdhaḥ vā antyakṣaṇa darśinām niścayāt 
PVSV_21,10–21,14	 paścāt asya anupalabdhyā asthitaḥ pratipatteḥ niścaya kālaḥ iti tadā anitya tā vyavasthāpyate kāryaḥ utpādana śakteḥ kāraṇa svabhāva tve api adṛṣṭa tat kāryasya kāraṇa darśane api apratipad na tat bhāvasya kārya darśanāt tat pratipatti vat anyathā artha antaram eva anitya tā syāt anya nimitta tve animitta tve vā tathā ca bhāvas 
PVSV_21,15–21,20	 tadvān na syāt tat anupayogāt upayoge vā saḥ eva asya sva ātma bhūtaḥ anitya tā iti kim anyayā svabhāvena vā acalasya artha antara yoge api tat bhāva anutpatteḥ sa ca artha antarāt bhavan anitya tā anyaḥ vā dharmaḥ hetuḥ phalam vā syāt ahetu phalasya asambandhāt tatra bhāva anumānasya asambhavāt tatra paścāt bhāvān na hetu tvam phale api ekānta tā kutas 
PVSV_21,21–22,5	 sa hi niṣpanne bhāve artha antarataḥ paścāt bhavan katham tasya hetuḥ syāt phalasya api na avaśyam hetau bhāvaḥ iti tat bhāva hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam tat na artha antara nimittaḥ dharmaḥ bhāve avaśyam bhāvi iti ananumānam yadi tarhi darśanaḥ adarśane na anvaya vyatireka gateḥ āśrayaḥ katham dhūmaḥ agnim na vyabhicarati iti gamyate yasmāt kāryam dhūmaḥ hutabhujaḥ kārya dharma anuvṛttitaḥ yeṣām upalambhe tat lakṣaṇam anupalabdham yat upalabhyate tatra ekaḥ abhāve api naḥ upalabhyate tat tasya kāryam tat ca dhūme asti sa bhavan tat abhāve tu hetumat tām vilaṅghayet 
PVSV_22,6–22,10	 sakṛt api tathā adarśanāt kāryam siddhaḥ akārya tve akāraṇāt sakṛt api abhāvāt kāryasya ca sva kāraṇam antareṇa bhāve ahetumat tā eva syāt na hi yasya yam antareṇa bhāvaḥ sa tasya hetuḥ bhavati bhavati ca dhūmaḥ agnim antareṇa tat na tat hetuḥ anyaḥ hetuka tvāt na ahetuka tvam iti ced na tatra api 
PVSV_22,11–22,15	 tulya tvāt tat abhāve api agnau bhavati iti katham vā tatas anyatas vā atat janana svabhāvāt bhavet svayam atat svabhāvasya ajananāt tasya ahetutā syāt na vai saḥ eva bhavati tādṛśasya bhāvāt anyaḥ adṛśāt bhavan katham tādṛśaḥ syāt tādṛśāt hi bhavan tādṛśaḥ syāt anyaḥ adṛśāt api tādṛśaḥ bhāve tat śakti niyama 
PVSV_22,16–22,21	 abhāvāt na hetu bhedaḥ bhedakaḥ iti akāraṇam viśvasya vaiśvarūpyam syāt sarvam vā sarvasmāt jāyeta tasmāt kāraṇa bhedaḥ abhedābhyām kārya bhedaḥ abhedau tat na dhūmaḥ arthāt dṛṣṭa ākāra vijātīyāt bhavati ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt tathā ca nityam sattvam asattvam vā ahetoḥ anyaḥ anapekṣaṇāt apekṣātaḥ hi bhāvānām kādācid ka tva sambhavaḥ 
PVSV_22,22–23,2	 sa hi dhūmaḥ ahetuḥ bhavat nirapekṣa tvāt na kadācid na bhavet tat bhāve vaikalya abhāvāt iṣṭa kāla vat tadā api vā na bhavet abhāva kāla aviśeṣāt apekṣayā hi bhāvāḥ kādācid kāḥ bhavanti bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ tat bhāva yogyatā ayogya tā yogāt tulya yogyatā yogyatayoḥ deśa kālayoḥ tadvat tā itarayoḥ niyama ayogāt sā ca 
PVSV_23,3–23,7	 yogya tā hetu bhāvāt kim anyat tasmāt eka deśa kāla parihāreṇa anya deśa kālayoḥ vartamānaḥ bhāvaḥ tat sa apekṣaḥ nāma bhavati tathā hi tathā vṛttiḥ eva apekṣā tat kṛtaḥ upakāra anapekṣasya tat niyama ayogāt tat niyata deśa kāla tvāt dhūmaḥ atra dṛṣṭaḥ sakṛt vaikalye ca punar na dṛṣṭaḥ tat janyaḥ asya svabhāvaḥ anyathā 
PVSV_23,8–23,15	 sakṛt api abhāvāt sa tat pratiniyataḥ anyatra katham bhavet bhavan vā na dhūmaḥ syāt tat janitaḥ hi svabhāva viśeṣaḥ dhūmaḥ iti tathā hetuḥ api tathā abhūta kārya janana svabhāvaḥ tasya anyatas api bhāve na sa tasya svabhāvaḥ iti sakṛt api na janayet na vā sa dhūmaḥ adhūma janana svabhāvāt bhāvāt tat svabhāva tve ca saḥ eva agniḥ iti avyabhicāraḥ agni svabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrddhā yadi agniḥ eva saḥ atha anagni svabhāvaḥ asau dhūmaḥ tatra katham bhavet 
PVSV_23,16–23,22	 dhūma hetu svabhāvaḥ hi vahniḥ tat śakti bhedavān adhūma hetoḥ dhūmasya bhāve sa syāt ahetukaḥ iti saṃgraha ślokau katham tarhi idānīm bhinnāt sahakāriṇaḥ kārya utpatteḥ yathā cakṣuḥ rūpaḥ ādeḥ vijñānasya na vai kiṃcid ekam janakam tat svabhāvam kim tu sāmagrī janikā tat svabhāvāḥ saḥ eva anumīyate saḥ eva ca sāmagrī svabhāva sthiti āśrayaḥ kāryasya atas eva sahakāriṇām api aparyāyeṇa jananam yat api kiṃcid 
PVSV_23,23–24,2	 vijātīyāt bhavat dṛṣṭam gomayaḥ ādeḥ śālukaḥ ādi tatra api tathā abhidhāne api asti eva sva bīja prabhavāt svabhāva bhedaḥ hetu svabhāva bhedāt yathā kadalī bīja kandaḥ udbhavāḥ sphuṭam eva tādṛśam lokaḥ vivecayati ākāra bhedāt tasmāt na su vivecitaḥ ākāram kāryam kāraṇam vyabhicarati anvaya vyatirekāt yaḥ yasya dṛṣṭaḥ anuvartakaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasya tat hetuḥ atas bhinnāt na sambhavaḥ 
PVSV_24,3–24,13	 iti saṃgraha ślokaḥ tasmāt sakṛt api darśanaḥ adarśanābhyām kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddheḥ bhavati tatas tat pratipattiḥ na anyathā anvaya vyatirekayoḥ niḥśeṣa darśanaḥ adarśanaḥ āyatta tvāt kvacid amūrta tve nitya tva darśane api anyatra anyathā adṛṣṭeḥ kvacid nitya tva abhāve api adṛṣṭasya punar dṛṣṭeḥ iti bhavatu kāryasya kāraṇena avinābhāvaḥ tad utpatteḥ svabhāvaḥ idānīm katham avinābhāvaḥ svabhāve api avinā abhāvaḥ bhāva mā atra anurodhini yaḥ hi bhāva mā atra anurodhī svabhāvaḥ tatra avinā abhāvaḥ bhāvasya iṣyate tat abhāve svayam bhāvasya abhāvaḥ syāt abhedataḥ 
PVSV_24,14–24,19	 yaḥ eva bhāvaḥ bhāva mā atra anurodhī svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate saḥ eva svayam vastutas bhāvaḥ sa ca ātmānam parityajya katham bhavet yaḥ eva tarhi kṛtakaḥ saḥ eva anityaḥ bheda abhāvāt pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ syāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt sarve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ svabhāva para bhāvābhyām yasmāt vyāvṛtti bhāginaḥ 
PVSV_24,20–25,2	 tasmāt yatas yatas arthānām vyāvṛttiḥ tat nibandhanāḥ jāti bhedāḥ prakalpyante tat viśeṣa avagāhinaḥ tasmāt yaḥ yena dharmeṇa viśeṣaḥ sampratīyate na sa śakyaḥ tatas anyena tena bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ sarve eva hi bhāvāḥ svarūpa sthitayaḥ te naḥ ātmānam pareṇa miśrayanti tasya aparatva prasaṅgāt yat api eṣām abhinnam ātma bhūtam rūpam na tat teṣām tadānīm teṣām abhāvāt tat eva hi syāt abhinnasya bhāvāt tat vyatiriktasya bhinnasya ca abhāvāt tasya eva ca punar bheda virodhāt tat ca ātmani vyavasthitam 
PVSV_25,3–25,7	 amiśram eva artha antaram api aneka sambandhe api na tat teṣām sāmānyam atat rūpa tvāt dvi tvaḥ ādi saṃyoga kārya dravyeṣu api prasaṅgāt na hi sambandhinā api anyena anye samānāḥ nāma tadvantaḥ nāma syuḥ bhūta vat kaṇṭhe guṇena na abhinna pratyaya viṣayāḥ bhūta vat tadā ātmānam eva hi buddhiḥ 
PVSV_25,8–25,12	 saṃsṛjantī sāmānya viṣayā pratibhāsate na eka sambandhinau iti bhūta vat tat darśinyāḥ sā bhrāntiḥ iti ced tat darśinī iti kutas nirbīja bhrānti ayogāt iti ced te eva tat eka kāryā bījam saṃkhyā saṃyoga kārya dravyaḥ ādimatsu bhūtaḥ ādiṣu abhāvāt ca tat na tathā sāmānya buddhau niveṣa abhāvāt sāmānyam anyat sati vā tasya api 
PVSV_25,13–25,17	 sva ātmani vyavasthānāt amiśraṇam anyena tasmāt ime bhāvāḥ sajātīya abhimatāt anyasmāt ca vyatiriktāḥ svabhāvena eka rūpa tvāt yatas yatas bhinnāḥ tat bheda pratyāyanāya kṛta saṃniveśaiḥ śabdaiḥ tatas tatas bhedam upādāya svabhāva abhede api aneka dharmāṇaḥ pratīyante te api śabdāḥ sarve bheda anākṣepe api eka 
PVSV_25,18–25,22	 bheda codanāt tat sva lakṣaṇa niṣṭhāḥ eva bhavanti tat ekasmāt api tasya bhedaḥ asti iti tasmāt ekasya bhāvasya yāvanti para rūpāṇi tāvat yaḥ tat apekṣayā vyāvṛttayaḥ tat asambhavi kārya kāraṇasya tat bhedāt yāvat yaḥ ca vyāvṛttayaḥ tāvat yaḥ śrutayaḥ atat kārya kāraṇa parihāreṇa vyavahāra arthāḥ yathā prayatna anantarīyakaḥ 
PVSV_25,23–26,3	 śabdaḥ śrāvaṇaḥ iti atat kārya kāraṇa parihāra arthaḥ tasmāt svabhāva abhede api yena yena dharmeṇa nāmnā yaḥ viśeṣaḥ bhedaḥ pratīyate na sa śakyaḥ anyena pratyāyayitum iti naḥ ekaḥ arthāḥ sarve śabdāḥ tat na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ iti katham punar etat gamyate vyavacchedaḥ śabda liṅgābhyām pratipādyate vidhinā na vastu rūpam eva iti pramāṇa antarasya śabda antarasya ca pravṛtteḥ tathā hi ekasya artha svabhāvasya pratyakṣasya sataḥ svayam kaḥ anyaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ bhāgaḥ syāt yaḥ pramāṇaiḥ parīkṣyate 
PVSV_26,4–26,13	 ekaḥ hi arthaḥ ātmā sa pratyakṣaḥ asiddhe dharmiṇi sādhana asambhavāt yathā anitya tve sādhye śabdaḥ tasya pratyakṣeṇa eva siddheḥ sarve ākāra siddhiḥ tat anyasya asiddhasya abhāvāt bhāve vā atat svabhāva tvam na hi yaḥ yat eka yogakṣemaḥ na bhavati sa tat svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ tat mā atra nibandhana tvāt bheda vyavahārasya anyathā abhāva prasaṅgāt iti uktam tasmāt pratyakṣe dharmiṇi tat svabhāva sākalya paricchedāt tatra anavakāśā pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ syāt no ced bhrānti nimittena saṃyojyeta guṇa antaram śuktau vā rajataḥ ākāraḥ rūpa sādharmya darśanāt 
PVSV_26,14–26,18	 yadi dṛṣṭa sarva tattvasya api bhāvasya tathā niścaya pratirodhinā bhrānti nimittena guṇa antaram na saṃyojyate yathā śuktau rajata ākāraḥ na hi śuktau dve rūpe samānam viśiṣṭam ca tathā pratipatti prasaṅgāt apratipattau vā vivekena dvi tva vikalpa ayogāt atiprasaṅgāt ca tasmāt paśyan śukti rūpam viśiṣṭam eva 
PVSV_26,19–27,4	 paśyati niścaya pratyaya vaikalyāt tu aniścinvan tat sāmānyam paśyāmi iti manyate tatas asya rajata samāropaḥ tathā sadṛśā para apara utpattyā alakṣita nānātvasya tat bhāva samāropāt sthitaḥ bhrāntiḥ yāvantaḥ asya para bhāvāḥ tāvantaḥ eva yathāsvam nimitta bhāvinaḥ samāropāḥ iti tat vyavacchedakāni bhavanti pramāṇāni sa phalāni syuḥ teṣām tu vyavaccheda phalānām na apratīta vastu aṃśa pratyāyane pravṛttiḥ tasya dṛṣṭa tvāt anaṃśasya ca eka deśena darśana ayogāt tasmāt dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭaḥ eva akhilaḥ guṇaḥ bhrānteḥ niścīyate naḥ iti sādhanam sampravartate 
PVSV_27,5–27,13	 iti saṃgraha ślokaḥ tasmāt na adṛṣṭa grahaṇāya dṛṣṭe pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ vastu grahe anumānāt ca dharmasya ekasya niścaye sarva dharma grahaḥ apohe na ayam doṣaḥ prasajyate na kevalam pratyakṣa dṛṣṭe pramāṇa antara avṛttiḥ kvacid yadā anumānam api vastu vidhinā pratyāyayati na vyavaccheda kṛt tadā eka dharma niścaye tat avyatirekāt sarva dharma niścayaḥ iti pramāṇa antara avṛttiḥ na hi tasmin niścite tad ātmā aniścitaḥ yuktaḥ yadā punar anumānena samāropa vyavacchedaḥ kriyate tadā naḥ eka 
PVSV_27,14–27,18	 samāropa vyavacchedāt anyaḥ vyavacchedaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavati iti tat artham anyat pravartate nanu na avaśyam viparyāsa pūrvakaḥ eva apratīta niścayaḥ bhavati yathā akasmāt dhūmāt agni pratipattiḥ na hi tatra anagni samāropaḥ sambhāvyate tat na sarvatra vyavacchedaḥ kriyate uktam atra dharmi pratipattau abhedāt sarve pratipattiḥ 
PVSV_27,19–28,7	 bhede vā asambaddhasya tatra apratipattiḥ iti tasmāt tatra api tat darśinaḥ tat svabhāva aniścayaḥ kutas viparyāsāt sa ca tam pradeśam tat viviktena rūpeṇa niścinvan agni sattā bhāvanā vimuktayā buddhyā katham aviparyastaḥ nāma tat ākāra samāropa saṃśaya rahitaḥ ca tat pratipattau na liṅgam anusaret na ca tasya anvaya vyatirekayoḥ ādriyeta tasmāt apoha viṣayam iti liṅgam prakīrtitam anyathā dharmiṇaḥ siddhau asiddham kim atas param iti saṃgraha ślokaḥ kvacid dṛṣṭe api yat jñānam sāmānya artham vikalpakam asamāropita anyaḥ aṃśe tat mā atra apoha gocaram 
PVSV_28,8–28,18	 yat rūpaḥ ādi darśana anantaram aliṅgam niścaya jñānam bhavati tat katham asati samārope bhavat vyavaccheda viṣayam bhavati samāropa viṣaye tasya abhāvāt yatra hi asya samāropaḥ yathā sthiraḥ sa ātmakaḥ iti vā na tatra bhede niścayaḥ bhavati niścayaḥ āropa manasoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvataḥ na hi sarvatas bhinnaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ api bhāvaḥ tathā eva pratyabhijñāyate kvacid bhede vyavadhāna sambhavāt yathā śukteḥ śukti tve yatra tu pratipattuḥ bhrānti nimittam na asti tatra eva asya tat darśana aviśeṣe api smārtaḥ niścayaḥ bhavati samāropa niścayayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvāt niścayasya samāropa viveke asya pravṛttiḥ iti gamyate 
PVSV_28,19–29,2	 tat vivekaḥ eva ca anya apohaḥ tasmāt tat api tat mā atra apoha gocaram na vastu svabhāva niścayaḥ ātmakam tathā hi kasyacid niścaye api anyasya apratipatti darśanāt tat svabhāva niścaye ca tasya ayogāt yāvantaḥ aṃśa samāropāḥ tat nirāse viniścayāḥ tāvantāḥ eva śabdāḥ ca tena te bhinna gocarāḥ 
PVSV_29,3–29,10	 anyathā ekena śabdena vyāptaḥ ekatra vastuni buddhyā vā na anyaḥ viṣayaḥ iti paryāyatā bhavet iti antaraślokaḥ yasya api nānā upādheḥ dhīḥ grāhika arthasya bhedinaḥ yaḥ api manyate bhinnāḥ eva upādhayaḥ parasparam āśrayāt ca tat nibandhanāḥ śrutayaḥ tat ādhāreṣu vartante tatra eva vā tat ayam aprasaṅgaḥ iti tasya api nānā upādhi upakāra aṅga śakti abhinnaḥ ātmanaḥ grahe 
PVSV_29,11–29,19	 sarva ātmanā upakārasya kaḥ bhedakaḥ syāt aniścitaḥ yadi api upādhayaḥ bhinnāḥ eva śabda jñāna antarāṇām nimittam arthe sa tu taiḥ tadvān ekaḥ eva upalīyate tasya nānā upādhīnām upakāraḥ āśraya śakti svabhāvasya sva ātmani abhedāt sarva ātmanā grahaṇe kaḥ eva upādhi bhedaḥ aniścitaḥ syāt sarve upādhi upakāraka tvena grahaṇāt na hi upakāraka tvam anyat eva tasya sva rūpeṇa gṛhyamāṇasya agṛhītam nāma atas yat eva asya svabhāvena grahaṇam tat eva upakāra tvena api iti tayoḥ ātmani sambandhāt eka jñāne dvaya grahaḥ 
PVSV_29,20–29,24	 ātma bhūtasya upādhi tadvatoḥ upakārya upakāraka bhāvasya grahaṇāt eka jñāne dvayoḥ api grahaṇam iti ekaḥ upādhi viśiṣṭe api tasmin gṛhyamāṇe sarve upādhīnām grahaṇam tat grahaṇa na antarīyaka tvāt upādhimat grahaṇasya anyathā tathā api na gṛhyeta na hi anyaḥ eva anyaḥ upakārakaḥ yaḥ na gṛhītaḥ syāt na ca api upakārake 
PVSV_29,25–30,2	 tathā gṛhīte upakārya agrahaṇam tasya api agrahaṇa prasaṅgāt sva svāmitva vat tasmāt artha antare upādhi vāde api samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ atha api syāt bhinnāḥ eva śaktayaḥ śaktimataḥ yābhiḥ upādhīn upakaroti tatas na ayam prasaṅgaḥ iti dharmaḥ upakāra śaktīnām bhede tāḥ tasya kim yadi na upakāraḥ tatas tāsām tathā syāt anavasthitiḥ 
PVSV_30,3–30,7	 yadi pratyupādhi upakāraka tvāni tasya na sva ātma bhūtāni eva na api tatas upakāram anubhavanti kim tasya iti tāḥ ucyante upakāre vā sva ātma bhūtābhiḥ ayam ekaḥ śaktibhiḥ śaktīḥ upakurvan ekaḥ upādhinā api gṛhyamāṇaḥ sarva ātmanā gṛhyate eva tathā hi ekaḥ upādhi grahaṇe tat upakāriṇyāḥ śakteḥ grahaṇam tat grahaṇe 
PVSV_30,8–30,12	 tat upakārī bhāvaḥ sva ātma bhūta sakala śakti upakāraḥ gṛhītaḥ sarvāḥ śaktīḥ grāhayati tāḥ ca svaḥ upādhīn iti tat avasthaḥ prasaṅgaḥ atha tāḥ api śakti upakāriṇyaḥ śaktayaḥ bhinnāḥ eva bhāvāt evam upādhīnām tat śaktīnām ca aparā parāsu eva śaktiṣu aparyavasānena ghaṭanāt saḥ ekaḥ tābhiḥ kadācid api agṛhīta s 
PVSV_30,13–30,17	 tat upakāraḥ ātmā tadvat tvena na gṛhyate yadi punar kevalān eva upādhīn śabda jñānāni upalīyeran tadā tasya asamāveṣāt na bhavati tat pratipatti mukhena sarve pratipattiḥ tadā api tasya śabdaiḥ anākṣepāt na syāt tatra pravṛttiḥ iti vyarthaḥ śabda prayogaḥ syāt artha kriyāḥ āśrayaḥ hi sarvaḥ vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām vyavahāraḥ 
PVSV_30,18–30,22	 upādhayaḥ ca tatra asamarthāḥ samarthaḥ ca naḥ eva ucyate iti kim śabda prayogaiḥ tatas ca upādhayaḥ naḥ upādhayaḥ syuḥ kvacid pravṛttau hi kasyacid pradhānasya aṅga bhāvāt tat apekṣayā tathā ucyate tasya śabdaiḥ anākṣepāt na te kasyacid aṅga bhūtāḥ iti kim upādhayaḥ lakṣita lakṣaṇāt adoṣaḥ iti ced samānaḥ 
PVSV_30,23–31,4	 prasaṅgaḥ sa tāvat taiḥ upādhibhiḥ na antarīyaka tayā upalakṣyamāṇaḥ ekena api upalakṣaṇe sarva ātmanā upalakṣitaḥ iti tat avasthaḥ prasaṅgaḥ kaḥ hi atra viśeṣaḥ śabdāḥ vai enam upalakṣayeyuḥ tat lakṣitāḥ vā upādhayaḥ sa tāvat tadānīm niścīyate sarve upakārakaḥ iti na kiṃcid etat tasmāt ekaḥ upakārake grāhye naḥ upakāraḥ tatas apare dṛṣṭe tasmin adṛṣṭāḥ ye tat grahe sakala grahaḥ 
PVSV_31,5–31,17	 iti saṃgraha ślokaḥ yadi bhrānti nivṛtti artham gṛhīte api anyat iṣyate syāt etat nirbhāgasya vastunaḥ grahaṇe kaḥ anyaḥ tadā na gṛhītaḥ nāma sa tu bhrāntyā na avadhāryate iti pramāṇa antaram pravartate yadi evam tat vyavaccheda viṣayam siddham tadvat tatas aparam asamāropa viṣaye vṛtteḥ tat tarhi bhrānti nivṛtti artham pravṛttam pramāṇam anya samāropa vyavaccheda phalam iti siddham anya apoha viṣayam tadvat anyat api asamāropa viṣaye vṛtteḥ yatra asya samāropaḥ na tatra niścayaḥ iti samāropa abhāve vartamānaḥ anya apoha viṣayaḥ siddhaḥ api ca niścayaiḥ yat na niścīyate rūpam tat teṣām viṣayaḥ katham 
PVSV_31,18–31,22	 iyam eva khalu niścayānām sva artha pratipattiḥ yat tat niścayanam tat ced ākāra antara vat aniścitam katham taiḥ gṛhītam katham idānīm aniścīyamānam pratyakṣeṇa api gṛhītam nāma na pratyakṣam kasyacid niścāyakam tat ayam api gṛhṇāti tat na niścayena kim tarhi tat pratibhāsena tat na niścaya aniścaya 
PVSV_31,23–32,2	 vaśāt pratyakṣasya grahaṇa agrahaṇe na evam niścayānām kiṃcid niścinvataḥ api anyatra aniścayena pravṛtti bhedāt grahaṇa agrahaṇam tasmāt tat eva asya grahaṇam yaḥ niścayaḥ anyathā ekaḥ ākāre api tat na syāt kim punar kāraṇam sarvatas bhinne vastu rūpe anubhavaḥ utpattau api tathā eva na smārtaḥ niścayaḥ bhavati sahakāri vaikalyāt tatas ca pratyakṣeṇa gṛhīte api viśeṣe aṃśa vivarjite yat viśeṣa avasāye asti pratyakṣaḥ sa pratīyate 
PVSV_32,3–32,7	 yadi api aṃśa rahitaḥ sarvatas bhinna svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ anubhūtaḥ tathā api na sarve bhedeṣu tāvatā niścayaḥ bhavati kāraṇa antara apekṣya tvāt anubhavaḥ hi yathā avikalpa abhyāsam niścaya pratyayān janayati yathā rūpa darśanaḥ aviśeṣe api kuṇapa kāminī bhakṣya vikalpāḥ tatra buddhi pāṭavam tat vāsanāḥ abhyāsaḥ prakaraṇam 
PVSV_32,8–32,14	 iti ādayaḥ anubhavāt bheda niścayaḥ utpatti sahakāriṇaḥ teṣām eva ca pratyāsatti tāratamya ādi bhedāt paurvāparyam yathā janakatva adhyāpaka tva aviśeṣe api pitaram āyāntam dṛṣṭvā pitā me āgacchati naḥ upādhyāyaḥ iti saḥ api bhavat niścayaḥ asati bhrānti kāraṇe bhavati tasmāt na abhūtaḥ iti eva sarve ākāra niścayaḥ tatra api ca anya vyāvṛttiḥ anya vyāvṛttaḥ iti api śabdāḥ ca niścayāḥ ca eva saṃketam anurundhate 
PVSV_32,15–32,23	 tatra api anya apohe na vyāvṛttiḥ anyā anyaḥ eva vyāvṛttaḥ tat vyāvṛtteḥ nivartamānasya tat bhāva prasaṅgāt tathā ca vyāvṛtteḥ abhāvaḥ tasmāt yā eva vyāvṛttiḥ saḥ eva vyāvṛttaḥ śabda pratipatti bhedaḥ tu saṃketa bhedāt na vācya bhedaḥ asti nanu ca vācya viśeṣa abhāvāt saṃketa bhedaḥ api ayuktaḥ dvayoḥ ekaḥ abhidhānāt tathā ca vyatirekiṇyā vibhakteḥ ayogaḥ tasyāḥ bhedaḥ āśraya tvāt dvayoḥ ekaḥ abhidhāne api vibhaktiḥ vyatirekiṇī bhinnam artham iva anveti vācye leśa viśeṣataḥ 
PVSV_32,24–32,28	 na vai śabdānām kācid viṣaya svabhāvaḥ āyattā vṛttiḥ icchātaḥ vṛtti abhāva prasaṅgāt te yathā vyatirikte avyatirikte vā prayoktum iṣyante tathā niyuktāḥ tam artham pratibandhena prakāśayanti tena gauḥ go tvam iti ekaḥ arthaḥ abhidhāne api kasyacid viśeṣasya pratyāyana artham kṛte saṃketa bhede vyatirikta arthā 
PVSV_33,1–33,8	 vibhaktiḥ artha antaram iva adarśayantī pratibhāti anartha antare api tathā prayoga darśana abhyāsāt na tāvatā sarvatra bhedaḥ anyatra api puruṣaḥ icchā vaśāt pravṛttasya pratibandha abhāvāt yathā ekam kvacid eka vacanena khyāpyate tat aviśeṣe api gaurava ādi khyāpana artham bahu vacanena prayojana abhāvāt tu saṃketa bhedaḥ na syāt tat api asti eva tathā hi bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepau tayoḥ dvayoḥ saṃketa bhedasya padam jñātṛ vāñcāḥ anurodhinaḥ 
PVSV_33,9–33,13	 yadā ayam pratipattā tat anyaḥ vyavaccheda bhāva anapekṣaḥ piṇḍa viśeṣe aśva vyavaccheda mātram jijñāsate tathā abhūta jñāpana artham tathā ākṛta saṃketena śabdena prabodhyata anaśva tvam asya asti iti yadā punar vyavaccheda antara anirākāṅkṣaḥ tam jñātum icchati tadā aparityakta vyavaccheda antare tatra eva aśva vyavacchede 
PVSV_33,14–33,23	 tathā aprakāśanāya prayuñjate anaśvaḥ ayam iti atas eva pūrvatra pratikṣipta bheda antara tvāt śabda vṛtteḥ na sāmānādhikaraṇyam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ vā go tvam asya śuklam iti tat mā atra viśeṣeṇa buddheḥ tat āśraya bhūtāyāḥ ekatvena apratibhāsanāt nirākāṅkṣa tvāt ca dvitīye tu bhavati tathā saṃketa anusāreṇa saṃhṛta sakala vyavaccheda dharmaiḥ vibhāgavataḥ ekasya iva sandarśanena pratibhāsanāt vyavaccheda antara sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt ca bhedaḥ ayam eva sarvatra dravya bhāva abhidhāyinoḥ śabdayoḥ na tayoḥ vācye viśeṣaḥ tena kaścana 
PVSV_34,1–34,6	 tasmāt na sarvatra dharma dharmi vācinoḥ śabdayoḥ vācye arthe niścaya pratyaya viṣaya tvena kaścid viśeṣaḥ ekaḥ tam eva pratyāyayan pratikṣipta bheda antaraḥ pratyāyayati anyaḥ pratikṣepeṇa iti ayam viśeṣaḥ jijñāpayiṣuḥ artham tam tat hitena kṛtāḥ api vā anyena vā yadi brūyāt bhedaḥ na asti tatas aparaḥ 
PVSV_34,7–34,11	 etāvantam eva ca bhedam darśayan tad hitena vā darśayet pācaka tvam iti kṛtā api vā pākaḥ iti anyena vā tathā abhūta jñāpanāya svayam kṛtena samayena na punar tathā abhidhāna mātreṇa artha antaram eva tat bhavati tathābhūtasya eva jñāpanāya śabdasya kṛta saṃketa tvāt nanu ca pācaka tvam iti sambandha 
PVSV_34,12–34,18	 ucyate na pākaḥ eva na vai pākena anyaḥ eva kaścid pācakaḥ nāma abhidhīyate yādṛśaḥ varṇyate yat punar asya abhidheyam tat kathitam tat eva pācaka tvena api iti alam apratiṣṭhaiḥ mithyā vikalpaiḥ yathā ca na artha antara bhūtā kriyā asti tat samavāyaḥ vā tat pratyāyayiṣyāmaḥ tena anya apoha viṣaye tadvat pakṣaḥ upavarṇanam pratyākhyātam pṛthaktve hi syāt doṣaḥ jāti tadvatoḥ 
PVSV_34,19–34,23	 yat āhuḥ anya apohe api śabdaḥ arthe tat viśiṣṭasya abhidhānāt tadvat pakṣaḥ uditaḥ sarvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ samānaḥ iti tat api anena prativyūḍham tatra hi artha antaram upādāya anyatra vartamānaḥ dhvaniḥ asvātantryaḥ ādi doṣaiḥ upadrūyate na ca artha antaram anyasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ vyāvṛttāt dvayoḥ ekaḥ abhidhānāt iti uktam katham 
PVSV_34,24–35,2	 idānīm ekasya vyāvṛttasya anyaḥ ananugamāt anya vyāvṛttiḥ sāmānyam tat buddhau tathā pratibhāsanāt na vai kiṃcid sāmānyam nāma asti śabdaḥ āśrayā buddhiḥ anādi vāsanā sāmarthyāt asaṃsṛṣṭān api dharmān saṃsṛjantī jāyate tasyāḥ pratibhāsa vaśena sāmānyam sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca vyavasthāpyate asat arthaḥ api arthānām saṃsarga bhedaḥ abhāvāt tasya sarvasya 
PVSV_35,3–35,7	 tat kārya kāraṇa tayā anyebhyaḥ bhidyamānāḥ arthāḥ samāśrayaḥ dhvaniḥ ca aniṣṭa parihāreṇa pravartayati iti anya apoha viṣayaḥ uktaḥ tatra anapekṣita bāhya tattvaḥ buddhi pratibhāsa vaśāt ekaḥ aneka vyāvṛttaḥ śabdaiḥ viṣayīkriyate tat anubhavaḥ āhita vāsanā prabodha janmabhiḥ vikalpaiḥ adhyavasita tat bhāva arthaiḥ tatra eva 
PVSV_35,8–35,12	 ca ayam dharma dharmi vyavahāraḥ parasparam tattva anya tvābhyām avācyaḥ pratanyate na hi anyaḥ dharmaḥ dharmiṇaḥ anartha antara abhidhānāt na api saḥ eva tat vācinām iva dharma vācinām api vyavaccheda antaraḥ ākṣepa prasaṅgāt tathā ca iṣṭa pratyāyanāt saṃketa bhedaḥ akaraṇam iti etat śabdaḥ arthe avācya tvam 
PVSV_35,13–35,19	 dharma dharmiṇoḥ vastuni tu sva lakṣaṇe sāmānya lakṣaṇam avācyam abhāvāt nanu ca dharma dharmiṇoḥ abhede bhede vā dṛṣṭāḥ ṣaṣṭhī ādi vibhaktayaḥ dharma bahu tvāt tatra dṛṣṭaḥ vacana bhedaḥ ca dharmiṇi na syāt uktam atra śabdānām svātantrya abhāvāt iti api ca yeṣām vastu vaśāḥ vācaḥ na vivakṣā para āśrayāḥ ṣaṣṭhī vacana bhedaḥ ādi ca udyam tān prati yuktimat 
PVSV_35,20–36,9	 yadi nāma ete śabdāḥ puruṣaiḥ kvacid praṇinīṣitāḥ api na śakyante praṇetum vastu pratibandhāt dhūmaḥ ādi vat tadā ayam upālambhaḥ syāt katham ṣaṣṭhī ādayaḥ iti yadā punar yat yathā vācaka tvena vaktṛbhiḥ viniyamyate anapekṣita bāhya artham tat tathā vācakam vacaḥ na hi vyatireke ṣaṣṭhī bāhulye jaḥ ādayaḥ iti etat api puruṣa abhiprāya nirapekṣam vastu saṃnidhi mātreṇa svayam pravṛttam te tu tatra tathā prayuñjate iti tatas tathā pratipattiḥ bhavati evam anyatra api kathaṃcid taiḥ prayuktāḥ tathā eva prati iti hetavaḥ bhavanti tatra vācyeṣu puruṣaḥ āyatta vṛttīnām śabdānām avastu 
PVSV_36,10–36,19	 sandarśinām yathā abhyāsam vikalpa prabodha hetūnām pravṛtti cintā tat vaśāt vastu vyavasthāpanam ca kevalam jāḍya khyāpanam tathā akṛta vyavasthāḥ śabdāḥ dharma dharmī ādiṣu na punar vyatireka vastu bhedāt iti kutas etat tathā vyavahāra ayogāt na hi dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhede tattva rūpa tve vā sāmānya tat sambandha sāmānādhikaraṇya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvāḥ yujyante śabdānām vā yathā avastu vṛttau iti vakṣyāmaḥ yaḥ ca ayam sarvatra vastu kṛtam eva śabda pravṛtti bhedam icchati tasya dārāḥ ṣaṇṇagarī iti ādau bhedaḥ abheda vyavasthiteḥ khasya svabhāvaḥ kha tvam ca iti atra vā kim nibandhanam 
PVSV_36,21–36,25	 yadā ekā api strī dārāḥ ekam api sikatā dravyam sikatā iti vyavahāraḥ tatra kim bāhulyam yena evam bhavati śakti bhedaḥ iti ced sarvatra utsannam idānīm eka vacanam eka śakteḥ abhāvāt yatnaḥ ca vyarthaḥ vastu abhedāt anyatra eka vacanam iti ced iha api astu tat ayam nirvastukaḥ niyamaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ svātantryam 
PVSV_36,26–37,4	 icchāyāḥ śabda prayoge khyāpayati ṣaṇṇagarī iti ca katham bahuṣu eka vacanam na hi nagarāṇi eva kiṃcid kutas teṣām samāhāraḥ prāsāda puruṣaḥ ādīnām vijātīyānām anārambhāt kutas tat samudāyaḥ dravyam asaṃyogāḥ ca na saṃyogaḥ prāsādasya svayam saṃyogaḥ ātmakasya pareṇa asaṃyogāt ca tatas eva saṃkhyāḥ abhāvaḥ tat saṃyoga puruṣa viśiṣṭā 
PVSV_37,5–37,9	 sattā nagaram iti ced kim asyāḥ niratiśayāyāḥ viśeṣaṇam sattāyāḥ ca eka tvāt nagara bahu tve api nagarāṇi iti bahu vacanam na syāt dvayasya paraspara sahita tā iti ced anupakārya upakārakaḥ kaḥ sahāyībhāvaḥ puruṣa saṃyoga sattānām ca bahu tvāt nagaram iti katham eka vacanam tathābhūtānām kvacid 
PVSV_37,10–37,14	 arthe abhinnā śaktiḥ asti sā nimittam iti ced na śakteḥ vastu rūpa avyatirekāt vyatireke vai anupakāryasya pāratantrya ayogāt upakāre vā śakti upakāriṇyāḥ api śakteḥ vyatirekaḥ iti anavasthiteḥ apratipattiḥ tat avyatireke vā ādyāyām api prasaṅgaḥ iti yat kiṃcid etat khasya svabhāvaḥ kha tvam iti vyatirekaḥ āśrayā 
PVSV_37,15–37,19	 ṣaṣṭhī na syāt na hi tatra sāmānyam asti na api vibhu tve ādayaḥ guṇāḥ tathā ucyante artha antarasya tat svabhāva tva ayogāt teṣām ca niḥsvabhāva tva prasaṅgāt tasya api artha antara svabhāva tve atiprasaṅgaḥ tathā ca apratipattiḥ evam ṣaṭ padārtha vargaḥ ādayaḥ api vācyāḥ na hi tatra sāmānyam saṃkhyā saṃyogaḥ vā sambhavati 
PVSV_37,20–37,24	 katham idānīm asati atiśaye khasya svabhāvaḥ iti na tu kham iti eva khasya artha antara sādhāraṇa rūpa aparāmarśena kha śabda pravṛtti nibandhanam rūpam tathā jijñāsāyām evam ucyate nanu sarvatas vyāvṛttasya rūpasya abhidhānam na sambhavati na vai tat eva rūpam buddhau samarpyate anatīndriya tva 
PVSV_37,25–38,2	 prasaṅgāt kevalam ayam tathābhūtam pratyāyayiṣyāmi iti śabdena śrotari asaṃsṛṣṭa tat svabhāvam vikalpa pratibimbam arpayati yat āha adṛṣṭa arthe artha vikalpa mātram iti na evam pratipādya pratipādakābhyām sva lakṣaṇam pratipannam pratipāditam vā bhavati svarge ādi śravaṇe api tat anubhāvinām iva 
PVSV_38,3–38,12	 pratibhāsa abheda prasaṅgāt tasmāt ayam apratipadyamānaḥ api bhāva svabhāvam tathābhūtaḥ eva vikalpa pratibimbe tat adhyavasāyī saṃtuṣyati tathābhūta tvāt eva śabdaḥ artha pratipatteḥ tena etat evam ucyate śabdaḥ sva rūpam āha iti na punar svarūpa pratibhāsasya eva vijñānasya jananāt katham tarhi idānīm ekānta vyāvṛtta rūpeṣu bhāveṣu sāmānyam nāma teṣām asaṃsargāt anyasya ca abhāvāt uktam yādṛśam sāmānyam asaṃsṛṣṭānām ekaḥ asaṃsargaḥ tat vyatirekiṇām samāna tā iti api ca para rūpam svarūpeṇa yayā saṃvriyate dhiyā ekaḥ artha pratibhāsinyāḥ bhāvān āśritya bhedinaḥ 
PVSV_38,13–38,21	 tayā saṃvṛta nānā arthāḥ saṃvṛtyā bhedinaḥ svayam abhedinaḥ iva ābhānti bhāvāḥ rūpeṇa kenacid tasyāḥ abhiprāya vaśāt sāmānyam sat prakīrtitam tat asat parama arthena yathā saṃkalpitam tayā buddhiḥ khalu tat anyaḥ vyatirekiṇaḥ padārthān āśritya utpadyamānā vikalpikā sve vāsanā prakṛtim anuvidadhatī bhinnam eṣām rūpam tirodhāya pratibhāsam abhinnam ātmīyam adhyasya tān saṃsṛjantī sandarśayati sā ca eka sādhya sādhana tayā anya vivekinām bhāvānām tat vikalpa vāsanāyāḥ ca prakṛtiḥ yat evam 
PVSV_38,22–38,26	 eṣā pratibhāti tat udbhavāḥ sā ca saṃvṛtiḥ saṃvriyate anayā sva rūpeṇa para rūpam iti te ca tayā saṃvṛta bhedāḥ svayam bhedinaḥ api abhedinaḥ iva kenacid rūpeṇa pratibhānti tat eṣām buddhi pratibhāsam anurundhānaiḥ buddhi parivartinām eva bhāvānām ākāra viśeṣa parigrahāt bahis iva parisphuratām sāmānyam 
PVSV_39,1–39,5	 iti ucyate katham idānīm anya apohaḥ sāmānyam saḥ eva khalu anya apohaḥ tam eva gṛhṇatī sā prakṛti vibhramāt vikalpānām vastu grāhiṇī iva pratibhāti sā hi tat anya vivekiṣu eva bhāveṣu bhavantī viveka viṣayāḥ iti gamyate nanu bāhyāḥ vivekinaḥ na ca teṣu vikalpa pravṛttiḥ iti katham teṣu bhavati vyākhyātāraḥ 
PVSV_39,6–39,10	 khalu evam vivecayanti na vyavahartāraḥ te tu sve ālambanam eva artha kriyāḥ yogyam manyamānāḥ dṛśya vikalpyau arthau ekīkṛtya pravartante tat abhiprāya vaśāt evam ucyate tat kāritayā atat kāribhyaḥ bhinnān tathā śabdena pratipādayanti iti pratibhāsa bhedaḥ ādibhyaḥ tu tattva cintakāḥ na abhedam anumanyante 
PVSV_39,11–39,15	 yadi pratipattṛ abhiprāyaḥ anuvidhīyate anya apohaḥ api sāmānyam mā bhūt na hi evam pratipattiḥ iti na vai kevalam evam apratipattiḥ vyakti vyatirikta avyatiriktaḥ eka nitya vyāpitaḥ ādi ākāraiḥ api naḥ eva pratipattiḥ kevalam abhinnaḥ ākārā buddhiḥ utpadyate tasyāḥ kaḥ āśrayaḥ iti anya apohaḥ ucyate tasya vastuṣu 
PVSV_39,16–39,21	 bhāvāt avirodhāt vyavahārasya ca śabdaḥ āśrayasya tathā darśanāt na punar vastu bhūtam kiṃcid sāmānyam nāma asti yathā iyam buddhiḥ pratibhāti yasmāt vyaktayaḥ na anuyanti anyat anuyāyi na bhāsate na hi imāḥ vyaktayaḥ parasparam anvāviśanti bheda abhāve na sāmānyasya eva abhāva prasaṅgāt anyat ca na tābhyaḥ vyatiriktam 
PVSV_39,22–39,26	 kiṃcid tathā buddhau pratibhāti apratibhāsamānam ca katham ātmanā anyam grāhayet vyapadeśayet vā na ca taiḥ sambaddham ekam iti eva sāmānyam bhavati atiprasaṅgāt iti uktam abhinna abhidhāna pratyaya nimittam ekam sāmānyam na sarvam iti ced katham anyatas anyatra pratyaya vṛttiḥ tat sambandhāt 
PVSV_39,27–40,5	 saṃkhyā kārya dravyaḥ ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ asāmānyaḥ ātmaka tvāt naḥ iti ced nanu saḥ eva ayam vicāryate kaḥ ayam sāmānyaḥ ātmā iti tatra sati sambandhe pratyaya vṛttiḥ tatas sāmānyam iti atra ucyate aneka sambandhebhyaḥ kārya dravyaḥ ādibhyaḥ nimitta sambhavāt pratyaya vṛttiḥ tatas ca sāmānyaḥ ātma tā anyathā anyatra api mā bhūt viśeṣa abhāvāt tathā ca dravya guṇa sāmānyānām rūpa saṃkaraḥ iti evam tarhi buddheḥ eva pratibhāsaḥ jñāna rūpa tvāt san eva sāmānyam tat na yasmāt jñānāt avyatiriktam ca katham artha antaram vrajet 
PVSV_40,6–40,16	 jñānasya rūpam katham arthānām sāmānyam tasya teṣu abhāvāt tat bhāva adhyavasāyāt tathā bhrāntyā vyavahāraḥ iti ced tatra tathā jñānaḥ utpatteḥ kim nibandhanam anāśrayasya ca utpattau sarvatra syāt athavā jñānāt avyatiriktam ekasmāt katham anyasya punar jñānasya rūpam syāt vyakti antara bhāvinaḥ te tas ca jñāna antaram vyakti antaram vā avyāpnuvat katham sāmānyam syāt tasmāt mithyā vikalpaḥ ayam artheṣu eka ātma tā grahaḥ na hi arthāḥ vyatiriktena avyatiriktena vā kenacid ātmanā samānāḥ tathā eṣām grahaṇam mithyā vikalpaḥ eva itaretara bhedaḥ asya bījam saṃjñā yat arthikāḥ 
PVSV_40,17–40,25	 yasya pratyāyana artham saṃketaḥ kriyate abhinna sādhyān bhāvān atat sādhyebhyaḥ bhedena jñātvā tat parihāreṇa pravarteta iti saḥ ayam itaretara bhedaḥ tasya eka ātma tā pratibhāsinaḥ mithyā vikalpasya bījam tam eva gṛhṇan eṣa vikalpaḥ sve vāsanā prakṛteḥ evam pratibhāti katham punar bhinnānām abhinnam kāryam yena tat anyebhyaḥ bhedāt abhedaḥ iti ucyate prakṛtiḥ eṣā bhavānām yat eka pratyavamarśa artha jñānaḥ ādi ekaḥ artha sādhane bhede api niyatāḥ kecid svabhāvena indriyaḥ ādi vat 
PVSV_41,1–41,8	 yathā indriya viṣayaḥ āloka manaskārāḥ ātmā indriya manaḥ artha tat saṃnikarṣāḥ vai asati api tat bhāva niyate sāmānye rūpa vijñānam ekam janayanti evam śiṃśapāḥ ādayaḥ api bhedāḥ paraspara ananvaye api prakṛtyāḥ eva ekam ekaḥ ākāram pratyabhijñānam janayanti anyām vā yathā pratyayam dahana gṛhe ādikān kāṣṭha sādhyām artha kriyām na tu bhedaḥ aviśeṣe api jalaḥ ādayaḥ śrotṛ ādi vat rūpaḥ ādi jñāne jvaraḥ ādi śamane kāścid saha pratyekam eva vā dṛṣṭāḥ yathā vai oṣadhayaḥ nānātve api na ca aparāḥ 
PVSV_41,9–41,13	 yathā vā guḍūcī vyakti ādayaḥ saha pratyekam vā jvaraḥ ādi śamana lakṣaṇam ekam kāryam kurvanti na ca tatra sāmānyam apekṣante bhede api tat prakṛti tvāt na tat aviśeṣe api dadhi trapusā ādayaḥ syāt etat sāmānyam eva kiṃcid tāsu tathābhūtāsu vidyate tatas eva tat ekam kāryam iti tat ayuktam 
PVSV_41,14–42,1	 aviśeṣān sāmānyasya na sāmānyam tat kārya kṛt tasya api aviśeṣa prasaṅgataḥ tāsām kṣetre ādi bhede api yadi hi sāmānyāt jvaraḥ ādi śamanam kāryam syāt tasya aviśeṣāt vyaktīnām kṣetre ādi bhede api cira śīghra praśamane ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ guṇa tāratamyam ca na syāt viśeṣe vā sāmānyasya svabhāva bhedāt svarūpa hānam dhrauvyāt ca sāmānyasya anupakārataḥ 
PVSV_42,2–42,6	 yadi hi upakuryāt anādheya viśeṣasya ananya apekṣaṇāt sakṛt sarvam sva kāryam janayet na vā tat janana svabhāvam vyaktayaḥ tu kāla deśa saṃskāra vaśena viśiṣṭaḥ utpattayaḥ viśeṣa vat kāryam kuryuḥ iti avirodhaḥ tadvat arthāḥ api kecid svabhāva bhede api eka pratyabhijñānaḥ ādikām artha kriyām kurvantaḥ tat akāribhyaḥ 
PVSV_42,7–42,11	 bhedāt abhinnāḥ iti ucyante ekena vā anekaḥ janitaḥ atat janyebhyaḥ bhedāt kim punar anena bheda lakṣaṇena sāmānyena sva lakṣaṇam samānam iti pratyeyam atha anyat eva kim ca atas yadi sva lakṣaṇam katham vikalpasya viṣayaḥ anyatas vā katham artha kriyā sva lakṣaṇe ca anitya tvaḥ ādi pratīteḥ atādrūpyam teṣām 
PVSV_42,12–42,16	 ca avastu dharmatā na eṣa doṣaḥ jñāna pratibhāsini arthe sāmānya sāmāna adhikaraṇya dharma dharmi vyavahārāḥ yat etat jñānam vastu svabhāva grāhiṇa anubhavena āhitām vāsanām āśritya vikalpakam utpadyate atad viṣayam api tat viṣayam iva tat anubhava āhita vāsanā prabhava prakṛteḥ adhyavasita tat bhāva svarūpam 
PVSV_42,17–42,21	 abhinna kārya padārtha prasūteḥ abhinnaḥ artha grāhī iva tat anyaḥ bheda parama artha samānaḥ ākāram tatra yaḥ arthaḥ ākāraḥ pratibhāti bāhyaḥ iva ekaḥ iva anartha kriyā kāry api tat kārī iva vyavahāriṇām tathā adhyavasāya pravṛtteḥ anyathā pravṛtti ayogāt tat artha kriyā kāritayā pratibhāsanāt tat akāribhyaḥ bhinnam iva na ca tat 
PVSV_42,22–42,26	 tattvam parīkṣā anaṅga tvāt iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ te arthāḥ buddhi niveśinaḥ tena samānāḥ iti gṛhyante kutaścid vyāvṛttyā pratibhāsanāt na sva lakṣaṇam tatra apratibhāsanāt te eva ca kutaścid vyāvṛttāḥ punar anyatas api vyāvṛttimantaḥ abhinnāḥ ca pratibhānti iti svayam asatām api tathā buddhyā upadarśanān 
PVSV_43,1–43,5	 mithyā arthaḥ eva sāmānya sāmānā adhikaraṇya vyavahāraḥ kriyate sarvaḥ ca ayam sva lakṣaṇānām eva darśanaḥ āhita vāsanā kṛtaḥ viplavaḥ iti tat pratibaddha janmanām vikalpānām atat pratibhāsi tve api vastuni avisaṃvādaḥ maṇi prabhāyām iva maṇi bhrānteḥ na anyeṣām tat bheda prabhave sati api yathā adṛṣṭa viśeṣa anusaraṇam parityajya 
PVSV_43,6–43,10	 kiṃcid sāmānya grahaṇena viśeṣa antara samāropāt dīpa prabhāyām iva maṇi buddheḥ tena na vikalpa viṣayeṣu artheṣu artha kriyā kāritvam na api sva lakṣaṇasya anitya tvaḥ ādi abhāvaḥ yasmāt na anitya tvam nāma kiṃcid anyat calāt vastunaḥ kṣaṇa pratyupasthāna dharma tayā tasya tathābhūtasya grahaṇāt etat 
PVSV_43,11–43,15	 evam bhavati anityaḥ ayam anitya tvam asya iti vā tat dharma tām eva avatarantaḥ vikalpāḥ nānā eka dharma vyatirekān sandarśayanti na ca te nirāśrayāḥ tat bheda darśanaḥ āśraya tvāt na avastu dharmatā tat svabhāvasya eva tathā khyāteḥ vastunaḥ tu nānā eka vyatireka grahaḥ vibhramaḥ syāt tasya ekaḥ aneka kārya kāriṇas 
PVSV_43,16–43,20	 tathā abhāva jijñāsāsu tathā abhāva khyāpanāya tathā akṛta sthiti tvāt na vastu bhedāt tasya ekasya aneka tva ayogāt anekasya ca ekatva ayogāt vyatiriktasya ca niṣedhāt teṣām prakṛti bhedāt yathā vastu śabdaḥ arthaḥ abhyupagame sāmāna adhikaraṇya ayogāt tat upādheḥ ekasya dvābhyām abhidhānāt adoṣaḥ iti ced anupakāriṇi 
PVSV_43,21–43,25	 pāratantrya ayogāt anupādhiḥ pāratantrye ca janya janaka bhāvāt saha anavasthiteḥ dvayoḥ anabhidhānam ekasya buddhyā adhyāhāre na vastu viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ syāt buddhi pratibhāsa viṣaya tve ca sarvam tathā eva astu tathā bhinnaḥ upādhim atas ekasya grahaṇe apratibhāsanāt upakārya upakāriṇoḥ api upādhi tadvatoḥ 
PVSV_43,26–43,30	 saha avasthānāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na niṣpannasya pāratantrya abhāvāt anupādhi tvam na aniṣpannasya svarūpa asiddheḥ sarvathā asat pāratantryam iti kalpanā āropitam kṛtvā vyavahāre sarvathā saḥ eva kim na buddhiḥ anuvidhīyate ekaḥ śabda pramāṇena viṣayīkaraṇe vastu balāt aśeṣaḥ ākṣepāt tat anyaḥ vaiyarthyam ca na syāt 
PVSV_44,1–44,5	 buddhi pratibhāsasya nirvastuka tvāt vastu sāmarthya abhāvinām doṣāṇām aprasaṅgaḥ tat abhinnam ekaḥ ākāra viṣayīkaraṇe api aniścita anyaḥ ākāram ākāra antara sa ākāṅkṣa buddhi grāhyam bhinna śabdaḥ artha upasaṃhāre api abhinnam buddhau pratibhāti iti sāmānya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva sāmāna adhikaraṇyāni yathā prati iti na virudhyante 
PVSV_44,6–44,10	 dharma dharmi bhedaḥ api asya aneka artha bheda sambhave tat ekaḥ artha bheda vidhi pratiṣedha jijñāsāyām tat eva vastu pratikṣipta bheda antareṇa dharma śabdena saṃcodya buddheḥ tathā pratibhāsanāt vyatiriktam dharmam iva aviśeṣeṇa aparam asya svabhāvam dharmi tayā vyavasthāpya pradarśyate tāvatā ca aṃśena 
PVSV_44,11–44,16	 dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedāt bhedavatī iva buddhiḥ pratibhāti na vastu bhedāt yathā ukta doṣāt tathā abhūta bheda bāhulya codanayā vacana bhedaḥ sādhya sādhana bhedaḥ ca tat svabhāva samāśrayaiḥ dharma pratibhāsa bhedaiḥ tat svabhāva pratipattaye kriyate iti tat svabhāva grahaṇāt yā dhīḥ tat arthāḥ iva api anarthikā vikalpikā atat kārya artha bheda niṣṭhā prajāyate 
PVSV_44,17–44,22	 tasyām yat rūpam ābhāti bāhyam ekam iva anyatas vyāvṛttam iva nistattvam parīkṣā anaṅga bhāvataḥ arthāḥ jñāna niviṣṭāḥ te yatas vyāvṛtti rūpiṇaḥ tena abhinnāḥ iva ābhānti vyāvṛttāḥ punar anyatas te eva teṣām sāmānya samānaḥ ādhāra gocaraiḥ jñāna abhidhānaiḥ mithyā arthaḥ vyavahāraḥ pratanyate 
PVSV_44,23–45,1	 sa ca sarvaḥ padārthānām anyonya abhāva saṃśrayaḥ tena anya apoha viṣayaḥ vastu lābhasya ca āśrayaḥ yatra asti vastu sambandhaḥ yathā ukta anumitau yathā na anyatra bhrānti sāmye api dīpa tejaḥ maṇau yathā tatra eka kāryaḥ anekaḥ api tat akārya anya tā āśrayaiḥ eka tvena abhidhā jñānaiḥ vyavahāram pratāryate 
PVSV_45,2–45,9	 tathā aneka kṛt ekaḥ api tat bhāva paridīpane atat kārya artha bhedena nānā dharma pratīyate yathā prati iti kathitaḥ śabdaḥ arthaḥ asau asan api sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca vastuni asya na sambhavaḥ dharma dharmi vyavasthānam bhedaḥ abhedaḥ ca yādṛśaḥ asamīkṣita tattva arthaḥ yathā loke pratīyate tam tathā eva samāśritya sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ parama artha avatārāya vidvadbhiḥ avakalpyate 
PVSV_45,10–45,15	 saṃsṛjyante na bhidyate svatas arthāḥ pāramārthikāḥ rūpam ekam anekam ca teṣu buddheḥ upaplavaḥ bhedaḥ tatas ayam bauddhe arthe sāmānyam bhedaḥ iti api tasya eva ca anya vyāvṛttyā dharma bhedaḥ prakalpyate sādhya sādhana saṃkalpe vastu darśana hānitaḥ bhedaḥ sāmānya saṃsṛṣṭaḥ grāhyaḥ na atra sva lakṣaṇam 
PVSV_45,16–45,23	 samāna bhinnaḥ ādi ākāraiḥ na tat grāhyam kathaṃcana bhedānām bahu bhedānām tatra ekasmin ayogataḥ tat rūpam sarvatas bhinnam tathā tat pratipādikā na śrutiḥ kalpanā vā asti sāmānyena eva vṛttitaḥ iti saṃgraha ślokāḥ kim punar kāraṇam sva lakṣaṇe śabdāḥ na prayujyante yasmāt śabdāḥ saṃketitam prāhuḥ vyavahārāya sa smṛtaḥ tadā sva lakṣaṇam na asti saṃketaḥ tena tatra na 
PVSV_45,24–46,1	 na hi śabdāḥ asaṃketitam artham prakāśayanti saṃketaḥ ca vyavahāra artham kriyate api nāma itas śabdāt kṛta saṃketāt uttara kālam imam artham pratipadyeta iti na ca prāk kṛta sambandhasya ekatra sva lakṣaṇe śabdasya paścāt prayogaḥ yuktaḥ tasya deśa kāla vyakti bheda anāskandhanāt tasmāt na sva lakṣaṇe samayaḥ sāmānyam tarhi vyatiriktam avyatiriktam vā vyāpi śabdaiḥ abhidhīyate tat na vyavahāra kāla abhāva doṣaḥ na etat asti yasmāt api pravarteta pumān vijñāya artha kriyā kṣamān tat sādhanāya iti artheṣu saṃyojyante abhidhāyakāḥ 
PVSV_46,2–46,6	 na khalu vai vyasanam eva etat lokasya yat ayam asaṃketayan aprayuñjānaḥ vā śabdān duḥkham āsīta kim tarhi sarve eva asya avadheyaḥ ārambhaḥ phala arthaḥ niṣphalaḥ ārambhasya upekṣanīya tvāt tat ayam śabdān api kvacid niyuñjānaḥ phalam eva kiṃcid īhitum yuktaḥ tat ca sarvam tyāgaḥ āpti lakṣaṇam iṣṭa aniṣṭayoḥ 
PVSV_46,7–46,12	 tena ayam iṣṭa aniṣṭayoḥ sādhanam asādhanam ca jñātvā tatra pravṛtti nivṛttī kuryām kārayeyam vā iti śabdāt niyuñjīta niyoge vā ādriyeta anyathā apekṣaṇīya tvāt tatra anartha kriyā yogyā jātiḥ na hi jātiḥ kvacid vā āha dohaḥ upatiṣṭhate na ca tādṛśam prakaraṇam antareṇa loke śabda prayogaḥ vyavahāreṣu vyakteḥ aśakya 
PVSV_46,13–46,17	 codana tvāt lakṣita lakṣaṇa artham jāti codanā iti ced aśabda codite sati api sambandhe katham pravarteta na hi kaścid daṇḍam chindhi iti ukte daṇḍinam chinatti na api asambhavāt vyaktau pravṛttiḥ evam hi asambaddha pralāpī syāt na tatas anyatra pravṛttiḥ balīvarda doha codanā vat na ca artha antara codanena artha antarasya lakṣaṇam 
PVSV_46,18–46,22	 na hi sambandhe sati api daṇḍa śabdāt daṇḍini pratipattiḥ aniyata sambandha tvāt tatra naḥ iti ced tat tulyam jātau api vyaktīnām apāye kevalāyāḥ jāteḥ avasthānāt bhrātṛ ādi śabdāḥ tu sambandhi śabda tvāt ākṣipeyuḥ param na tathā go tvaḥ ādi śrutayaḥ sambandhi vācinyaḥ apeta vyaktīnām api jātīnām 
PVSV_46,23–46,27	 tat śrutibhyaḥ nityam anugamana prasaṅgāt sarvadā tat sambandha yogyatā pratīteḥ iṣṭam eva iti ced sarvadā tarhi go śabdāt apravṛttiḥ sahita asahita avasthayoḥ viśeṣeṇa anākṣepāt vyakti sambandhinyāḥ jāteḥ codanāt adoṣaḥ iti ced sarvadā tarhi tat viśeṣaṇa tvena avasthitā vyaktiḥ ākṣiptāḥ eva iti tadvān abhidheyaḥ syāt 
PVSV_46,28–47,6	 na ca jāti vyaktyoḥ kaścid sambandhaḥ anyonyam ajanya janaka tvena anupakārāt tatas lakṣaṇam api ayuktam tasmāt na jātau śabda niveśanam phala abhāvāt evam tarhi tadvān alam artha kriyāsu iti tatra śabdaḥ niyojyate sa ca sākṣāt na yojyate kasmāt yadi vyaktau śabda niveśanam phala vat sa ca śabdaḥ kasmāt sākṣāt vyaktiṣu eva na niyujyate kim tatra anyena vyavadhinā ānantyāt ced idam samam 
PVSV_47,7–47,18	 syāt etat ānantyāt vyaktīnām aśakyaḥ śabdena sambandhaḥ kartum evam sati idam ānantyam tadvatī api samānam jātyāḥ api hi vyaktasya eva vaktavyāḥ iti akṛta sambandhasya anabhidhānāt avaśyam tatra sambandhaḥ karaṇīyaḥ sa ca na śakyate tat sambandhini karaṇāt tatra api kṛtaḥ eva iti ced uktam atra sambandhe api ekatra kṛtāt anyatra apratītiḥ na ca sambandhaḥ asti iti api ca tat kāriṇām atat kāri bheda sāmye na kim kṛtaḥ yām artha kriyām adhikṛtya ayam artheṣu śabdāt niyuṅkte tat kāriṇām arthānām anyebhyaḥ bhedāt tatra eva ca eṣām abhede kim na śabdaḥ prayujyate tadvat doṣasya sāmyāt ced astu jātiḥ alam parā 
PVSV_47,19–48,3	 syāt etat anya vyāvṛtte api śabdaḥ arthe vyāvṛtti viśiṣṭasya tadvataḥ abhidhānāt na tadvat pakṣāt viśeṣaḥ kaḥ hi atra viśeṣaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ jātiḥ vyāvṛttimān jātimān iti astu nāma tadvat doṣaḥ jātiḥ anyāḥ mā bhūt jātim api hi abhyupagacchatā avaśyam bhāvānām bhedaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tat abhāve tasyāḥ api abhāva 
PVSV_48,4–48,10	 prasaṅgāt sa ca ekasmāt bhedaḥ tat anyeṣām abhedaḥ tat viśiṣṭeṣu artheṣu pratipattiḥ astu sarvathā doṣa parihārasya kartum aśakya tvāt artha antara abhyupagame prayojana abhāvāt tat arthasya anyena sādhanāt tat abhyupagamasya ca avaśyam bhāvi tvāt api ca tat anyaḥ parihāreṇa pravarteta iti ca dhvaniḥ ucyate tena tebhyaḥ asya avyavacchede katham ca saḥ 
PVSV_48,11–48,15	 śabdam hi eṣa prayuñjānaḥ artheṣu aniṣṭa parihāreṇa pravarteta iti ca prayuṅkte tatra anyatra ca pravṛtti anujñāyām tat nāma grahaṇa vaiyarthyāt pravṛtti nivṛtty anujñāyām ca eka codanā anādarāt avacanam eva syāt anya vyāvṛtti anabhidhāne tasmāt avaśyam śabdena vyavacchedaḥ codanīyaḥ sa ca abhinnaḥ tat anyeṣu 
PVSV_48,16–48,21	 iti jāti dharmaḥ api asti tat niyataḥ abhyupagamam niyata codanam jāti artha prasādhanam ca parityajya artha antara kalpanam kevalam anartha nirbandhaḥ eva yathā kalpanam asya ayogāt na vai vyavacchedaḥ na kriyate pravṛtti viṣayam tu kathayadbhiḥ jātiḥ uktāḥ vyavacchedaḥ asti ced asya nanu etāvat prayojanam śabdānām iti kim tatra sāmānyena apareṇa vaḥ 
PVSV_48,22–48,26	 nanu uktam pravṛtti viṣayaḥ pradarśyate iti uktam idam ayuktam tu uktam tathā hi na sā pravṛtti yogyāḥ iti niveditam etat tat dvāreṇa acodite pravṛttiḥ api pratyuktāḥ tadvat codane ca vyavadhānam jāti tadvatoḥ pravṛtti viṣaya tve vyāvṛtti tad vantau kim naḥ iṣyete vyāvṛtteḥ avastu tvena asādhana tvāt ced tat 
PVSV_48,27–49,3	 tulyam jāteḥ tadvataḥ sādhanāt adoṣaḥ iti ced tulyam tat vyāvṛttimataḥ avastu grāhī ca vyāvṛtti vādinām śābdaḥ pratyayaḥ sa vibhrama vaśāt akārake api kāraka adhyavasāyī pravartayati vastu saṃvādaḥ tu vastu utpattyā tat pratibandhe sati bhavati anyathā naḥ eva asti vastu utpatteḥ abhrāntiḥ iti ced na atat pratibhāsinaḥ 
PVSV_49,4–49,8	 tat adhyavasāyāt maṇi prabhāyām maṇi bhrānti darśanena vyabhicārāt ca bhrānteḥ avastu saṃvādaḥ iti ced na yathā uktena eva vyabhicārāt vitatha pratibhāsaḥ hi bhrānti lakṣaṇam tat na antarīyaka tayā tu saṃvādaḥ na pratibhāsa apekṣī vastuni tu yathābhāvam arpita cetasaḥ pravṛttau grāhyasya sāmānyasya 
PVSV_49,9–49,17	 anartha kriyā yogya tvāt apravṛttiḥ anyatra ca pravṛttau atiprasaṅgaḥ tadvat grahaṇe ca sāmānya vaiyarthya ādayaḥ proktāḥ jāti grahaṇe api sambandhāt śliṣṭaḥ ābhāsā buddhiḥ pravartayati iti ced tadā na jātiḥ na tadvān ekasya api svabhāva sthiteḥ agrahaṇāt iti para vādaḥ eva āśritaḥ syāt evam tarhi anvayinaḥ kasyacid arthasya abhāvāt prakṛti bhinneṣu artheṣu tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñānam na syāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt jñānaḥ ādi artha kriyām tām tām dṛṣṭvā bhede api kurvataḥ arthān tat anya viśleṣa viṣayaiḥ dhvanibhiḥ saha 
PVSV_49,18–49,22	 saṃyojya pratyabhijñānam kuryāt api anya darśane uktam etat bhede api bhāvāḥ tulya artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi vat iti tām ekām jñānaḥ ādikām artha kriyām teṣu paśyataḥ vastu dharma tayā eva anyebhyaḥ bhidyamānā bhāvāḥ tat vyāvṛtti viṣaya dhvani saṃsṛṣṭam tat eva idam iti sva anubhava vāsanā prabodhena saṃsṛṣṭa 
PVSV_49,23–49,27	 bhedam mithyā pratyayam janayanti anyathā na bheda saṃsargavatī buddhiḥ syāt yathā daṇḍiṣu na hi tatra eka daṇḍa yoge api anyatra saḥ eva ayam iti bhavati kim tarhi tat iha iti na ca evam pratyabhijñānam kim tarhi tat eva idam iti tat na tat ekam anekatra paśyataḥ api bheda saṃsarga vat yuktam vibhrama 
PVSV_50,1–50,5	 balāt tu tathā jñāne na virodhaḥ nimitta abhāvāt vibhramaḥ ayuktaḥ iti ced te eva bhāvaḥ tat ekaḥ artha kāriṇaḥ anubhava dvāreṇa prakṛtyā vibhrama phalāyāḥ vikalpa vāsanāyāḥ hetu tvāt nimittam marīcikaḥ ādiṣu api hi jalaḥ ādi bhrānteḥ tau ekaḥ abhinnaḥ ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya nimitta anubhava jananau bhāvau kāraṇam bhinnau= 
PVSV_50,6–50,10	 api na hi tatra anyat eva kiṃcid sāmānyam asti yat tathā pratīyeta sattve vā sat artha grāhiṇī buddhiḥ bhrāntiḥ na syāt abhūta ākāra samāropāt bhrāntiḥ iti ced na tarhi sā tat sāmānya grāhiṇī yam eva khalu ākāram iyam āropayati saḥ eva asyāḥ viṣayaḥ iti aviṣayīkṛtasya aśakya samāropāt ākāra antara vat sa 
PVSV_50,11–50,15	 ca tatra na asti iti asāmānyam sati sāmānya grahaṇe tat āropaḥ na anyathā atiprasaṅgāt iti ced sati eka kārya kāri grahaṇaḥ iti kim naḥ iṣyate avaśyam ca icchatā api sāmānyam vyaktīnām eka kārya janana śaktiḥ eṣṭavyāḥ tatas te eva anyebhyaḥ bhidyamānāḥ tādṛśam pratyayam janayanti iti kim atra sāmānyena yathābhāvam 
PVSV_50,16–50,20	 eva asaṃsṛṣṭa bhedam kim na pratyeti iti ced aśaktiḥ eṣā vikalpānām avidyā prabhavāt na vai bāhya apekṣāḥ eva bhrāntayaḥ bhavanti kim tu viplavāt āntarāt api keśaḥ ādi vibhrama vat avidyā udbhavāt viplava tve cakṣuḥ vijñānaḥ ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ na tasyāḥ vikalpa lakṣaṇa tvāt vikalpaḥ eva hi avidyā sā svabhāvena 
PVSV_51,1–51,5	 eva viparyasyati na evam indriya jñānāni vikalpakāni na vā teṣu api eṣa doṣaḥ advayānām dvaya nirbhāsāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ sarveṣām viplave api pramāṇa tat ābhāsa vyavasthā ā āśraya parāvṛtteḥ artha kriyā yogya abhimata saṃvādanāt mithyātve api praśama anukūla tvāt mātṛ saṃjñā ādi vat marīcikāyām jala jñānasya anyasya 
PVSV_51,6–51,10	 ca bhinna bhāvaḥ utpatteḥ vibhramasya ca aviśeṣe api abhimata artha kriyāḥ yogya ayogyaḥ utpatteḥ artha saṃvādāḥ itarau ayogyāt katham utpattiḥ iti ced vikalpānām artha pratibandha niyama abhāvāt na hi vikalpāḥ yathārtham eva jāyante sati marīcika adarśane jala bhrāntiḥ iti tat udbhavāḥ iti ucyate na tu yathā svabhāvam 
PVSV_51,11–51,17	 ajala vivekinaḥ arthena svabhāva anukāra pratyarpaṇena jananāt sā tu viśeṣa lakṣaṇa apāṭavāt pratyaya apekṣiṇā sve vāsanā prabodhena janyate tasmāt bhinna bhāva janmanaḥ vikalpa vibhramāt tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñānam na vyatiriktasya sāmānyasya darśanāt na avyatiriktasya vyakti vat ananvayāt api ca parasya api na sā buddhiḥ sāmānyāt eva kevalāt 
PVSV_51,18–52,4	 na hi paraḥ api enām buddhim kevala sāmānya bhāvinīm vaktum arhati nityam tat mā atra vijñāne vyakti ajñāna prasaṅgataḥ yadi hi nityam anayā buddhyā sāmānyam eva gṛhyeta apratītāḥ eva vyaktiḥ syāt anena jñānena tadā kadācid sambaddhasya agṛhītasya tadvataḥ tadvat tā aniścayaḥ na syāt vyavahāraḥ tatas katham yadā sāmānya grāhiṇaḥ vijñānasya na bhedaḥ ālambana bhāvena upayujyate tadā na tau kadācid api śliṣṭau gṛhītau iti idam asya sāmānyam ayam vā tadvān iti na syāt tathā ca tat pratipattyā tadvati pratipattiḥ na syāt artha antara vat eka vastu sahāyāḥ ced vyaktayaḥ jñāna kāraṇam 
PVSV_52,5–52,16	 syāt etat bhavanti vyaktayaḥ tasya ālambana bhāvena kāraṇam na tu kevalāḥ yadā punar āsām ekam sahakārī asti tadā tat sahitāḥ gṛhyante iti tat ekam vastu kim tāsām nānātvam samapohati nānā tvāt ca eka vijñāna hetu tā tāsu naḥ iṣyate kim vai teṣām bhedānām tena ekena nānātvam nirākriyate nānātvam hi teṣu eka vijñāna akāraṇa tve kāraṇam ucyate anekam api yadi ekam apekṣya abhinna buddhi kṛt na brūmaḥ anekam ekam pratyayam na janayati bhedāt iti na bhedaḥ janana virodhī kim tarhi kaivalyam tena ekena sahitāḥ janayanti eva evam tarhi tābhiḥ vinā api pratyekam kriyamāṇām dhiyam prati 
PVSV_52,17–53,1	 tena ekena api sāmarthyam tāsām naḥ iti agrahaḥ dhiyā katham idānīm vyaktīnām tatra jñāne sāmarthya gatiḥ pratyekam tāsām abhāve api tat bhāvāt asati sāmānye abhāvāt itarathā ca bhāvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yathā nīlaḥ ādiṣu ekaḥ apāye api cakṣuḥ vijñānam bhavati iti na samūhe api teṣām asāmarthyam tathā iha api pratyekam ekaḥ apāye api bhavati iti na sarvadā sāmarthyam viṣamaḥ upanyāsaḥ tathā hi nīlaḥ ādeḥ netra vijñāne pṛthak sāmarthya darśanāt 
PVSV_53,2–53,7	 śakti siddhiḥ samūhe api na evam vyakteḥ kathaṃcana nīlaḥ ādīnām hi cakṣuḥ vijñāne pratyekam api sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam iti samūhe api śaktiḥ aviruddhāḥ tathā na kadācid vyaktayaḥ sāmānya nirapekṣāḥ anvayi vijñānam janayanti tasmāt asamarthāḥ eva vyaktayaḥ tatra iti na tena gṛhyeran tāsām anyatama apekṣam tat ced śaktam na kevalam 
PVSV_53,8–53,13	 atha api syāt na vema rahitaḥ kuvindaḥ paṭam karoti prati ekam vema abhāve api kuvindaḥ karoti iti na tatas eva paṭe utpattiḥ tathā na kevalam ekaika vyakti apāye vijñānaḥ utpattau api sāmānyam tat hetuḥ kim tarhi vyaktīnām ekām kāṃcid apekṣya vijñānam utpādayati evam sati tat ekam upakuryuḥ tāḥ katham ekām dhiyam ca na 
PVSV_53,14–53,20	 bhinnānām hi arthānām ekaḥ arthaḥ upakriyā virodhinī iti sarvaḥ ayam ārambhaḥ tāḥ ced vyaktayaḥ bhinnāḥ api ekam sāmānyam upakurvanti kaḥ punar āsām vijñānena aparādhaḥ kṛtaḥ yat tat naḥ upakurvanti kim antar gaḍunā sāmānyena yathā asambhinnānām api eka sāmānyaḥ upakaraṇa śaktiḥ evam tat eva ekam vijñānam kurvantu kim ca kāryaḥ ca tāsām prāptaḥ asau jananam yat upakriyā 
PVSV_53,21–53,25	 na hi anatiśayam ātmānam asya pūrvavat bibhrataḥ kaścid upakārakaḥ nāma atiprasaṅgāt artha antara janane api tasya kim tena tasya tat āśraya tve anupakāriṇaḥ kaḥ ayam āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ vā upakāre api tatra eva tat pratibandhaḥ iti kim anyaḥ tat karaṇāt tat upakārī tat apekṣasya āśrayasya 
PVSV_53,26–54,3	 tat upayoge anupakārya tve kā iyam apekṣā nāma tad utpatti dharmāḥ dharmāḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāva pratibandhāt apekṣate nāma anādheya atiśaya ātmā paraiḥ apekṣate ca iti vyāhatam etat tasmāt yaḥ kaścid kasyacid kvacid pratibandhaḥ sa sarvaḥ janyatāyām eva antarbhavati para bhāvaḥ utpādane tat anupakārāt akiṃcitkarasya 
PVSV_54,4–54,8	 ca anupakārāt tasmāt vyakti upakṛtasya sāmānyasya vijñāna janane janane vyaktam asya tat kārya tā anuyujyate kevalasya sāmarthye api vyaktīnām kvacid api atra sāmarthya asiddheḥ agrāhya tvam samarthāḥ vyaktayaḥ vijñāne pratibhāsanāt iti ced katham asiddhaḥ upakārāṇām pratibhāsaḥ iti saḥ eva sāmānya abhyupagame 
PVSV_54,9–54,13	 cintyate yasmāt na anupakārakaḥ viṣayaḥ atiprasaṅgāt na aviṣayasya vijñāne pratibhāsaḥ anupakārakasya aviṣaya tve atīta anāgataḥ ādīnām aviṣaya tvam asatām upakāra asāmarthyāt iti ced bhavantu nāma tat viṣayāṇi nirviṣayāṇi nirviṣaya tve api tat anukārī pratibhāsaḥ tat rūpa anubhavaḥ āhita vāsanāḥ utpatteḥ 
PVSV_54,14–54,18	 ātma bhūtaḥ eva vijñānasya bhāva abhāva anuvidhānāt ca sāmarthyam na pratibhāsanāt apratibhāsinaḥ api vyakti vyatirekeṇa sāmānyasya bhāvāt pratibhāsinām api keśaḥ ādi viplavānām abhāvāt abhinna pratibhāsā dhīḥ na bhinneṣu iti ced matam na brūmaḥ anekam eka kārya kṛt na bhavati iti kim tarhi na 
PVSV_54,19–55,2	 bhinneṣu artheṣu arpita tat ākārā buddhiḥ abhinna pratibhāsinī syāt na vai sāmānya grāhiṇīṣu sva lakṣaṇa pratibhāsaḥ tat abhāve api tāsām bhāvāt ākāra antareṇa ca sva jñāne pratibhāsanāt anekaḥ ākāra ayogāt ekasya atiprasaṅgāt ca tasmāt naḥ iyam bhinnaḥ artha grāhiṇī abhinnā pratibhāti tat udbhavāḥ atat pratibhāsiny 
PVSV_55,3–55,7	 api adhyavasāya vibhramāt vyavahārayati lokam sa tu tasyām pratibhāsamānaḥ ākāraḥ na artheṣu asti anyatra bhedāt abhedinaḥ sa ca arūpaḥ tam eva eṣā gṛhṇatī tathā viplavataḥ iti uktam prāk api ca vastu sāmānya vādinaḥ api hi bhinnāḥ eva vyaktayaḥ katham tāsu abhinnaḥ ākārā buddhiḥ iti tulyam ca udyam
