PVSV_55,8–55,14	 na tulyam tatra abhinnasya sāmānyasya sadbhāvāt nanu tatra tasya ābhāsaḥ sataḥ api na lakṣyate sā hi varṇa saṃsthāna pratibhāsavatī vibhāvyate na ca īdṛśam sāmānyam na ca tatas vyatiriktaḥ kaścid abhinnaḥ ākāraḥ asti ākṛti sāmānya vādinaḥ api viśeṣa vat tasya avyatirekāt artha antare avṛttiḥ iti bhedāt na abhinna pratibhāsaḥ yujyate athavā astu pratibhāsaḥ dhiyam bhinnaḥ samānāḥ iti tat grahāt 
PVSV_55,15–55,19	 na eva tāsu abhinnaḥ pratibhāsaḥ asti samānāḥ iti grahāt na hi ekasmin pratibhāse samānāḥ iti yuktam kim tarhi tat eva iti dvayasya grahaṇāt adoṣaḥ iti ced tathā api tat iha iti syāt na samānaḥ iti tat eva tāsām sāmyam iti ced katham anyonyasya sāmyam tat sambandhāt iti ced na pratibaddhasya sambandha 
PVSV_55,20–56,10	 ayogāt atiprasaṅgāt ca katham tāḥ bhinna dhī grāhyāḥ samāḥ ced nanu samānāḥ iti grahaṇāt eva āsu abhinna pratibhāsaḥ na vai tat darśane bhinnaḥ abhinnayoḥ pratibhāsanāt samānāḥ iti pratītiḥ kim tarhi eka kārya tā sādṛśyam na hi vayam artha jñāne dvau ākārau paśyāmaḥ apaśyantaḥ ca katham artha dvaya kalpanena ātmānam eva vipralabhāmahe eka kāryāḥ tu vyaktayaḥ kalpanāḥ viṣaya tām upayāntyaḥ tathā anayā vibhramāt miśrīkriyante iti anavadyam etat nanu dhīḥ kāryam tāsām sā ca vibhidyate 
PVSV_56,11–56,17	 pratibhāvam tadvat tat pratibhāsinaḥ vijñānasya api bhedāt katham eka kāryāḥ tat hi tāsām kāryam tat ca bhidyate yat api udakaḥ āharaṇaḥ ādikam ekam ghaṭaḥ ādi kāryam tat api pratidravyam bhedāt bhidyate eva iti naḥ ekam bhedānām kāryam asti na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt eka pratyavamarśasya hetu tvāt dhīḥ abhedinī eka dhī hetu bhāvena vyaktīnām api abhinnatā 
PVSV_56,18–57,1	 niveditam etat yathā na bhāvānām svabhāva saṃsargaḥ asti iti tatra saṃsṛṣṭaḥ ākārā buddhiḥ bhrāntiḥ eva tām tu bhedinaḥ padārthāḥ krameṇa vikalpa hetavaḥ bhavantaḥ janayanti svabhāvataḥ iti ca sa tu eṣām abhinnaḥ bhedaḥ iti ucyate jñānaḥ ādeḥ kasyacid ekasya karaṇāt atat kāri svabhāva vivekaḥ tat api 
PVSV_57,2–57,6	 pratidravyam bhidyamānam api prakṛtyāḥ eka pratyavamarśasya abheda avaskandinaḥ hetuḥ bhavat abhinnam khyāti tathā abhūta pratyavamarśa hetoḥ abheda avabhāsinaḥ jñānaḥ ādeḥ arthasya hetu tvāt vyaktayaḥ api saṃsṛṣṭa ākāram svabhāva bheda parama artham svabhāvataḥ ekam pratyayam janayanti iti asakṛt uktam etat tasmāt 
PVSV_57,7–57,18	 eka kārya tā eva bhāvānām abhedaḥ sā ca atat kārya viśleṣaḥ eva tat anyasya anuvartinaḥ vastunaḥ adṛṣṭeḥ pratiṣedhāt ca na hi dṛśyam vibhāgena apratibhāsamānam asti iti uktam etat sati vā kvacid anāśritam katham jñāna hetuḥ iti pratiṣedhasya ca vidhānāt tat kalpanāḥ ayuktāḥ iti tasmāt saṃketaḥ api tat vid arthikaḥ 
PVSV_57,19–58,2	 eva yuktaḥ yaḥ ayam anyonyam vivekaḥ bhāvānām tat pratītayaḥ eva saṃketaḥ api kriyamāṇaḥ śobheta atat kāri vivekena pravṛtti artha tayā yadi hi na tat prati iti arthaḥ saṃketaḥ tasya vyavahāra kāle api asaṃsparśāt na anyaḥ parihāreṇa pravarteta na hi sa teṣām tebhyaḥ vivekaḥ śabdena coditaḥ iti sā ca śrutiḥ akārya kṛti tat kāri tulya rūpa avabhāsinīm dhiyam vastu pṛthak bhāva mā atra bījām anarthikām 
PVSV_58,3–58,9	 janayanti api atat kāri parihāra aṅga bhāvataḥ vastu bhedaḥ āśrayāt ca arthe na visaṃvādikā matā tatas anya apoha viṣayā tat kartṛ āśrita bhāvataḥ eka svabhāva rahiteṣu artheṣu tam adhyāropya utpadyamānām mithyā pratibhāsi tvāt akārya kāriṇam api tat kārya kāriṇam iva adhyavasyantīm vastu pṛthak bhāva mā atra bījām samāna adhyavasāyām mithyā buddhim śrutiḥ janayanti api tat anyaḥ parihāra aṅga abhāvāt 
PVSV_58,10–58,19	 paramārthataḥ tat vyatirekiṣu padārtheṣu na visaṃvādikāḥ iti ucyate tathā hi sa teṣu vyatirekaḥ bhūtaḥ sarvathā avyatikramaṇīya tvāt na ekaḥ vyatiriktaḥ avyatiriktaḥ vā sarvathā ayogāt tasya samāveśane vastuni dūraḥ utsṛṣṭam eva vastu syāt śabda jñānābhyām tat viṣaya abhimatasya tasya abhāvāt anyasya ca vastu dharmasya kasyacid asaṃsparśāt tatas eva ca sā śrutiḥ anya apoha viṣayayā iti ucyate anya vyāvṛtteṣu artheṣu vyāvṛtti bhedam upādāya aviśeṣeṇa niveśanāt vyavahāre api anyaḥ parihāreṇa pravartanāt avṛkṣa vyatirekeṇa vṛkṣaḥ artha grahaṇe dvayam 
PVSV_58,20–59,6	 anyonyaḥ āśrayam iti eka graha abhāve dvaya agrahaḥ saṃketa asambhavaḥ tasmāt iti kecid pracakṣate yadi avṛkṣebhyaḥ bhedaḥ vṛkṣaḥ tasya avṛkṣa grahaṇam antareṇa tathā grahītum aśakya tvāt avijñāta vṛkṣeṇa avṛkṣasya api tat vyavaccheda rūpasya aparijñānāt buddhau anārūḍhe arthe na saṃketaḥ śakyate iti eke teṣām avṛkṣāḥ saṃkete vyavacchinnāḥ na vā yaḥ evam ekam vastu sāmānyam abhyupagamya itaretaraḥ āśrayam anyaḥ vyavacchedena saṃkete codayanti teṣām tatra api saṃketa karaṇe avṛkṣāḥ vyavacchinnāḥ na vā yadi vyavacchinnāḥ katham jñātāḥ prāk vṛkṣa grahaṇāt ṛte 
PVSV_59,7–59,16	 na hi tadā pratipattā vṛkṣam vetti na avṛkṣam tat jñānāya eva tat arthi tayā upagamāt saḥ ajānānaḥ katham avṛkṣa vyavacchedam pratipadyeta saṃkete apratipattau ca aparihṛta tat anya niveśinaḥ śabdāt anirākaraṇe teṣām saṃkete vyavahāriṇām na syāt tat parihāreṇa pravṛttiḥ vṛkṣa bheda vat na hi saṃkete para avyavacchedena niveśitāt śabdāt vyavahāre tat parihāreṇa pravṛttiḥ yuktāḥ śiṃśapāḥ ādi bheda vat atha api syāt avidhāya niṣidhya anyat pradarśya ekam puras sthitam vṛkṣaḥ ayam iti saṃketaḥ kriyate tat prapadyate 
PVSV_59,17–60,3	 vyavahāre api tena ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced na vai vastu sat sāmānya vādinā kasyacid vyavacchedena kiṃcid vidhīyate kim tarhi ekam agratas vyavasthitam vastu sandarśya vṛkṣaḥ ayam iti saṃketaḥ kriyate saṃketa kāle tathā dṛṣṭam eva ayam artham tat sambandhinam vā vyavahāre api pratipadyate iti na samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ na samānaḥ yasmāt tatra api taruḥ ayam api ayam eva iti prasaṅgaḥ na nivartate 
PVSV_60,4–60,8	 ekam pradarśya ayam vṛkṣaḥ iti api bruvāṇaḥ ayam api ayam eva iti ubhayīm gatim na ativartate tayoḥ ca saḥ eva doṣaḥ na doṣaḥ dṛṣṭa viparītasya su jñāna tvāt ekam hi kiṃcid paśyataḥ anyatra tat ākāra vivekinīm buddhim anubhavatas tatas anyat iti yathā anubhavam tat vivecanaḥ vaidharmya niścayaḥ utpadyate sa hi 
PVSV_60,9–60,15	 ayam eva vṛkṣaḥ iti pradarśya vyutpāditaḥ yatra eva tam na paśyati tam eva avṛkṣam svayam eva pratipadyate na idam vyavaccheda vādinaḥ sambhavati ekatra dṛṣṭasya rūpasya kvacid ananvayāt darśanena pratipattau vyakti antare api na syāt tathā pratītiḥ evam tarhi tatra api tulyam etat yasmāt eka pratyavamarśaḥ ākhye jñānaḥ ekatra hi sthitaḥ prapattā tat atat hetūn arthān vibhajate svayam 
PVSV_60,16–60,22	 niveditam etat prāk yathā ete bhāvāḥ prakṛti bhedinaḥ api jñānaḥ ādikam ekam kāryam kecid kurvanti na anyaḥ iti tān ayam tatra svayam eva tat hetūn atat hetūn ca vibhajya pratyeti tasya tat buddhi vartinaḥ bhāvān bhātaḥ hetu tayā dhiyaḥ ahetu rūpa vikalān eka rūpān iva svayam bhedena pratipadyeta iti uktiḥ bhede niyujyate tam tasyāḥ pratiyatī dhīḥ bhrāntyā ekam vastu iva īkṣyate 
PVSV_60,23–60,27	 teṣām prakṛtyāḥ eva pratyaya vaśāt tathābhūta vikalpa kāraṇānām anvayāt tat draṣṭuḥ buddhau viparivartamānān tat jñāna hetu tayā tat anya vyāvṛttyā ca atathābhūtān api tathā adhyavasitān avibhakta bāhya adhyātmika bhedān pratipattā pratipattim anusṛtya ete vṛkṣāḥ iti sva para vikalpeṣu eka pratibhāsān ādarśya vikalpa 
PVSV_60,28–61,4	 vijñāne vyavasthitaḥ tat vijñāna hetūn bhedena pratipadyeta iti uktim atat hetubhyaḥ bhede niyuṅkte tam tasyāḥ pratipadyamānā buddhiḥ vikalpikāḥ bhrānti vaśāt eva eka vastu grahiṇī iva pratibhāti na punar ekam vastu tatra dṛśyam asti yasya darśana adarśanābhyām bhinna darśane api eṣa vṛkṣa avṛkṣa vibhāgam 
PVSV_61,5–61,13	 kurvīta tasya śākhāḥ ādi pratibhāsa vibhāgena daṇḍa vat daṇḍinī agrahaṇāt agṛhītasya ca apara pravibhāgena anupalakṣaṇāt ākṛteḥ api ekatra dṛṣṭāyāḥ anyatra draṣṭum aśakya tvāt tat atadvatoḥ vṛkṣa avṛkṣa tve vyaktiḥ ekaḥ eva vṛkṣaḥ syāt bhavatu nāma ghaṭaḥ ādi śabdeṣu artha antara vyavacchedaḥ atha jñeyaḥ ādi padeṣu katham na hi ajñeyam kiṃcid asti yatas bhedaḥ syāt tatas bhedena viṣayīkaraṇaḥ eva tasya jñeya tvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt kvacid niveśanāya arthe vinivartya kutaścana buddheḥ prayujyate śabdaḥ tat arthasya avadhāraṇāt 
PVSV_61,14–61,20	 vyarthaḥ anyathā prayogaḥ syāt tat jñeyaḥ ādi padeṣu api vyavahāraḥ upanīteṣu vyavacchedyaḥ asti kaścana śabdam hi prayuñjānaḥ sarvaḥ anvaya vyatirekau na ativartate tasya pravṛtti nivṛtti artha tvāt yadi hi ayam na kasyacid kutaścid nivartayet pravartayet vā buddhim yathābhūta anujñānāt sarva vyavahāreṣu na kiṃcid vyāharet vyāhārasya avadhāraṇa na antarīyaka tvāt yathā ghaṭena udakam ānaya iti yadi ghaṭena añjalinā 
PVSV_61,21–61,26	 vā udakaḥ ānayanam yathā kathaṃcid abhimatam syāt udakam ānaya iti eva vaktavyam syāt na ghaṭena iti tathā paṃśunā vā anena vā yena kenacid ānītena arthaḥ ānaya iti eva syāt anākṣipta karaṇa karmakam evam ānayanam anyat vā yat kiṃcid anuṣṭhānam vai abhimatam tadā ānaya iti api na brūyāt vyartha tvāt vacanasya tathā vyavahāraḥ upanītānām jñeyaḥ ādi 
PVSV_62,1–62,5	 padānām api kenacid vyavacchedyena bhavitavyam ananyaḥ āśaṅkāyām prayoga ayogāt tatra hi yat eva mūḍha mateḥ āśaṅkā sthānam tat eva nivartyam anāśaṅkamānaḥ vā kim parasmāt upadeśam apekṣate aśrotṛ saṃskāram ca bruvāṇaḥ katham naḥ unmattaḥ tat saṃskārāya eva śabdānām kṛta saṃketa tvāt avyavahāra 
PVSV_62,6–62,10	 upanītaḥ ca naḥ eva kaścid jñeyaḥ ādi śabdaḥ asti vākya gatasya padasya artha cintanāt kva punar ete śabdāḥ prayujyante iti prayoga viṣaya cintāyām anya apohaḥ ucyate anirdiṣṭa prayogam tu jñeya śabdasya kaḥ arthaḥ iti praśne na kaścid arthaḥ tatas kvacid apratipatteḥ tathā ghaṭaḥ ādi śabdānām api yāḥ api kvacid prakaraṇe 
PVSV_62,11–62,17	 kevala śabda śravaṇāt pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭa prayoga anusāreṇa sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt sā aparisamāpta tat viplavaḥ eva ghaṭaḥ ādi śabdeṣu tādṛśaḥ jñeyaḥ ādi śabdeṣu api yathā darśanam asti eva tasmāt sarve eva śabda prayogaḥ kutaścid buddhim nivartya kvacid niveśana arthaḥ tat sāphalyāt niveśanam ca yaḥ yasmāt bhidyate vinivartya tam tat bhede bhidyamānānām samānaḥ ākāra bhāsini 
PVSV_62,18–63,1	 sa ca ayam anya vyāvṛttyā gamyate tasya vastunaḥ kaścid bhāgaḥ iti proktaḥ rūpam na asya api kiṃcana tat gatau eva śabdebhyaḥ gamyate anyaḥ nivartanam na tatra gamyate kaścid viśiṣṭaḥ kenacid paraḥ na ca api śabdaḥ dvaya kṛt anyonya abhāvaḥ iti asan arūpaḥ rūpavat tvena darśanam buddhi viplavaḥ niveśyamānaḥ api eṣa śabdaḥ yasmāt bhidyate tam vinivartya bhidyamānānām bhede samāna rūpa pratibhāsini ākṣipta tat anya vyāvṛttiḥ niveśyate iti saḥ eva ayam artha antara vyāvṛttyā tasya vastunaḥ kaścid bhāgaḥ gamyate śabdaḥ artha antara nivṛtti viśiṣṭān eva bhāvān āha iti ādinā nirdiṣṭaḥ sa hi tam bhedam 
PVSV_63,2–63,6	 kathayan artha antara vyavacchedam ākṣipan eva vartate eka gata bheda codanāyāḥ tat anya vyāvṛtti ākṣepa na antarīyaka tvāt saḥ eva bhedaḥ tat vyāvṛttyā gataḥ bhāgaḥ tat gateḥ tat upādhi tvāt tat viśiṣṭaḥ gataḥ iti ucyate na punar artha antara nivṛttiḥ viśeṣaṇa bhūtā keṣāṃcid arthānām yayā viśiṣṭāḥ śabdaiḥ codyante daṇḍi vat 
PVSV_63,7–63,11	 dvayoḥ hi bhidyamānayoḥ bhedasya ubhaya gata tvāt eka bhedaḥ abhidhāne api na antarīyakaḥ tat anyaḥ ākṣepaḥ bhavati iti tayoḥ na viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ eka bhedaḥ abhidhāne api anya vyāvṛtti gateḥ anvaya vyatireka codanayā vyavahāra aṅga tām śabdānām darśayan tat vyāvṛttyā gamyate tat viśiṣṭaḥ vā iti āha ata 
PVSV_63,12–64,2	 eva ca śabdasya na dvau vyāpārau tat anya vyāvartanam sva artha abhidhānam ca sva artha abhidhānāt eva tat anya vyāvṛtti gateḥ sva arthasya bheda rūpa tvāt na hi anvayaḥ avyatirekaḥ ananvayaḥ vā vyatirekaḥ ekaḥ anvayasya parihārya abhāve niṣphala codana tvāt tathā eka parihārasya kvacid sthiti abhāve sa ca ayam bhedaḥ arūpaḥ rūpavat tvena tu asya darśanam kevalam buddhi viplavaḥ eva tena eva aparama arthaḥ asau anyathā na hi vastunaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ vastu bhavati bhedaḥ asya asmāt iti īraṇāt 
PVSV_64,3–64,7	 rūpam hi parama arthaḥ bhedaḥ ced rūpam syāt tat rūpam vā syāt atat rūpam vā tādrūpye tat eva iti na anyaḥ tatas bhidyeta na hi tasya rūpam anyasya syāt na tat eva bhedasya rūpam rūpam ca anyat eva syāt tatas ca bhāvaḥ tasmāt vyāvarteta tatas asmāt tasya bhedaḥ iti na syāt yat khalu yat bhedāt vyāvartate 
PVSV_64,8–64,12	 tat eva tat bhavati iti saḥ asya bhedaḥ iti ca na syāt na hi anyonyasya bhedaḥ bhavati sambandha abhāvāt sati vā sa kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti rūpam tat janitam bhedaḥ iti aviśeṣāt sarva kāryāṇi sva kāraṇānām vyāvṛttayaḥ syuḥ rūpa antara tve ca bhedasya tatas api asya bhedaḥ iti bhedaḥ upādhi tvāt dravya antara van 
PVSV_64,13–64,20	 na bhedaḥ syāt na hi bhedaḥ upādhiḥ eva bhedaḥ ayam atas iti viśeṣa nirdeśāt tatas ca upādhi abhāve bhedasya eva abhāvaḥ syāt tasmāt na vyatiriktaḥ tat anyaḥ gati abhāvāt ca vastunaḥ na parama arthaḥ katham tarhi abhinnasya vastunaḥ śabdena codane tasya eva anyatas api bhedāt anaṃśaya eka bheda codane sarve bheda gateḥ tatra śabda pramāṇa antarāṇi vyarthāni na syuḥ yasmāt ekaḥ artha śleṣa vicchedaḥ ekaḥ vyāpriyate dhvaniḥ liṅgam vā tatra vicchinnam vācyam vastu na kiṃcana 
PVSV_64,21–64,27	 yasya abhidhānataḥ vastu sāmarthyāt akhile gatiḥ bhavet nānā phalaḥ śabdaḥ ekaḥ ādhāraḥ bhavati atas uktam prāk yathā saṃsṛṣṭa bāhya adhyātmika bhedāḥ buddhiḥ svam eva ābhāsam vyavahāra viṣayam artha kriyā yogyam adhyavasāya śabda artham upanayati iti tatra eva ca te śabdāḥ taiḥ taiḥ bhrānti kāraṇaiḥ saṃsṛṣṭa rūpaḥ iva ābhāti yathā saṃketam vicchedāya vyāpriyante na ca eka sādhyam vyavacchedam anyaḥ karoti saṃketa 
PVSV_65,1–65,5	 pratiniyamāt na ca vicchinnam kiṃcid vastu ākṣipyate yasya abhidhānāt vastu balena akhile gatiḥ syāt śabdānām buddhi viplava viṣaya tvāt tatra ca avastuni vastu sāmarthya abhāvāt tathābhūta artha darśana dvāreṇa ayam nānā eka dharma bhedaḥ abheda pratibhāsa viplava anusārī vyavahāraḥ iti tasya tat pratibandhe sati 
PVSV_65,6–65,11	 tat avyabhicāraḥ tatas vitathāt api ante tathābhūtaḥ eva vastuni jñāna saṃvādāt na punar bhinnaḥ ākāra grāhiṇām jñāna śabdānām eka vastu viṣaya tvāt nānā phalaḥ śabdaḥ ekaḥ ādhāraḥ vyāghātāt yathā varṇite tu buddhi pratibhāsaḥ āśraye na doṣaḥ iti vicchedam sūcayan ekam apratikṣipya vartate yadā anyam tena sa vyāptaḥ eka tvena ca bhāsate 
PVSV_65,12–65,18	 sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt tadā buddhi anurodhataḥ vastu dharmasya saṃsparśaḥ viccheda karaṇe dhvaneḥ syāt satyam sa hi tatra iti naḥ eka vastu abhidhāyini buddhau abhāsamānasya dṛśyasya abhāva niścayāt iti antaraślokāḥ tena anya apoha viṣayāḥ proktāḥ sāmānya gocarāḥ śabdāḥ ca buddhayaḥ ca eva vastuni eṣām asambhavāt 
PVSV_65,19–65,24	 yadi hi vidhi rūpeṇa vastu eva śabdaiḥ vikalpaiḥ vā api viṣayīkriyeta saḥ ayam sarve artha sarve ākāra prati iti prasaṅgaḥ asāmāna ādhikaraṇya ādayaḥ ca iti manyamānaḥ praṇetā nyāya śāstrasya anya apoha viṣayau etau prāha tathā hi eka tvāt vastu rūpasya bhinna rūpā matiḥ kutas anvaya vyatirekau vā naḥ ekasya ekaḥ artha gocarau 
PVSV_65,25–66,1	 tat ekam anaṃśam vastu katham bhinnaḥ ākārābhiḥ buddhibhiḥ viṣayīkriyate ākāra bhedaḥ āśraya tvāt bhedasya tasya ca abhedāt tad ā ātmanaḥ api sāmānyasya tat eka yogakṣema tvāt tat ayam anyonya artha parihāreṇa eka viṣayayoḥ vṛtti abhāvāt sāmānādhikaraṇya ādiḥ na ca vastu ātmanaḥ ekasya tatra eva vṛttiḥ 
PVSV_66,2–66,6	 avṛttiḥ ca yuktā vyāghātāt na ca anyatra avartamānam sāmānyam syāt sāmānyasya vṛttiḥ na viśeṣasya iti ced na bheda abhāvāt tat hi eka rūpam sāmānyam vā bhavet viśeṣaḥ vā na hi asati rūpa bhede ayam pravibhāgaḥ yuktaḥ sati vai avyatirekaḥ na syāt iti uktam tat ayam avibhāgaḥ anviyāt vā na vā na punar ananvayaḥ anvayī 
PVSV_66,7–66,12	 ca yaḥ api bhinnam eva sāmānyam āha tasya api abheda vyavahārāḥ ca bhede syuḥ anibandhanāḥ yathāsvam śabdāḥ bhinnam artham abhidadhānāḥ katham ekaḥ artha buddhi āśrayāḥ syuḥ artha antare abhidhāyinaḥ ca anākṣepakāḥ nirākāṅkṣa tvāt katham viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ āśrayāḥ sarvatra bhāvāt vyāvṛtteḥ na ete doṣāḥ prasaṅginaḥ 
PVSV_66,13–66,18	 yathā hi ekaḥ tasmāt bhinnaḥ tathā anyaḥ api iti bhedasya asāmānya doṣaḥ api na asti pariśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ tu prāk eva uktaḥ api ca eka kāryeṣu bhedeṣu tat kārya paricodane gaurava aśakti vaiphalyāt bhedaḥ ākhyāyāḥ samā śrutiḥ kṛtā vṛddhaiḥ atat kārya vyāvṛtti vinibandhanāḥ na bhāve sarva bhāvānām svabhāvasya vyavasthiteḥ 
PVSV_66,19–66,26	 yat rūpam śābaleyasya bāhuleyasya na asti tat atat kārya parāvṛttiḥ dvayoḥ api ca vidyate arthaḥ abhedena ca vinā śabdaḥ abhedaḥ na yujyate tasmāt tat kārya tā api iṣṭāḥ atat kāryāt eva bhinna tā cakṣuḥ ādau yathā rūpa vijñānaḥ eka phale kvacid aviśeṣeṇa tat kārya codanā sambhave sati sakṛt sarve prati iti artham kaścid sāṃketikīm śrutim kuryāt ṛte api tat rūpa sāmānyāt vyatirekiṇaḥ 
PVSV_67,1–67,6	 yaḥ api manyate katham abhinnam artham antareṇa bahuṣu ekā śrutiḥ teṣām asāmyāt eka vṛtteḥ anyatra pratyaya ajananāt apratyāsattike ca pratyayaḥ utpāde atiprasaṅgāt teṣu ca eka śabda niveśana vaiphalyāt ekaḥ artha niyoga abhāvāt bhinna svabhāvānām pṛthak niyoge ca tathā coditānām vibhāga aparijñānāt iti tasya api ekam asti iti eva lokena śabdaḥ niveśanīyaḥ tat 
PVSV_67,7–67,11	 vai ekam enām śrutim vastu śaktyā eva dhvanayati iti na asti etat kim tarhi kenacid prayojanena kecid śabdāḥ kvacid niveśyante tatra yadi anekam ekatra upayujyeta tat avaśyam tatra codanīyam tasya pṛthak pṛthak codane ati gauravam syāt na ca asya ananya sādhāraṇam rūpam śakyam codayitum na api asya āyāsa asya 
PVSV_67,12–67,16	 kiṃcid sāphalyam kevalam anena tatra yogyāḥ te arthāḥ codanīyāḥ te ekena vā śabdena ca udyeran bahubhiḥ vā iti svātantryam atra vaktuḥ tat iyam ekā śrutiḥ bahuṣu vaktṛ abhiprāya vaśāt pravartamānā naḥ upālambham arhati na ca iyam aśakya pravartanā icchā adhīna tvāt yadi hi na prayoktuḥ icchā katham 
PVSV_67,17–67,21	 iyam ekatra api pravarteta icchāyām vā kaḥ enām bahuṣu api pratibandhum samarthaḥ prayojana abhāvāt eva apravartanam iti ced uktam prayojanam bhinneṣu ekasmāt pratītiḥ atat prayojana bhedena iti uktam na punar svabhāvasya eka tvāt yathāsvam vyavasthita svabhāvānām anyonya rūpa aśleṣāt katham eka svabhāva nimittaḥ 
PVSV_67,22–67,26	 śabdaḥ bhinneṣu bhavet iti uktam prāk atat prayojana vyāvṛttiḥ tu bhinnānām aviruddhāḥ iti saḥ eva arthaḥ abhedaḥ śabdaḥ abhedasya kāraṇam bhavatu tena ime tat prayojanāḥ iti atat prayojanebhyaḥ bhinnāḥ eva uktāḥ na punar eṣām anyā tat kārya tā anyatra anyatas bhedāt yathā cakṣuḥ rūpaḥ āloka manaskāresu ātmaḥ indriya manaḥ artha 
PVSV_68,1–68,5	 tat saṃnikarṣeṣu vā rūpa vijñānaḥ eka kāryeṣu tat kārya sāmānya codanā sambhave kutas rūpa vijñānam iti vyavahāra lāghava artham kaścid sāṃketikīm śrutim niveśayet yaraḥ rūpa vijñāna hetuḥ śasaḥ vā iti api nāma sarveṣām tat hetūnām sakṛt pratītiḥ yathā syāt iti na ca atra anugāmi kiṃcid rūpam asti kevalam tat artha tayā 
PVSV_68,6–68,10	 te bhāvāḥ atat arthebhyaḥ bhinnāḥ iti bhedaḥ eva eṣām abhedaḥ evaṃjātīyāḥ ca sarve samūha santāna avasthāḥ viśeṣa śabdāḥ ye samastāḥ kiṃcid ekam kāryam kurvanti teṣām tatra viśeṣa abhāvāt apārthikāḥ viśeṣa codanā iti sakṛt sarveṣām niyojana artham ekam ayam lokaḥ śabdam teṣu niyuṅkte ghaṭaḥ iti te api sajātīyāt anyatas ca 
PVSV_68,11–68,15	 bhedaḥ aviśeṣe api tat prayojana aṅgatayā tat anyebhyaḥ bhidyante iti abhedāt tatas aviśeṣeṇa pratīyante tatra ghaṭasya rūpaḥ ādayaḥ iti api ghaṭa svabhāvāḥ rūpaḥ ādayaḥ udaka dhāraṇa viśeṣaḥ ādi kārya samarthāḥ iti yāvat sāmānya kārya sādhana prasiddhena ātmanā rūpa ādi śabdaiḥ prasiddhā viśiṣṭa kārya sādhanaḥ ākhyena viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭāḥ 
PVSV_68,16–68,20	 te evam ucyante na punar atra anyat kiṃcid yathā varṇita lakṣaṇam dravyam asti tasya tādṛśasya anupalambhāt eka vacanam api tat ekaḥ śakti sūcana artham saṃketa paratantram vā tathā ye hetu phala viśeṣa bhūtāḥ kiṃcid ekam sādhayanti sādhyante vā te api sakṛt pratyaya artham vrīhi ādi śabdaiḥ kṛta saṃketāḥ 
PVSV_68,21–68,25	 kathyante iti pūrvavat vācyam ye api pṛthak samastāḥ vā kvacid upayujyante te avasthā viśeṣa vācibhiḥ sakṛt eva śabdaiḥ pratyaya artham khyāpyante sa nidarśanāḥ sa pratighāḥ vā iti tat anyebhyaḥ bheda sāmānyena yathā eka kāryāḥ tat kārya codanāyām tat anyaḥ bhedena ghaṭaḥ ādi śabdaiḥ kṛta samayāḥ tathā kāraṇa apekṣayā 
PVSV_69,1–69,5	 api anekaḥ ekena vyavahāra artham eva yathā śābaleyaḥ bāhuleyaḥ prayatna anantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtakaḥ vā iti tathā tat kārya pratiṣedhena api acākṣuṣaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ anātmaḥ iti tat kāraṇa pratiṣedhena api asvāmikaḥ śūnyaḥ iti evam yathāyogam anyat api vācyam śūnya anityaḥ ādi śabdeṣu yathā kalpanam samīhita 
PVSV_69,6–69,16	 ākāram buddhau āropya tat vyavacchedena vyapadeśaḥ kriyate buddhi samīhā sandarśita vibhāga tvāt sarvasya śabdaḥ arthasya apratipakṣa doṣaḥ upakṣepaḥ ādayaḥ durmati vispanditāni iti upekṣanīyāḥ atha eka vṛtteḥ anekaḥ api yadi eka śrutimān bhavet na kevalam eka kāryāḥ tat anyaḥ bhedaḥ aviśeṣāt eka śabdena ucyante api tu eka vṛttyā api anekaḥ eka śabdena ucyeta kaḥ virodhaḥ syāt uktam atra tasya upalabhya abhimatasya anupalabdheḥ abhāvāt anupalabhyatāyām vā tat darśanaḥ āśrayāḥ vyapadeśa pratyabhijñāna ādayaḥ na bhaveyuḥ iti ādi api ca vṛttiḥ ādheya tā vyaktiḥ iti tasmin na yujyate 
PVSV_69,17–69,22	 yat etat ekam anekatra vartamānam ekām śrutim vartayati tasya kā iyam vṛttiḥ ādheya tā vā syāt yathā kuṇḍe badarāṇi vartante iti vyaktiḥ vā taiḥ abhivyakteḥ yadi ādheya tā nityasya anupakārya tvāt naḥ ādhāraḥ nityam hi sāmānyam iṣyate anitya tve aparāparaḥ utpatteḥ aneka tvāt bheda vat eka pratyaya ayogāt nityasya ca kim kurvāṇa 
PVSV_69,23–70,4	 ādhāraḥ syāt tasya tatra samavāyāt ādhāraḥ iti ced kaḥ ayam samavāyaḥ nāma apṛthak siddhānām āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ tat eva idam anupakārakasya āśraya tvam na sambhāvayāmaḥ atiprasaṅga bhayāt tasmāt samavāya saṃyogau ekaḥ artha samavāya ādayaḥ api vastu sambandhāḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt na vyatiricyante 
PVSV_70,5–70,15	 parasparam anyatas vā anupakāriṇām apratibandhāt apratibaddhasya ca asambandhāt yadi api ekaḥ artha samavāyinām parasparam anupakāraḥ tatas ekasmāt upakāreṇa bhāvyam abhāve yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgāt atas svaḥ upakāra dvāreṇa eva param api buddhyā saṃghaṭayya khyāpyate tasmāt tatra api kārya kāraṇa bhāva kṛtaḥ eva pratibandhaḥ tat ayam āśrayaḥ sāmānyasya sva ātmani anupakurvāṇaḥ anapekṣasya ādhāraḥ iti yācitaka maṇḍanam etat katham tarhi idānīm ajanakam kuṇḍam badarāṇām ādhāraḥ pravisarpataḥ śaktiḥ tat deśa jananam kuṇḍaḥ ādeḥ badaraḥ ādiṣu 
PVSV_70,16–70,20	 prakṛtyāḥ eva guruṇaḥ dravyasya asamānaḥ deśa kāryaḥ utpādana dharmaṇaḥ samānaḥ deśa kāryaḥ utpādana bhāvaḥ ādhāra kṛtaḥ tasmāt tat pūrva kṣaṇa sahakāri kuṇḍam tatra eva badara kāryam janayat ādhāraḥ iti ucyate anyathā iha kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti api na syāt na vai tat upakāra kṛtaḥ ayam vyapadeśaḥ kim tarhi saṃyoga kṛtaḥ 
PVSV_70,21–70,25	 kim punar sa tayoḥ eva saṃyogaḥ tābhyām jananāt samavāyāt vā sa kim ekatra eva na samavaiti janyate vā tasya asāmarthyāt tat asamartham pṛthak tat sahitam api tādṛśam eva iti anupakāraka tvāt na saṃyogena tadvat syāt sahitasya tat anyaḥ upakārāt viśeṣaḥ utpatteḥ sāmarthyam kaḥ ayam ajanya janaka bhūtānām 
PVSV_70,26–71,5	 upakāraḥ svarūpasya siddheḥ akārya tvāt para rūpa kriyāyām api tatra anupakārāt ubhayathā kārakasya akiṃcitkara tvena anupakāraka tvāt iti ukta prāyam tasmāt sarve eva vastu sambandhāḥ janakasya eva upayoga viśeṣa vaśāt pravibhāgena kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vyavasthāpyante tat ayam kuṇḍaḥ ādīnām api ādhāra bhāvaḥ badaraḥ ādiṣu janana śaktiḥ eva 
PVSV_71,6–71,12	 na sambhavati sā api atra na hi ayam janana viśeṣa lakṣaṇaḥ ādhāra bhāvaḥ sāmānye sāmānya āśrayasya sambhavati tasya ajanya tvāt tat abhāve api avasthiteḥ na sthitiḥ atha api syāt sthāpakaḥ āśrayaḥ sāmānyasya tatas sthiti hetu tvāt ādhāraḥ na jananāt iti tat ayuktam tasya tat abhāve api sthānāt 
PVSV_71,13–71,17	 patana dharmāṇām hi bhāvānām pāta pratibandhāt ajanakaḥ api sthāpakaḥ bhavet atra api yadi kaścid pratibandham na paryanuyuñjīta sa hi pāta pratibandhaḥ na artha antaram eva yaḥ sthāpayitrā kriyeta artha antara tve tatra eva asya upayogaḥ iti kaḥ patataḥ pratibandhaḥ pratibandhāt apāte api tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ anavasthā 
PVSV_71,18–71,22	 vā tasmāt pāta abhāvaḥ pāta pratibandhaḥ sa katham kenacid kriyate abhāvam karoti iti hi na abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid kāryaḥ tasya kathaṃcid kārya rūpa tve abhāva ayogāt tasmāt bhāva kriyā pratiṣedha nirdeśaḥ eṣa bhāvam na karoti iti yāvat tathā ca ayam na kiṃcid karoti iti akiṃcitkaraḥ ca kaḥ kasya sthāpakaḥ nāma tena 
PVSV_71,23–71,30	 ayam kenacid apratibaddhaḥ iti na kadācid tiṣṭhet tasmāt pāta pratibandhaḥ iti api kṣaṇikānām bhāvānām upādāna samāna deśaḥ utpādanam ucyate astu nāma ajananam pātinām tat pratibaddhaḥ tat karaṇāt gatimatas dravyasya kaścid sthāpakaḥ api astu sāmānyasya akriyasya kim lakṣaṇām sthitim kurvāṇaḥ sthāpakaḥ syāt sthitiḥ hi tasya svarūpa apracyutiḥ eva sā ca naḥ āśraya āyattā nitya tvāt sā api ayuktāḥ eva bhedaḥ abheda vivecane 
PVSV_72,1–72,5	 astu nāma āśraya hetukā sthitiḥ sāmānyasya sā sāmānyāt anyā vā syāt ananyā vā sā anyā ced tām eva saḥ āśrayaḥ karoti sā ca apratibaddhā sāmānyaḥ iti kim sāmānyasya āśrayeṇa pratibaddhe vā kaḥ pratibandhaḥ iti vācyam sthiti karaṇam ced tatra api tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ anavasthā ca tatas upakāra anavadhāraṇāt asya iyam 
PVSV_72,6–72,15	 sthitiḥ iti apratītiḥ jananam ced kim āśrayeṇa apekṣitena anupakāriṇā apekṣāḥ iti hi tat pratibandhaḥ sa ca anādheya viśeṣasya sāmānyasya ayuktaḥ iti kevalam janayet iti na asti anyaḥ sthiti hetuḥ abhede vā sthiteḥ sāmānyāt svarūpam eva tat tasya tat ca nityam asti iti na sthitiḥ asya kenacid kriyate tasmāt na sāmānyasya ādhāraḥ asti tat naḥ ādheya tā asya vṛttiḥ atha punar sataḥ api sāmānyasya avyaktasya vyaktyā jñāna kāraṇa tvāt tat vyaktiḥ tatra vṛttiḥ syāt na yuktam evam bhavitum yasmāt vijñānaḥ utpatti yogya tvāya ātmani anyaḥ anurodhi yat tat vyaṅgyam yogyatāyāḥ ca kāraṇam kārakam matam 
PVSV_72,17–72,23	 prāk eva asya ca yogya tve tat apekṣā na yujyate sāmānyasya avikāryasya tat sāmānyavataḥ kutas na khalu vai kārakāt vyañjakasya kaścid bhedaḥ sva viṣaya vijñāna utpādana samartham aparam sajātīyaḥ upādāna apekṣam anapekṣam vā janayan bhāvam eva vyañjakaḥ ucyate paratra tu jñāna janana śaktiḥ anākṣiptāḥ janyasya iti janana mātreṇa kāraka tvam yaḥ hi yatas vijñānaḥ utpādana yogyatām pratilabhate sa ced 
PVSV_72,24–73,1	 na tasya janyaḥ syāt sā asya svabhāva bhūtā yogyatā prāk eva asti iti na vijñāna janane tam apekṣeta para bhūtāyām ca asyām saḥ eva tatas bhavati iti sthiti vat prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt vyañjakaḥ na tam karoti na api anyam iti akiṃcitkaraḥ ca apekṣyate iti vyāhatam etat nanu ajanakāḥ api kāryatvāt dhūmaḥ ādayaḥ vyañjakāḥ 
PVSV_73,2–73,6	 satyam vyañjakāḥ na tu dhūmam apekṣya agniḥ ātmani jñānam janayati tathābhūtasya agneḥ sākṣāt ajanaka tvāt kevalam upādāna balena eva tatra jñānam utpadyate na viṣaya balena asati api tasmin bhāvāt paraṃparayā liṅga anusāreṇa na api sāmānya lakṣaṇa avabhāsinām pratyayānām saṃnihita viṣaya tā viṣaya 
PVSV_73,7–73,11	 balena utpattiḥ vā iti niveditam etat nivedayiṣyate ca tasmāt ye viṣayāḥ sākṣāt upayogena vijñānam janayantaḥ tatra param apekṣante te avaśyam tatas ātmānam pratilabhante na ca ayam ātma pratilambhaḥ sāmānyasya nityasya kutaścid sambhavati tasmāt na tat kenacid vyaṅgyam na vai yogya tā pratilambham 
PVSV_73,12–73,21	 sāmānyasya vyaktim brūmaḥ kim tarhi sva āśraya samavāyam sva āśraya samavetam hi tat ātmani anyatra vā vijñāna hetuḥ iti uktam atra ajanya janakayoḥ kaḥ ayam āśraya āśrayi bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ samavāyaḥ iti sva āśraya samavāya apekṣaḥ vijñāna hetuḥ tena janyaḥ eva syāt tat hetoḥ svabhāvasya prāk abhāvāt paścāt ca tatas bhāvāt nityam tat svabhāva sadbhāve prāk api samavāyāt vijñāna udaya prasaṅgāt na vai vyaktiḥ sāmānyasya saṃskārāt vyañjikā kim tarhi tat grāhiṇaḥ indriyasya saḥ api añjanaḥ ādeḥ iva vyakteḥ saṃskāraḥ naḥ indriyasya ca pratipatteḥ abhinna tvāt tat bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ 
PVSV_73,22–74,2	 saṃskṛtam añjanaḥ ādibhiḥ indriyam pratipattau kiṃcid atiśayam āsādayati spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa bhedāt atat kāriṇaḥ ca atat saṃskāraka tvāt na evam vyakteḥ indriyasya kaścid saṃskāraḥ tat bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ pratipattim prati aviśeṣāt viṣaya saṃskāraḥ tu indriya aviśeṣe api tat viśeṣaḥ ādhānāt upakārī syāt na indriya saṃskāraḥ 
PVSV_74,3–74,7	 prāk adṛśye darśana śakti ādhānāt upakārakaḥ iti ced saḥ atīndriyam artham darśayan katham na pratipatteḥ bhedakaḥ eka pratiniyame ca sāmānya antarasya darśakaḥ na syāt vyaktyā ca indriya saṃskārāt tat darśane tat vyaṅgyeṣu sāmānyeṣu kadācid aniścayaḥ na syāt eka niścayaḥ vā tasyāḥ avibhāgāyāḥ teṣu viśeṣa abhāvāt 
PVSV_74,8–74,12	 vyakteḥ yadi indriya saṃskāraḥ yadi naḥ indriya saṃskāraḥ sāmānyasya vijñāna janana svabhāvaḥ iti svabhāvāt apracyuteḥ anapekṣya eva indriya saṃskāram vijñānam janayet saṃskṛtaḥ indriya sahakāri tvāt kevalam asamartham iti ced kaḥ ayam anādheya atiśayasya sahakāra arthaḥ anityāḥ hi bhāvāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ ātma lābhāt 
PVSV_74,13–74,21	 tam apekṣeran yaḥ hi eṣām janakaḥ ātmā sa tadā eva tatas bhavati iti janyatā eva eṣām parasparataḥ apekṣā sāmānyam punar anāsādya param nityam tat svabhāvam kim iti indriyam apekṣate hi tasya kevalasya yaḥ na tat svabhāvaḥ sa punar kathaṃcid bhāvī vyakteḥ indriya saṃskāraḥ tat sahakāri sāmānyam vijñāna hetuḥ iti api pāraṃparyeṇa vyakteḥ kāryam eva sāmānyam uktam syāt api ca vyañjakasya ca jātīnām jāti mattā yadi iṣyate prāptaḥ go tvaḥ ādinā tadvān pradīpaḥ ādiḥ prakāśakaḥ 
PVSV_74,22–75,2	 yaḥ hi yat viṣaya vijñāna hetuḥ sa tasya vyañjakaḥ vijñāna hetu tvam go tvaḥ ādiṣu pradīpaḥ ādeḥ api asti tejaḥ saṃskāra apekṣiṇaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ artha pratipatteḥ tatas pradīpaḥ ādayaḥ go tvaḥ ādinā tadvantaḥ syuḥ na hi vyakteḥ api jñāna hetu tām muktvā anyā kācid asti abhivyaktiḥ sāmānyasya svabhāva atiśayasya ādhātum aśakya tvāt 
PVSV_75,3–75,11	 samavāyaḥ abhivyaktiḥ iti ced uktāḥ uttaram etat tasya samavāya ayogāt iti samavāya mātram hi vyaktyā saha asya jātam na anyaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti pūrvavat paścāt api na jñāna hetuḥ syāt samavāyāt eva jñāna hetu tve sva āśraya samavāyinām anyeṣām api dṛśyatā āpattiḥ tasmāt jñāna hetu tāḥ eva vyañjaka tvam tat ca tulyam pradīpaḥ ādau iti saḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ tat naḥ ādheya tā na vyaktiḥ vṛttiḥ sāmānyasya iti avṛtteḥ na anekatra jñāna hetuḥ atas eva vyakteḥ anyā athavā ananyā yeṣām jātiḥ tu vidyate teṣām vyaktiṣu apūrvāsu katham sāmānya buddhayaḥ 
PVSV_75,12–75,20	 vidyate eva iti avadhāraṇa arthaḥ tu śabdaḥ vidyamānaḥ hi padārthaḥ sva sāmarthyena anyatra buddhim janayan svarūpa anukāriṇīm tat sambandham apekṣate anyathā atiprasaṅgāt sa ca sāmānyasya sataḥ tattva anyat tva pakṣayoḥ na sambhavati ekatra dṛṣṭasya anyatra darśana asambhavāt sā hi buddhiḥ eka bhāvinī vyakti antaram evam āskandet bhūta grāhiṇī yadi tatra dṛṣṭam kiṃcid anyatra paśyet tat ca sataḥ ananya tve anvaya abhāvāt anya tve api anapāśrayāt 
PVSV_75,21–75,25	 na sambhavati svabhāvaḥ hi svabhāvāt na tattvam anya tvam vā laṅghayati rūpasya atadbhūtasya anya tva avyatikramāt idam eva khalu rūpasya anya tvam yat na tat ākāra antara vat aviśeṣāt tat ced sāmānyasya rūpam ananyat tat eva tat bhavati atattve vastu antara vat anyatva prasaṅgāt na ca eka vyakti ātmanaḥ vyakty 
PVSV_75,26–76,3	 antara anvāveśaḥ avyakti antaratva prasaṅgāt tatas na avyatirekiṇaḥ sāmānyāt anvayinī buddhiḥ syāt na api vyatirekiṇaḥ tasya kvacid anāśrayāt anyasya api vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāva ādeḥ sambandhasya kenacid anupakāryasya apratibandhena abhāvāt asambandhāt ca jñānaḥ utpattau api prasaṅgāt tat ayam eka vastu 
PVSV_76,4–76,8	 darśanena eka vṛtteḥ pratyayasya anyatra vṛttim icchan tattva anyat tve na atikrāmati iti ayuktam etat tasmāt iyam artheṣu eka rūpā pratītiḥ vikalpa vāsanā samutthitā bhrāntiḥ eva bhāva bhedaḥ vāsanā prakṛtiḥ ca tasya āśrayaḥ iti nirloṭhitam etat katham tarhi idānīm pradhānaḥ īśvaraḥ ādi kārya śabdāḥ bhāveṣu atat bhūta bhedeṣu 
PVSV_76,9–76,13	 abhedena vartante te api yathā saṃketaḥ āhita vāsanāḥ upaskṛta tvāt vijñāna santateḥ sarve artha darśaneṣu anapekṣya api tat bhedam tathā adhyavasāyāt atathābhūta kalpita vyavacchedena vikalpa vijñāna pratibhāsini arthaḥ upādāna bala prabhava vikalpa samutthitāḥ pravartante na hi teṣu atathābhūteṣu kiṃcid vyatiriktam avyatiriktam 
PVSV_76,14–76,18	 vā sāmānyam asti tathā abhāva kalpanayā tu tat anya bhedaḥ pratipattṛ abhiprāya vaśāt syāt tat abhiprāyāt eva sāmānyam kim naḥ iti ced tena avaśyam hi tatra bhedaḥ na antarīyaka tvāt eṣṭavyaḥ saḥ eva sāmānya kārye paryāptaḥ iti niḥ prayojanā sāmānya kalpanā yadi satsu asatsu vā bhāveṣu sāmānya buddhiḥ 
PVSV_76,19–76,23	 na iyam arthavatī kevalam viplavaḥ eva iti na asmākam asyāḥ viṣaya nirūpaṇam prati kaścid ādaraḥ kvacid avisaṃvādaḥ asyāḥ vastuni kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratibandhāt na tathābhūta grāhya samāveśāt pratyakṣa vat atatha abhāve api bhāvāt iti nivedayiṣyāmaḥ niveditam ca bheda viṣaya tvam punar asyāḥ bahulam bhinna padārtha 
PVSV_76,24–77,3	 darśana balena teṣu bhāva adhyavasāyāt tathā bhāva kalpanāyām eva aparatra bhāvāt api ca ayam sāmānyam artha antaram kalpayan sva āśraya mā atra gatam vā kalpayet sarva gatam vā ākāśaḥ ādi vat tatra yadi sva āśraya mā atra gatam ghaṭa tve ādi śūnyeṣu pradeśeṣu ghaṭa ādi utpattau katham teṣu bhinna deśa dravya vartinaḥ sāmānyasya 
PVSV_77,4–77,15	 sambhavaḥ yasmāt tat pūrva dravyāt utpitsu dravyam na yāti niṣkriyatve upagamāt na hi anyaḥ dravya vṛtteḥ bhāvasya tatas avicalataḥ bhinna deśena bhāvena tat ubhaya antarāla avyāpinaḥ yogaḥ yuktaḥ prāk sa na ca tatra āsīt asti paścān na ca tatra utpannaḥ na kutaścid āyātaḥ iti kaḥ imam vyāghāta bhāram udvoḍhum samarthaḥ anyatra jāḍyāt api ca na ca aṃśa vat jahāti pūrvam naḥ ādhāram utpitsu deśāt bhinna deśam tayoḥ ca vartate iti aho vyasana santatiḥ 
PVSV_77,16–77,20	 bhinna deśayoḥ hi bhāvayoḥ sambandhaḥ dvidhā bhavet nānā avayava ātma tayā anyonyābhyām avayavābhyām tat sambandhāt āloka rajju vaṃśa daṇḍaḥ ādi vat na hi sa avayava tvam antareṇa bhinna deśābhyām yugapad kasyacid yogaḥ yuktaḥ tasya dvitīyaḥ ātma abhāvāt eka ātmanaḥ ca tat pradeśa varti sambandhi rūpa tvāt anyathā 
PVSV_77,21–78,3	 tat sambandha ayogāt ekasya ādheyasya tatra sthānam tadā eva tatra tena eva ātmanā asthānam iti tat sthitaḥ asthitaḥ ātmanoḥ ekasya virodhāt ayuktam etat sarvatra sarvadā sarve ākāra sthitaḥ ātmā iti ced tat svabhāva darśanaḥ āśrayaḥ pratyayaḥ sarvatra sarve ākāraḥ syāt tathā ca gām api aśvaḥ iti pratīyāt aśva sthitaḥ ātmanā dravya tvena 
PVSV_78,4–78,11	 sambandhāt tat svabhāva pratipattyā ca tathā niścayāt tasya ca ekasya adṛṣṭaḥ ākāra antara abhāvāt tasmāt na anavayavam aneka deśe yugapad ādhīyate pūrvaḥ ādhāra tyāge tu bhinna deśe api varteta sa ca na abhimataḥ anyatra vartamānasya tatas anyaḥ sthāna janmani svasmāt acalataḥ sthānāt vṛttiḥ iti ati yuktimat yatra asau vartate bhāvaḥ tena sambadhyate api na tat deśinam ca vyāpnoti kim api etat mahā adbhutam 
PVSV_78,12–78,20	 iti antara ślokau yasya tu sarva gatam sāmānyam tasya api vyaktāḥ eva ekatra sā vyaktyai abhedāt sarvatragāḥ yadi jātiḥ dṛśyeta sarvatra na jāteḥ nityāyāḥ kācid vyaktiḥ iti niṣiddham etat tasmāt nityam anapekṣita paraḥ upaskārā dṛśyeta vā na vā kadācid tasmin svabhāve vyavasthānāt svabhāva antarasya kutaścid anutpatteḥ abhyupagamya api vyaktim vyāpini ekatra vyaktyā bhedaḥ abhāvāt vyaktāḥ eva sarvatra iti vyakti śūnyeṣu api pradeśeṣu dṛśyeta na ca sā vyakti apekṣiṇī 
PVSV_78,21–79,1	 yadi hi vyakti apekṣiṇī syāt vyañjaka apratipattau hi na vyaṅgyam sampratīyate viparyayaḥ punar kasmāt iṣṭaḥ sāmānya tadvatoḥ yaḥ api hi sva āśrayaḥ indriya saṃyoga apekṣa pratipattikam sāmānyam āśraya śūnyeṣu pradeśeṣu na dṛśyate iti pratisamādadhīta tasya api asti eva āśraya indriya saṃyogaḥ upakārakaḥ iti tatas tat darśī yathā sthitām paśyet na hi tasyām dṛśyamānāyām adṛṣṭam tadīyam yuktam vyakti vyaṅgya tvāt sāmānyasya vyañjaka rahiteṣu 
PVSV_79,2–79,6	 pradeśeṣu adarśanam iti api mithyā tathābhūtasya vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāvasya tatra abhāvāt sva pratipattyā apara pratipatti hetuḥ hi vyañjakaḥ pradīpaḥ ādiḥ svarūpa śūnye deśe sva vyaṅgyam na darśayat na evam vyaktiḥ viparyayāt katham hi sā vyañjikā ca syāt sāmānyasya tat pratipatti dvāreṇa ca dṛśyā syāt vyaṅgyā 
PVSV_79,7–79,12	 ca sā eva prasajyate pradīpa ghaṭa vat kathaṃcid tat pratipattim antareṇa adṛśya rūpa tvāt api ca anena kim asambhavat abhisamīkṣya evam bahu āyāsaḥ sāmānya vādaḥ āśritaḥ para sparataḥ bhedāt vyatirekiṇīṣu vyaktiṣu anvayinaḥ pratyayasya ayogāt katham idānīm pācakaḥ ādiṣu abhinnena vinā api arthena vācakaḥ 
PVSV_79,13–79,17	 pācaka pāṭhakaḥ ādiṣu anyonyam ananvayiṣu api śabda pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ asti pācakaḥ pāṭhakaḥ iti na hi teṣu anyat ekam abhinnam asti yena bhinnāḥ tathā pratīyeran karma asti ced vyaktibhyaḥ eva tarhi sa pratyayaḥ astu kim idānīm karmaṇā anyena vā bhinnam abhinna pratyaya hetuḥ na bhavati iti ekam sāmānyam iṣṭam 
PVSV_79,18–79,26	 tat yadi bhinnam api karma abhinnam pratyayam janayet vyaktibhiḥ kaḥ aparādhaḥ kṛtaḥ yena tāḥ tathā naḥ iṣyante tāsām eka rūpa tvāt asya idam iti vyatireka pratītiḥ atat ākāra viśeṣavatī ca na syāt iti ced uktam atra yathā vyatirekaḥ viśeṣa pratyayāḥ ca yathāsvam artha antara vivekāt iti tasmāt vyakti vat bhedāt na hetuḥ karma asya pācakaḥ ādi abheda pratyayasya tat karma jātiḥ abhedāt hetuḥ iti ced na jātiḥ karma saṃśrayāt 
PVSV_80,1–80,12	 na hi artha antara sambandhinī jātiḥ artha antare pratyaya hetuḥ go tvam iva karkaḥ ādiṣu pācaka karmasu ca karma jātiḥ na ca tāni karmāṇi pācaka śabdena abhidhīyante kim tarhi tat karma āśrayaḥ dravyam tasya karma sāmānyasya śruti antara nimitta tvāt ca pākaḥ pākaḥ iti hi tatas syāt na punar pācakaḥ iti tasya karma nimitta tve proktam kim ca sthiti abhāvāt ca karmaṇaḥ na hi anityam karma sarvadā asti tasya ca pratyayasya karma nimitta tve niruddhe karmaṇi na pācakaḥ iti ucyeta pacataḥ eva karma sadbhāvāt tatas eva asambandhāt na sāmānyam na ayuktam śabda kāraṇam 
PVSV_80,13–80,20	 atiprasaṅgāt vinaṣṭe hi karmaṇi tat sāmānyam na karmaṇi na kartari iti sambaddha sambandhe api asya na asti iti asambandhāt na śabda jñāna hetuḥ anyathā hi atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt atītam anāgatam vā nimittīkṛtya tayoḥ pravṛttiḥ iti ced karma api na asat jñānaḥ abhidhānayoḥ nimittam tayoḥ anaimittika tā āpatteḥ 
PVSV_80,21–81,6	 asat hi nirupākhyam katham nimittam syāt kārya karaṇa lakṣaṇa tvāt vastu tvasya tat pracyuta asamprāpta rūpam atīta anāgatam karma nimittam anyat ca vyakti ādikam naḥ iṣṭam iti animitte te syātām tathā ca na jāti siddhiḥ tasyāḥ jñāna abhidhānayoḥ nimitta tve naḥ iṣṭa tvāt śaktiḥ pācakaḥ ādi śabda nimittam na karma na sāmānyam iti ced na ca śaktiḥ ananvayāt 
PVSV_81,7–81,16	 na hi śaktiḥ nāma kiṃcid anyat eva pācakaḥ ādīnām tasyāḥ eva pācakaḥ ādi artha kriyāḥ upayogena dravyasya anupayogitva prasaṅgāt tasyām tasya upayogaḥ iti ced kim idānīm śaktyā śakti upayogāya śakti antarasya vyatirekiṇaḥ abhyupagame atiprasaṅgāt dravyam eva upayujyate iti vācyam tasya upayoge śaktau artha kriyāyām eva upayujyate iti kim naḥ iṣyate iti kim antarāle anarthikayā śaktyā tasmāt śaktiḥ iti dravyam eva tat kāryam tat ca na anveti iti tatas anvayī śabdaḥ na syāt sāmānyam pācaka tve ādi yadi prāk eva tat bhavet vyaktam sattā ādi van no ced na paścāt aviśeṣatas 
PVSV_81,17–81,25	 atha api pācaka tvam iti sāmānyam eva kiṃcid bhavet sati arthe tat samavāyasya akādācitka tvāt sattā ādi vat prāk eva vyaktam syāt yāvanti hi sāmānyāni arthe samavāya dharmāṇi tāni saha utpādena asya samavayanti iti samayaḥ tat vyatikrame tasya paścāt api aviśeṣāt na tat samavāyaḥ syāt tat sambandhi svabhāva vaiguṇyāt hi sa tasya prāk naḥ āsīt tatra eva ca asya svabhāve sthitasya paścāt bhavati iti duranvayam etat kriyāḥ upakāra apekṣasya vyañjaka tve avikāriṇaḥ na apekṣa atiśaye api asya kṣaṇika tvāt kriyā kutas 
PVSV_81,26–82,4	 karma upakāram apekṣya pācaka tvam dravyeṇa vyajyate iti ced sthira svabhāvasya anatiśayāt aviśeṣaḥ ādhāyini kā apekṣāḥ atiśaye vā kṣaṇika tvāt karmaṇaḥ pratikṣaṇam svabhāva bhūtasya anyāni asya atiśayasya utpatteḥ tat api kṣaṇikam syāt tatas svaḥ utpatti sthāna vināśinaḥ kriyā kutas yat apekṣam vyañjakam syāt katham 
PVSV_82,5–82,9	 tarhi idānīm asti abhinne vastuni jñāna śabdayoḥ anvayinoḥ vṛttiḥ yathā pācakaḥ ādiṣu nanu tat eva idam cintyate katham teṣu api iti cintitam etat yathā na teṣu sambhavati tat kim idānīm animitte te syātām na animitte kim tarhi na bāhya tat tva nimitte yathāsvam vāsanā prabodhāt vikalpaḥ utpattiḥ tatas śabdāḥ 
PVSV_82,10–82,14	 na punar vikalpa abhidhānayoḥ vastu sattā samāśrayaḥ iti ukta prāyam etat yathāsvam samayaḥ vāsanā vaśāt virodhi rūpa samāveśena aparāpara darśane api anvayinoḥ tayoḥ darśanāt na ca tatra tat nibandhanaḥ kaścid svabhāvaḥ asti paraspara virodhinoḥ yugapad ekatra samāveśa ayogāt aniyamena tarhi syāt na hi animittam 
PVSV_82,15–82,19	 bhavat kvacid bhavati kvacid na bhavati iti niyamam arhati na khalu vai tat animittam vāsanā viśeṣa nimitta tvāt bāhyam tu tathābhūtam dṛśyam na asti iti brūmaḥ na ca asati tasmin na bhavitavyam supta taimirikaḥ upalabdheṣu artheṣu abhāveṣu samayaḥ vāsanāḥ āropita rūpa viśeṣeṣu ca tathā vikalpaḥ utpatteḥ na 
PVSV_82,20–82,27	 ca te asatsu utpadyante iti sarvatra sarve ākāraḥ vibhāge naḥ eva tathā upalabdhānām vikalpanāt uktam ca atra kiṃcid asmābhiḥ prakṛtyāḥ api kecid eka jñāna kāryāḥ svabhāva bhedāt iti api ca tulye bhede yayā jātiḥ pratyāsattyā prasarpati kvacid na anyatra saḥ eva astu śabda jñāna nibandhanam iti antaraślokaḥ na nivṛttim vihāya asti yadi bhāva anvayaḥ aparaḥ ekasya kāryam anyasya na syāt atyanta bhedataḥ 
PVSV_82,28–83,8	 yadi ete bhāvāḥ vyāvṛttim muktvā svabhāvena kenacid anvayinā śūnyāḥ na eṣām bahūnām ekam kāryam syāt yaḥ hi tasya svabhāvaḥ janakaḥ na hi saḥ anyasya asti yaḥ asti sa na janakaḥ vyatirekaḥ yaḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt yat janakam tat eva vastu tat janakam ca aparatra na asti iti na aparam janayet sa hi tasya svabhāvaḥ yaḥ janakaḥ saḥ anyasya api yadi syāt sa tena svabhāvena tatas abhinnaḥ syāt iti asti svabhāva anvayaḥ yadi eka ātma tayā anekaḥ kāryasya ekasya kārakaḥ ātmā ekatra api saḥ asti iti vyarthāḥ syuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ 
PVSV_83,9–83,19	 yadi eka svabhāva tvāt anekaḥ ekasya kārakaḥ sa teṣām abhinnaḥ svabhāvaḥ eka saṃnidhāne api asti iti avaikalyāt kāraṇasya ekaḥ api janakaḥ syāt yasmāt na apaiti abhinnam tat rūpam viśeṣāḥ khalu apāyinaḥ na hi tasya abhinna svabhāvasya artha antare viśeṣaḥ asti viśeṣaḥ abheda hāneḥ sa ca tatra api asti iti naḥ eka sthitau api tasya apāyaḥ asti ye viśeṣāḥ teṣām saha sthiti niyama abhāvāt syāt apāyaḥ na ca te janakāḥ iṣṭāḥ sahakāriṇām eka svabhāvatayā janakatva abhyupagamāt tatas janakasya sthānāt asthāyinaḥ ca ajanaka tvāt eka sthitau api kāryaḥ utpattiḥ syāt na ca bhavati atas ekaḥ apāye phala abhāvāt viśeṣebhyaḥ tat udbhavaḥ 
PVSV_83,20–83,24	 tat kāryam aneka sahakāri sādhāraṇam eka viśeṣa apāye api na bhavati punar api avikaleṣu sarveṣu viśeṣeṣu bhavati na tu avikale api abhinne rūpe kāryam hi kutaścid bhāva dharmi yat na bhavati tat tasya eva vaikalyāt na ca abhinnasya rūpasya eka sthitau api vaikalyam asti avikale api tasmin abhavat tasya ajanakaḥ ātma tām 
PVSV_83,25–84,9	 sūcayati yat sākalya vaikalyābhyām ca kāryam bhāva abhāva vat tatas eva utpattiḥ tasmin sati niyamena bhavataḥ tat anyasmāt utpatti kalpanāyām atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt viśeṣāḥ eva janakāḥ na sāmānyam tatas te eva vastu yasmāt sa pāramārthikaḥ bhāvaḥ yaḥ eva artha kriyā kṣamaḥ idam eva hi vastu avastunoḥ lakṣaṇam yat artha kriyā yogya tā ayogya tā ca iti vakṣyāmaḥ sa ca artha kriyā yogyaḥ arthaḥ na anveti yaḥ anveti na tasmāt kārya sambhavaḥ 
PVSV_84,10–84,14	 tasmāt sarvam sāmānyam anartha kriyā yogya tvāt avastu vastu tu viśeṣaḥ eva tatas eva tat niṣpatteḥ svabhāva ananvayāt tarhi ekasya janakam rūpam anyasya na asti iti ajanakaḥ syāt janaka tve vā bhedaḥ aviśeṣāt sarvaḥ janakaḥ syāt na etat asti yasmāt tena ātmanā hi bhede api hetuḥ kaścid na ca aparaḥ 
PVSV_84,15–84,20	 svabhāvaḥ ayam ekasya janakāt ātmanaḥ bhidyamānāḥ sarve samam janakāḥ na vā aviśeṣe kaścid iti syāt etat yadi eṣām na viśeṣaḥ sambhavet tatas bheda api kutaścid ātma atiśayāt kaścid janakaḥ na aparaḥ sa hi tasya svabhāvaḥ na aparasya na hi svabhāvāḥ bhāvānām paryanuyogam arhanti kim agniḥ dahati uṣṇaḥ vā naḥ udakam iti etāvat tu 
PVSV_84,21–85,3	 syāt kutas ayam svabhāvaḥ iti nirhetuka tve anapekṣiṇaḥ niyama abhāvena atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt svabhāvaḥ asya sva hetoḥ iti ucyate tasya api tat jananaḥ ātma tā tat anyasmāt iti anādiḥ hetu paraṃparā bhinnānām hi kaścid hetuḥ na anyaḥ svabhāvāt iti atra na kiṃcid bādhakam abhede tu syātām nāśaḥ udbhavau sakṛt 
PVSV_85,4–85,9	 abhedāt svabhāvena eva viśvasya sva ātma vat vibhāgaḥ utpatti sthiti nirodhaḥ ādayaḥ na syuḥ tathā upalakṣaṇāt abhedasya idam eva hi bhedaḥ abheda lakṣaṇam ekaḥ ākārasya api vyatirekaḥ avyatirekaḥ ca virodhinoḥ eka ātmani asambhavāt bhedaḥ api tena naḥ evam ced na vai sarve ākāra avyatirekam brūmaḥ yena evam syāt kaścid asya ātmā 
PVSV_85,10–85,17	 bhinnaḥ na anyaḥ iti bhedāt na saha utpatti ādayaḥ evam tarhi yaḥ ekasmin vinaśyati tiṣṭhati ātmā na tasya bhedaḥ sthāna asthānayoḥ eka ātmaḥ āśraya tve kaḥ anyaḥ dharmaḥ bhedakaḥ iti nānātvam eva kvacid na syāt sarve ākāra viveka avivekinoḥ vā arthayoḥ abhyupagamāt nāma kevalam naḥ iṣṭam syāt na vastu iti uktam tat ime na eka yogakṣemāḥ bhāvāḥ bhinnāḥ eva atas na syāt sāmānya bheda dhīḥ 
PVSV_85,18–85,24	 tat idam artha antaram anāyattam ajanya tvāt asya idam sāmānyam bhedaḥ vā iti vyapadeśam na arhati anya apohe api eṣa tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na tulyaḥ yatas nivṛtteḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt na sthāna asthāna kalpanā na hi anyāpohaḥ nāma kiṃcid tasya ca svabhāva anuṣaṅgiṇyaḥ svabhāva sthiti pracyuti kalpanāḥ na kalpante upaplavaḥ ca sāmānya dhiyaḥ tena api adūṣaṇā 
PVSV_85,25–86,5	 nirviṣayam eva khalu idam mithyā jñānam yat anekatra ekaḥ ākāram iti na tat viṣayasya abhāvāt sthitiḥ asthitiḥ vā yat punar etat uktam tat janakaḥ hi sa tasya svabhāvaḥ yat tasya janakam rūpam tatas anyaḥ janakaḥ katham tatra na brūmaḥ anyasya tat janakam rūpam na asti iti kim tarhi yat ekasya tat janakam tat anyasya naḥ iti anyaḥ api sva rūpeṇa eva 
PVSV_86,6–86,14	 janakaḥ na para rūpeṇa atattvāt te yathāsvam bhinnāḥ ca tat janakāḥ ca svabhāvena iti kaḥ atra virodhaḥ eka rūpa vikalaḥ tat rūpaḥ na syāt na atat kāryaḥ tena eva ca tat kāryam kartavyam iti kaḥ atra nyāyaḥ api ca bhinnā viśeṣāḥ janakāḥ iti uktam na ca te viśeṣāḥ tena ātmanā parasparam anuyanti yat ekasya janakam rūpam anyasya tat na asti na ca tāvatā ajanakāḥ api abhedaḥ api teṣu ced 
PVSV_86,15–86,21	 syāt etat satyam viśeṣāḥ janakāḥ na punar teṣām viśiṣṭam eva rūpam kim tu abhinnam api tat ekaḥ śakti yogāt janakāḥ tena te ajanakāḥ proktāḥ sati api sāmānye rūpe na tena te janakāḥ tasya anapāyāt eka sthitau api kāryaḥ utpatti prasaṅgāt iti uktam prāk kim ca pratibhāsaḥ api bhedakaḥ ananya bhāj 
PVSV_86,22–87,1	 utpatti sthiti vināśaḥ ādi bhedaḥ naḥ iti api śabdāt yaḥ ayam abhinnān sarve arthān manyate tasya ayam artheṣu buddhi pratibhāsa bhedaḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ ca na syāt sati vā tasmin abhede api na kaścid bhedaḥ syāt tathā ca ayam pravibhāgaḥ na syāt eka ātma vat tasmāt ayam bhinna pratibhāsaḥ ādiḥ viśeṣaḥ eva na ca atra aparam abhinnam pratibhāsam paśyāmaḥ yat balena abheda pratītiḥ syāt atas viśeṣaḥ eva saḥ eva arthaḥ tasya vyāvṛttayaḥ apare 
PVSV_87,2–87,9	 tat kāryam kāraṇam ca uktam tat sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate tat tyāgaḥ āpti phalāḥ sarvāḥ puruṣāṇām pravṛttayaḥ yat artha kriyā kāri tat eva vastu iti uktam sa ca viśeṣaḥ eva yat punar etat sāmānyam nāma tat tasya eva aparasmāt bhedaḥ na hi tasya artha tve dṛśyasya rūpa anupalakṣaṇam yuktam tat upalakṣaṇa kṛta tvāt bhedeṣu abhinna pratyayasya api ca yathā abheda aviśeṣe api na sarvam sarve sādhanam tathā bhedaḥ aviśeṣe api na sarvam sarve sādhanam 
PVSV_87,10–87,16	 yat uktam katham tat janaka svabhāvāt bhinnaḥ asya janakaḥ syāt janaka tve vā aviśeṣāt sarvaḥ janakaḥ syāt iti uktam atra yadi aviśeṣaḥ syāt syāt etat iti yathā ca asya svayam abheda vādinaḥ abheda aviśeṣe api na sarvaḥ sarvasya janakaḥ iti tathā bhedaḥ aviśeṣe api bhaviṣyati athavā bhede hi kārakam kiṃcid vastu dharma tayā bhavet abhede tu virudhyete tasya ekasya kriyāḥ akriye 
PVSV_87,17–87,25	 bheda mātra aviśeṣe api sva hetu pratyaya niyamita svabhāva tvāt kecid eva kārakāḥ syuḥ na anye atat svabhāva tvāt iti atra naḥ eva kiṃcid viruddham asti ekatve tu tasya tatra eva tathā kāraka tvam akāraka tvam ca iti vyāhatam etat bhedaḥ api asti akriyātaḥ ced na kuryuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ na vai sarve ākāra avivekam brūmaḥ bhedasya api bhāvāt tasmāt kaścid akārakaḥ api iti tathā api kathaṃcid bhedāt sahakāriṇaḥ akārakāḥ syuḥ paryāyeṇa atha kartṛ tvam sa kim tasya eva vastunaḥ 
PVSV_87,26–88,4	 atha api syāt naḥ eva kaścid akārakaḥ asti sarveṣām sarvatra paryāyeṇa upayogāt śakteḥ vā vipariṇatāyāḥ tat niveśinyāḥ rūpa antareṇa upayogāt saḥ eva khalu ayam paryāyaḥ bhedaḥ āśrayaḥ ekasya katham pariṇāmaḥ vai avyatirekiṇyāḥ viśeṣe vā kathaṃcid ekatva hāniḥ iti yat kiṃcid etat kim ca atyanta bhedaḥ abhedau ca syātām tadvati vastuni anyonyam vā tayoḥ bhedaḥ sadṛśa asadṛśaḥ ātmanoḥ 
PVSV_88,5–88,15	 bhāvāḥ ced abhinnena ātmanā sva ātma bhūtena bhedinaḥ tadvantaḥ syuḥ tat abhinna svabhāvaḥ ātma tvāt bhedasya api kutas parasparam bhedaḥ atha na sa tasya samānaḥ ātmā tathā sati tad ātmanā tena api na yuktam tathā bhavitum tathā abhāve hi atat dharmā syāt na hi ayam pravṛtti nivṛttimān svabhāvaḥ ekaḥ yuktaḥ na sarva ātmanā abhedaḥ eva tayoḥ api bhavet bhedaḥ yadi na hi kvacid asya ekāntikaḥ bhedaḥ abhedaḥ vā vivekena vyavasthāpanāt sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ iti yena ātmanā tayoḥ bhedaḥ sāmānyam iti etat yadi bhedaḥ tad ātmanā 
PVSV_88,16–88,22	 bhedaḥ eva yadi sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ yam ātmānam āśritya sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ iti sthitiḥ tena ātmanā bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva yasmāt tau hi tayoḥ sva ātmānau tau ced vyatirekiṇau vyatirekaḥ eva sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ svabhāva bhedāt svabhāvaḥ hi bhāvaḥ iti tathā ca syāt niḥsāmānya viśeṣa tā bheda sāmānyayoḥ yadvat ghaṭaḥ ādīnām parasparam 
PVSV_88,23–89,1	 vyatireke ca bheda sāmānyayoḥ na bhedaḥ sāmānyāt na sāmānyam bheda vat sambandha abhāvāt parasparam ghaṭaḥ ādi vat iti uktam api ca yam ātmānam puraskṛtya puruṣaḥ ayam pravartate tat sādhya phala vāñchāvān bhedaḥ abhedau tat āśrayau cintyete sva ātmanā bhedaḥ vyāvṛttyā ca samāna tā asti eva vastu na anveti pravṛtti ādi prasaṅgataḥ 
PVSV_89,2–89,6	 sarve eva gauḥ aśvāt bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā iti bhedam abhedam vā pṛcchan viśeṣam eva bhāvasya svabhāvaḥ ākhyam adhikṛtya pravartate saḥ eva hi tathā ucyate dravya tve ādayaḥ tu na tatra śabda coditāḥ yathāsvam pṛthak abhidhānāt arthasya tat avyabhicārāt tatas gatiḥ syāt nirloṭhitam ca etat ācāryeṇa tat ayam gavaḥ ādi śabda 
PVSV_89,7–89,11	 pratyupasthāpitam artham bhinnam abhinnam vā pṛcchan artha antare upakṣepeṇa tatra kim iti dvi mukha buddhiḥ kriyate tasmāt yaḥ asya ātmā ananya sādhāraṇaḥ yam puraskṛtya puruṣaḥ viśiṣṭa artha kriyā arthī pravartate yathā goḥ vā āha dohe ādau na anya sambhavinaḥ arthasya yathā yuddha praveśe saḥ eva svabhāvaḥ 
PVSV_89,12–89,16	 yathāsvam śabda coditaḥ na dravya tve ādi sāmānyam tat codanayā tadā prāptum anabhipreta tvāt gavaḥ ādi samāveśāt tat ātma bhūtānām ca ananvayena tatra anubhaya rūpa tvāt tam eva ca ayam bhāvam prakāraiḥ paryanuyuṅkte tasya bhede dravya tve ādi abhedaḥ asya abādhakaḥ eva sarvatra svabhāvena bhedasya abhyupagamāt 
PVSV_89,17–89,28	 sāmānyasya ca vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇasya svabhāva bhūtasya ca sāmānyasya abhede api uktam sva ātmanā eva abhede tu tat svabhāva nibandhana artha kriyā arthī samam dvayoḥ api pravarteta ekaḥ api tām artha kriyām tat svabhāva tvāt eva karoti tat anyasya api tat tulyam iti saḥ api kim na karoti etena eva yat ahrīkāḥ kim api aślīlam ākulam pralapanti pratikṣiptam tat api ekānta sambhavāt yat ayam ahrīkaḥ syāt uṣṭraḥ dadhi syāt naḥ iti kim api aślīlam ayuktam aheyaḥ upādeyam apariniṣṭhānāt ākulam pralapanti tat api anena nirastam svabhāvena ekānta bhedāt tat anvaye vā sarvasya ubhaya rūpa tve tat viśeṣa nirākṛteḥ coditaḥ dadhi khāda iti kim uṣṭram na abhidhāvati 
PVSV_90,1–90,7	 tathā hi uṣṭraḥ api syāt dadhi na api saḥ eva uṣṭraḥ ye na anyaḥ api syāt uṣṭraḥ tathā dadhi api syāt uṣṭraḥ na api tat eva dadhi yena anyat api syāt dadhi tat anayoḥ ekasya api kasyacid tat rūpa abhāvasya abhāvāt svarūpasya vā atat bhāvinaḥ sva niyatasya abhāvāt na kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti dadhi khāda iti coditaḥ uṣṭram api khādet atha asti atiśayaḥ kaścid yena bhedena vartate saḥ eva dadhi saḥ anyatra na asti iti anubhayam param 
PVSV_90,8–90,15	 atha anayoḥ kaścid atiśayaḥ asti yena ayam tathā coditaḥ kṣīra vikāraḥ eva pravartate na anyatra saḥ eva atiśayaḥ artha kriyā arthi pravṛtti viṣayaḥ dadhi tat phalaḥ upādāna bhāva lakṣita svabhāvam hi vastu dadhi iti sa ca tādṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ anyatra na asti iti pravṛtti abhāvāt arthinaḥ tasmāt tat naḥ ubhaya rūpam iti ekānta vādaḥ api ca sarva ātma tve ca sarveṣām bhinnau syātām na dhī dhvanī bheda saṃhāra vādasya tat abhāvāt asambhavaḥ 
PVSV_90,16–90,20	 saḥ ayam ahrīkaḥ kvacid api ekam ākāram pratiniyatam apaśyan vibhāga abhāvāt bhāvānām katham asaṃsṛṣṭa anyaḥ ākāravatyā buddhi ādhimucyeta arthān abhilapet vā tatas bheda agrahāt tat saṃhāra vādaḥ na syāt syāt uṣṭraḥ dadhi syāt naḥ iti atha punar asaṃsṛṣṭau ākārau pratipadya saṃharet eka rūpa saṃsargiṇyāḥ buddheḥ 
PVSV_90,21–90,25	 kvacid pratiniyamāt tat pratibhāsa bheda kṛtaḥ eva tayoḥ rūpayoḥ svabhāva bhedaḥ api syāt ekaḥ aneka vyavasthiteḥ pratibhāsa viṣaya tvāt tathā ca naḥ ekaḥ tat ubhaya rūpaḥ syāt iti mithyā vādaḥ eṣaḥ sthitam etat na bhāvānām kaścid svabhāva anvayaḥ asti bheda lakṣaṇam eva tu sāmānyam atha ca prakṛtyā kecid eka jñāna 
PVSV_90,26–91,4	 ādi phalāḥ kecid naḥ iti bhavatu nāma bhāvānām svabhāva bhedaḥ sāmānyam yeṣām tu nirupākhyānām svabhāvaḥ eva na asti tatra katham svabhāva bheda viṣayāḥ śabdāḥ teṣu avaśyam śabda pravṛttyā bhāvyam kathaṃcid avyavasthāpiteṣu vidhi pratiṣedha ayogāt tathā ca sarvatra ayam anvaya vyatirekaḥ āśrayaḥ vyavahāraḥ 
PVSV_91,5–91,9	 na syāt uṣṇa svabhāvaḥ agniḥ na anuṣṇaḥ iti api svabhāva antarasya asataḥ kathaṃcid avyavasthāpanāt sarvathā apratipatteḥ agni svabhāvasya apratipattiḥ iti vyāmūḍham jagat syāt syāt etat na tatra kasyacid asataḥ niṣedhaḥ anuṣṇam sat eva artha antaram niṣidhyate iti katham idānīm sat asat nāma na brūmaḥ sarvatra 
PVSV_91,10–91,14	 asat tatra na asti iti deśa kāla dharma niṣedhaḥ eva sarva bhāveṣu kriyate na dharmiṇaḥ tat niṣedhe tat viṣaya śabda pravṛtti abhāvāt anirdiṣṭa viṣayasya nañaḥ aprayogāt saḥ api tarhi deśaḥ ādi pratiṣedhaḥ katham yasmāt na tatra api deśaḥ ādīnām pratiṣedhaḥ na api arthasya sambandhaḥ niṣedhyate iti ced nanu tat niṣedhe 
PVSV_91,15–91,19	 api tulyaḥ doṣaḥ niṣedhāt asati śabdaḥ apravṛttiḥ iti ādi asataḥ vai asya niṣedhe tadvat dharmiṇaḥ api niṣedhaḥ na vai sambandhasya na asti iti niṣedhaḥ kim tarhi na iha ghaṭaḥ naḥ idānīm na evam iti uktau na anena sambandhaḥ asti na etat dharmāḥ vā iti pratītiḥ tathā ca sambandhaḥ niṣiddhaḥ bhavati iti tathā api katham niṣiddhaḥ yāvat 
PVSV_91,20–92,2	 asya sambandhaḥ dharmaḥ vā na asti iti matiḥ na bhavati na ca asyāḥ kathaṃcid bhāve sambhavaḥ abhāveṣu tathā abhāvāt tasmāt sambandha abhāva pratīteḥ na ayam iha iti ādyā pratītiḥ sa tat abhāve na syāt pratītau vā tat abhāvasya yathā prati iti mataḥ tat prabhavāḥ śabdāḥ kena nivāryante saḥ eva hi śabdānām na viṣayaḥ 
PVSV_92,3–92,7	 yaḥ na vitarkāṇām te ced pravṛttāḥ kaḥ vacanasya niṣeddhāḥ na hi avācyam artham buddhayaḥ samīhante sambandhasya tu svarūpeṇa anabhidhānam uktam abhidhāne sambandhi tvena buddhau upasthānāt yathā abhiprāyam apratītiḥ tat ayam pratīyamānaḥ api sambandhi rūpaḥ eva iti svarūpeṇa na abhidhīyate tasmāt 
PVSV_92,8–92,17	 na abhāva vat sambandhe api prasaṅgaḥ api ca ayam abhāvam abhidheyam bruvāṇam prati pratividadhat abruvāṇaḥ katham pratividadhyāt vacane vai asya katham abhāvaḥ anuktaḥ atha abhāvam eva na icchet tena avacanam tat eva idānīm katham abhāvaḥ na asti iti yat punar etat artha niṣedhe anarthaka śabdaḥ aprayogāt nirviṣayasya nañaḥ aprayogaḥ iti atra uttaram vakṣyate tasmāt santi abhāveṣu śabdāḥ teṣu katham svabhāva bhedaḥ iti tatra api rūpa abhāvāt abhāvasya śabdāḥ rūpaḥ abhidhāyinaḥ na āśaṅkyāḥ eva siddhāḥ te vyavacchedasya vācakāḥ 
PVSV_92,18–92,22	 vastu vṛttīnām śabdānām kim rūpam abhidheyam āhosvit bhedaḥ iti śaṅkā syāt abhāvaḥ tu viveka lakṣaṇaḥ eva nimittīkartavyasya kasyacid rūpasya abhāvāt tat bhāve abhāva ayogāt tat bhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt bhāvasya tasmāt ayam eva sa mukhyaḥ vivekaḥ tasya tathā abhāva khyāpinaḥ śabdāḥ kim viveka viṣayāḥ iti asthānam 
PVSV_92,23–93,7	 eva etat āśaṅkāyāḥ tasmāt siddham etat sarve śabdāḥ viveka viṣayāḥ vikalpāḥ ca te ete eka vastu pratiśaraṇāḥ api yathāsvam avadhi bhedaḥ upakalpitaiḥ bhedaiḥ bhinneṣu iva pratibhātsu buddhau vivekeṣu upalayanāt bhinna viṣayāḥ eva tena svabhāvasya eva sādhya sādhana bhāve api na sādhya sādhana saṃsargaḥ tau na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ iti sa ca ayam hetu tvena apadiśyamānaḥ upādhi bheda apekṣaḥ vā svabhāvaḥ kevalaḥ athavā ucyate sādhya siddhi artham nāśe kāryatva sattva vat 
PVSV_93,8–93,16	 apekṣita para vyāpāraḥ hi svabhāva niṣpattau bhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ tena iyam kṛtaka śrutiḥ svabhāva abhidhāyini api paraḥ upādhim enam ākṣipati etena pratyaya bheda bheditve ādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ evam upādhi bheda apekṣaḥ kvacid svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ucyate kvacid anapekṣaḥ sāmānyena yathā anitya tvaḥ eva sattvam kvacid svabhāva bhūta dharma viśeṣa parigraheṇa yathā tatra eva utpattiḥ anayā diśāḥ anye api svabhāva hetu pravibhāgāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ sattā svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ced na sattā sādhyate katham ananvayaḥ hi bhedānām vyāhataḥ hetu sādhyayoḥ 
PVSV_93,17–94,2	 yadi sattvam anitya tve anyatra vā hetuḥ syāt sādhyam api kasmāt naḥ iṣyate tat kila evam prasādhyamānam viśeṣībhavati na ca viśeṣaḥ sādhāyitum śakyate ananvayāt yathā āha pramāṇa viśeṣayā ajñānāt iti saḥ ayam viśeṣaḥ na sādhyaḥ eva vyāhanyate kim tarhi hetau api tulya doṣa tvāt na hi hetuḥ ananvayaḥ siddheḥ aṅgam tatas saṃśayāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt bhāvaḥ upādāna mātre tu sādhye sāmānya dharmiṇi na kaścid arthaḥ siddhaḥ syāt aniṣiddham ca tādṛśam 
PVSV_94,3–94,10	 na sarvathā sattā sādhane viśeṣaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavati bhāva mātra viśeṣaṇaḥ asti kaścid dharmī iti prasādhayataḥ anirdiṣṭa svabhāva viśeṣasya kasyacid sattā mātre virodha abhāvāt na iha sattā sādhana pratiṣedhaḥ kim tu sa tathā asti kaścid iti kaṃcana asya bhedam aparāmṛśan bruvāṇaḥ kam sva artham puṣṇāti tasmāt anena upātta bhedaḥ eva sādhyaḥ upātta bhede sādhye asmin bhavat hetuḥ ananvayaḥ sattāyām tena sādhyāyām viśeṣaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavet 
PVSV_94,11–94,15	 sa hi dharmī pradhāna lakṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ nityaḥ sukhaḥ ādi ātmakaḥ anyaḥ vā iti yathā kathaṃcid api viśeṣitaḥ tat svabhāvaḥ prasādhitaḥ bhavati sa ca tathā na anveti yat api sattā mātram anveti na tena siddhena kiṃcid nanu evam agni ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ tatra api na agni sattā mātre kaścid vivādaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ ādhāra viśeṣasya tu abhimatasya 
PVSV_94,16–94,20	 ananvayāt asiddhiḥ na vai saḥ ādhāraḥ tam viśeṣīkaroti tat ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt iti uktam vakṣyate ca tasmāt tatra sāmānyam eva sādhyate tat ayoga vyavacchedena na tathā iha api kvacid sattāyāḥ sādhanam pradhānaḥ ādi śabda vācyasya eva arthasya kvacid abhāvāt nirviśeṣaṇāḥ eva sā katham abhāvaḥ 
PVSV_94,21–94,25	 jñeyaḥ abhidheya prameya tvaiḥ saḥ api siddhaḥ eva tat kim idānīm jñeyam asti iti siddhiḥ astu tathā api kim siddham syāt anyatra tu tat eva agni sāmānyam tatra asiddham iti sādhyate nanu tatra api tat ayoga virahiṇā sāmānyena anvayaḥ na siddhaḥ eva na vai kaścid tathā abhūtena anvayam karoti pratipādayatā hi param dhūmaḥ 
PVSV_94,26–95,3	 agni na antarīyakaḥ darśanīyaḥ yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti sa tathā agni mātreṇa vyāptaḥ siddhaḥ yatra eva svayam dṛśyate tatra eva agni buddhim janayati tatra ca sādhya nirdeśena na kiṃcid tatra darśana sambandhaḥ ākhyāna mātrāt iṣṭa siddheḥ tat anirdeśe ca katham tat viśiṣṭena anvayaḥ tat ayam agninā avinā bhāvī 
PVSV_95,4–95,12	 siddhaḥ arthāt eva agneḥ tat pradeśa ayogam vyavacchinatti iti sa tathā sādhyaḥ ucyate na punar tathā asya upanyāsa pūrvakaḥ anvayaḥ sādhyaḥ ukteḥ iha anaṅga tvāt tat pūrvaka tve vā kaḥ pratijñām sādhanāt apākaroti tathā ca āha liṅgasya avyabhicāraḥ tu dharmeṇa anyatra darśyate tatra prasiddham tat yuktam dharmiṇam gamayiṣyati tasmāt na agni ādi sādhana vat sattā sādhanam api anavadyam iti aparāmṛṣṭa tat bhede vastu mātre tu sādhane tat mā atra vyāpinaḥ sādhyasya anvayaḥ na vihanyate 
PVSV_95,13–95,18	 sādhane punar sattve svabhāva viśeṣa aparigraheṇa vastu mātra vyāpini sādhya dharme na anvaya vyāghātaḥ na hi tatra avaśyam viśeṣa parigrahaḥ kāryaḥ san mātre āśraye api sādhana sāmarthyāt na sādhya tve vaiphalyāt api ca na asiddhe bhāva dharmaḥ asti vyabhicāri ubhayaḥ āśrayaḥ dharmaḥ viruddhaḥ abhāvasya sā sattā sādhyate katham 
PVSV_95,19–96,3	 sattāyām hi sādhyāyām sarvaḥ tat hetuḥ na trayīm doṣa jātim atipatati asiddhim vyabhicāram virodham ca tatra yadi bhāva dharmaḥ hetuḥ ucyate sa katham asiddha sattāke syāt yaḥ hi bhāva dharmam tatra icchati sa katham bhāvam na icchet svabhāvaḥ eva hi kayācid apekṣayā dharmaḥ iti vyatirekī iva dharmiṇaḥ 
PVSV_96,4–96,8	 nirdiśyate na hi dharma dharmi vācinoḥ śabdayoḥ vācye kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti iti uktam etat atha punar ubhaya dharmam brūyāt anāśrita vastunaḥ aparyudāsena vyatireka mātrasya abhāve api avirodhāt yathā na bhavati mūrtaḥ iti amūrta tvam nirupākhye api syāt nirupākhyasya abhāvāt na pratiṣedha viṣaya tā iti ced tat kim 
PVSV_96,9–96,13	 idānīm vidhi viṣayaḥ astu tat api naḥ iti ced katham idānīm na pratiṣedha viṣayaḥ vidhi nivṛtti rūpa tvāt pratiṣedhasya tat etat vyavaccheda mātram dvayoḥ api sambhavat vipakṣa pracāra śaṅkā vyavacchedena labhyam gamaka tvam katham ātmasāt kuryāt sa ca svayam sva vācaḥ ubhaya dharma tām bruvāṇaḥ sataḥ 
PVSV_96,14–96,18	 anyatra api asya vṛttim bhāṣate sattāyām ca avyabhicāram iti katham naḥ unmattaḥ abhāva dharmam tu bhāva mā atra vyāpinaḥ arthasya vyavacchedam hetum sattāyām vadataḥ asya viruddhaḥ hetuḥ syāt tasya bhāve kvacid asambhavāt abhāve ca bhāva vyavacchedasya bhāvāt tat ayam tri prakāraḥ api dharmaḥ sattā 
PVSV_96,19–96,23	 sādhane na hetu lakṣaṇa bhāj na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt na sattā sādhyate sādhana tve punar asyāḥ sāmānyena tat mā atra vyāpini vastu dharme siddha sattāke dharmiṇi na asiddhiḥ tena ca sādhya dharmeṇa vyāptiḥ yadi kathaṃcid niścīyate na virodha vyabhicārau iti na ayam prasaṅgaḥ aniścitāyām tu vyāptau dharmi 
PVSV_96,24–97,7	 samāśraye vā tat svabhāvatayā gamakaḥ na kaścid gamakaḥ atas eva sva dharmeṇa vyāptaḥ siddhaḥ svabhāvaḥ gamakaḥ vācyaḥ na hi prakāśa tayā prakāśayan pradīpaḥ tat rūpa apratipattau svām artha kriyām karoti vyāpakaḥ tasya niścitaḥ gamyaḥ svabhāvaḥ tat dharma niścayāt eva niścitaḥ vyāpaka tvena tasya dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ gamyaḥ tasya ayam nivṛttau vā nivartakaḥ 
PVSV_97,8–97,13	 tasya vyāpyasya dharmasya ayam nivartakaḥ vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ svayam nirvartamānaḥ evam hi ayam asya vyāpakaḥ siddhaḥ bhavati yadi asya abhāve na bhavet tat anena dvividhasya api sādhana prayogasya gamaka tā lakṣaṇam uktam veditavyam dvividhaḥ hi prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca yathā āhuḥ eke anvayī vyatirekī ca iti na anayoḥ vastutas kaścid bhedaḥ anyatra 
PVSV_97,14–97,19	 prayoga bhedāt sādharmyeṇa api hi prayoge arthāt vaidharmya gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhyena hetoḥ anvaya abhāvāt tathā vaidharmye api anvaya gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvasya sandehāt iti vistareṇa vakṣyāmaḥ anitya tve yathā kāryam akāryam vā avināśini anena udāharaṇam anayoḥ darśayati tatra anvayī yat kiṃcid kṛtakam 
PVSV_97,20–97,25	 tat sarvam anityam yathā ghaṭaḥ ādayaḥ śabdaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ iti kṛtaka tvasya api anitya tvena vyāptim pradarśya śabdaḥ yaḥ kṛtaka tve kathite sāmarthyāt eva anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti tasmāt na avaśyam iha pakṣa nirdeśaḥ iti ayam anvayinaḥ prayogaḥ vyatireke api na anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvam bhavati śabdaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ iti siddha tat svabhāvatayā tat abhāve na bhavataḥ 
PVSV_97,26–98,6	 kṛtaka tvasya śabde ca bhāva khyātau tadātmanaḥ sataḥ bhāvaḥ iti sāmarthyāt siddheḥ pūrvavān na pratijñā vacanam anvayaḥ tu arthāpattyā siddhaḥ na hi atadātma niyatasya tat nivṛttau nivṛttiḥ tasmāt tat niyamam prasādhya nivṛttiḥ vaktavyā sā ced sidhyati tad ātma niyamam arthāt sūcayati iti siddhaḥ anvayaḥ katham idānīm kṛtakaḥ avaśyam anityaḥ iti pratyetavyaḥ yena evam ucyate yasmāt ahetu tvāt vināśasya svabhāvāt anubandhitā 
PVSV_98,7–98,13	 na hi bhāvāḥ vinaśyantaḥ tat bhāve hetum apekṣante sva hetoḥ eva vinaśvarāṇām bhāvāt tasmāt yaḥ kaścid kṛtakaḥ sa prakṛtyāḥ eva naśvaraḥ tathā hi sa apekṣāṇām hi bhāvānām na avaśyaṃbhāvitā īkṣyate nirapekṣaḥ bhāvaḥ vināśe sa apekṣa tve hi ghaṭaḥ ādīnām keṣāṃcid nityatā api syāt yena bāhulye api hi tat hetoḥ bhavet kvacid asambhavaḥ 
PVSV_98,14–98,24	 yadi api bahulam vināśa kāraṇāni santi teṣām api sva pratyaya adhīna saṃnidhi tvāt na avaśyam saṃnidhānam iti kaścid na vinaśyet api na hi avaśyam hetavaḥ phalavantaḥ vaikalya pratibandha sambhavāt etena vyabhicāri tvam uktam kārya avyavasthiteḥ sarveṣām nāśa hetūnām hetumat nāśa vādinām iti antaraślokaḥ tat ayam bhāvaḥ anapekṣaḥ tat bhāvam prati tat bhāva niyataḥ asambhavat pratibandhāḥ iva kāraṇa sāmagrī sakalā kāryaḥ utpādane nanu anapekṣāṇām api keṣāṃcid kvacid na avaśyam tat bhāvaḥ bhūmi bījaḥ udaka sāmagryām api kadācid aṅkura anutpatteḥ na tatra api santāna pariṇāma apekṣa tvāt na evam bhāvasya kācid 
PVSV_98,25–99,3	 apekṣā tatra api antyā kāraṇa sāmagrī yā avyavahitā kāryaḥ utpatteḥ sā phalavatī eva saḥ eva ca tatra aṅkura hetuḥ anyaḥ tu pūrvaḥ pariṇāmaḥ tat arthaḥ eva na ca tām tatra kaścid pratibandhum samarthaḥ ekatra bhāve vikāra anutpatteḥ utpattau vai ekatva hāneḥ tad ātmanaḥ ca apracyutasya tat utpādanam prati vaiguṇyam kāraṇasya 
PVSV_99,4–99,8	 akurvāṇasya pratibandha hetoḥ apratibandhaka tvāt nanu yava bījaḥ ādayaḥ api śāli aṅkure janye na sa apekṣāḥ tat utpatti pratyayānām kadācid tatra api saṃnidhānāt katham na sa apekṣāḥ yāvatā saḥ eva eṣām svabhāvaḥ na asti yaḥ tat utpādanaḥ śāli bījasya iti tat svabhāva apekṣāḥ evam tarhi kṛtakānām api keṣāṃcid 
PVSV_99,9–99,13	 satām vā saḥ eva svabhāvaḥ na asti yaḥ vinaśvaraḥ tasmāt tat svabhāva apekṣa tvāt na vinaśvarāḥ śāli bījaḥ ādīnām api sa svabhāvaḥ sva hetoḥ iti yaḥ na tat hetuḥ saḥ atat svabhāvaḥ syāt niyata śaktiḥ ca sa hetuḥ sva rūpeṇa pratītaḥ eva na ca svabhāva niyamaḥ arthānām ākasmikaḥ yuktaḥ anapekṣasya deśa kāla dravya niyama 
PVSV_99,14–99,18	 ayogāt tathā atra api niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ yatas ime kecid naśvaraḥ ātmanaḥ jātā na ca atra kaścid niyāmakaḥ svabhāvasya asti sarva janminām vināśa siddheḥ janmi svabhāvaḥ na āśī iti ced na vai janma nāśi svabhāvasya hetuḥ na ca ahetoḥ svabhāva niyamaḥ tasmāt na atra kaścid hetoḥ svabhāva pravibhāgaḥ tat abhāvāt 
PVSV_99,19–99,23	 phalasya api na asti iti asamānam sā iyam nirapekṣatā vināśasya kvacid kadācid ca bhāva virodhinī tat abhāvam svabhāvena sādhayati yaḥ hi svabhāvaḥ nirapekṣaḥ sa yadi kadācid bhavet kvacid vā tat kāla dravya apekṣaḥ iti nirapekṣaḥ eva na syāt iti uktam sa tarhi naśvaraḥ svabhāvaḥ nirapekṣaḥ iti ahetukaḥ 
PVSV_99,24–99,28	 syāt na ahetukaḥ sattā hetoḥ eva bhāvāt tathā utpatteḥ sataḥ hi bhavataḥ tādṛśasya eva bhāvāt na avaśyam sataḥ kutaścid bhāvaḥ iti ced ākasmikī tarhi sattā iti na iyam kasyacid kadācid kvacid viramet tat hi kiṃcid upalīyeta na vā yasya yatra kiṃcid pratibaddham apratibaddham vā sā iyam sattā apratibandhinī ced 
PVSV_100,1–100,5	 niyamavatī na syāt tasmāt naḥ iyam ākasmikī kvacid katham tarhi idānīm ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ uktaḥ jātasya tat bhāve anyaḥ anapekṣaṇāt uktam ca atra na vināśaḥ nāma anyaḥ eva kaścid bhāvāt svabhāvaḥ eva hi nāśaḥ saḥ eva hi eka kṣaṇa sthāyī jātaḥ iti tam asya mandāḥ svabhāvam ūrdhvam vyavasyanti na prāk darśane api 
PVSV_100,6–100,11	 pāṭava abhāvāt iti tat vaśena paścāt vyavasthāpyate vikāra darśanena iva viṣam ajñaiḥ tat ayam sattā vyatirekeṇa na anyat kiṃcid vināśaḥ apekṣate iti tat vyāpī katham punar etat gamyate nirapekṣaḥ vināśaḥ iti asāmarthyāt ca tat hetoḥ abhāva kāriṇaḥ kriyā pratiṣedhāt ca iti ca śabdāt katham asāmarthyam 
PVSV_100,12–100,22	 siddhe hi bhāve kārakaḥ na tam karoti na api anya kriyāyām tasya kiṃcid iti tat atat rūpa akaraṇāt ca akiṃcitkaraḥ na apekṣyate iti katham kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ vināśaḥ iti hi te bhāva abhāvam manyante tat ayam vināśa hetuḥ abhāvam karoti iti prāptam tatra yadi abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid kāryaḥ syāt svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva bhāvaḥ iti na abhāvaḥ syāt tasmāt abhāvam karoti iti bhāvam na karoti iti kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ asya kṛtaḥ syāt tathā api ayam akiṃcitkaraḥ kim iti apekṣyate iti siddhāḥ vināśam prati anapekṣayā bhāvasya tasmāt bhavati eṣa svabhāvataḥ yatra nāma bhavati asmāt anyatra api svabhāvataḥ 
PVSV_100,23–101,4	 saḥ ayam kvacid bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ anapekṣa tvāt svabhāvataḥ eva bhavati tathā anyatra api svabhāva bhāvī viśeṣa abhāvāt iti yā kācid bhāva viṣayāḥ dvidhā eva anumitiḥ tatas sva sādhye kārya bhāvābhyām sambandha niyamāt tayoḥ tasmāt dvi prakārāḥ eva vastu viṣaya anumitiḥ kārya liṅgā svabhāva liṅgā ca yathāsvam vyāpini sādhye tayoḥ eva pratibandhāt liṅgayoḥ liṅgini yathā uktam prāk pravṛtteḥ buddhi pūrva tvāt tat bhāva anupalambhane pravartitavyam naḥ iti uktaḥ anupalabdheḥ pramāṇatā 
PVSV_101,5–101,9	 tṛtīyaḥ tu hetuḥ anupalabdhiḥ aviśeṣeṇa kvacid arthe gamakaḥ iti ucyate san niścaya śabda vyavahāra pratiṣedhe hi sarvāḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ liṅgam san niścayāt hi śabda vyavahārāḥ pravartante te pravṛttiḥ iti uktāḥ tathā hi anupalabdhiḥ eva asattvam iti uktam prāk tat ca pratipattṛ vaśāt na vastu vaśāt tāvat hi 
PVSV_101,10–101,14	 sa bhāvaḥ asya na asti yāvat atra apratipattiḥ satā api te na tat artha akaraṇāt vastutas tu anupalabhyamānaḥ na san na asan satām api svabhāvaḥ ādi viprakarṣāt kadācid anupalambhāt tasya asatsu api tulya tvāt tat etat pratipattuḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt nivṛttam sattvam anupalabdhi lakṣaṇam sva nimittān śabda vyavahārān nivartayati 
PVSV_101,15–101,22	 tena yāḥ api iyam anupalabdhiḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptānām vastutas api asattva rūpāḥ apravṛtti yogya tvāt tasyāḥ api etat tulyam prāmāṇyam atra viṣaye asat niścaya phalāḥ api sā asattāyām api iyam pramāṇam eva na hi asti sambhavaḥ yat upalabdhi yogyaḥ sakaleṣu anyeṣu kāraṇeṣu san naḥ upalabhyeta na punar pūrvā asattā sādhānī yasmāt śāstra adhikāra asambaddhāḥ bahavaḥ arthāḥ atīndriyāḥ aliṅgāḥ ca katham teṣām abhāvaḥ anupalabdhitaḥ 
PVSV_101,23–102,4	 saḥ ayam asattām sādhayan anupalabdhi mātreṇa sarva arthānām pramāṇa traya nivṛttyā sādhayet tatra na śāstra nivṛttiḥ abhāva sādhanī tasya kvacid anadhikāre apravṛtteḥ śāstram hi pravartamānam kaṃcid puruṣa artha sādhanam upāyam āśritya pravartate anyathā abaddha pralāpasya aprāmāṇyāt tatra ca prakaraṇe 
PVSV_102,5–102,9	 bahavaḥ arthāḥ na avaśyam nirdeśyāḥ yathā pratyātma niyatāḥ kāścana puruṣāṇām cetaḥ vṛttayaḥ aniyata nimitta bhāvinyaḥ deśa kāla vyavahitāḥ vā prakaraṇa anupayoginaḥ dravya viśeṣāḥ na tān śāstram viṣayīkaroti na ca tathā viprakṛṣṭeṣu sva sāmarthya upadhānau jñānaḥ utpādana śaktiḥ asti na ca avaśyam eṣām kāryaḥ upalambhaḥ 
PVSV_102,10–102,19	 yena anumīyeran na ca te pramāṇa traya nivṛttau api na santi iti śakyante vyavasātum tasmāt na sarve anupalabdhiḥ sādhanī nivṛtti niścayasya tat iyam sat asat niścaya phalāḥ naḥ iti syāt vā apramāṇa tā na eva vā iyam anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇam vyavasāya phalatvāt pramāṇānām na hi pravṛtti niṣedhe api iyam niḥśaṅka paricchedam cetaḥ karoti saṃśayāt api kvacid lokasya pravṛtteḥ tathā tve tat niravadyam yadi niścaya pūrvam vyavaharet iti sā iyam apravṛtti phalā proktā pramāṇam api kācid syāt liṅga atiśaya bhāvinī 
PVSV_102,20–103,2	 atra na sarve anupalabdhiḥ apramāṇam pramāṇam api kācid liṅga viśeṣa bhāvinī yathā udāhṛtā prāk yat punar uktam apramāṇam anupalabdhiḥ iti svabhāva jñāpakaḥ ajñānasya ayam nyāya udāhṛtaḥ yasya kasyacid svabhāvaḥ naḥ upalabhyate deśaḥ ādi viprakarṣāt na sa tat anupalambha mātreṇa asat nāma yathoktam prāk yaḥ api 
PVSV_103,3–103,7	 jñāpakasya liṅgasya abhāvāt atīndriyaḥ pratikṣipyate arthaḥ svabhāva viśeṣaḥ vā yathā na asti viraktam cetaḥ devatāḥ viśeṣaḥ vā na asti dāna hiṃsā virati cetanānām abhyudaya hetu tāḥ iti pratyakṣe api arthe phalasya ānantarya abhāvāt atat phala sādharmyāt viparyastaḥ apavadeta api na tāvatā tat abhāvaḥ eva vyavahitānām 
PVSV_103,8–103,15	 api hetoḥ phalānām utpatti darśanāt mūṣika alarka viṣa vikāra vat tat bhāve virodha abhāvāt atra anupalabdhi mātram apramāṇam bhāve kim pramāṇam iti ced atas eva saṃśayaḥ astu bhavet vā pramāṇam iti apratikṣepaḥ tat atra keṣāṃcid arthānām svabhāvānām vā darśana pāṭava abhāvāt kāraṇānām kāryaḥ utpādana niyama abhāvāt ca bhavet jñāpaka asiddhiḥ neyatā tat abhāvaḥ punar paryāyeṇa keṣāṃcid abhivyakteḥ kārye tu kāraka ajñānam abhāvasya eva sādhakam 
PVSV_103,16–103,20	 svabhāva abhāve sādhye tat anupalambhaḥ eva apramāṇam ucyate kāraka anupalambhaḥ tu pramāṇam eva na hi asti sambhavaḥ yat asati kāraṇe kāryam syāt nanu kadācid kāraṇa nāśe api kārya sthitiḥ dṛṣṭāḥ na brūmaḥ kāraṇa sthiti kāla bhāvī kāryam iti hetu rahitā tu bhāvaḥ utpattiḥ na asti iti ucyate na ca tathā sthāyī bhāvaḥ tat upādānaḥ 
PVSV_103,21–103,27	 pāraṃparyeṇa tu santānaḥ upakārāt tat kārya vyapadeśaḥ yadi asya kathaṃcid abhāvaḥ sidhyet tat phalam na asti iti niścīyate svabhāva anupalambhaḥ ca svabhāve arthasya liṅgini svabhāva abhāvaḥ eva liṅgini svabhāva anupalambhaḥ api kaścid pramāṇam eva eva yadi anupalabhyamānaḥ vyāpakaḥ svabhāvaḥ asya siddhiḥ syāt yathā vṛkṣa tvam śiṃśapāyāḥ tat abhāvaḥ pratīyeta hetunā yadi kenacid 
PVSV_104,1–104,7	 yadi asya kāraṇasya svabhāvasya vyāpakasya vā abhāvaḥ kutaścid gamakāt hetoḥ sidhyet saḥ ayam asan eva sva kāryam vyāpyam vā nivartayati tat abhāva asiddhau nivartye api saṃśayāt katham idānīm bhāvasya svayam anupalabdheḥ abhāva siddhiḥ dṛśyasya darśanaḥ abhāva kāraṇa asambhave sati bhāvasya anupalabdhasya bhāva abhāvaḥ pratīyate 
PVSV_104,8–104,14	 bhāvaḥ hi yadi bhavet yathāsvam grāhakeṇa karaṇena upalabhyaḥ eva bhavet sa darśana pratibandhiṣu vyavadhānaḥ ādiṣu asatsu upalabhyaḥ eva anupalabdhaḥ tu asan iti niścīyate tādṛśaḥ sataḥ upalambha avyabhicārāt ayam eva hetuḥ hetu vyāpakayoḥ abhāve api veditavyaḥ viruddhasya ca bhāvasya bhāve tat bhāva bādhanāt tat viruddhaḥ upalabdhau syāt asattāyāḥ viniścayaḥ 
PVSV_104,15–104,19	 yaḥ hi bhāvaḥ yena saha na avatiṣṭhate tat upādānayoḥ anyonya vaiguṇya āśraya tvena ārambha virodhāt tayoḥ viruddhayoḥ ekasya bhāve api anyaḥ abhāva gatiḥ bhavati yathoktam prāk idam anupalabdheḥ na pṛthak vyavasthāpyate tatas eva virodha gateḥ virodhāt ca abhāva sādhanāt bhavatu nāma evaṃvidhāyāḥ anupalabdheḥ abhāva 
PVSV_104,20–104,24	 gatiḥ sā punar katham anumānam katham ca na syāt dṛṣṭānta anapekṣaṇāt na hi asyām kaścid dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti kim na nirupākhyam vyomakusumaḥ ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ tat asat katham avagantavyam yena evam syāt anupalabdheḥ eva iti ced tatra katham adṛṣṭāntikā asattā siddhiḥ sa dṛṣṭānta tve vā anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ 
PVSV_104,25–104,29	 tathā ca apratipattiḥ tasmāt nirupākhya abhāva siddhi vat anyatra api dṛṣṭānta anapekṣaṇāt ananumānam śṛṇvan api devānāṃpriyaḥ na avadhāraṇa paṭuḥ nimittam hi asat śabda vyavahārāṇām upalabhya anupalabdhiḥ sā sva saṃnidhānāt sva nimittān etān sādhayati iti sva nimitta sāmagrī yogya saṃnidhānaḥ sarvaḥ atra 
PVSV_105,1–105,5	 dṛṣṭāntaḥ asattā punar atra anupalabdhiḥ eva atas eva iyam kāraṇāt kārya anumāna lakṣaṇa tvāt svabhāva hetau antar bhavati iti vakṣyāmaḥ sat śabda vyavahāra pratiṣedhe api pramāṇa nivṛttyā nimitta vaikalya abhāvinaḥ aṅkuraḥ ādayaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ na kevalam nirupākhyam nirupākhye api iyam eva pravṛttiḥ niṣidhyate anupalabdhi 
PVSV_105,6–105,10	 lakṣaṇāḥ asattā siddhāḥ eva saḥ ayam mūḍhaḥ nimittam tat abhāvam vā abhyupagamya pravṛtti nivṛttī vilomayan yathā abhyupagamam pratipādyate nirupākhya vat anyaḥ vat vā iti saḥ eva tāvat upalabdhi abhāvaḥ katham siddhaḥ iti ced etat uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ anyatra api anumāne sādhya dharmeṇa vyāptam sādhanam 
PVSV_105,11–105,15	 icchan kim iti dṛṣṭāntena pratyāyyaḥ vyāpya nirdeśāt eva vyāpnuvataḥ siddheḥ niścita arthasya api smṛti arthaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti ced tat itaratra api samānam saḥ ayam anyatra anupalambha mātrāt asat vyavahāram pratipadyamānaḥ api iha vyāmūḍhaḥ iti smāryate atha yat idam na santi pradhānaḥ ādayaḥ anupalabdheḥ 
PVSV_105,16–105,23	 iti tatra katham asat vyavahāra vidhiḥ sat vyavahāra niṣedhaḥ vā katham ca na syāt tat artha pratiṣedhe dharmi vācinaḥ aprayogāt abhidhānasya nirviṣayasya ca pratiṣedhasya ayogāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt anādi vāsanāḥ udbhūta vikalpa pariniṣṭhitaḥ śabdaḥ arthaḥ trividhaḥ dharmaḥ bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ ubhayaḥ āśrayaḥ tasmin bhāva anupādāne sādhye asya anupalambhanam tathā hetuḥ na tasya eva abhāvaḥ śabda prayogataḥ 
PVSV_105,24–106,1	 niveditam etat yathā naḥ ete śabdāḥ sva lakṣaṇa viṣayāḥ anādi vāsanā prabhava vikalpa pratibhāsinam artham viṣaya tvena ātmasāt kurvanti vaktuḥ śrotuḥ ca tat vikalpa bhājaḥ yathāpratibhāsi vastu pratipādana sami iha aprayogāt tat ākāra vikalpa jananāt ca na ca upādāna kārya pratyaya apratibhāsi rūpam śakyam tat viṣaya tvena 
PVSV_106,2–106,6	 adhyavasātum sa tu vikalpaḥ sat asat ubhaya pratyayaḥ āhita vāsanā prabhavaḥ iti tat pratibhāsi ākāra adhyavasāya vaśena ca bhāva abhāvaḥ ubhaya dharmaḥ iti ucyate tat atra dharmiṇi vyavasthitāḥ sat asat tvam cintayanti kim ayam pradhāna śabda pratibhāsi arthaḥ bhāvaḥ upādānaḥ na vā iti tasya bhāva anupādāna tve 
PVSV_106,7–106,14	 sādhye saḥ eva pratyātma vedya tvāt apratikṣepa arhaḥ arthaḥ dharmī na ca saḥ eva arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum asamprāpta niruddhayoḥ api arthayoḥ tasya anapāyāt vastu viparītaḥ ākāra niveśiṣu api tīrtha anantarīya pratyayeṣu bhāvāt parama arthaḥ eka tāna tve śabdānām anibandhanāḥ na syāt pravṛttiḥ artheṣu darśana antara bhediṣu atīta ajātayoḥ vai api na ca syāt anṛta artha tā vācaḥ kasyāścid iti eṣā bauddha artha viṣayā matā 
PVSV_106,15–106,21	 iti saṃgraha ślokau tasya ca yathā samīhita rūpa anupādāna tve sādhye tathā anupalambhaḥ asya dharmaḥ asti iti na sādhana dharma asiddhiḥ na punar atra ayam eva śabda vikalpa pratibhāsi arthaḥ apahnūyate tasya buddhau upasthāpanāya śabda prayogāt tat abhāve tat ayogāt api ca śabdaḥ artha apahnave sādhye dharmaḥ ādhāra nirākṛteḥ na sādhyaḥ samudāyaḥ syāt siddhaḥ dharmaḥ ca kevalaḥ 
PVSV_106,23–106,30	 yadi hi śabdaḥ arthaḥ eva apohyeta pradhāna śabda vācyasya dharmiṇaḥ eva nirākaraṇāt nirādhāraḥ sādhya dharmaḥ syāt tat ayam ādhāra vyavaccheda anapekṣaḥ na vivādaḥ āśrayaḥ iti naḥ upanyasanīyaḥ eva syāt kim ca sat asat pakṣa bhedena śabdaḥ artha anapavādibhiḥ vastu eva cintyate hi atra pratibaddhaḥ phalaḥ udayaḥ artha kriyā samarthasya vicāraiḥ kim tat arthinām ṣaṇḍhasya rūpa vairūpye kāminyāḥ kim parīkṣayā 
PVSV_107,1–107,5	 na hi śabdaḥ arthaḥ asan san vā kaṃcid puruṣa artham uparuṇaddhi samādadhāti vā yathā abhiniveśam atattvāt yathā atattvam ca asamīhita tvāt tat ayam pravartamānaḥ sarvadā sat asat cintāyām avadhīrita vikalpa pratibhāsaḥ vastu eva adhiṣṭhānīkaroti yatra ayam puruṣa arthaḥ pratibaddhaḥ yathā agnau śīta pratīkāraḥ ādiḥ na hi 
PVSV_107,6–107,12	 atra śabdaḥ arthaḥ samarthaḥ tat anubhavaḥ āptau api tat abhāvāt tat ayam artha kriyā arthī tat asamartham prati dattā anuyogaḥ bhavitum na yuktaḥ na hi vṛṣasyantī ṣaṇḍhasya rūpa vairūpya parīkṣāyām avadhat te yat punar etat uktam kalpitasya anupalabdhiḥ dharmaḥ iti tasya kaḥ arthaḥ śabda arthaḥ kalpanā jñāna viṣaya tvena kalpitaḥ dharmaḥ vastu āśraya asiddhiḥ asya uktaḥ nyāya vādinā 
PVSV_107,13–107,21	 kalpanā viṣaya tvāt śabdaḥ arthaḥ eva kalpitaḥ tasya vastu āśraya anupalambhaḥ dharmaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ yat uktam na pramāṇa traya nivṛttau api bhāva abhāva siddhiḥ iti tat mā bhūt anyaḥ pramāṇa anivṛttau nivṛttiḥ tayoḥ asakala viṣaya tvāt āgamaḥ punar na kiṃcid na vyāpnoti tat nivṛttiḥ katham na gamikāḥ iti uktam atra naḥ āgameṣu sarve arthāḥ upanibadhyante aprakaraṇaḥ āpanna tvāt iti api ca na antarīyaka tā abhāvāt śabdānām vastubhiḥ saha na artha siddhiḥ tatas te hi vaktṛ abhiprāya sūcakāḥ 
PVSV_107,22–108,1	 na hi śabdāḥ yathābhāvam vartante yatas tebhyaḥ artha prakṛtiḥ niścīyeta te hi vaktuḥ vivakṣāḥ vṛttayaḥ iti tat na antarīyakāḥ tām eva gamayeyuḥ na ca puruṣaḥ icchāḥ sarvāḥ yathārtha bhāvinyaḥ na ca tat apratibaddha svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ anyam gamayati yat tarhi idam āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumāna tā iti āgamasya 
PVSV_108,2–108,8	 prāmāṇyam anumāna tvam uktam tat katham na ayam puruṣaḥ anāśritya āgama āsitum samarthaḥ atyakṣa phalānām keṣāṃcid pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ mahā anuśaṃsā pāpa śravaṇāt tat bhāve virodha adarśanāt ca tat sati pravartitavye varam evam pravṛttaḥ iti parīkṣayā prāmāṇyam āha tat ca sambaddha anuguṇaḥ upāyam puruṣa artha abhidhāyakam parīkṣā adhikṛtam vākyam atas anadhikṛtam param 
PVSV_108,9–108,13	 sambaddhaḥ vākyānām ekaḥ arthaḥ upasaṃhāraḥ upakāraḥ na daśa dāḍimaḥ ādi vākyānām iva anupasaṃhāraḥ eva anyathā vaktuḥ vaiguṇyam udbhāvayet aśakyaḥ upāya phalāni ca śāstrāṇi phala arthī naḥ ādriyeta vicārayitum apuruṣa artha phalāni ca viṣa śamanāya takṣaka phaṇa ratna alaṃkāraḥ upadeśa vat kāka danta parīkṣā vat ca tat viparyayeṇa 
PVSV_108,14–108,19	 upasaṃhāra vat śakyaḥ upāyam puruṣa arthaḥ abhidhāyi ca śāstram parīkṣyeta anyatra avadhānasya eva ayukta tvāt tat yadi na parīkṣāyām visaṃvāda bhāj pravartamānaḥ śobheta kaḥ punar asya avisaṃvādaḥ pratyakṣeṇa anumānena dvividhena api abādhakam dṛṣṭaḥ adṛṣṭa arthayoḥ asya avisaṃvādaḥ tat arthayoḥ
