PVSV_108,20–108,24	 pratyakṣeṇa abādhanam pratyakṣa abhimatānām arthānām tathā abhāvaḥ yathā nīlaḥ ādi sukha duḥkha nimittaḥ upalakṣaṇa rāgaḥ ādi buddhīnām atathā abhimatānām ca apratyakṣatā yathā śabdaḥ ādi rūpa saṃniveśinām sukhaḥ ādīnām dravya karma sāmānya saṃyogaḥ ādīnām ca tathā anāgamaḥ apekṣa anumāna viṣaya abhimatānām tathā abhāvaḥ 
PVSV_108,25–109,6	 yathā catūrṇām ārya satyānām ananumeyānām tathā abhāvaḥ yathā ātmaḥ ādīnām āgama apekṣa anumāne api yathā rāgaḥ ādi rūpam tat prabhavam ca adharmam abhyupagamya tat prahāṇāya snāna agnihotraḥ ādeḥ anupadeśaḥ saḥ iyam śakya pariccheda aśeṣa viṣaya viśuddhiḥ avisaṃvādaḥ āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumāna tā buddheḥ agatyāḥ abhihitā parokṣe api asya gocare 
PVSV_109,7–109,14	 tasya ca asya evaṃbhūtasya āpta bhūtasya avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt adṛṣṭa vyabhicārasya pratyakṣa anumānaḥ āgamye api arthe pratipatteḥ tat āśraya tvāt tat anye pratipatti vat avisaṃvādaḥ anumīyate tatas śabda prabhavāḥ api satī na śābda vat abhiprāyam nivedayati eva iti artha avisaṃvādāt anumānam api athavā anyathā āpta vādasya avisaṃvādāt anumāna tvam ucyate heyaḥ upādeya tattvasya saḥ upāyasya prasiddhitaḥ pradhāna arthaḥ avisaṃvādāt anumānam paratra vā 
PVSV_109,15–109,19	 heyaḥ upādeya tat upāyānām tat upadiṣṭānām avaiparītyam avisaṃvādaḥ yathā catūrṇām ārya satyānām vakṣyamāṇa nītyā tasya asya puruṣa arthaḥ upayoginaḥ abhiyoga arthasya avisaṃvādāt viṣaya antare api tathā tva upagamaḥ na vipralambhāya anuparodhāt niṣprayojana vitatha abhidhāna vaiphalyāt ca vaktuḥ tat etat agatyāḥ ubhayathā 
PVSV_109,20–110,2	 api anumāna tvam āgamasya upavarṇitam varam āgamāt pravṛttau evam pravṛttiḥ iti na khalu evam anumānam anapāyam anāntarīyaka tvāt artheṣu śabdānām iti niveditam etat puruṣa atiśaya apekṣam yathārtham apare viduḥ yathārtha darśane ādi guṇa yuktaḥ puruṣaḥ āptaḥ tat praṇayanam avisaṃvādaḥ iti anye iṣṭaḥ ayam arthaḥ śakyeta jñātum saḥ atiśayaḥ yadi 
PVSV_110,3–110,10	 sarve eva āgamam anāgamam vā pravṛtti kāmaḥ anveṣate prekṣā pūrva kārī na vyasanena api nāma anuṣṭheyam atas jñātvā pravṛttaḥ arthavān syām iti sa śakya darśana avisaṃvāda pratyayena anyatra api pravartate evaṃprāya tvāt loka vyavahārasya puruṣa parīkṣayā tu pravṛttau apravṛttiḥ eva tasya tathābhūtasya jñātum aśakya tvāt na aniṣṭeḥ tādṛśām avitathaḥ abhidhānāt tathā hi ayam evam na vā iti anyaḥ doṣa anirdoṣa tā api vā durlabha tvāt pramāṇānām durbodhāḥ iti apare viduḥ 
PVSV_110,11–110,18	 ca etasyebhyaḥ hi guṇa doṣebhyaḥ puruṣāḥ samyak mithyā pravṛttaḥ te ca atīndriyāḥ sva prabhava kāya vāc vyavahāra anumeyāḥ syuḥ vyavahārāḥ ca prāyaśas buddhi pūrvam anyathā api kartum śakyante puruṣaḥ icchā vṛtti tvāt teṣām ca citra abhisandhi tvāt tat ayam liṅga saṃkarāt katham aniścinvan pratipadyeta atha kim naḥ eva sa tādṛśaḥ puruṣaḥ asti yaḥ nirdoṣaḥ sarveṣām sa vipakṣa tvāt nirhrāsa atiśaya śritām saḥ ātmībhāvāt tat abhyāsāt dhīyeran āśravāḥ kvacid 
PVSV_110,19–110,28	 sa tu prahīṇaḥ āśravaḥ durjñānaḥ doṣāḥ hi nirhrāsa atiśaya dharmaṇaḥ vipakṣa abhibhavaḥ utkarṣa apakarṣam sādhayanti jvālā ādi vat te hi vikalpa prabhavāḥ sati api upādāne kasyacid manaḥ guṇasya abhyāsāt apakarṣiṇaḥ tat pāṭave niranvaya vināśa dharmāṇaḥ syuḥ jvālā ādi vat eva tena syāt api nirdoṣaḥ katham nirdoṣaḥ nāma yāvatā doṣa vipakṣa sa ātma tve api doṣa sa ātmanaḥ vipakṣaḥ utpatti vat yathā pratyayam doṣaḥ utpattiḥ api na ayam doṣaḥ yasmāt nirupadrava bhūta artha svabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ na bādhā yatnavat tve api buddheḥ tat pakṣa pātataḥ 
PVSV_111,1–111,5	 na hi svabhāvaḥ ayatnena vinivartayitum śakyaḥ śrotriya kāpālika ghṛṇā vat yatnaḥ ca prāpya nivartyayoḥ svabhāvayoḥ guṇa doṣa darśanena kriyeta tat ca vipakṣa sa ātmanaḥ puruṣasya doṣeṣu na sambhavati tasya nirupadrava tvāt aśeṣa doṣa hāneḥ paryavasthāna janma pratibaddha duḥkha vivekāt praśama sukha 
PVSV_111,6–111,14	 rasasya anudvejanāt ca abhūta artham khalu api upādāna bala bhāvi santānasya viparyayaḥ upādānāt na syāt na tu bhūta artham vastu balaḥ utpatteḥ abhūta arthāḥ ca doṣāḥ na pratipakṣa sātmya bādhinaḥ tasmāt na punar doṣaḥ utpattiḥ yatne api buddheḥ guṇa pakṣa pātena pratipakṣaḥ eva yatnaḥ ādhānāt parīkṣāvataḥ viśeṣeṇa aduṣṭa ātmanaḥ kaḥ punar eṣām doṣāṇām prabhavaḥ yat pratipakṣa abhyāsāt prahīyante sarvāsām doṣa jātīnām jātiḥ sat kāya darśanāt sā avidyā tatra tat snehaḥ tasmāt dveṣaḥ ādi sambhavaḥ 
PVSV_111,15–111,22	 na hi na aham na mama iti paśyatam parigraham antareṇa kvacid snehaḥ na ca ananurāgiṇaḥ kvacid dveṣaḥ ātmaḥ ātmīya anuparodhinī uparodha pratighātini ca tat abhāvāt tasmāt samāna jātīya abhyāsa jam ātma darśanam ātmīya graham prasūte tau ca tat sneham sa ca dveṣaḥ ādīni iti sat kāya darśana jāḥ sarve doṣāḥ tat eva ca ajñānam iti ucyate mohaḥ nidānam doṣāṇām atas eva abhidhīyate satkāya dṛṣṭiḥ anyatra tat prahāṇe prahāṇataḥ 
PVSV_111,23–112,2	 moham doṣa nidānam āhuḥ amūḍhasya doṣa anutpatteḥ punar anyatra sat kāya dṛṣṭim tat ca etat pradhāna nirdeśe sati syāt aneka janmanām doṣāṇām ekaḥ utpatti virodhāt na ca dvayoḥ prādhānye ekaika nirdeśaḥ para bhāga bhāj ubhayathā api ekasya nirdeśe na virodhaḥ prādhānyam punar tat upādāna tvena 
PVSV_112,3–112,9	 tat prahāṇe doṣāṇām prahāṇāt tasmāt sambhavati satkāya darśana janmanām doṣāṇām tat pratipakṣa nairātmya darśana abhyāsāt prahāṇam sa tu kṣīṇa doṣaḥ duranvayaḥ yat upadeśāt ayam pratipadyeta mā bhūt puruṣaḥ āśrayam vacanam āgamaḥ praṇetuḥ duranvaya tvāt girām mithyātva hetūnām doṣāṇām puruṣaḥ āśrayāt apauruṣeyam satya artham iti kecid pracakṣate 
PVSV_112,10–112,15	 na khalu sarve eva āgamaḥ sambhāvya vipralambhaḥ vipralambha hetūnām doṣāṇām puruṣaḥ āśrayāt apauruṣeyam satya artham iti eke kāraṇa abhāvaḥ hi kārya abhāvam sādhayati iti yaḥ evaṃvādinaḥ tān eva prati girām satya artha hetūnām guṇānām puruṣaḥ āśrayāt apauruṣeyam mithyā artham kim naḥ iti anye pracakṣate 
PVSV_112,16–112,20	 yathā rāgaḥ ādi parītaḥ puruṣaḥ mṛṣā vādī dṛṣṭaḥ tathā dayā dharmatā ādi yuktaḥ satya vāc tat yathā vacanasya puruṣaḥ āśrayāt mithyā artha tā tathā satya artha tā api iti sa nivartamānaḥ tām api nivartayati iti ānarthakyam syāt viparyayaḥ vā na hi śabdāḥ prakṛtyāḥ arthavantaḥ samayāt tatas artha khyāteḥ kāya saṃjñā ādi vat aprātikūlyam 
PVSV_112,21–113,3	 tu yogyatā samaye tat icchā praṇayanāt nisarga siddheṣu icchā vaśāt pratipādana ayogāt te anarthakāḥ puruṣa saṃskārāt arthavantaḥ syuḥ tat saṃskāryatā eva ca eṣām pauruṣeya tā yuktā naḥ utpattiḥ tatas eva artha vipralambhāt utpannaḥ api anyathā samitaḥ naḥ uparodhī tat anyaḥ puruṣa dharma vat tat ayam nivartamānaḥ sva kṛta samaya sambhavām artha pratibhām nivartayati tat kutas tat nivṛttyā satya artha tā atha punar utpattiḥ eva pauruṣeya tā na samayaḥ ākhyānam artha jñāpana hetuḥ hi saṃketaḥ puruṣaḥ āśrayaḥ girām apauruṣeya tve api atas mithyātva sambhavaḥ 
PVSV_113,4–113,13	 kim hi asya apauruṣeya tayā yatas hi samayāt artha pratipattiḥ sa pauruṣeyaḥ vitathaḥ api syāt śīla sādhana svarga vacanam tat anyathā samayena viparyāsayet tena ayathārtham api prakāśana sambhavāt saḥ eva doṣaḥ sambandha apauruṣeya tve syāt pratītiḥ asaṃvidaḥ syāt etat akārya sambandhāḥ eva śabdāḥ na te artheṣu puruṣaiḥ anyathā viparyasyante tena adoṣaḥ iti kim idānīm saṃketena sa hi sambandhaḥ yatas artha pratītiḥ sa ced apauruṣeyaḥ na ayam samayam apekṣeta apratīti āśrayaḥ vā katham sambandhaḥ saṃketāt tat abhivyaktau asamartha anya kalpanā 
PVSV_113,14–113,18	 na vai sambandhaḥ vidyamānaḥ api anabhivyaktaḥ prati iti hetuḥ saṃketaḥ tu enam abhivyanakti sa tarhi siddhaḥ upasthāyī kim akāraṇam poṣyate nanu iyān sambandhasya vyāpāraḥ yat artha prati iti jananam tat samayena eva kṛtam iti na ayogye samayaḥ samarthaḥ iti yogyatā tat sambandhaḥ ced tat kim vai śabdaḥ 
PVSV_113,19–113,23	 sambandhaḥ astu samartham hi rūpam śabdasya yogyatā kārya kāraṇa yogyatā vat sā ced artha antaram kim śabdasya iti sambandhaḥ vācyaḥ yogya tā upakāraḥ iti ced na nityāyāḥ niratiśaya tvāt tatra api atiprasaṅgāt upakāra asiddheḥ yogyatāyām ca svatas yogya tve arthaḥ eva kim naḥ iṣyate samayaḥ tarhi katham śabdaḥ artha 
PVSV_113,24–114,1	 sambandhāḥ puruṣeṣu vṛtteḥ na amiśrāṇām siddhānām kaścid sambandhaḥ abheda prasaṅgāt anapekṣaṇāt ca artha viśeṣa samīha apreritā vāc atas idam iti viduṣaḥ sva nidānaḥ ābhāsinam artham sūcayati iti buddhi rūpa vāc vijñaptyoḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ tatas śabdāt pratipattiḥ avinā abhāvāt tat ākhyānam 
PVSV_114,2–114,9	 samayaḥ tatas pratyāyaka sambandha siddheḥ sambandhaḥ ākhyānāt na tu saḥ eva sambandhaḥ astu vai anyaḥ eva nityaḥ sambandhaḥ tena girām ekaḥ artha niyame na syāt artha antare gatiḥ na hi tena sambandhena asambaddhe arthe pratītiḥ yuktāḥ tasya vaiphalya prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭaḥ ca icchā vaśāt kṛta samayaḥ sarvaḥ sarvasya dīpakaḥ aneka artha abhisambandhe viruddha vyakti sambhavaḥ 
PVSV_114,10–114,15	 atha mā bhūt dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ iti sarve sarvasya vācakāḥ tathā na sarvaḥ sarva sādhanaḥ asaṃkarāt kārya kāraṇa tāyāḥ tatra pratiniyata sādhane abhimate arthe sarva sādhya sādhana sādhāraṇasya śabdasya iṣṭa vyaktim eva samaya kāraḥ karoti iti kutas etat saḥ aniyataḥ niyamam puruṣāt pratipadyate tadā apauruṣeya tāyāḥ ca vyarthā syāt parikalpanā 
PVSV_114,16–114,23	 api nāma asaṃkīrṇam artham jānīyām iti saṃkara hetuḥ puruṣaḥ upākīrṇaḥ tatra yādṛśāḥ puruṣaiḥ kvacid prayuktāḥ saṃkīryante tādṛśāḥ eva sarva sādhāraṇāḥ santaḥ kvacid taiḥ viniyamitāḥ tattva aparijñānāt prakṛtyāḥ eva vaidikāḥ niyatāḥ iti ced na upadeśam apekṣeran na anyathā saṃketena prakāśayeyuḥ vyākhyā vikalpaḥ ca na syāt upadeśasya ca iṣṭa saṃvādaḥ śakya vikalpe na asti iti vyarthāḥ eva apauruṣeya tā vācyaḥ ca hetuḥ bhinnānām sambandhasya vyavasthiteḥ 
PVSV_114,25–115,4	 arthāḥ hi bāhyāḥ na rūpam śabdasya na śabdaḥ arthānām yena abhinna ātma tayā vyavasthā bhede api na antarīyaka tā syāt kṛtaka tva anitya tva vat na api ete vivakṣāḥ janmānaḥ dhvanayaḥ ajanmānaḥ vā vivakṣāḥ vyaṅgyāḥ na arthaḥ āyattāḥ tatas katham idānīm tat pratiniyama saṃsādhyam tat anvayam sādhayeyuḥ na hi apratibaddhaḥ tat sādhanaḥ iti asaṃskārya tayā pumbhiḥ sarvathā syāt nirarthatā saṃskāraḥ upagame mukhyam gaja snānam idam bhavet 
PVSV_115,5–115,9	 iti saṃgraha ślokaḥ api ca śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ nityaḥ vā syāt anityaḥ vā yadi anityaḥ puruṣaḥ icchā vṛttiḥ avṛttiḥ vā apuruṣa adhīna tve puruṣāṇām yathā abhiprāyam deśaḥ ādi parāvṛttyā tena pratipādanam na syāt icchāyām api anāyattasya kadācid ayogāt parvataḥ ādi vat ayam eva nitya tve api doṣaḥ tasya sthira rūpasya 
PVSV_115,10–115,14	 parāvṛtti ayogāt iti samam sarve avasthāne api iṣṭa pratiniyama abhāvāt tatas viśeṣa pratipattiḥ na syāt iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ icchā vṛttau ca pauruṣeya tvam iti vipralambhaḥ āśaṅkā api ca sambandhinām anitya tvāt na sambandhe asti nitya tā para āśrayaḥ hi sambandhaḥ apratibandhe tayoḥ sambandhitāḥ ayogāt 
PVSV_115,15–115,23	 sa ca āśrayaḥ anityaḥ apāye asya sambandhasya api apāyaḥ anyathā anāśritaḥ syāt tatas na nityaḥ tat āśraya arthaḥ ca vaktavyaḥ nityasya anupakārya tvāt anupakurvāṇaḥ ca anāśrayaḥ jāteḥ vācya tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na tat vacane prayojana abhāvāt iti nirloṭhitam etat sarvatra ca jāti asambhavāt ayogaḥ yādṛt chikeṣu vyakti vāciṣu sarvadā jāti codane viśeṣa antara vyudāsena pravṛtti ayogāt ca tasmāt anvaya vyatirekiṇaḥ bhāvasya bhāva abhāvau sambandhaḥ arthaiḥ atas sa śabdānām saṃskāryaḥ puruṣaiḥ dhiyā 
PVSV_115,24–116,4	 tau eva bhāva abhāvau āśritya asaṃsṛṣṭau api saṃsṛṣṭau iva puruṣasya vyavahāra bhāvanātaḥ pratibhātaḥ iti pauruṣeyaḥ bhāvānām saṃśleṣaḥ kim ca āśraya vināśāt naṣṭe sambandhe sa śabdaḥ punar asambandha tvāt na apūrveṇa yojyeta utpannaḥ utpannāḥ ca bhāvāḥ sthita sambandha abhāvāt asambandhinaḥ avācyāḥ syuḥ tatra 
PVSV_116,5–116,18	 api arthaiḥ eva saha utpāde kalpyamāne na svabhāva viparyayaḥ śabdeṣu yuktaḥ atha mā bhūt naṣṭa sambandhasya śabdasya artha antare vaiguṇyam arthānām ca avācya tā iti utpannaḥ arthaḥ sambandhavān yadi utpadyeta sa sambandhaḥ utpannaḥ api na śabde syāt tasya tena asambandhi svabhāvasya svabhāva viparyayam antareṇa tat bhāva ayogāt arthena saha utpannasya anyatas siddhasya anupakāriṇi śabde asamāśrayāt ca tasya api tat utpatti sahakāri tve samarthasya nityaḥ utpādana prasaṅgaḥ anapekṣa tvāt nityasya anupakārāt asāmarthye api paścāt api svabhāva atyāgāt aśaktiḥ sambandhe na ayam doṣaḥ vikalpite 
PVSV_116,19–116,25	 na hi bhāva śleṣa apekṣī puruṣa bhāvanā pratibhāsī tat apekṣa alakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ saḥ ayam nityānām api aparāvartayan svabhāvam kutaścid svayam utprekṣya ghaṭayet iti te api tathā syuḥ na ca cyavana dharmāṇaḥ yat uktam āśraya apāyena āśrita sambandha vināśāt anityaḥ saḥ iti tatra nitya tvāt āśraya apāye api anāśaḥ yadi jāti vat nityeṣu āśraya sāmarthyam kim yena iṣṭaḥ saḥ āśrayaḥ 
PVSV_116,26–117,2	 śrūyate etat nityā jātiḥ āśrayitā ca na api āśrayeṇa saha naśyati iti kevalam nityeṣu āśraya sāmarthyam na paśyāmaḥ yena asau āśrayaḥ kṛtasya karaṇa abhāvāt akārakasya ca anapekṣa tvāt vyaktiḥ upakāraḥ jāteḥ sambandhasya ca āśrayāt tena āśrayaḥ iti ced jñānaḥ utpādana hetūnām sambandhāt sahakāriṇām tat utpādana yogya tvena utpattiḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate 
PVSV_117,3–117,10	 ghaṭaḥ ādiṣu api yukti jñaiḥ aviśeṣe avikāriṇām vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ kutas kaḥ arthaḥ vyaktāḥ taiḥ te yatas matāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ sakāśāt upādāna apekṣāt jñāna janana yogya kṣaṇa antara utpattiḥ eva ghaṭaḥ ādīnām abhivyaktiḥ anyathā anapekṣya tat upakāram jñānaḥ utpādana prasaṅgāt sāmarthya kāriṇaḥ ca janaka tvāt tasya ca tad ātmaka tvāt artha antara tve ca bhāva anupakāra prasaṅgāt sāmarthyāt ca jñānaḥ utpatteḥ nityam ghaṭaḥ ādīnām 
PVSV_117,11–117,15	 agrahaṇaḥ āpatteḥ anāloka apekṣa grahaṇa prasaṅgāt anapekṣaḥ ātma anupakārāt tat ime sva viṣaya jñāna janane param apekṣamāṇāḥ tatas svabhāva atiśayam svīkurvanti tena asya te janyāḥ jñeya rūpa asādhanāt tu jñāna vaśena kārya atiśaya vācinā śabdena viśeṣa khyāti artham vyaṅgyāḥ khyāpyante na evam jāti sambandhaḥ ādayaḥ 
PVSV_117,16–117,20	 kathaṃcid api anupakārya tvāt anupakāriṇā vyaktā yujyate sambandhasya ca vastu tve syāt bhedāt buddhi citra tā sa ca ayam sambandhaḥ vastu bhavat niyamena śabda arthābhyām bhedaḥ abhedau na ativartate rūpam hi vastu tasya atattvam eva anyat tvam iti uktam sa ca ayam aindriyaḥ san sva buddhau tat anya vivekina 
PVSV_117,21–117,25	 apratibhāsamānaḥ rūpeṇa katham tathā syāt dṛśya avivekaḥ adarśanayoḥ viveka sattā viparyayaḥ āśraya tvāt anyathā tat sthiteḥ abhāva prasaṅgāt atīndriya tvāt apratibhāse api indriyaḥ ādiṣu iva adoṣaḥ iti ced na tatas apratipatti prasaṅgāt aprasiddhasya ajñāpaka tvāt saṃnidhi mātreṇa jñāpane avyutpannānām api syāt 
PVSV_117,26–118,4	 na anumānāt pratipattiḥ liṅga abhāvāt dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ ca tatra api atīndriya tvena sādhana apekṣaṇāt tulyam indriyaḥ ādiṣu api iti ced na teṣām anyathā anumānāt jñānam hi keṣucid satsu vyatireka anvaya vat tat mā atra asambhavam tat vyatirikta apekṣām ca sādhayati tatas kārya dvāreṇa indriya siddhiḥ na evam sambandhasya tasya asiddhau 
PVSV_118,5–118,9	 tat kāryasya eva jñānasya abhāvāt na hi tatra śabda rūpam arthaḥ vā liṅgam tayoḥ sarvatra yogya tvāt viśeṣa prati iti samāśrayasya apratyāyanāt apratītiḥ asya na hi asati sambandha viśeṣe sā yuktāḥ tasyām vā animittāyām tat viśeṣa prati iti niyama vat artha pratipādanam api śabdānām animittam kim naḥ iṣyate tasmāt 
PVSV_118,10–118,14	 tat sadṛśam liṅgam sarve sambandhe tatas aviśeṣeṇa gamayet tatas aviśeṣeṇa eva pratītiḥ syāt sarvasya ca tasmāt sambandha siddhi artha pratīteḥ na kaścid sampradāyam apekṣeta sampradāya sahitasya liṅga tvam iti ced tat kim anayā paraṃparayā saḥ eva sampradāya apekṣaḥ artha jñāpanam kim na karoti sa ca śabdaḥ 
PVSV_118,15–118,20	 yat abhiprāyaiḥ prayujyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ anyathā na dṛṣṭaḥ darśana adarśanābhyām dhūmaḥ ādi vat tat pratītim janayati iti saḥ eva sambandhaḥ avinā abhāvaḥ ākhyaḥ na ca atra anyasya sāmarthyam paśyāmaḥ na api siddhi upāyam atha punar na śabda arthayoḥ anyaḥ eva sambandhaḥ tābhyām abhede tau eva na atas anyā vastunaḥ gatiḥ 
PVSV_118,21–119,1	 rūpa bheda nibandhana tvāt vyavasthā antarasya tat rūpam tat eva syāt dharma bhedaḥ tu syāt pūrvaḥ ukta krameṇa sa ca aviruddhaḥ eva na vastu bhedaḥ na ca bhedaḥ abhedau muktvā vastunaḥ anyā gatiḥ tasya rūpa lakṣaṇa tvāt rūpasya ca etat vikalpa anativṛtteḥ api ca bhinna tvāt vastu rūpasya sambandhaḥ kalpanā kṛtaḥ iti uktam prāk na hi śleṣa lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ aśliṣṭeṣu padārtheṣu sambhavati na ca artha antaram eṣām sambandhaḥ yasmāt sat dravyam syāt para adhīnam sambandhaḥ anyasya vā katham 
PVSV_119,3–119,11	 na hi siddham sat param apekṣate na anapekṣaḥ svatantraḥ sambandhaḥ dravyam iti ca svabhāvaḥ ucyate sa katham para bhāvasya śleṣaḥ syāt na hi svabhāva antara sat tayā anyaḥ śliṣṭaḥ nāma mā bhūt aśliṣṭena śliṣṭena tu syāt iti ced na tasya eva tābhyām śleṣa asiddheḥ saḥ eva asiddhaḥ yaḥ tau śleṣayet tat ayam ati prasaṅgaḥ yadi arthau artha antareṇa śliṣyataḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt kim ca varṇāḥ nirarthakāḥ santaḥ padaḥ ādi parikalpitam avastuni katham vṛttiḥ sambandhasya asya vastunaḥ 
PVSV_119,12–119,16	 vācakaḥ hi vacana aṅgena tadvān syāt santaḥ api avācakāḥ varṇāḥ tat na teṣu vācya vācaka sambandhaḥ tat vṛttau svarūpa hāni prasaṅgāt krama viśeṣeṇa vācakāḥ varṇāḥ iti ced na kramasya anartha antara tvena abhedaka tvāt tat rūpasya krama antare api aviśeṣāt tulyā syāt pratipattiḥ artha antara tvam api kramasya niṣetsyāmaḥ 
PVSV_119,17–119,21	 tat asati varṇānām vācaka tve padaḥ ādi vācakam syāt tat ca na kiṃcid vyatireka avyatireka virodhāt tasmāt indriya vijñāna viśeṣa anubandhī sabhāga vāsanāḥ upādāna vikalpa pratibhāsa vibhramaḥ padam vākyam ca ekaḥ avabhāsi mithyā eva ekaḥ aneka tva ayogāt na hi ekam anekayā buddhyā krameṇa grahaṇa ayogāt 
PVSV_119,22–119,26	 na ca tat ekayā grāhyam varṇa anukrama grahaṇāt eka varṇa grahaṇa kāle ca aneka buddhi vyatikramāt kṣaṇika tvāt buddhīnām kṣaṇasya eka paramāṇu vyatikrama kāla tvāt ādhikye vibhāgavataḥ paryavasāna ayogāt aneka aṇu vyatyaya nimeṣa tulya kāla tvāt antya varṇa parisamāpteḥ yathā anubhavam smaraṇāt 
PVSV_119,27–120,1	 smṛtiḥ api tat kālaḥ eva anubhava smaraṇa anukramayoḥ viśeṣa anupalakṣaṇa tvāt ca na api anekam padaḥ ādi abheda pratibhāsanāt buddheḥ tat aneka tvasya niṣetsyamāna tvāt ca tat na vastu tasya etat vikalpa anatikramāt vastu ca sambandhaḥ sa katham tat āśrayaḥ syāt āśrayanīya ayogāt anāśritaḥ hi evam syāt 
PVSV_120,2–120,11	 tathā ca asambandhaḥ tasmāt na svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ tat abhiprāyasya prayogāt utpannaḥ abhivyaktaḥ vā śabdaḥ tat avyabhicārī iti tattvam asya sambandhaḥ sā ca utpattiḥ abhivyaktiḥ vai avyabhicāraḥ āśrayaḥ pauruṣeyī iti pauruṣeyaḥ eva sambandhaḥ tat dvāreṇa ca artha pratyāyane aniyamaḥ śabdānām iti apauruṣeya tve api saḥ eva vipralambhaḥ apauruṣeya tā api iṣṭā kartṛṛṇām asmṛteḥ kila yāḥ api iyam apauruṣeya tā veda vākyānām kartuḥ asmaraṇāt varṇyate santi asya api anuvaktāraḥ iti dhik vyāpakam tamaḥ 
PVSV_120,12–120,16	 tasya eva tāvat īdṛśam prajñā skhalitam katham vṛttam iti sa vismaya anukampam naḥ cetaḥ tat apare api anuvadanti iti nirdaya ākrānta bhuvanam dhik vyāpakam tamaḥ kaḥ prāṇinaḥ hitaḥ īpsā vipralabdhasya aparādhaḥ tathā hi smaranti saugatāḥ mantrāṇām kartṛṛn aṣṭakaḥ ādīn hiraṇyagarbham ca kāṇādāḥ teṣām 
PVSV_120,17–120,21	 sa mithyā vādaḥ iti ced kaḥ idānīm evam pauruṣeyaḥ anyaḥ api kumāra sambhavaḥ ādiṣu ātmānam anyam vā praṇetāram upadiśantaḥ yat evam prativyūhyeran tatra prativahane abhyupeta bādhāḥ iti ced nanu idam eva abhyupagama aṅgam iti kasya bādhā tat parasya api tulyam eva tasya iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced kutas asya iyam 
PVSV_120,22–120,26	 iṣṭiḥ apramāṇikā prāk āsīt akasmāt grāhī ca ayam kim punar kvacid sādhanam apekṣate yat pauruṣeya apauruṣeya cintayā ātmānam āyāsayati tatas eva iṣṭeḥ anabhyupeta bādhāyām tat anyasya api tulyam iti anupālambhaḥ anatiśaya darśī ca ayam vākyeṣu evaṃprakārāṇām apauruṣeya tva sādhanānām kārya dharmāṇām 
PVSV_121,1–121,8	 vā kvacid atiśayam abhyupetaḥ iti apratyayaḥ eva asya vṛttiḥ dṛśyante ca vicchinna kriyā sampradāyāḥ kṛtakāḥ ca tān yatnavantaḥ upalabhante iti ced na niyama abhāvāt anyatra anupalambhasya upalambhasya vā paraḥ upadeśāt apratyayāt aniścaya artha tvāt svayam kṛtānām api apahnotṛ darśanāt niṣṭhā gamanasya aśakya tvāt yathā ayam anyatas aśrutvā na imam varṇa pada kramam vaktum samarthaḥ puruṣaḥ tathā anyaḥ api iti kaścana 
PVSV_121,9–121,19	 tasya api tat eva uttaram evam apauruṣeya tve api kim idānīm pauruṣeyam iti ādi tathā hi anyaḥ vā racitaḥ granthaḥ sampradāyāt ṛte paraiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kaḥ abhihitaḥ yena saḥ api evam na anumīyate na khalu kiṃcid anyat apauruṣeya tve āśrayaḥ anyatra idānīntanānām anupadeśa pāṭha aśakteḥ sā ca anyatra api ekena racite granthe anyasya tulyā tat anusāriṇā sarvaḥ tathā unneyaḥ na vā kaścid tasya tathā aniṣṭa tvāt iti ādau api uktam iṣṭeḥ tat āśraya tvāt iti ādi api ca yat jātīyaḥ yatas siddhaḥ sa tasmāt agni kāṣṭha vat adṛṣṭa hetuḥ anyaḥ api aviśiṣṭaḥ sampratīyate 
PVSV_121,20–121,24	 na adarśanāt hetuḥ ahetukaḥ nāma adṛṣṭa hetavaḥ api hi bhāvāḥ tat anyaiḥ svabhāva abhedam anubhavantaḥ tathāvidhāḥ samunnīyante hetu rūpa nivṛttau api tat rūpam anivṛttam kārya dharma vyatikramāt na tatas syāt iti na kaścid tathā vacanīyaḥ rūpa viśeṣaḥ vā tathā darśanīyaḥ yaḥ enam hetum anuvidadhyāt yena iṣṭa 
PVSV_121,25–122,2	 aniṣṭayoḥ iṣṭa viparyayaḥ na syāt svabhāva nivṛtteḥ ca hetoḥ abhedane bhāvānām bhedaḥ syāt ākasmikaḥ iti na kvacid vinivarteta tasmāt yaḥ svabhāvaḥ yat janmā dṛṣṭaḥ saḥ anyatra api avibhajyamānaḥ sva ātmanā tat kārya dharma tām na ativartate agni indhana vat tatra apradarśya ye bhedam kārya sāmānya darśanāt hetavaḥ pravitanyante sarve te vyabhicāriṇaḥ 
PVSV_122,3–122,7	 yathā adyaḥ api pathika kṛtaḥ agniḥ jvālā antara pūrvakaḥ na araṇi nirmathana pūrvakaḥ pathika agni tvāt anantara agni vat iti katham punar pathika agneḥ vyabhicāraḥ jvālā udbhava sāmarthyam hi āśritya dahanasya hetu antaram pratikṣipyate yadi hi vinā jvālayā syāt anyatra api syāt iti tatra jvālā itara janmanoḥ abādhya bādhaka tve 
PVSV_122,8–122,12	 jvālā aprabhava tvam anyathā api syāt iti dharmayoḥ ekatra arthe sambhavāt sa pathika agniḥ anyaḥ vai arthaḥ eka pratiniyataḥ na syāt iti āśaṅkyate vyabhicāraḥ saḥ api anyonya vyatirekī dharma dvaya avatāraḥ vastu sāmānye aviruddhaḥ iti ucyate na avasthā bhedini viśeṣe niṣkalasya ātmanaḥ tat atattva virodhāt na ca 
PVSV_122,13–122,17	 jvālā itara janmanoḥ bādhya bādhaka tā pathika agnau tasya jvālā prabhava vyatirekeṇa asambhava abhāvāt evaṃbhūtaḥ pathika agniḥ jvālā prabhavaḥ iti syāt na sarvaḥ tatra viśeṣa pratikṣepasya kartum aśakya tvāt sambhavat viśeṣasya ca tādavasthya aniyamāt yat api vinā jvālayā syāt anyatra api syāt iti bhavati eva 
PVSV_122,18–122,23	 yayā sāmagryā sambhavati sā yadi syāt asyāḥ sambhavam pradarśya tat abhāvam pradarśayet tatra vā jvālām syāt etat tasmāt naḥ ekasya para pūrvakam adhyayanam sarvasya tathā abhāvam sādhayati tasya anyathā asambhava abhāvāt tathāvidhasya tu tat kriyā pratibhā rahitasya tathā syāt iti tathābhūtam evam vācyam syāt tat aviśeṣeṇa sambhavat viśeṣam ucyamānam 
PVSV_122,24–122,28	 chāyām na puṣṇāti katham viśeṣasya sambhavaḥ yāvatā teṣām api puruṣāṇām aśaktiḥ eva idāni intana puruṣa vat atra api śakti puruṣayoḥ na kiṃcid virodha darśanam iti na aviruddha vidhiḥ anupalabdhi prayogaḥ gamakaḥ na hi atīndriyeṣu virodha gatiḥ asti iti uktam na ca ayam pūrva prayogāt bhidyate yadi puruṣāḥ 
PVSV_122,29–123,4	 śaktāḥ syuḥ idānīntanāḥ api iti viśeṣa asambhavaḥ etat syāt sa ca duḥsādhaḥ yatra ekasya aśaktiḥ tatra sarve puruṣāṇām iti api pūrvavat vyabhicāri bhārataḥ ādiṣu idānīntanānām aśaktau api kasyacid śakti siddheḥ tasmāt kāraṇāni vivecayata artheṣu api tat atat pratibhaveṣu svabhāva bhedaḥ darśanīyaḥ tat abhāve 
PVSV_123,5–123,9	 sarvaḥ tad ātmā na vā kaścid na ca atra laukika vaidikayoḥ svabhāva bhedam paśyāmaḥ asati tasmin tayoḥ sāmānyasya eva dṛṣṭeḥ ekasya kaścid dharmam vivecayan tat svabhāva sambhavinā tena āśaṅkya vyabhicāra vādaḥ kriyate nanu veda avedayoḥ tattva lakṣaṇaḥ asti eva viśeṣaḥ satyam asti na kevalam 
PVSV_123,10–123,14	 tayoḥ eva kim tarhi ḍiṇḍika purāṇaḥ itarayoḥ api na ca sva prakriyā bheda dīpanaḥ nāma bhedaḥ puruṣa kṛtim bādhate anyatra api prasaṅgāt yadi tādṛśīm racanām puruṣāḥ kartum na śaknuyuḥ kṛtām vā akṛta saṃketaḥ vivecayet vyaktam apauruṣeyaḥ vedaḥ nanu na śaknuvanti eva puruṣāḥ mantrān kartum etat 
PVSV_123,15–123,19	 uttaratra vicārayiṣyāmaḥ api ca na mantraḥ nāma anyat eva kiṃcid kim tarhi satya tapaḥ prabhāvavatām samīhita artha sādhanam vacanam tat adya tve api puruṣeṣu dṛśyate eva yathāsvam satya adhiṣṭhāna balāḥ viṣa dahanaḥ ādi stambhana darśanāt śabarāṇām ca keṣāṃcid adya api mantra karaṇāt avaidikānām 
PVSV_123,20–123,24	 ca bauddhaḥ ādīnām mantra kalpānām darśanāt teṣām ca puruṣa kṛteḥ tatra api apauruṣeya tve katham idānīm apauruṣeyam avitatham tathā hi bauddhaḥ itarayoḥ mantra kalpayoḥ hiṃsā maithunaḥ ātma darśane ādayaḥ anabhyudaya hetavaḥ anyathā ca varṇyate tat katham ekatra viruddha abhidhāyi dvayam satyam 
PVSV_123,25–124,1	 syāt tatra artha antara kalpane tat anyatra api tulyam iti artha anirṇayāt kvacid apratipattiḥ tathā ca sat api anupayogam apauruṣeyam bauddhaḥ ādīnām amantra tve tat anyatra api koṣa pānam syāt karaṇīyam viṣa karma adhikṛtaḥ bauddhāḥ api dṛśyante tatra amantra tvam api vipratiṣiddham mudrā maṇḍala dhyānaiḥ api 
PVSV_124,2–124,6	 anakṣaraiḥ karmāṇi kriyante na ca tāni apauruṣeyāṇi nityāni yujyate teṣām kriyā sambhave akṣara racanāyām kaḥ pratighātaḥ puruṣāṇām tasmāt na kiṃcid aśakya kriyam eṣām katham idānīm satya prabhavau mantra kalpau paraspara virodhinau na vai sarvatra tau satya prabhavau prabhāva yukta puruṣa pratijñā 
PVSV_124,7–124,11	 lakṣaṇau api tau staḥ sa prabhāvaḥ gati siddhi viśeṣābhyām api syāt yadi pauruṣeyāḥ mantrāḥ kim na sarve puruṣāḥ mantra kāriṇaḥ tat kriyā sādhana vaikalyāt yadi tādṛśaiḥ satya tapaḥ prabhṛtibhiḥ yuktāḥ syuḥ kurvanti eva api ca kāvyāni puruṣaḥ karoti iti sarvaḥ puruṣaḥ kāvya kṛt syāt akaraṇe vā naḥ eva kaścid tadvat 
PVSV_124,12–124,16	 iti apūrvā eṣā vācaḥ yuktiḥ satyam mantra kriyā sādhana vikalāḥ mantrān na kurvate tat tu kasyacid sākalyam na paśyāmaḥ puruṣāṇām samāna dharma tvāt uktam atra na mantraḥ nāma anyat eva kiṃcid satyaḥ ādimatām vacana samayāt iti tāni ca kvacid puruṣeṣu dṛśyante sarva puruṣāḥ tat rahitāḥ iti api tat sambhava 
PVSV_124,17–124,21	 virodha abhāvāt anirṇayaḥ na ca atyakṣa svabhāveṣu anupalabdhiḥ niścaya hetuḥ na ca smṛti mati prativedha satya śaktayaḥ sarva bhāvinyaḥ tat sādhana sampradāya bheda vat guṇa antara sādhanāni api syuḥ na api san api sarvaḥ draṣṭum śakyaḥ atas eva adṛṣṭasya anapahnavaḥ na api puruṣeṣu utpitsoḥ kasyacid guṇasya 
PVSV_124,22–124,26	 pratiroddhā bādhya adṛṣṭeḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāva asiddheḥ etena sarva jñāna pratiṣedhaḥ ādayaḥ api nirvarṇitaḥ uttarāḥ tatra api evaṃbhūtaḥ yādṛśaḥ ayam asambhavat tat sādhana sampradāyaḥ naḥ iti nyāyaḥ na adṛṣṭa jñāpakaḥ atat svabhāvaḥ iti api satām api kārya anārambha sambhavāt svabhāva viprakarṣeṇa draṣṭum aśakya tvāt ca 
PVSV_124,27–124,31	 tasmāt adhyayanam adhyayana antara pūrvakam adhyayanāt iti bhārata adhyayane api bhāvāt vyabhicāri nanu vedane viśeṣaṇāt adoṣaḥ kaḥ punar atiśayaḥ veda adhyayanasya yat anyathā adhyetum na śakyate na hi viśeṣaṇam aviruddham vipakṣeṇa asmāt hetum vyāvartayati aviruddhayoḥ ekatra sambhavāt idānīntanānām 
PVSV_125,1–125,6	 adhyayanāt iti ced uktaḥ uttaram etat adarśanāt iti ced idam api prativyūḍham na api adarśana mātram abhāvam gamayati iti vyabhicāraḥ eva tasmāt na viśeṣaṇam atiśaya bhāk iti anupātta samam yat kiṃcid veda adhyayanam sarvam tat adhyayana antara pūrvakam iti api vyāptiḥ na sidhyati sarvasya tathā abhāva asiddheḥ yādṛśam tu tat nimittam dṛṣṭam 
PVSV_125,7–125,12	 tat tathā iti syāt dṛṣṭe viśeṣe tat nimitta tayā tat tyāgena sāmānya grahaṇam vyabhicāri eva hutāśana saṃsiddhau pāṇḍu dravya tva vat etena vacanaḥ ādayaḥ rāgaḥ ādi sādhane pratyuktāḥ astu vedam adhyayanam adhyayana pūrva tā sādhanam sarvathā anāditā sidhyet evam na apuruṣaḥ āśrayaḥ tasmāt apauruṣeya tve syāt anyaḥ api anaraḥ āśrayaḥ 
PVSV_125,13–125,22	 puruṣaḥ eva hi svayam abhyūhya paratas vā ādhīyate na eṣām avyāpṛta karaṇānām svayam śabdāḥ dhvananti yena apauruṣeyāḥ syuḥ api syuḥ apauruṣeyāḥ yadi puruṣāṇām ādiḥ syāt tadā api anyaḥ pūrvakam na sidhyati adhyāpayituḥ abhāvāt tat prathamaḥ adhyetā kartā eva syāt tat ayam anādiḥ pūrva pūrva darśana pravṛttaḥ ḍimbhaka pāṃsu krīḍā ādi vat puruṣa vyavahāraḥ iti syāt na apauruṣeyaḥ iti anādi tvāt apauruṣeya tve bahutaram idānīm apauruṣeyam tathā hi mlecchaḥ ādi vyavahārāṇām nāstikya vacasām api anādi tvāt tathā abhāvaḥ pūrva saṃskāra santateḥ 
PVSV_125,23–125,27	 mleccha vyavahārāḥ api kecid mātṛ vivāhaḥ ādayaḥ madanaḥ utsave ādayaḥ ca anādayaḥ nāstikya vacāṃsi ca apūrva para loke ādi apavādīni na hi tāni anāhita saṃskārāḥ paraiḥ pravartayanti sva pratibhā racita samayānām api yathā aśruta artha vikalpa saṃhāreṇa eva pravṛtteḥ tat kiṃcid kutaścid āgatam iti ekasya upadeṣṭuḥ prabandhena abhāvāt 
PVSV_125,28–126,7	 apara pūrvakam iti ucyate prāk eva yathā darśana pravṛttayaḥ samyak mithyā pravṛttayaḥ loka vyavahārāḥ nanu ādi kalpikeṣu adṛṣṭāḥ eva vyavahārāḥ paścāt pravṛttāḥ iṣyante na teṣām api anye saṃskāraḥ āhitānām yathā pratyayam prabodhāt bhavatu sarveṣām apauruṣeya tvam iti ced tādṛśe apauruṣeya tve kaḥ siddhe api guṇaḥ bhavet kāmam avisaṃvādakam iti apauruṣeya tvam iṣṭam tat visaṃvādakānām api keṣāṃcid anādi tvāt asti iti kim apauruṣeya tvena sati vā veda vākyānām eva apauruṣeya tve artha saṃskāra bhedānām darśanāt saṃśayaḥ punar 
PVSV_126,8–126,12	 yadi apauruṣeya tve api pratiniyatām eva tat artha pratibhām janayet āśvāsanam syāt yatheṣṭam tu samāropa apavādābhyām nairukta mīmāṃsakaḥ ādayaḥ veda vākyāni viśasantaḥ dṛśyante na ca te arthāḥ teṣām na saṃghaṭante samaya prādhānyāt artha niveśasya ekasya api vākyasya aneka vikalpa sambhavāt prakṛti pratyayānām 
PVSV_126,13–126,18	 aneka artha pāṭhāt rūḍheḥ api ekāntena ananumateḥ arūḍha śabda bāhulyāt tat arthasya puruṣaḥ upadeśa apekṣaṇāt tat upadeśasya tat icchā anuvṛtteḥ anirṇayaḥ eva veda vākya artheṣu api ca ayam apauruṣeya tvam sādhayan varṇānām vā sādhayet vākyasya vā tatra anyaḥ aviśeṣāt varṇānām sādhane kim phalam bhavet 
PVSV_126,19–127,1	 na hi loka vedayoḥ nānā varṇāḥ bhede api ca pratyabhijñāna aviśeṣāt tatas ekatva asiddhi prasaṅgāt bheda anupalakṣaṇāt ca vaidika varṇa asiddhiḥ pratyabhijñānāt apratipatti prasaṅgāt anabhyupagamāt ca teṣām ca apauruṣeya tva sādhane te tulyāḥ sarvatra iti kim anena pariśeṣitam tathā ca sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ apauruṣeyaḥ na ca sarvaḥ avitathaḥ iti vyarthaḥ pariśramaḥ atha vākyam apauruṣeyam iṣṭam vākyam na bhinnam varṇebhyaḥ vidyate anupalambhanāt 
PVSV_127,3–127,7	 na hi vayam devadattaḥ ādi pada vākyeṣu dakāraḥ ādi pratibhāsam muktvā anyam pratibhāsam buddheḥ paśyāmaḥ dvitīya varṇa pratibhāsa vat na ca apratibhāsamānam grahaṇe grāhya tayā iṣṭam asti anyat vā iti śakyam avasātum ākāra antara vat anyaḥ asambhavi kāryam gamakam iti ced syāt etat yadi teṣu varṇeṣu satsu api 
PVSV_127,8–127,12	 tat kāryam na syāt na bhavati teṣām aviśeṣe api pada vākya antare abhāvāt iti ced na teṣām aviśeṣa asiddheḥ aviśeṣaḥ pratyabhijñānāt siddhaḥ iti ced na tasya vyabhicārāt anidarśana tvāt ca varṇaḥ aviśeṣe api vākya bhedāt pratipatti bhedaḥ kārya bhedaḥ syāt sā ca vākyāt tat ca atīndriyam iti kutas syāt saṃnidhāna 
PVSV_127,13–127,20	 mātreṇa janane avyutpannasya api syāt tasmāt na vākyam nāma kiṃcid artha antaram varṇebhyaḥ yasya apauruṣeya tvam sādhyeta tat abhāvāt veda aviśiṣṭa varṇaḥ apauruṣeya tvam api prathama pakṣe pratyuktam api ca astu artha antaram vākyam tat aneka avayavaḥ ātmakam vā syāt anavayavam vā aneka avayavaḥ ātma tve pṛthak teṣām nirarthatā te api tasya bahavaḥ avayavāḥ pṛthak prakṛtyāḥ yadi anarthakāḥ atat rūpe ca tādrūpyam kalpitam siṃhatā ādi vat 
PVSV_127,21–128,2	 arthavān eva ātmā vākyam te ca avayavāḥ svayam anarthakāḥ teṣu saḥ ātmā kalpanā samāropitaḥ syāt siṃhatā ādi vat māṇavaka ādiṣu iti pauruṣeyaḥ eva atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣaḥ iti pratyekam te avayavāḥ sā arthakāḥ iṣyante pratyekam sā arthaka tve api mithyā aneka tva kalpanā ekaḥ avayava gatyā ca vākya artha pratipad bhavet 
PVSV_128,3–128,7	 parisamāpta artham hi śabda rūpam vākyam te ca avayavāḥ tathāvidhāḥ pṛthak pṛthak iti pratyekam te vākyam tathā ca na aneka avayavam vākyam ekaḥ avayava pratipattyā ca vākya artha pratipatteḥ avayava antara apekṣā kāla kṣepaḥ ca na syāt tasya niṣkala ātmanaḥ kṣaṇena pratipatteḥ eka jñānaḥ utpattau niḥśeṣa avagamāt 
PVSV_128,8–128,13	 anyathā ca ekatva virodhāt sakṛt śrutau ca sarveṣām kāla bhedaḥ na yujyate atha mā bhūt avayava antara apratīkṣaṇena ekasmāt eva avayavāt vākya artha siddheḥ aneka avayava tva hāniḥ vākyasya iti sakṛt sarva avayavānām śravaṇam iṣyate tadā api kāla kṣepaḥ na yuktaḥ eva ekaḥ avayava pratipatti kālaḥ eva sarveṣām śravaṇāt krama śravaṇe 
PVSV_128,14–128,23	 ca pṛthak arthavatām ekasmāt eva tat artha siddheḥ anyasya vaiyarthyāt sakṛt śrutau ca pṛthak artheṣu adṛṣṭa sāmarthyānām arthavat tā ca na sidhyati sahiteṣu artha darśanāt adoṣaḥ na pṛthak asataḥ rūpasya saṃghāte api asambhavāt artha antara anutpatteḥ ca śabdaḥ utpāda vādinaḥ tāvat ayam adoṣaḥ eva pṛthak asamarthānām api avayavānām upakāra viśeṣāt atiśayavatām kārya viśeṣaḥ upayogāt pratyekam tu avayaveṣu samartheṣu vyarthā syāt anya kalpanā atha punar ekam eva anavayavam vākyam tatra eka tve api hi abhinnasya kramaśas gati asambhavāt 
PVSV_128,24–128,28	 kāla bhedaḥ eva na yujyate na hi ekasya krameṇa pratipattiḥ yuktāḥ gṛhīta agṛhītayoḥ abhedāt krameṇa ca vākya pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭā sarva vākya vyāhāra śravaṇa smaraṇa kālasya aneka kṣaṇa nimeṣa anukrama parisamāpteḥ varṇa rūpa asaṃsparśinaḥ ca eka buddhi pratibhāsinaḥ śabdaḥ ātmanaḥ apratibhāsanāt varṇaḥ anukrama pratīteḥ 
PVSV_128,29–129,4	 tat aviśeṣe api anukrama kṛta tvāt vākya bhedasya anukramavatī vākya pratītiḥ varṇa anukramaḥ upakāra anapekṣaṇe taiḥ yathā kathaṃcid prayuktaiḥ api yat kiṃcid vākyam pratīyeta vinā vā varṇaiḥ taiḥ anukramavadbhiḥ akramasya upakāra ayogāt akrameṇa ca vyāhartum aśakya tvāt gati antara abhāvāt ca na eva 
PVSV_129,5–129,9	 vākye varṇāḥ santi tat ekam eva śabda rūpam vyañjaka anukrama vaśāt anukrama vat varṇa vibhāga vat ca pratibhāti iti ced anukramavatā vyañjakena akramasya vyaktiḥ pratyuktāḥ vyakta avyakta virodhāt avarṇa bhāge ca vākye asakala śrāviṇaḥ asakala vākya gatiḥ na syāt ekasya śakala abhāvāt sakala śrutiḥ na vā kasyacid 
PVSV_129,10–129,14	 samasta varṇa saṃskāravatyā antyayā buddhyā vākya avadhāraṇam iti api mithyā tasya avarṇa rūpa saṃsparśinaḥ kasyacid kadācid apratipatteḥ varṇānām ca akrameṇa apratipatteḥ kutas akramam eka buddhi grāhyam vākyam nāma na ca antya varṇa pratipatteḥ ūrdhvam anyam aśakalam śabdaḥ ātmānam upalakṣayāmaḥ na api 
PVSV_129,15–129,19	 svayam ayam vaktā vibhāvayati kevalam evam yadi syāt sādhu me syāt iti kalyāṇa kāma tā mūḍha matiḥ antyāyām buddhau samāpta kalaḥ śabdaḥ bhāti iti svapnāyate na hi smaryamāṇāyoḥ api pada vākyayoḥ varṇāḥ krama viśeṣam antareṇa vibhāvyante akramāyām buddhau paurvāparya abhāvāt teṣām tat kṛtaḥ pada 
PVSV_129,20–130,2	 vākya bhedānām bhedaḥ na syāt na api avarṇa kramam anyat śabda rūpam paśyāmaḥ iti uktam sati vā tat anityam vā syāt nityam vā yadi anityam yatna sambhūtam pauruṣeyam katham na tat avaśyam hi anityam utpattimat kutaścid bhavati tathā hi ākasmika tve sattvasya deśaḥ ādi niyamaḥ na syāt iti uktam tat ca yatna prerita aviguṇa karaṇānām dṛṣṭam anyathā naḥ iti kāraṇa dharma darśanāt puruṣa vyāpāraḥ eva kāraṇam atas pauruṣeyam syāt nityaḥ upalabdhiḥ nitya tve api anāvaraṇa sambhavāt 
PVSV_130,3–130,7	 atha tat śabda rūpam nityam syāt upalabhya svabhāvam ca sa ca tasya svabhāvaḥ kadācid na apaiti iti nityam upalabhyeta evam hi sa nityaḥ syāt yadi na kutaścid sāmarthyāt pracyavet jñāna janana sāmarthyasya tad ātmaka tvāt artha antara tvasya ca prāk eva niṣiddha tvāt na api tasya upalabhya ātmanaḥ kiṃcid upalambha 
PVSV_130,8–130,12	 āvaraṇam sambhavati tasya sataḥ api tad ātmanam akhaṇḍayataḥ sāmarthya tiraskāra ayogāt na hi tatra atiśayam anutpādayan kiṃcitkaraḥ nāma akiṃcitkaraḥ ca kaḥ kasya āvaraṇam anyat vā iti nirloṭhita prāyam etat kuḍyaḥ ādayaḥ ghaṭaḥ ādīnām kam atiśayam utpādayanti khaṇḍayanti vā yena āvaraṇam iṣyante na brūmas 
PVSV_130,13–130,17	 te kaṃcid atiśāyayanti iti api tu na sarve ghaṭa kṣaṇāḥ sarvasya indriya vijñāna hetavaḥ paraspara sahitāḥ tu viṣayaḥ indriyaḥ ālokāḥ parasparataḥ viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa antaraḥ utpādāt vijñāna hetavaḥ anupakāryasya apekṣāḥ ayogāt śakta svabhāvasya nityam jananam ajananam vā anyasya sarvadā syāt iti uktam te ca avyavahitāḥ pratighātinā 
PVSV_130,18–130,22	 anyena anyonyasya upakāriṇaḥ avyavadhāna deśa yogyatā sahakāri tvāt teṣām anyonya atiśayaḥ utpatteḥ vyavadhāne tu hetu abhāvāt samartha kṣaṇa antara anutpatteḥ jñāna anutpattiḥ tasmāt pūrvaḥ utpanna samartha nirodhāt sati kuḍye anyasya utpitsoḥ kāraṇa abhāvena anutpatteḥ kāraṇa vaikalyāt jñāna anutpattiḥ iti kuḍyaḥ ādayaḥ āvaraṇam 
PVSV_130,23–130,27	 ucyante na prāk yogyasya pratibandhāt tasya svabhāvāt apracyuteḥ athavā sambhavati api bhāvānām kṣaṇikānām anyonyaḥ upakāraḥ acintya tvāt hetu pratyaya sāmarthyasya asarva vidā tena yat indriya viṣaya madhya sthitam āvaraṇam tat tau vijñānaḥ utpatti vaiguṇya tāratamya bhedena atiśayayet api āvaraṇa bhede na śabda 
PVSV_130,28–131,4	 ādau śruti māndya pāṭava darśanāt anyathā kvacid api akiṃcitkarasya saṃnidhānasya api asaṃnidhāna tulya tvāt tasya idam iti upasaṃhāraḥ vikalpa nirmitaḥ eva syāt na vastu āśrayaḥ na ca samāropa anuvidhāyinaḥ artha kriyāḥ na hi māṇavakaḥ dahanaḥ upacārāt ādhīyate pāke tasmāt satyām api kalpanāyām atat parāvṛttayaḥ 
PVSV_131,5–131,9	 bhāvāḥ yathā svabhāva vṛttayaḥ eva syuḥ tat sati api āvaraṇe vijñāpayeyuḥ eva indriyaḥ ādayaḥ na ca tathā tasmāt tena ādheya viśeṣāḥ iti gamyante na khalu evam nityānām śabdānām kasmiṃścid sati atiśaya hāniḥ utpattiḥ vā tat yadi teṣām jñāna jananaḥ svabhāvaḥ sarvasya sarvadā sarvāṇi sva viṣaya jñānāni sakṛt 
PVSV_131,10–131,15	 janayeyuḥ no ced na kadācid kasyacid kiṃcid iti ekāntaḥ eṣaḥ aśrutiḥ vikala tvāt ced kasyacid sahakāriṇaḥ syāt etat na āvaraṇāt nityam sarve śabdāḥ na śrūyante api tu kiṃcid teṣām pratipattau sahakāri pratiniyatam asti tat kadācid kasyacid bhavati iti tat kṛtam eṣām kadācid kvacid śravaṇam iti kāmam anye pratīkṣā astu niyamaḥ tu virudhyate 
PVSV_131,16–131,20	 na vai vayam kāraṇānām saha kārīṇi pratikṣipāmaḥ kim tu apekṣante eva kāraṇāni tat avasthā upakāriṇam tatas labhyasya atiśayasya kāryaḥ upayogāt tathā śabdaḥ api yadi kiṃcid apekṣya kāryam kuryāt karotu pūrva svabhāva niyataḥ iti etat na syāt tasya pracyuteḥ apekṣyāt ca svabhāva antara pratilambhāt 
PVSV_131,21–131,25	 na hi anupakārī apekṣyate iti uktam etat tat upakārasya ca artha antara tve tasya iti sambandha abhāvaḥ ādayaḥ api uktāḥ tasya ca ajñeya tvam upakārāt eva jñānaḥ utpatteḥ tasmāt eva śabdaḥ naḥ indriyam na saṃnikarṣam na ātmānam anyat vā kiṃcid jñānaḥ utpatti samāśrayam sva vijñāna janane apekṣate sarvasya tatra akiṃcitkara tvāt 
PVSV_131,26–132,5	 api ca ete śabdāḥ vyāpinaḥ vā syuḥ avyāpinaḥ vā sarvatra anupalambhaḥ syāt teṣām avyāpitā yadi katham ekaḥ deśa vartitam tat śūnya deśa sthitaḥ upalabdheta aprāpta grahaṇa pakṣe adoṣaḥ iti ced na tatra api yogya deśa sthiti tāratamya apekṣaṇāt ayaskāntaḥ ādi vat anyathā spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa śruti bhedaḥ na syāt sati ca upalambha pratyaye sarvatra deśe tulyam upalabhyeran tasmāt na avyāpinaḥ sarveṣām upalambhaḥ syāt yugapad vyāpitā yadi 
PVSV_132,6–132,13	 na hi kaścid śabda kvacid na asti iti sarve yugapad upalabhyeran sarve deśa sthitaiḥ ca yogyaḥ indriya tvāt viṣaya saṃnidhānāt apratibandhāt ca saṃskṛtasya upalambhe ca kaḥ saṃskartā avikāriṇaḥ syāt etat san api na sarvaḥ śabdaḥ upalabhyate sarveṇa saṃskṛtasya saṃskṛtena eva upalambhāt iti tatra na saṃskṛtasya upalambhaḥ anādheya vikārasya saṃskāra ayogāt indriyasya hi saṃskāraḥ śṛṇuyāt nikhilam ca tat 
PVSV_132,14–132,23	 tatra yadi saṃskṛtena upalambhaḥ iti asaṃskṛtena indriyaḥ naḥ upalabhate yasya saṃskāraḥ indriyasya kṛtaḥ sa sarve śabdān yugapad śṛṇuyāt iti prasaṅgaḥ anivṛttaḥ eva saṃskāra bhedāt bhinna tvāt ekaḥ artha niyamaḥ yadi aneka śabda saṃghāte śrutiḥ kalakale katham atha api syāt pratiniyatāḥ te saṃskārāḥ śabdānām tatra kenacid saṃskṛtam indriyam kasyacid eva grāhakam iti na yugapad sarva śabda śrutiḥ iti saṃskāra viśeṣāt śruti niyame indriyāṇām aneka śabda saṃghātasya kalakalasya śrutiḥ na syāt na hi ekaḥ śabdaḥ kalakalaḥ nāma bhinna svabhāvānām yugapad śravaṇāt 
PVSV_132,24–133,4	 svabhāva bhedaḥ āśraya tvāt ca bheda vyavasthiteḥ laghu vṛtteḥ sakṛt śrutiḥ bhrāntiḥ iti ced vaṃśaḥ ādi svara dhārāyām gamaka avayava saṃhārāt saṃkulā pratipattiḥ syāt vakṣyate ca atra pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt eka gati śakti pratiniyamāt indriyasya aneka ātmā kalakalaḥ na śrūyeta dhvanayaḥ kevalam tatra śrūyante ced na vācakāḥ na vai kalakale varṇa pada vākyāni śrūyante dhvanīnām eva kevalānām śravaṇāt vācake ca pratiniyata śakti indriyam na dhvaniṣu tatra dhvanibhyaḥ bhinnam asti iti śraddhā iyam ati bahu idam 
PVSV_133,5–133,10	 na hi vayam dhvanim śabdam ca vācakam pṛthak rūpam upalakṣayāmaḥ ekam eva ekadā varṇaḥ anukrama śravaṇe śabdaḥ ātmānam vyavasyāmaḥ tat katham vyavasāya pūrvakam vyavahāram avyavasyantaḥ pravartayāmaḥ tasmāt dhvani viśeṣaḥ eva iyam varṇaḥ ādi ākhyaḥ api ca sthiteṣu anyeṣu śabdeṣu śrūyate vācakaḥ katham 
PVSV_133,11–133,20	 na dhvaniḥ atas bhinnaḥ tena saha pṛthak vā na hi pratyakṣe arthe paraḥ upadeśaḥ garīyān tat ayam sthiteṣu anyeṣu vyāhartṛṣu kevalam eva śabdam śṛṇvan tat upalambha pratyayānām tat anya niṣpādane sāmarthya abhāvam pratyeti yadi hi samarthāḥ syuḥ tat sādhitam tat upalabhyeta tat svabhāvāḥ eva punar pratyayāḥ katham kalakale artha antaram ārabheran na hi kāraṇa abhede kārya bhedaḥ yuktaḥ bhedasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt iti uktam na ca kalakale vācakaḥ na śrūyate pada vākya vicchedānām upalakṣaṇāt katham vā śakti niyamāt bhinna dhvani gatiḥ bhavet 
PVSV_133,21–134,3	 tāni pratiniyata śaktīni api indriyāṇi nānā rūpān prati śabda niyatān dhvanīn śṛṇvanti na tu evam śabdān iti kaḥ śabdeṣu eṣām nirvedaḥ yat uktam na dhvanayaḥ bhedena vācakebhyaḥ siddhāḥ iti katham na siddhāḥ vacanāt artha pratipatteḥ na hi dhvani bhāgāt alpīyasaḥ śabdaḥ artha pratītiḥ na ca saḥ anyam samaḥ iti 
PVSV_134,4–134,8	 tat iyam samasta pada vākya rūpa sādhya artha pratītiḥ asamasta bhāgeṣu dhvaniṣu na sambhavati iti siddham akrama sattvam śabda rūpam kramavat bhāgaḥ ca dhvaniḥ iti tat na akramasya krama vat vyatirekiṇaḥ prāk eva niṣiddha tvāt atiprasaṅgaḥ ca evam karma bhāgānām pūrveṇa aparasya apratisandhānāt ekaḥ aṃśāt 
PVSV_134,9–134,15	 ca apratipatteḥ tat vyatirekī hasta saṃjñā ādiṣu artha pratipatti hetuḥ samasta rūpaḥ karma ātma abhyupagantavyaḥ syāt śabda vat eva krama bhāvinaḥ eva yathāsvam karaṇa prayogāt bhinnāḥ varṇa bhāgāḥ karma bhāgāḥ vā krameṇa vikalpa viṣayāḥ yathā saṃketam eva artha pratītim janayanti iti nyāyyam kim ca dhvanayaḥ sammatāḥ yaiḥ te doṣaiḥ kaiḥ api avācakāḥ dhvanibhiḥ vyajyamāne asmin vācake api katham na te 
PVSV_134,16–134,20	 kramaḥ utpādibhiḥ dhvani bhāgaiḥ vyaktaḥ kila vācakaḥ vakti tam api te naḥ eva sakṛt prakāśayanti krama bhāvāt na api ekaḥ eva bhāgaḥ śabdam vyanakti tat anyaḥ vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt eka varṇa bhāga kāle ca samasta rūpa anupalakṣaṇāt tat ayam apratisaṃhita sakale upalambhaḥ dhvani vat upalambha sākalya saṃnidhāna 
PVSV_134,21–134,25	 artham katham sādhayet kaḥ hi viśeṣaḥ atyanta anupalambhe sat asatoḥ upalambha sādhyeṣu artheṣu na ca saṃnidhi mātreṇa sādhanaḥ vyakti apekṣaṇāt sā ca iyam krama bhāvinī sat asatoḥ tulyaḥ upayogaḥ iti dhvanibhiḥ aśakya sādhanam kāryam tatra api tathā iti alam anyena tasmāt na varṇeṣu vākye vā apauruṣeya tā 
PVSV_134,26–135,7	 varṇaḥ anupūrvī vākyam ced na varṇānām abhedataḥ na artha antaram eva śabda rūpam vākyam apauruṣeyam kim tarhi varṇaḥ anukrama lakṣaṇam hi naḥ vākyam tat apauruṣeyam sādhyam iti ced na varṇānām ānupūrvyā abhedāt na iyam artha antaram varṇebhyaḥ dṛśyāyām vibhāgaḥ upalambhāt adṛśyāyām tatas apratipatteḥ liṅga abhāvāt bhedavatyāḥ ca ānupūrvyā abhāve varṇa mātram avaśiṣṭam sarvatra iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ teṣām ca na vyavasthānam krama antara virodhataḥ 
PVSV_135,8–135,12	 yadi akṛtaka anupūrvī varṇānām te ca na bahavaḥ samāna jātīyāḥ yena kecid vyavasthita kramāḥ syuḥ anye yathā iṣṭa parāvṛttayaḥ kim tarhi ekaḥ eva trailokye akāraḥ tathā gakāraḥ tadā agniḥ iti eva syāt na gaganam iti akāra gakārayoḥ pūrva apara bhāvasya vyavasthita tvāt kṛtakānām api hetu pariṇāma niyamavatām 
PVSV_135,13–135,17	 aśakyaḥ krama viparyayaḥ kartum yathā bīja aṅkura patre ādīnām ṛtu saṃvatsaraḥ ādīnām ca kim punar acalita avasthā svabhāvānām akṛtakānām kathaṃcid sthitānām pūrva avasthā tyāgam antareṇa anyathā abhāva ayogāt tyāge vā vināśa prasaṅgāt viśeṣeṇa nityāyām ānupūrvyām tat etat pratipadam krama anya tvam varṇa 
PVSV_135,18–135,23	 anya tve apūrvaḥ utpādāt varṇa bāhulyāt vā syāt tat ca anabhimatam api ca deśa kāla krama abhāvaḥ vyāpti nitya tva varṇanāt sā ca iyam ānupūrvī vā arṇānām deśa kṛtā vā syāt yathā pipīlikānām paṅktau kāla kṛtā vā yathā bīja aṅkuraḥ ādīnām sā dvividhāḥ api varṇeṣu na sambhavati vyāpteḥ nitya tvāt ca anyonya deśa 
PVSV_136,1–136,7	 parihāreṇa vṛttiḥ hi deśa paurvāparyam tat sarvasya sarveṇa tulya deśa tvāt varṇeṣu na sambhavati vātaḥ ātapa vat ātmaḥ ādi vat ca tathā kāla parihāreṇa vṛttiḥ kāla paurvāparyam yadā ekaḥ na asti tadā anyasya bhāvāt tat api nityeṣu na sambhavati sarvadā sarvasya bhāvāt na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tat katham varṇa paurvāparyam vākyam yat apauruṣeyam sādhyeta anitya avyāpitāyām ca doṣaḥ prāk eva kīrtitaḥ 
PVSV_136,8–136,16	 atha mā bhūt ayam doṣaḥ iti anityān avyāpinaḥ ca varṇān icchet tau api pakṣau prāk eva nirākṛtau iti aparihāraḥ vyakti kramaḥ api vākyam na nitya vyakti nirākṛtaḥ na varṇānām rūpa anupūrvī vākyam kim tarhi tat vyakteḥ sā yathā sva varṇaḥ abhivyakti pratyaya kramāt bhavantī krama yoginī iti tadā anupūrvī vākyam iti api mithyā tasyāḥ nityeṣu prāk eva niṣiddha tvāt kārya tā viśeṣaḥ eva sākṣāt śakti upadhānena jñāna janakānām vyaktiḥ iti ākhyātam etat vyāpārāt eva tat siddheḥ karaṇānām ca kārya tā 
PVSV_136,17–136,21	 yat khalu rūpam yatas eva upalabhyate tasya tat upalabdhi na antarīyakām upalabdhim eva āśritya lokaḥ kārya tām prajñāpayati sā varṇeṣu api asti saḥ eva ca anyatra api tat āśrayaḥ na viśeṣaḥ tat katham tulye abhyupagama nibandhane na varṇāḥ kāryāḥ na ca etat upalabdhi āśrayā kārya tā sthitiḥ kim tarhi yat sati eva 
PVSV_136,22–137,1	 bhavati iti sattā āśrayā sā sattā kutas siddhāḥ ye na kārya tām sādhayet na hi asiddhāyām asyām evam bhavati iti tasmāt sattā siddhiḥ tat sādhanī sā ca upalabdhiḥ eva satyam evam yadi tasya prāk na sattā siddhā syāt sā hi sattā siddhiḥ yā asiddhi pūrvikā nanu tat rūpam asiddham eva yat tathā abhūta vijñāna avyavadhāna 
PVSV_137,2–137,6	 upayogi siddham eva tat anyaḥ vaikalyāt naḥ upayuktam iti ced katham idānīm upayukta anupayuktayoḥ abhedaḥ na api bhedaḥ śabda svabhāva asaṃsparśī tasya eva atiśayasya upayoga siddheḥ tasyāḥ kāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt yasya eva bhāve sādhya siddhiḥ tat eva hi tatra upayogi yuktam tat atiśayaḥ upayoge api asya tadvat prasaṅgaḥ 
PVSV_137,7–137,13	 tasmāt atiśetaḥ eva avyavahita sāmarthya upayogaḥ avasthā bhedaḥ tat anyam anatiśayasya apekṣā ca prāk eva niṣiddhāḥ sa ca karaṇa vyāpārāt eva siddhaḥ iti sarva kārya tulya dharmāḥ tasya tādṛśasya vyaktau sarvam vyaṅgyam na vā kiṃcid api aviśeṣāt tathā hi sva jñānena anyaḥ dhī hetuḥ siddhe arthe vyañjakaḥ mataḥ yathā dīpaḥ anyathā vai api kaḥ viśeṣaḥ asya kārakāt 
PVSV_137,14–137,18	 sva pratipatti dvāreṇa anye pratipatti hetuḥ loke vyañjakaḥ siddhaḥ dīpa ādi vat sa ced prāk siddhaḥ syāt samāna jātīyaḥ upādāna kṣaṇa siddheḥ na tasya eva atiśayasya jñāna hetoḥ tasya tat sāmagrī pratyaya tvāt ye punar asiddhaḥ upalambhanāḥ kārakāḥ eva kulāle ādi vat ghaṭaḥ ādau pratyabhijñānaḥ ādayaḥ api siddhi hetavaḥ na hetu lakṣaṇam 
PVSV_137,19–138,2	 puṣṇanti yat api kiṃcid uttarā akāra pratītiḥ akāra pratīteḥ pūrva abhinna viṣayā tadvat iti ādi tat api na sva lakṣaṇayoḥ abheda sādhane samartham tat svabhāva siddheḥ sāmānyena vacane bhinna viṣaya tvasya api avirodhaḥ eka viṣayayoḥ ca pratītyoḥ pūrva apara bhāva ayogāt saṃnihita asaṃnihita kāraṇa tvena utpāda anutpādāt 
PVSV_138,3–138,7	 saṃnidhāne api anutpannasya atat kāraṇa tvāt tayoḥ bhinnaḥ akhila kāraṇa tvam tatra ekaḥ abhede api śaktasya apratīkṣaṇāt yukti viruddham pūrva aparayoḥ pratītyoḥ eka viṣaya tvam prati iti pratibhāsa svabhāva bhede api nāma sāmyāt eka viṣaya tvam api ayuktam ghaṭaḥ ādiṣu api prasaṅgāt tatra dṛṣṭa virodhāt asādhana tvam 
PVSV_138,8–138,15	 iti ced iha api virodha abhāvaḥ kena siddhaḥ yāvat tathā abhidheya tā artha bhedena vyāptā na sādhyate tāvat sandigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ pratikaraṇa bhedam ca bhinna svabhāvaḥ śabdaḥ śrutau niviśamānaḥ yadā ekaḥ sādhyate kim na ghaṭaḥ ādayaḥ tatra api śakyam evam vyañjaka bhedāt pratibhāsa bhedaḥ iti pratyavasthātum api ca karaṇānām samagrāṇām vyāpārāt upalabdhitaḥ niyamena ca kārya tvam vyañjake tat asambhavāt 
PVSV_138,16–138,20	 na hi kadācid vyāpṛteṣu karaṇeṣu śabdaḥ anupalabdhiḥ na ca avaśyam vyañjaka vyāpāraḥ artham upalambhayati kvacid prakāśe api ghaṭaḥ ādi anupalabdheḥ sā iyam niyamena upalabdhiḥ tat vyāpārāt śabdasya tat udbhave syāt akartuḥ vyāpāre api tat siddhi ayogāt vyāpi nitya tvāt upalambhaḥ iti ced kaḥ idānīm ghaṭaḥ ādiṣu 
PVSV_138,21–138,25	 samāśvāsaḥ teṣām tathā aniṣṭeḥ iti ced śabdaḥ kim iṣṭaḥ tat samāna dharmāḥ na ca asya kaścid atiśayaḥ iti uktam pratiṣiddhe ca vyāpi nitya tve ghaṭaḥ ādīnām vyañjaka antara sambhavāt adoṣaḥ prakāśaḥ hi eṣām vyañjakaḥ siddhaḥ kulālaḥ ādīnām vyañjaka tve tādṛśāḥ eva syuḥ atiśerate ca tatas vyañjaka atiśayāt kārakāḥ eva 
PVSV_138,26–139,6	 upakārakasya gati antara abhāvāt tat etat śabdeṣu api tulyam tatra api indriya yogya deśatāḥ ādibhyaḥ karaṇānām atiśayāt ghaṭaḥ ādi kāraka dharmasya ca karaṇeṣu dṛṣṭeḥ tasya eva pradīpaḥ ādeḥ viṣaya antarasya ca kasyacid vyañjaka antara abhāvāt tat kāraṇāni teṣām vyañjakāni syuḥ tasmāt na vyaktiḥ śabdasya bhavantī vā karaṇebhyaḥ atiśayattā vā śabdasya vyaktiḥ āvaraṇa vigamaḥ vijñānam vā gati antara abhāvāt tatra na atiśayaḥ utpattiḥ anitya tā prasaṅgāt tasyāḥ pūrva apara rūpa hāni upajanana lakṣaṇa tvāt atha tat rūpaḥ āvaraṇānām ca vyaktiḥ te vigamaḥ yadi abhāve karaṇa grāma sāmarthyam kim nu tat bhavet 
PVSV_139,7–139,14	 na hi āvaraṇasya akiṃcitkarāṇi karaṇāni samarthāni nāma vigamaḥ ca abhāvaḥ na ca abhāvaḥ kāryam iti niveditam etat na api śabdasya nityasya kiṃcid āvaraṇam asāmarthyāt iti api uktam tasmāt na āvaraṇe karaṇaḥ upakṣepaḥ na api eṣām asāmarthyam tat vyāpāra abhāve śabdaḥ anupalabdheḥ atas yuktam ete yat śabdān kuryuḥ anyathā śabdaḥ aviśeṣāt anyeṣām api vyaktiḥ prasajyate tathā abhyupagame sarva kāraṇānām nirarthatā 
PVSV_139,15–139,19	 yadi sarva kāraṇa samāna dharmāṇi api karaṇāni vyañjakāni na kiṃcid idānīm kāryam syāt na ca etat yuktam sarva kāraṇānām ānarthakya prasaṅgāt vastunaḥ anādheya viśeṣa tvāt āvaraṇa abhāvasya akārya tvāt vastu vat eva jñānasya api siddha tvāt jñānam prati kāraka tve kasyacid tathābhūtānām anyeṣām api tathā abhāva 
PVSV_139,20–139,25	 prasaṅgena sarvasya kārya tā prasaṅgāt tasmāt ayam kāraka abhimataḥ artha kalāpaḥ na vyaktau na kriyāyām iti vyarthaḥ eva syāt tathā ca idam anupakārya upakārakam nirīham jagat syāt śabda nitya tve ca sādhanam pratyabhijñānam sat prayogaḥ ādi yat matam anudāharaṇam sarva bhāvānām kṣaṇa bhaṅgataḥ 
PVSV_140,1–140,5	 kṣaṇa bhaṅginaḥ hi sarve bhāvāḥ vināśasya akāraṇa tvāt iti uktam vakṣyate ca utpattimantaḥ ca paratas sattāyāḥ ākasmika tva ayogāt tat naḥ idam pratyabhijñānam sat prayogaḥ ādikam kvacid anveti sthiraḥ eka rūpe aparāpara svabhāva parāvṛttiṣu eva dīpaḥ ādiṣu dṛṣṭam iti viruddham eva na abhinna janmanaḥ sādharmya vipralambhāt 
PVSV_140,6–140,10	 bhrāntyā dīpaḥ ādiṣu bhāvāt abhinna janma iti kena avaṣṭambhena ucyate tasya eva abhedasya sarvatra paurvāparyeṇa cintya tvāt tathā bhedasya api iti ced tena eva saṃśayaḥ astu na ca saṃśayitāt siddhiḥ viveka adarśanāt ekatvam iti ced na jñāna paurvāparyeṇa sat asat tva siddheḥ svabhāva viveka sadbhāvāt 
PVSV_140,11–140,15	 yadi aparāṇi jñānāni prāk saṃnihita kāraṇāni pūrva jñāna vat jātāni eva syuḥ ajātāni tu kāraṇa vaikalyam sūcayanti samarthasya jananāt asamarthasya api punar sāmarthya apratilambhāt pratilambhe vā sthairya ayogāt tat ayam sat prayogaḥ iti api jananam eva prayoktuḥ sāmarthyāt svayam samarthe tasya anupayogāt 
PVSV_140,16–140,26	 prayogaḥ iti api iṣṭa sādhana samarthaḥ utpādanam eva samāna jātīyaḥ upādāna apekṣam anapekṣam vā vā asi ādi prayoga vat karma ādi prayoga vat ca kathyate yaḥ api manyate samakṣe pratyabhijñānam pratyakṣam eva tatas pratyakṣāt eva sthairya siddhiḥ iti tat api uttaratra niṣetsyāmaḥ dūṣyaḥ kuhetuḥ anyaḥ api na eva kaścid dharmaḥ yaḥ samāna jātīyam anveti sarva dharmāṇām etat avastha tvāt sarve sthairya pratijñāyāḥ ca yathā abhidhānam yukti virodhāt anye api nitya hetavaḥ vācya doṣāḥ buddheḥ apuruṣaḥ āśraye bādhāḥ abhyupeta pratyakṣa pratīta anumitaiḥ samam 
PVSV_140,27–141,9	 yadi vyaktiḥ buddhiḥ tadā ānupūrvī vādyam tasyāḥ apauruṣeya tva prasādhane buddhīnām puruṣa guṇa tva abhyupagamāt sama yaḥ asya bādhyate pratyakṣam khalu api etat yat imāḥ buddhayaḥ puruṣa saṃkhyātebhyaḥ puruṣa guṇebhyaḥ vā manaskāraḥ ādibhyaḥ bhavanti iti na ca kārya tā nāma anyāḥ bhāvaḥ abhāva viśeṣābhyām sa ca bhāvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ abhāvaḥ api anupalabdhi lakṣaṇaḥ pratyakṣa sāmarthya siddhaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ tatas eva puruṣa kārya tā buddhīnām anumeya anvaya vyatireka liṅga tvāt asyāḥ kim ca ānupūrvyāḥ ca varṇebhyaḥ bhedaḥ sphoṭena cintitaḥ kalpanā āropitā sā syāt katham vā apuruṣaḥ āśrayāḥ 
PVSV_141,10–141,14	 varṇa vyatirekiṇī ānupūrvī sphoṭa vicāra anukrameṇa eva prativihitāḥ na api sā varṇa svabhāvāḥ vastu svabhāvasya etat vikalpa anatikramāt atat rūpeṣu tat rūpa samāropa pratibhāsinyā buddheḥ ayam vibhramaḥ syāt ānupūrvī iti sā ca katham apauruṣeyī buddhi viṭhapana pratyupasthāpanāt api ca ātyantikasya kasyacid 
PVSV_141,15–141,20	 svabhāvasya abhāvāt bhavatā dhvaninā anātyantikena bhavitavyam sa ca ahetukaḥ anyaḥ hetukaḥ vā nityam bhavet na ca puruṣa vyāpārāt tasmāt na apauruṣeyaḥ katham idam gamyate anātyantikaḥ dhvaniḥ anyaḥ vā bhāvaḥ iti sattā mā atra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya anitya tā dhvaneḥ na hi nāśaḥ bhāvānām kutaścid bhavati tat bhāva svabhāvaḥ bhavet 
PVSV_141,21–141,25	 bhāvasya eva sva hetubhyaḥ tat dharmaṇaḥ bhāvāt na ca bhāva viśeṣa svabhāvaḥ tasya niṣetsyamāna tvāt tasmāt bhāva mā atra svabhāvaḥ syāt tena śabdaḥ anyaḥ vā sattā bhājanaḥ sarve eva bhāvaḥ anātyantikaḥ iti siddham na siddham tasya eva vināśasya apara janma asiddheḥ tathā hi agninā kāṣṭham daṇḍena 
PVSV_142,1–142,6	 ghaṭaḥ iti vināśa hetavaḥ bhāvānām dṛśyante anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam hetu tadvatoḥ lakṣaṇam āhuḥ na pūrvasya sva rasa nirodhe anyasya viśiṣṭa pratyayaḥ āśrayeṇa vikṛtasya utpatteḥ astu vai agniḥ kāṣṭha vināśa hetuḥ sa vināśaḥ agni janmā kim kāṣṭham eva āhosvit artha antaram agneḥ artha antaraḥ utpattau bhavet kāṣṭhasya darśanam 
PVSV_142,7–142,14	 avināśāt kim iti artha antarāt artha antara janmani kāṣṭham abhūtam nāma na dṛśyate vā atiprasaṅgaḥ hi evam syāt saḥ eva asya vināśaḥ iti ced yadi saḥ eva arthaḥ agni janmā abhāvaḥ tat idam abhūta tvāt na dṛśyate iti bhavatu tasya idam nāma abhāvaḥ iti tathā api katham anyaḥ anyasya vināśaḥ na hi kasyacid arthasya nāma karaṇa mātreṇa 
PVSV_142,15–142,19	 kāṣṭham na dṛśyate iti yuktam na ca anyaḥ anyasya vināśaḥ atiprasaṅgāt viśeṣa abhāvāt tasya artha antara tvena vastu bhūtasya tat anyebhyaḥ kāṣṭhe agni kṛtaḥ svabhāvaḥ vināśaḥ na sarve iti ced kāṣṭhāḥ iti kaḥ sambandhaḥ āśraya āśrayi sambandhaḥ ced na tasya niṣetsyamāna tvāt janya janaka bhāvāḥ ced agneḥ iti 
PVSV_142,20–142,24	 kim kāṣṭhāt eva bhāvāt tat apekṣāt utpatteḥ adoṣaḥ iti ced anatiśaya lābhinaḥ kā apekṣāḥ lābhe vā apara kāṣṭha janma syāt pūrvam tu apracyuti kāraṇam tathā eva dṛśyate tatas eva agneḥ pūrva vināśaḥ iti ced pūrveṇa asya kaḥ sambandhaḥ iti saḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ aparyavasānaḥ ca tat avaśyam vināśa sambandha yogyam uttaram 
PVSV_142,25–143,5	 atiśayam pratyupakurvāṇaḥ agniḥ apūrvam eva janayati iti pūrvam tat avastham dṛśyeta kāṣṭha vināśaḥ iti ca kāṣṭha abhāvaḥ ucyate na ca abhāvaḥ kāryaḥ tat kārī ca akārakaḥ eva iti anapekṣaṇīyaḥ iti uktam svabhāva abhāvasya ca tatas bhede tatas nivartamānasya bhāvasya svabhāvaḥ eva samarthitaḥ syāt iti katham abhūtaḥ nāma tasmāt na anyaḥ anyasya vināśaḥ astu kāṣṭham kasmāt na dṛśyate 
PVSV_143,6–143,16	 kaḥ ayam artha antara bhāva kāṣṭha darśanayoḥ virodhaḥ tat parigrahataḥ ced na tena anāvaraṇam yatas yadi tena artha antareṇa parigṛhītam iti kāṣṭham na dṛśyeta tat kāṣṭhasya āvaraṇam iti āpannam na ca etat yuktam āvaraṇam hi darśanam bibadhnīyāt na abhighāṭaḥ ādīni dravya sāmarthyāni sarve pratibandhe ca nanu anena eva dravyam vināśitam syāt sarva śakti pracyāvanāt punar tatra api agnau iva prasaṅgāt anavasthā apracyuteṣu vai asya abhighāṭa sāmarthya ādiṣu satā vā tena anyena kim vināśitam yadi ca agni samudbhavasya vināśaḥ ākhyasya arthasya parigrahāt kāṣṭham na dṛṣṭam vināśasya vināśi tvam syāt utpatteḥ tatas punar 
PVSV_143,17–144,3	 kāṣṭhasya darśanam avaśyam hi utpattimatā vināśena vinaṣṭavyam tasmin vinaṣṭe punar kāṣṭhaḥ ādīnām unmajjanam syāt hantṛ ghāte caitra apunarbhavaḥ yathā atra api evam iti ced dhantuḥ na amaraṇa tvataḥ vināśa vināśe api ca vastunaḥ pratyāpattiḥ na hi hantari hate api tadvatas pratyujjīvati iti ced na hantuḥ tat ghāta hetu tvāt na brūmaḥ vināśa hetoḥ agni daṇḍaḥ ādeḥ nivṛttau bhāvena bhavitavyam iti kim tarhi bhāva abhāvasya atyanta anupalabdhi lakṣaṇasya tat nivṛttau kā anyā gatiḥ svabhāva sthiteḥ hantā hi caitrasya na nāśa kalpaḥ kim tarhi daṇḍaḥ ādi kalpaḥ na āśa kalpam hi asya maraṇam tat nivṛttau ca syāt eva asya punarbhāvaḥ ananya tve api nāśasya syāt nāśaḥ kāṣṭham eva tu tasya sattvāt ahetu tvam na atas anyā vidyate gatiḥ 
PVSV_144,4–144,8	 anartha antara bhūtaḥ vināśaḥ kāṣṭhāt tat eva tat bhavati tat ca prāk eva asti iti kim atra sāmarthyam vahni ādīnām tasmāt tat anupakārāt tena na apekṣyante kathaṃcid na api asya idam iti sambandham arhati tasya upakāra nibandhana tvāt anyathā atiprasaṅgāt pāraṃparyeṇa upakāre api avaśyam ayam vikalpaḥ anveti 
PVSV_144,9–144,16	 sa kim upakāraḥ artha antaram āhosvit tat eva iti tat artha antara tve api tasya iti punar upakāra tvaḥ ādi paryanuyogaḥ tat avasthā eva tathā ananya tve tasmāt sataḥ rūpasya tattva anyat tva avyatikramāt upakāraḥ utpādanasya ca rūpa niṣpādana lakṣaṇa tvāt tat atat kriyā vikalaḥ na kartā eva iti na kasyacid hetuḥ ahetuḥ ca na apekṣate tasmāt svayam ayam bhāvaḥ tat svabhāvaḥ iti siddham ahetu tve api nāśasya nitya tvāt bhāva nāśayoḥ sahabhāva prasaṅgaḥ ced asataḥ nityatā kutas 
PVSV_144,17–144,23	 syāt etat yasya api vināśaḥ ahetukaḥ saḥ avaśyam nityaḥ iti bhāvaḥ tat abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ vināśaḥ ca saha syātām iti na tasya nitya anitya dharma ayogāt na hi asati ayam vikalpaḥ sambhavati tayoḥ vastu dharma tvāt vināśasya ca akiṃcitvāt bhavataḥ hi kenacid sahabhāvaḥ syāt na ca vināśaḥ bhavati tasmāt adoṣaḥ asattve abhāva nāśitva prasaṅgaḥ api na yujyate yasmāt bhāvasya nāśena na vināśanam iṣyate 
PVSV_144,24–145,3	 katham asan vināśaḥ bhāvam nāśayet atas avināśī bhāvaḥ syāt iti aprasaṅgaḥ eva vināśāt bhāva nāśa anabhyupagamāt yaḥ hi vināśaḥ iti kiṃcid naḥ iti āha sa katham tatas bhāva nāśam icchet katham idānīm asati vināśe bhāvaḥ naṣṭaḥ nāma na hi asat vināśāḥ naṣṭāḥ gaṇyante pratyutpanna avasthāyām na hi yaḥ yena atadvān 
PVSV_145,4–145,13	 sa tena tathā vyapadiśyate pratīyate vā yathā aśvaḥ viṣāṇena na vai vināśaḥ na asti eva sa tu na asti yaḥ bhāvasya bhavanti bhāvaḥ eva tu kṣaṇa sthiti dharmāḥ vināśaḥ tam asya svabhāvam uttara kālam vibhāvayantaḥ vināśaḥ asya bhūtaḥ iti yathā prati iti vyapadiśanti iti uktam na hi bhāvasya kiṃcid kadācid bhavati saḥ eva kevalam sva hetubhyaḥ tathābhūtaḥ bhavati tat na kenacid bhavatā sa naṣṭaḥ kim tarhi svabhāvaḥ eva asya yena sa naṣṭaḥ nāma katham tarhi idānīm ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ bhavati iti ucyate naśyan bhāvaḥ apara apekṣaḥ iti tat jñāpanāya sā avasthā ahetuḥ uktāḥ asyāḥ bhedam āropya cetasā 
PVSV_145,14–145,18	 na bhāvaḥ jātaḥ aparasmāt nāśam pratilabhate tathābhūtasya eva svayam jāteḥ iti apara apekṣa dharma antara pratiṣedha artham tat svabhāva jñāpanena artha antaram iva dharmiṇaḥ dharmam cetasā vibhajya tat mā atra jijñāsāyām svabhāvaḥ eva tathā ucyate tat etat manda buddhayaḥ kvacid tathā darśanāt ghoṣa mā atra vipralabdhā 
PVSV_145,19–145,26	 nāśam guṇam tasya ca bhāvam āropya sa hetukam ahetukam vā apratiṣṭhita tattvayā bhāva cintayā ātmānam ākulayanti svatas api bhāve abhāvasya vikalpaḥ ced ayam samaḥ nanu apara bhāvi tve api vināśasya svatas eva bhāvasya bhavataḥ ayam tattva anyat tva vikalpaḥ tulyaḥ tadā kim artha antara bhāve bhāvaḥ na dṛśyate anartha antara tve api tat eva tat bhavati tat na kiṃcid asya jātam iti katham vinaṣṭaḥ nāma nanu atra na tasya kiṃcid bhavati na bhavati eva kevalam 
PVSV_145,27–145,31	 iti uktam na hi ayam vināśaḥ anyaḥ vā kaścid bhāvasya bhavati iti āha kim tarhi saḥ eva bhāvaḥ na bhavati iti yadi hi kasyacid bhāvam brūyāt na bhāvaḥ anena nivartitaḥ syāt tathā ca bhāva nivṛttau prastutāyām aprastutam eva uktam syāt na hi kasyacid bhāvena bhāvaḥ na bhūtaḥ nāma tadā na bhūtaḥ yadi svayam na 
PVSV_146,1–146,5	 bhavet na bhavati iti ca prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ eṣa na paryudāsaḥ anyathā iha api kasyacid bhāve na pratiṣedha paryudāsayaḥ rūpa bhedaḥ syāt ubhayatra vidheḥ prādhānyāt evam ca apratiṣedhāt kasyacid paryudāsaḥ api kvacid na syāt yadi hi kiṃcid kutaścid nivarteta tadā tat vyatireki saṃspṛśyeta tat paryudāsena tat 
PVSV_146,6–146,10	 ca na asti sarvatra nivṛttiḥ bhavati iti ukte kasyacid bhāvasya eva pratītiḥ tathā ca anena artha antara bhāvaḥ eva uktaḥ syāt na tayoḥ parasparam vivekaḥ aviveke ca na paryudāsaḥ tat evam vyatireka abhāvāt anvayaḥ api na syāt tasya eka svabhāva sthiti lakṣaṇa tvāt tat sthitiḥ ca tat anyaḥ vyatireke sati syāt sa ca na asti iti apravṛtti 
PVSV_146,11–146,15	 nivṛttikam jagat syāt tasmāt yasya nāśaḥ bhavati iti ucyate sa svayam eva na bhavati iti uktam syāt na vai ghoṣa sāmyāt viṣaya antara dṛṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ sarvatra yojanām arhati na hi gardabhaḥ iti nāma karaṇāt bāleya dharmāḥ manuṣye api saṃyojyāḥ tathā na caitrasya putraḥ bhavati iti atra dṛṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ nāśe api virodhāt 
PVSV_146,16–146,21	 evam ca abhidhāne api prayojanam āveditam eva atas bhāve hi eṣa vikalpaḥ syāt vidheḥ vastu anurodhataḥ bhāvaḥ avaśyam bhavantam apekṣate sa ca svabhāvaḥ eva niḥsvabhāvasya kvacid vyāpāre samāveśa abhāvāt vyāpāraḥ iti hi tathā abhūta svabhāvaḥ utpattiḥ sā niḥsvabhāvasya katham syāt katham idānīm bhavati abhāvaḥ śaśa viṣāṇam iti ādi vyavahāraḥ 
PVSV_146,22–146,26	 na vai śaśa viṣāṇam kiṃcid bhavati iti ucyate api tu evam asya na bhavati iti bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ eva kriyate api ca vyavahartāraḥ eva etat evam vyāpāra vat iva samāropya ādarśayanti prakaraṇena kenacid na tu tat tathā sarve artha vivecanam hi tatra tattvam na kasyacid samāveśaḥ na khalu evam vināśaḥ vastuni 
PVSV_146,27–147,3	 tat bhāvāt asau api yadi vaktṛbhiḥ evam khyāpyate na tu svayam tathā tadā na kiṃcid bhavati iti iṣṭam eva tasmāt svayam bhavan svabhāvaḥ vikalpa dvayam na ativartate tattvam anyat tvam iti atattvam eva svabhāvasya anyat tvam na hi rūpa rasayoḥ api anyat eva parasparam anyat tvam svabhāva apratibandhaḥ 
PVSV_147,4–147,8	 anyat tvam iti ced kaḥ ayam pratibandhaḥ nāma yena sa ca na syāt na anya svabhāvaḥ ca janma iti ced sarva kāraṇānām parasparam avācya tā syāt tathā ca sarvaḥ sarvasya kathaṃcid upayogi iti na kaścid kutaścid anyaḥ syāt evam ca avācya tā iti api kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva śabda antareṇa uktaḥ syāt na artha bhedaḥ svabhāva ananugamanam 
PVSV_147,9–147,14	 tu anyat tvam brūmaḥ sa ca svabhāvavatām parasparam asti eva iti anyat tvam eva na ca tat janma lakṣaṇāt svabhāva pratibandhāt anyaḥ pratibandhaḥ nāma anāyattasya vyabhicāra avirodhāt tatas dharma bhedāt ca anyat tvam jñāna kṛtaḥ pratibandhaḥ iti ced syāt etat yat pratipatti na antarīyakam yat jñānam tat gatau niyamena tat pratibhāsanāt tat atat rūpam 
PVSV_147,15–147,19	 api avācyam iti na tasya niḥsvabhāva tvāt svayam saḥ eva hi tasya svabhāvaḥ yaḥ pratibhāti svabhāvavat tve asya tadvat pratibhāsa prasaṅgāt apratibhāsamānasya ca dṛśya abhāvāt adṛśya tve api na tat rūpam jñānam iti kasya kim āyattā pratipattiḥ na ca yat yat āyattā pratītikam tasya svabhāva pratibhāsaḥ eva naśyati 
PVSV_147,20–147,24	 prakāśaḥ āyatta pratītīnām iva nīlaḥ ādīnām kā vā tasya pratyāsattiḥ tatra yat tasmin anātma rūpe pratīyamāne sa svayam pratyupatiṣṭhate atiprasaṅgaḥ hi evam syāt pratīyamānasya tat upādānatā iti ced kaḥ ayam upādāna arthaḥ na kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā na kārya kāraṇe anyonya 
PVSV_147,25–148,7	 prati iti pratyupasthāpane pratīteḥ eva tat na antarīyaka tā pratyāsattiḥ iti ced nanu saḥ eva asati pratibandhe na yuktāḥ iti ucyate na akārya kāraṇayoḥ kaścid pratibandhaḥ iti ca uktam yat pratipatti na antarīyakam yat jñānam iti api tat jñāne sati syāt na hi yaḥ vijñāne svarūpeṇa asvarūpa asaṃsargeṇa na pratibhāsate tasya kiṃcid jñānam tat abhāvāt na sidhyati avācya tā lakṣaṇam artha rūpasya tat bhavatā vastutas tattva anyat tva bhājā bhavitavyam yasya tu vinaśyataḥ bhāvasya na kiṃcid bhavati tena na bhāvaḥ bhavati iti uktam abhāvaḥ bhavati iti api 
PVSV_148,8–148,13	 yat api ayam bhāvasya abhāvaḥ bhavati iti āha tat api bhāvaḥ na bhavati iti eva uktam bhavati evam hi sa nivartitaḥ bhavati pratiṣedhe vidheḥ asambhavāt tatas eva asya vināśe na kaścid hetuḥ tathā hi apekṣyeta paraḥ kāryam yadi vidyata kiṃcana yat akiṃcitkaram vastu kim kenacid apekṣyate 
PVSV_148,14–148,18	 sati hi kārye kāraṇam bhavati na ca naśyataḥ bhāvasya kiṃcid kāryam iti uktam tasmāt yaḥ nāma nāśa hetuḥ sa bhāve na kiṃcid karoti iti akiṃcitkaraḥ na apekṣyaṇīyaḥ tat katham idānīm anutpannaḥ atiśayaḥ tat avasthaḥ eva bhāvaḥ naṣṭaḥ nāma nanu atiśayaḥ utpattau api saḥ eva tasya atiśayaḥ utpannaḥ iti katham 
PVSV_148,19–148,26	 sa naṣṭaḥ nāma tena na ayam tat avasthaḥ naṣṭaḥ nāma yena svayam na bhavati tena naṣṭaḥ na artha antaraḥ utpādāt iti uktam na hi atiśayaḥ utpattyā svayam na bhūtaḥ nāma abhāvasya sarve atiśayaḥ upākhyā nivṛttyā sarve bhāva dharma viveka lakṣaṇa tvāt bhāvasya ca utpatti samāveśa lakṣaṇa tvāt tasmāt na abhāve kasyacid bhāvaḥ upakṣepaḥ anyasya etena ahetuka tve api hi abhūtvā nāśa bhāvataḥ sattā nāśitva doṣasya pratyākhyātam prasañjanam 
PVSV_148,27–149,5	 yaḥ api manyate ahetuke api vināśe abhūtvā asya bhāvāt sattā anitya tvam ca durnivāram abhūtvā bhavan ahetukaḥ bhavati iti api viruddham iti saḥ api anenaḥ eva pratyākhyātaḥ kasyacid bhāvān abhyupagamāt yathā keṣāṃcid eva iṣṭaḥ pratighaḥ janminām tathā nāśaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvānām na anutpattimatām yadi 
PVSV_149,6–149,11	 atha api syāt bhavatu nāma svabhāvaḥ eṣa bhāvānām ye ime kṣaṇa sthiti dharmāṇāḥ sa tu utpattimatām eva bhaviṣyati na hi svabhāvaḥ iti sarvaḥ sarvasya svabhāvaḥ bhavati pratighaḥ ātma tā vat satyam etat tathā api svabhāva niyamāt hetoḥ svabhāva niyamaḥ phale na anitye rūpa bhedaḥ asti bhedakānām abhāvataḥ 
PVSV_149,12–149,16	 na vai pratighaḥ anyaḥ vā svabhāvaḥ akasmāt pratiniyamavān yādṛśī tu sva hetoḥ śakti sthitiḥ tādṛśam phalam bhavati iti hetu svabhāva niyamāt phala svabhāva niyamaḥ ākasmika tve api asya uktaḥ doṣaḥ pratighātaḥ ātma tā hetu svabhāva pratiniyama vat na naśvara janana pratiniyata svabhāvam bhāvam paśyāmaḥ yena tat janmā 
PVSV_149,17–149,21	 tathā syāt na anyaḥ sarve ākāra janmanām vināśa darśanāt nanu idam api aniśceyam eva sarve ākāra janmānaḥ naśyanti iti tāsām aniḥśeṣa darśanāt vicitra śaktayaḥ hi sāmagryaḥ dṛśyante tatra kācid syāt api yā anaśvaraḥ ātmānam janayet na jñeyaḥ adhikārāt ye kadācid kvacid kenacid jñātāḥ santaḥ na jñāyante 
PVSV_149,22–149,26	 teṣām sattā anubandhī nāśaḥ iti brūmaḥ te eva kṛtakāḥ anityāḥ sādhyante na hi ayam sambhavaḥ asti yat te jñāna janana svabhāvāḥ punar anaṣṭāḥ na janayeyuḥ apekṣeran vā param tat janana svabhāvasya niṣpatteḥ na ca teṣu anapekṣeṣu kasyacid kadācid kiṃcid jñānam nivarteta na ca evaṃbhūtam kiṃcid asti 
PVSV_149,27–150,4	 sarvasya kenacid kadācid jñānāt jñāna mā atra artha kriyāyām api asāmarthye vastu eva na syāt tathā hi tat lakṣaṇam vastu iti vakṣyāmaḥ tasya ca vināśa avyabhicārāt sa sattā anubandhī pratyākhyeyāḥ atas eva eṣām sambandhasya api nityatā atas eva yathā uktāt vastu mā atra anubandhāt vināśasya śabda vat 
PVSV_150,5–150,13	 sambandha nityatā api pratyākhyeyāḥ yā ca śabda śaktiḥ yogyatā ākhyāḥ artha pratipattyā āśrayaḥ jaiminīyaiḥ varṇyate sa artha antaram eva na bhavati tathā hi yogya tā iti rūpa atiśayaḥ eva bhāvānām iti āveditam prāk astu vai artha antaram tathā api sambandha doṣaiḥ prāk uktaiḥ śabda śaktiḥ ca dūṣitā uktaḥ hi sambandha artha antara vāde aneka prakāraḥ doṣaḥ tena eva sā śabda śaktiḥ dūṣitāḥ iti na punar ucyate api ca na apauruṣeyam iti eva yathā artha jñāna sādhanam dṛṣṭaḥ anyathā api vahni ādiḥ aduṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ āgasāḥ 
PVSV_150,14–150,18	 bhavantu nāma apauruṣeyāḥ vaidikāḥ śabdāḥ tathā api sambhāvyam eva eṣām ayathārtha jñāna hetu tvam na hi puruṣa doṣaḥ upadhānāt eva artheṣu jñāna vibhramaḥ tat rahitānām api pradīpaḥ ādīnām nīlaḥ utpala ādiṣu vitatha jñāna jananāt tat ime śabdāḥ saṃskāra nirapekṣāḥ prakṛtyā ca artheṣu pratibhāna hetavaḥ syuḥ svabhāva viśeṣāt 
PVSV_150,19–150,23	 vahni ādi vat vitatha vyaktayaḥ ca niyamena eva niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt ayuktam iti ced avitatha vyakti niyame kim kāraṇam tasmāt yathārtha vyakti niyama vat prakṛtyāḥ ayathārtha vyakti niyamaḥ kim na kalpyate athavā vahni ādi vat eva artheṣu ubhaya jñāna hetu tvam syāt na hi apauruṣeyāḥ api vahni ādaya 
PVSV_150,24–151,4	 ekatra yathārtha jñāna hetavaḥ api sarvatra tathā bhavanti iti tathā śabdānām api apauruṣeya tve api ubhayam syāt iti bhavatu vahni ādīnām kṛtaka tvāt yathā pratyayam anyatra anyathātvam na punar nityeṣu śabdeṣu etat asti nanu evaṃvidhaḥ anyatra api asti eva dharmaḥ teṣām api saṃketa balāt anyathā vṛtteḥ kārya janana svabhāva sthitau ca eṣām samayaḥ ādeḥ apekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt tatas pratītiḥ artheṣu sarvasya sarvadā syāt na ca asti tasmāt na śabdāḥ sthita svabhāvāḥ iti api ca na jñāna hetu tāḥ eva syāt tasmin akṛtake mate nityebhyaḥ avastu sāmarthyāt na hi janma asti kasyacid 
PVSV_151,5–151,9	 yadi akṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ na tasmāt artheṣu pratītiḥ eva syāt prati iti janmaḥ itara kālayoḥ tulya rūpasya prati iti janmani sāmarthya sambhāvanāḥ ayogāt evam ayam janakaḥ naḥ evam iti vivecanīyasya rūpa bhedasya abhāvāt na yādṛśaḥ asya ajanakaḥ tādṛśaḥ eva janakaḥ yuktaḥ anyaḥ apekṣāḥ api niṣiddhāḥ eva tasmāt na nityānām kvacid 
PVSV_151,10–151,15	 vijñāna janana sāmarthyam kadācid ajanane nityam ajanana prasaṅgāt kārya sātatya adarśanāt ca na te kathaṃcid kartāraḥ iti ukta prāyam yāḥ api etāḥ nitya abhimateṣu ākāśaḥ ādiṣu pratipattayaḥ tāḥ api na tat svabhāva bhāvinyaḥ tathā hi vikalpa vāsanāḥ udbhūtāḥ samāropita gocarāḥ jāyante buddhayaḥ tatra kevalam na artha gocarāḥ 
PVSV_151,16–151,20	 sva lakṣaṇa viṣayā hi buddhiḥ niyamena tat yogyatā upasthāpana anuvidhāyinī iti tasmin sati asyāḥ kāraṇe yogye sā bhavati eva tat yadi nityānām padārthānām sva lakṣaṇe kasyacid jñānam syāt sarvasya sarvadā syāt kārya viśeṣāḥ hi vyaktayaḥ kathaṃcid kvacid upayujyamānāḥ tat upajanana yogya atiśaya pratilambha hetum 
PVSV_151,21–151,25	 vastu viśeṣam apekṣante iti yuktam tathā akārya viśeṣaḥ nityaḥ bhāvaḥ kenacid gṛhyamāṇaḥ tat kāraṇa apekṣaḥ yadi grahaṇam asya janayet yuktam yat tena eva gṛhyeta tat ca sthita svabhāva tvāt na sambhavati iti sarveṇa samam gṛhyeta na vā kenacid iti san kenacid dṛṣṭaḥ na nityaḥ kaścid atīndriyaḥ syāt na ca etat asti 
PVSV_151,26–152,2	 tasmāt artha sāmarthya anapekṣāḥ samāropita gocarāḥ āntaram eva upādānam vikalpa vāsanā prabodham āśritya bāhya artha śūnyāḥ bhrāntayaḥ eva ākāśaḥ ādiṣu sarvasya sambhavanti iti tasmāt na aparāvṛtti dharmāḥ śabdāḥ tattve vā kutas etat avitathaḥ artha pratītayaḥ eva iti na hi agniḥ himasya bheṣajam iti ādiṣu śīta pratighāta 
PVSV_152,3–152,7	 sāmarthyam loka prasiddham agneḥ khyāpyate iti sarvam tathā bhavati lokasya svaḥ icchā kṛta saṃketa anuvyavahārāt kim ayam lokaḥ sva saṃketam anuvidadhat evam pratyeti āhosvit śabda svabhāva sthiteḥ iti sandehaḥ loke icchayā api parāvartyamānāḥ śabdāḥ punar anyatra anyathā dṛśyante iti loka prasiddhi anuvidhāne 
PVSV_152,8–152,13	 api sambhavati eṣām anyathā bhāvaḥ tasmāt kasyacid avaiparītya darśane api sarveṣām tathā abhāvaḥ na sidhyati akṛtaka svabhāva tve api hi eṣām kaścid mithyā artha niyataḥ api syāt iti svabhāva aparijñānāt sarvatra saṃśayaḥ syāt mithyātvam kṛtakeṣu eva dṛṣṭam iti akṛtam vacaḥ satya artham vyatirekasya virodhi vyāpanāt yadi 
PVSV_152,14–152,23	 atha yat mithyā artham vacanam tat akhilam kṛtakam iti hetu vyatirekeṇa sādhya vyatirekasya vyāpteḥ anyatra asambhavāt akṛtakam satya artham iti syāt vinā api anvayena yaḥ hi yena avyāptaḥ tatra tat vyatirekaḥ śaṅkyeta na ca viruddhayoḥ ekatra sambhavaḥ asti asambhave ca vijātīyasya gati antara abhāvāt iṣṭa artha siddheḥ tat sādhana tvāt ca liṅgasya vyartham anvaya darśanam vyatireka mātreṇa eva siddheḥ iti satyam etat yadi vipakṣayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ sidhyet sa tu na siddhaḥ yasmāt hetau asambhave anukte bhāvaḥ tasya api śaṅkyate viruddhānām padārthānām api vyāpaka darśanāt 
PVSV_152,24–153,2	 yadi hetoḥ sādhya vipakṣe abhāvaḥ sidhyet tadā sādhya vyatirekam hetu vyatirekaḥ vyāpnuyāt na ca tatra tasya asambhave pramāṇam paśyāmaḥ na ca aviruddha vidhiḥ pratiṣedha sādhanaḥ yuktaḥ atiprasaṅgāt na ca ekatra dṛṣṭasya anyatra asambhavaḥ eva pṛthak viruddha saha bhāvinām api darśanāt anitya tva vat prayatna anantarīyakaḥ itarayoḥ na ca tathāvidhasya adarśanāt asattvam eva yasmāt na asattā siddhiḥ iti uktam sarvatas anupalambhanāt asiddhāyām asattāyām sandigdhā vyatirekitā 
PVSV_153,3–153,7	 na hi ayam puruṣa mātrakaḥ sarvam draṣṭum samarthaḥ yena asya darśana nivṛttyā na tathā syāt yasya hi jñānam jñeya sattām na vyabhicarati saḥ evam bruvāṇaḥ śobheta adarśanāt na asti iti tat ime svabhāva deśa kāla viprakarṣeṇa santaḥ api anupalakṣyāḥ syuḥ tathā hi kaḥ atyanta parokṣe arthe saṃvādanam itarad 
PVSV_153,8–153,12	 vā sarva darśī vacanasya akṛtakasya itarasya vā vibhāvayitum samarthaḥ pratipāditam ca etat kvacid tathā dṛṣṭānām api arthānām punar kathaṃcid anyathā bhāvaḥ yathā kvacid deśe madhurāṇi nimba phalāni saṃskāra viśeṣāt āmalakī phalāni ca na ca idānīm atat darśinā tāni pratikṣeptavyāni eva iti tasmāt akṛtakam 
PVSV_153,13–153,18	 ca syāt syāt mithyā artham ca iti na virodham paśyāmaḥ na hi iyam anupalabdhiḥ adṛśyaḥ ātmasu abhāva sa adhikāḥ iti uktam tena yat kiṃcid mithyā artham tat sarvam pauruṣeyam iti aniścayāt avyāptiḥ tathā hi anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā sattvam vā sādhya dharmiṇi tat niścaya phalaiḥ jñānaiḥ sidhyanti yadi sādhanam 
PVSV_153,19–153,24	 tathā ca uktam yaḥ eva tu ubhaya niścita vācī sa sādhanam dūṣaṇam vā na anyatara prasiddha sandigdha vācī punar sādhana apekṣa tvāt iti kaḥ hi adṛṣṭa virodhasya sambhavam pratyācakṣīta tat ayam vyatirekaḥ saṃśayāt asādhanam api ca yatra sādhya vipakṣasya varṇyate vyatirekitā saḥ eva asya sa pakṣaḥ syāt sarvaḥ hetuḥ atas anvayī 
PVSV_154,1–154,5	 yat kiṃcid mithyā artham tat sarvam pauruṣeyam iti hetu vipakṣeṇa sādhya vipakṣasya vyāptiḥ tat abhāve abhāva siddhau syāt tat abhāve bhavataḥ tena vyāpti ayogāt yāḥ eva ca vijātīyayoḥ vyāvṛtti siddhiḥ sā eva anvaya sthitiḥ vipakṣa vyavaccheda lakṣaṇa tvāt sādhyasya pratiṣedha dvayāt ca vidhi siddhiḥ iti kā ananvaya avyatireka vyāpti 
PVSV_154,6–154,10	 siddhiḥ tat na kaścid hetuḥ ananvayaḥ nāma eka vyavacchedasya tat vijātīya siddhi na antarīyaka tvāt anitya nirātmatā ādi vyavacchede api tathā syāt na vyatireka vyavacchedasya bhāva rūpa tvāt na bhāva rūpa vyavacchede bhāva anuṣaṅgaḥ abhāva vyavacchedaḥ tu niyamena bhāvaḥ upasthāpanaḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ anyonya viveka 
PVSV_154,11–154,15	 rūpa tvāt abhāva rūpaḥ tu vyatirekaḥ sa ca vyatiricyamānaḥ bhāvam upasthāpayati na evam nairātmyaḥ ādayaḥ svabhāva viśeṣāt kriyā bhoga adhiṣṭhāna asvatantraḥ hi ātmā nirātmā tat svātantrya lakṣaṇa tvāt ātmanaḥ tat rūpam nairātmyam naḥ ātma nivṛtti mātram anyathā nirupākhye kṛtaka tvaḥ ādi ayogāt na tatas nairātmya 
PVSV_154,16–154,20	 siddhiḥ syāt ātma vyavacchedena nirātmanaḥ bhāvasya parāmarśāt adoṣaḥ iti ced paryudāsena vastu saṃsparśāt tat eva vastu rūpam nairātmyam āyātam yasya api na abhāva rūpaḥ vyatirekaḥ tasya bhāva rūpa vyavacchede na bhāva siddhiḥ syāt iti na anvaya anuṣaṅgaḥ tathā anairātmye api na bhāva siddhiḥ yathā 
PVSV_154,21–154,25	 na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇaḥ ādimattvāt iti vipakṣayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva cintāyām aprāṇaḥ ādimattvaḥ eva nairātmyam dṛṣṭam tat abhāve ca na asti iti svayam na bhavat api prāṇaḥ ādīnām naḥ ātmani siddhim upasthāpayati tathā sādhye api prāṇaḥ ādibhiḥ vyudasyamānam syāt kevalam nairātmye abhāvāt prāṇa 
PVSV_154,26–154,30	 ādayaḥ tat nirasanāḥ naḥ ātmaḥ upasthāpanāḥ tatra bhāva asiddheḥ na ca nairātmya nivṛttyā ātma siddhiḥ syāt vipakṣa vyatireka darśane api prasaṅgāt tat na viparyaya vyāptiḥ vyatireka asiddhau tat siddhiḥ eva ca anvaya siddhiḥ asiddhau vā tat vyatireka nivṛtti siddhau api tat asiddhiḥ iti sādhye api prasaṅgaḥ tat na ananvayā 
PVSV_154,31–155,4	 vyatireka vyāptiḥ mithyā artha tāyāḥ tu pauruṣeya tvena vyāptyai apauruṣeyān nivṛttau api na satya artha tvam prakāra antara sambhavāt dvairāśye tu śabdānām etat syāt eka nivṛttau gati antara abhāvāt te tu anarthakāḥ api syuḥ iti naḥ iṣṭa siddhiḥ artha pratīteḥ na anarthakāḥ iti ced eṣa puruṣa vyāpāraḥ syāt artha antara vikalpa vat 
PVSV_155,5–155,9	 yathā atat artha tve api bharataḥ urvaśī ādi caritaḥ ādikam artham anye anyathā vyācakṣate tat anusāreṇa ca keṣāṃcid pratītiḥ tathā ayam anarthakeṣu artha vikalpaḥ puruṣa kṛtaḥ na tu śabda svabhāva kṛtaḥ puruṣaḥ upadeśa apekṣaṇāt artha antara vat eva na hi prakṛtyā prakāśanāḥ tam apekṣante vahni ādayaḥ puruṣas 
PVSV_155,10–155,14	 tu sva samaya vyāpāram ācakṣāṇe upadiśati iti nyāyyam puruṣa samita nisarga siddhayoḥ upadeśa apekṣaṇa aviśeṣāt anya viśeṣa abhāvāt ca ekaḥ naisargikaḥ anyaḥ tu pauruṣeyaḥ iti duravasānam asti viśeṣaḥ pramāṇa saṃvādaḥ iti ced etat uttaratra niṣetsyāmaḥ na asti atyanta parokṣe arthe pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ iti samāna dharmiṇoḥ 
PVSV_155,15–155,19	 arthayoḥ pramāṇa saṃvāda mā atra viśeṣāt ekatra apauruṣeya tve bahutaram idānīm apauruṣeyam santi puruṣa kṛtāni api vākyāni kānicid evaṃvidhāni iti teṣu api prasaṅgaḥ tadvat eṣām api abhimata arthavat tā pauruṣeyī ca syāt pramāṇa anurodhinī ca api ca idam mantrāḥ apauruṣeyāḥ ca iti vyāhatam paśyāmaḥ tathā hi 
PVSV_155,20–155,26	 samaya tve hi mantrāṇām kasyacid kārya sādhanam yuktam yadi ete mantrāḥ kasyacid samayaḥ yathā mat praṇītam etat abhimata arthaḥ upanibandhanam vākyam evam niyuñjānam anena arthena yojayāmi iti para artha para tā anurodhena anyatas vā kutaścid hetoḥ kṛtaḥ syāt tadā mantra prayogāt kadācid artha niṣpattiḥ yuktā kavi samayāt iva pāṭhakānām atha api bhāva śaktiḥ syāt anyatra api aviśeṣatas 
PVSV_155,27–156,4	 na vai puruṣa samayāt mantrebhyaḥ artha siddhiḥ kim tarhi bhāva svabhāvaḥ eṣa yat ime kathaṃcid niyuktāḥ phala dāḥ tat tarhi rūpam varṇānām sarvatra aviśiṣṭam iti yathā kathaṃcid prayuktāt api phalam syāt varṇāḥ eva hi mantraḥ na anyat kiṃcid tat kramaḥ mantraḥ iti ced kramasya artha antara tvam ca pūrvam eva nirākṛtam 
PVSV_156,5–156,9	 na varṇa vyatiriktaḥ anyaḥ kramaḥ iti niveditam etat avyatireke ca varṇāḥ eva mantraḥ te ca aviśiṣṭāḥ sarvatra iti sarvadā phala dāḥ syuḥ upaplavaḥ tu alpīyasaḥ api kramasya bhraṃśāt dṛṣṭaḥ kasyacid anuṣṭhānāt devatā saṃnidheḥ asākalyena virādhanāt ca sarva bhraṃśe tu kasyacid eva samayasya ananuṣṭhānāt asaṃnidheḥ 
PVSV_156,10–156,18	 na artha anarthau kim ca kramasya artha antara tve anartha antara tve vā varṇaḥ ātmanaḥ tat kramaḥ ātmanaḥ vā mantrasya artha hetoḥ akṛtaka tvāt nityasya nityam saṃnidhānam iti nityam tat artha siddhiḥ syāt yatas hi bhāva śakteḥ phalaḥ utpattiḥ sā avikalāḥ iti na phala vaikalyam syāt na hi kāraṇa sākalye kārya vaikalyam yuktam tasya akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt na kevalāt mantra prayogāt iṣṭa siddhiḥ tasya vidhāna apekṣa tvāt iti ced asāmarthyam apekṣaṇe 
PVSV_156,19–156,24	 yadi mantrāḥ vidhānāt anyatas vā kaṃcid svabhāva atiśayam āsādayeyuḥ sa tatra samarthaḥ apekṣyaḥ syāt na ca nityeṣu etat asti iti uktam tat kim ayam asamarthaḥ apekṣyate iti anapekṣāḥ sadā kuryuḥ na vā kadācid anatiśayāt sarvasya sādhanam te syuḥ bhāva śaktiḥ yat īdṛśī prayoktṛ bheda apekṣā ca na asaṃskāryasya yujyate
