PVSV_156,25–157,5	 yadi bhāva śaktayā eva mantrāḥ siddhi pradā na te kaṃcid parihareyuḥ yajamānam anyam vā na hi anyam prati svabhāvaḥ atat bhāvaḥ bhavati tasya tena anapakarṣaṇāt anyena ca anutkarṣaṇāt kenacid saha kārya kāraṇa bhāva ayogāt pratyāsatti viprakarṣa abhāvāt atas eva asya asaṃskārya tvāt prayoktā api na asti atas prayoktā phalam aśnuvīta saṃskāryasya api bhāvasya vastu bhedaḥ hi bhedakaḥ prayoktṛ bhedāt niyamaḥ śaktau na samaye bhavet 
PVSV_157,6–157,10	 ādheya viśeṣāḥ hi anityāḥ bhāvāḥ tat hetoḥ svabhāva bhede tatas samāsādita atiśaya tvāt anyatra anyathā syuḥ na abhede kāraṇa aviśeṣe kārya aviśeṣāt viśeṣe tasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt iti ukta prāyam tat ime mantrāḥ svabhāva atiśayāt phala dāyinaḥ kāryāḥ api na śūdraḥ ādi prayoge api anyathā syuḥ śūdra vipra abhidhānayoḥ 
PVSV_157,11–157,15	 puruṣayoḥ svabhāva abhedāt na hi puruṣaḥ icchā anuvidhāyinaḥ nāma vyavahāra bhedāt svabhāva bhedaḥ anubandhinām arthānām anyathātvam asti tayoḥ jāti bhedaḥ iti ced sa khalu ākṛti guṇa śakti bhede dṛṣṭaḥ gava aśva vat anupadeśam ca enam lokaḥ pratipadyate na tadvat anayoḥ kaṃcid api guṇam viniyatam paśyāmaḥ apaśyanta ḥ 
PVSV_157,16–157,20	 ca katham bhedam pratipadyemahi yaḥ api ayam nāma bhedaḥ anvayaḥ loke prati iti bhedaḥ saḥ asati api jāti bhede vyāpāra viśeṣa anuṣṭhānāt anvayāt ca syāt vaidya vaṇij vyapadeśaḥ ādi vat tat ime aviśiṣṭena prayujyamānāḥ mantrāḥ tatas aviśiṣṭam eva svabhāvam āsādayanti tena aviśeṣeṇa eva phala dāḥ syuḥ yadā 
PVSV_157,21–157,29	 tu samayāt ebhyaḥ phalam tadā ayam adoṣaḥ samaya kārasya ruceḥ phalaḥ utpatti niyamāt svabhāva vṛttayaḥ hi bhāvāḥ tat mukhena prasaṅgam arhanti na puruṣaḥ icchā vṛttayaḥ teṣām yathā kathaṃcid vṛtteḥ yat api prayoktā phalam aśnutaḥ iti prayogam samīhita artha yogyasya utpādanam santāna pariṇāmanam vā paśyāmaḥ tat ubhayam viśeṣa janmani syāt anyathā anādheya viśeṣāṇām kim kurvāṇaḥ prayojakaḥ yena tatas kaścid phalam aśnute anyaḥ na prayogaḥ yadi abhivyaktiḥ sā prāk eva nirākṛtāḥ 
PVSV_158,1–158,10	 na hi nityānām kācid abhivyaktiḥ iti uktam yatas abhivyañjakaḥ prayoktā syāt vyaktiḥ ca buddhiḥ sā yasmāt sa phalaiḥ yadi yujyate syāt śrotaḥ phala sambandhaḥ vaktā hi vyakti kāraṇam na hi śabdasya anyatas svarūpa pariṇāmaḥ vyaktiḥ na api āvaraṇa vigamanam kim tu tat viṣayā pratītiḥ aśrūyamāṇe avyakta vyapadeśāt tatra yadi buddhi hetuḥ vaktā syāt tat tulyam śrotari api iti saḥ api phalam vaktṛ vat aśnuvīta na hi vaktuḥ kaścid anyaḥ tat bhāvaḥ anyatra tat buddhi hetu tvāt paraḥ upādhi buddhiḥ śrotuḥ 
PVSV_158,11–158,15	 na vaktuḥ iti viśeṣaḥ iti ced kaḥ punar upayogaḥ vaktuḥ śrotari yena upādhiḥ iṣyate tatas śabda śrutiḥ iti ced nanu tat eva idam paryanuyujyate katham tatas iti asambandhāt viṣayaḥ upanayanāt ayam asya śrāvakaḥ syāt tat ca na śakyam tasya kathaṃcid api apariṇāmāt indriya saṃskāraḥ ādayaḥ api uktāḥ mām 
PVSV_158,16–158,25	 śrāvayati aham śrāvayāmi iti tayoḥ pratyayāt vaktṛ śrotṛ bhedaḥ iti ced anupakārya upakārakāt bhrānti mātrāt tat bhāve atiprasaṅgāt anyatra api bhrāntyā pratyaya darśanāt sarvathā upakāra abhāve ca tathā pratyayaḥ na yuktaḥ sarveṣām parasparam evam prasaṅgāt bhrāntiḥ api kutaścid upakāre sati kayācid pratyāsattyai anyatra bhavati sa api atyanta anupakāre na syāt tasmāt vaktṛ śrotroḥ vyakti hetu tve aviśeṣāt tulyaḥ phala sambandhaḥ syāt api ca anabhivyakta śabdānām karaṇānām prayojanam manojapaḥ vā vyarthaḥ syāt śabdaḥ hi śrotra gocaraḥ 
PVSV_158,26–159,1	 śrotra grahaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ śabdaḥ tat atikrame atiprasaṅgāt nanu evam sāmānye api prasaṅgaḥ na brūmaḥ śabdaḥ eva iti śabdaḥ tu avaśyam tat lakṣaṇaḥ tasya lakṣaṇa antara abhāvāt tatra yadi śabdaḥ ātmanām mantrāṇām vyakti hetuḥ prayoktā anabhivyakta śruti viṣayāṇām karaṇānām prayoktā jāpī na mantra phalena 
PVSV_159,2–159,10	 yujyate na api manasā japan na hi tadā śrotreṇa kaṃcid artham vibhāvayāmaḥ na ca aśabdaḥ ātmā mantraḥ pāraṃparyeṇa tad ja tvāt tat vyaktiḥ sā api ced matiḥ na hi manasā dhyāyataḥ api mantraḥ ābhāsā buddhiḥ śabda śravaṇāt ṛte tatas śabda prabhavāt sā api śabda vyaktiḥ eva anavasthā evam syāt śabdaḥ artha vikalpānām api paraṃparayā prasūtiḥ asti iti te api tathā syuḥ tat arthā ced asiddham kalpanā anvayāt 
PVSV_159,11–159,15	 na brūmaḥ sarvā śabda prabhavā buddhiḥ tat vyaktiḥ iti yā tu tat viṣayā sā tasya vyaktiḥ iti manaḥ vikalpasya tat viṣaya tvam asiddham na hi sva lakṣaṇe vikalpānām vṛttiḥ iti nivedayiṣyāmaḥ te hi yathāsvam āntarāt vikalpa vāsanā prabodhāt anapekṣita bāhya arthaḥ upanidhayaḥ bhavanti bāhya apāyānaḥ āgame api bhāvāt 
PVSV_159,16–159,20	 na hi yaḥ yasya sattā upadhānam na apekṣate sa tasya hetuḥ ahetuḥ ca katham viṣayaḥ tasmāt na manaḥ vikalpaḥ śabda vyaktiḥ yatas tadvān prayoktā syāt tat prasūtā tat viṣayā buddhiḥ tat vyaktiḥ tat āśrayaḥ prayoktā iti atra api uktam śrotari api prasaṅgaḥ iti tat jñāne ca prayoge śabdaḥ puruṣe vyāpriyate tasya jñāna 
PVSV_159,21–159,26	 jananāt na puruṣaḥ śabde tad ātmani anupakārāt atha ca puruṣaḥ śabdānām prayoktā iti alaukikaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ sarvathā śabda svabhāvānām mantrāṇām prayogāt phala avāptau vyarthaḥ manojapaḥ vikalpasya śabda rūpa asaṃsparśāt sva sāmānya svabhāvānām eka bhāva vivakṣayā ukteḥ samaya kārāṇām avirodhaḥ na vastuni 
PVSV_159,27–160,2	 samaya kāraḥ tu sva lakṣaṇam indriya viṣayam sāmānya lakṣaṇam ca vikalpa pratibhāsam yathā vyavahāram saṃvṛtyā saṃkalayya samayam ārocayet yathā samayam ca artham niṣpādayet iti na manaḥ japaḥ ādāu doṣaḥ vastu svabhāvāt tu phalau āptau atat svabhāva saṃsparśe na syāt yat uktam na varṇebhyaḥ anyā kācid 
PVSV_160,3–160,11	 ānupūrvī iti tatra ānupūrvyām asatyām syāt saraḥ rasaḥ iti śrutau na kārya bhedaḥ iti ced na hi saraḥ rasaḥ iti ādi pādeṣu kaścid varṇa bhedaḥ na ca varṇa vyatiriktam anyat yatas kārya bhedaḥ syāt bhinnām ca tayoḥ pratibhām paśyāmaḥ ānupūrvīm eva ca atulyām na ca kāraṇa abhede kārya bhedaḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt asti sā bhedavatī yatas ayam prati iti bhedaḥ satyam asti sā puruṣaḥ āśrayāḥ 
PVSV_160,12–161,1	 tathā hi yaḥ yat varṇa samutthāna jñāna jāt jñānataḥ dhvaniḥ jāyate tat upādhiḥ sa śrutyā samavasīyate tat jñāna janita jñānaḥ sa śrutau apaṭu śrutiḥ apekṣya tat smṛtim paścāt ādhatte smṛtim ātmani iti eṣā pauruṣeyī eva tat hetu grāhi cetasām kārya kāraṇa tā varṇeṣu ānupūrvī iti kathyat citta samutthānā hi vāc vijñaptiḥ varṇa pada vākya abhidhānāḥ tatra sakāra samutthāpana cetasā samanantara pratyayena akaraḥ utthāpana cittam utthāpyate tathā rephaḥ ākāra visarjanīyaḥ utthāpanāni pūrva pūrva pratyayāni tat ime anyānya hetavaḥ varṇāḥ sva kāraṇa ānupūrvī janmānaḥ śruti kāle api yadā manda cāriṇaḥ pūrva 
PVSV_161,2–161,13	 varṇa jñāna sahakāri pratyaya apekṣāḥ sva jñānam janayanti tadā pūrva varṇa smaraṇa apekṣāḥ eva smṛtim upalīyante saḥ eṣa varṇānām bhinna kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratyaya nirvṛtti dharmāḥ bhinna nirvartana dharmā ca svabhāvaḥ puruṣa saṃskāra bheda bhinnaḥ kramaḥ iti ucyate anyat eva tatas rūpam tat varṇānām padam padam kartṛ saṃskārataḥ bhinnam sahitam kārya bheda kṛt tasmāt na khalu ekaḥ eva padeṣu varṇānām svabhāvaḥ kartṛ citta saṃskāra bhedena bhedāt sa ca paraspara sahitaḥ kārya bheda hetuḥ sā ca ānupūrvī varṇānām pravṛttā racanaḥ ākṛtaḥ icchā aviruddha siddhīnām sthita krama virodhataḥ 
PVSV_161,14–161,22	 kārya kāraṇa bhūta pratyayaḥ utpanna svabhāva viśeṣaḥ varṇānām ānupūrvī iti uktam sā ca puruṣa vitarka vicāra kṛtāḥ iti na sthita kramāḥ varṇāḥ icchā aviruddha siddhi krama tvāt krama viśeṣa anukrama vat na hi sthita kramāṇām deśa kālayoḥ himavat vindhya malaya ādīnām bīja aṅkuraḥ ādīnām ca svaḥ icchayā krama racanā śakyate kartum tatas eva puruṣa dharma saṃkhyāte vikalpa anukrame sati bhāvāt asati ca abhāvāt kārya kāraṇa tā siddheḥ puṃsām varṇa kramasya ca sarvaḥ varṇa kramaḥ pumbhyaḥ dahanaḥ indhana yukti vat 
PVSV_161,23–162,2	 sati indhane dāha vṛtteḥ asati abhāvāt adṛṣṭaḥ indhanaḥ api dahanaḥ na anindhanaḥ tasya deśa kāla niyama ayogāt niyame ca tasya eva indhana tvāt dahanaḥ upādāna lakṣaṇa tvāt indhanasya tathā ayam api varṇa anukramaḥ puruṣa vikalpam yadi na apekṣeta nirālambanaḥ svayam prakāśeta yatne api na śakyeta atat prabhavāt 
PVSV_162,3–162,7	 kvacid śaktau sarvaḥ tathā syāt viśeṣa abhāvāt tat bhāva bhāvinaḥ atat viśiṣṭasya ca atat kṛtau sarvatra kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ca nirākṛtaḥ syāt anvaya vyatireka lakṣaṇa tvāt tasya lakṣaṇa antaram vā vaktavyam sarve api ghaṭaḥ ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ kṛtrimāḥ akṛtrimā prasajanti tatra api evam vikalpanāyāḥ sambhavāt viśeṣa abhāvāt 
PVSV_162,8–162,13	 ca tān api hi para kriyā darśana pūrvakam eva anyaḥ karoti avidita kartāraḥ ca kecid iti sarveṣām keṣāṃcid vā akriyāḥ abhiniveśaḥ astu tasmāt sarvāḥ eva iyam varṇaḥ ānupūrvī prasiddha kārya kāraṇa bhāva vastu dharma anatikramāt puruṣa kṛtā atas eva asādhāraṇa tā siddhā mantraḥ ākhya krama kāriṇām puṃsām jñāna prabhāvābhyām anyeṣām tat abhāvataḥ 
PVSV_162,14–162,18	 ayam kramaḥ varṇānām viṣa nirghātaḥ ādi samarthaḥ na anyaḥ iti yadi anyaḥ api jānīyat tam tathā eva pratipadyeta na ca evam tasmāt ayam anukramaḥ svabhāvataḥ api kārya kṛt kaiścid eva vijñātaḥ iti asti parokṣa artha darśī puruṣaḥ na hi ayam arthaḥ samarthaḥ na ayam iti śakyam unnetum asaṃkīrṇasya liṅga viśeṣasya asiddheḥ 
PVSV_162,19–162,23	 pratyakṣayoḥ api anupadiṣṭayoḥ mantra amantrayoḥ aparijñānāt upadeśe api kathaṃcid svabhāva viveka apratīteḥ anyatra kārya saṃvādāt tasya ca karaṇāt prāk draṣṭum aśakya tvāt na ca ayam anukramaḥ svabhāvataḥ kārakaḥ kasyacid āśu siddheḥ anyasya cirāt aparasya vrata caraṇaḥ ādi apekṣaṇāt ekasmāt api 
PVSV_162,24–163,1	 karmaṇaḥ kayościd arthaḥ anartha sandarśanāt vahatām api mantrāṇām punar kvacid visaṃvādāt na hi ayam prakāraḥ svabhāve yuktaḥ svabhāvasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt puruṣaḥ tu svaḥ icchā pravṛttiḥ sattva sabhā gatā ādi vaśāt sā iva aviśeṣāt vā kaṃcid anugṛhṇāti na aparam iti yuktam vrata caryā bhraṃśa 
PVSV_163,2–163,6	 ādinā dharma adharme upacaye dharmaḥ adharmaḥ ātmanoḥ vā prakṛtyā siddhi asiddhī iti ced na dharma viruddhānām api kraurya steya maithuna hīna karma ādi bahulānām vratānām ḍākinī bhaginī tantraḥ ādiṣu darśanāt taiḥ ca siddhi viśeṣāt na ca evaṃvidhaḥ dharma svabhāvaḥ iti ca yathāvasaram nivedayiṣyāmaḥ maitrī 
PVSV_163,7–163,11	 śauca dharma parāyaṇānām ca tat nimittam eva kasyāścid siddheḥ asiddheḥ viparyaye ca punar siddheḥ na ca eka rūpāt karmaṇaḥ sa tat virodhī dharmaḥ yuktaḥ adharmaḥ ca katham idānīm dharma phalam iṣṭam adharmaḥ ātmanaḥ vrataḥ ādeḥ aśnute na vai tasya eva tat iṣṭam phalam vrataḥ ādeḥ vipākaḥ api tu pūrvasya karmaṇaḥ 
PVSV_163,12–163,16	 brahma hati ādeśa anuṣṭhānāt grāma pratilambha vat tasya tu adharmaḥ ātmanaḥ vratasya āgāmi phalam aniṣṭam sa tu mantraḥ ādi prayogaḥ tasya iṣṭa phalasya karmaṇaḥ kathaṃcid upakārāt pācakaḥ citra tvāt upakāraka śakteḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ āśraya vipāka dharmā sa dharmaḥ tena kṛtaḥ sa tathā tat ārādhanena phalati iti 
PVSV_163,17–163,24	 tat prayogaḥ upakāra vipāka dharmaṇaḥ kṛta tvāt tat phalasya karmaṇaḥ vinā api puruṣeṇa tat upakārāt phalam iti ced na puruṣaḥ ākāra svabhāva caryā adhimukti vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt tasya api upakāra tve siddhaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ asādhāraṇa guṇaḥ tat adhimukteḥ eva hi viṣa karma ādi karaṇāt tasmāt ca mantrāḥ puruṣa pranītāḥ api tat upayoga nirapekṣāḥ svabhāvena phala dāḥ ye api tantra vidaḥ kecid mantrān kāṃścana kurvate prabhu prabhāvaḥ teṣām sa tat uktaḥ nyāya vṛttitaḥ 
PVSV_163,25–163,29	 rathyā puruṣāḥ api kecana tantra jñāḥ svayam kṛtaiḥ mantraiḥ kiṃcid karma kurvanti tathā anyaḥ api anatiśayaḥ ca kartā ca mantrāṇām iti na teṣām prabhāvavatā eva adhiṣṭhānāt tat kṛtam hi te samayam anupālayantaḥ tat upadeśena ca vartamānāḥ samarthāḥ tat samayaḥ upadeśa nirapekṣāṇām asāmarthyāt tatra api 
PVSV_164,1–164,9	 tat ākāra dhyānaḥ ādeḥ eva prayogāt tasmāt tat adhiṣṭhānam eva tat tādṛśam iti unneyam api ca saḥ api tādṛśaḥ prabhāvavān eva ananya sādhāraṇa śakti tvāt iti puruṣa viśeṣaḥ eva samarthitaḥ kṛtakāḥ pauruṣeyāḥ ca vācyāḥ mantrāḥ phalaḥ īpsunā na hi akṛtakānām prayogaḥ sambhavati na ca aprayuktebhyaḥ phalam iti prayogāt phalam icchatā kṛtakāḥ mantrāḥ vācyāḥ pauruṣeyāḥ ca puruṣa adhiṣṭhānam antareṇa anyatas asambhavat phalānām phala darśanāt kṛta samaya kāvyaḥ ādi vat aśakti sādhanam puṃsām anena eva nirākṛtam 
PVSV_164,10–164,19	 pratipāditāḥ hi puruṣa kṛtāḥ tat adhiṣṭhānāt ca phala dāḥ mantrāḥ tat asti kaścid atiśayavān iti tat pratikṣepa sādhanāni api prativyūḍhāni buddhi indriyaḥ ukti puṃstve ādi sādhanam yat tu varṇyate pramāṇaḥ ābham yathārthāḥ asti na hi śeṣavataḥ gatiḥ yat tu buddhi indriya vacana yogāt puṃstvāt iti puruṣa atiśaya pratikṣepa sādhanam tat tu agamakam eva pratikṣepa sāmānya sādhanayoḥ asambhavāt na hi atīndriyeṣu atat darśinaḥ pratikṣepaḥ sambhavati satām api eṣām ajñānāt atas eva virodha asiddheḥ avirodhinā ca saha sambhava avirodhāt iti api uktam 
PVSV_164,20–165,2	 na api itara sāmānya siddhiḥ viśeṣa asambhavasya jñātum aśakya tvāt īdṛśeṣu ca anupalabdheḥ hetu tva pratikṣepāt puṃstve ādi sāmye api kasyacid viśeṣasya darśanāt sambhavat viśeṣe ca sāmya asiddhiḥ iti uktam tasmāt śeṣavat anumānam etat vyatirekasya sandehāt asamartham adarśane api vipakṣa vṛtteḥ api ca evaṃvādinaḥ jaiminīyāḥ svam eva vādam sve vācā vidhurayanti tathā hi arthaḥ ayam na ayam arthaḥ naḥ iti śabdāḥ vadanti na kalpyaḥ ayam arthaḥ puruṣaiḥ te ca rāgaḥ ādi saṃyutāḥ 
PVSV_165,3–165,10	 tatra ekaḥ tattva vid na anyaḥ iti bhedaḥ ca kim kṛtaḥ tadvat puṃstve katham api jñānī kaścid katham na vaḥ na khalu ete vaidikāḥ śabdāḥ evam vikrośanti eta bhavantaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ayam asmākam arthaḥ grāhyaḥ na anyaḥ iti kevalam anabhivyakta artha viśeṣa saṃsargāḥ śrutim abhipatanti tatra ekaḥ puruṣaḥ kaṃcid artham kalpayati anyaḥ aparam na ca śabdānām kaścid svabhāva pratiniyamaḥ yena ekam artham anurundhate na aparam 
PVSV_165,11–165,15	 kevalam samaya vaśāt tam tam āviśantaḥ dṛśyante teṣām avidita artha niyamānām atyakṣaḥ āveśāt avidvān eva doṣaḥ upaplavaḥ kaścid tattvam vyācaṣṭe na aparaḥ iti na nyāyyam atha kutaścid atiśayāt buddhi indriyaḥ ādīnām saḥ eva vetti na aparaḥ tasya kutas ayam atīndriya jñāna atiśayaḥ tathā anyaḥ api draṣṭā deśa kāla 
PVSV_165,16–165,21	 svabhāva viprakṛṣṭānām arthānām kim asambhavī dṛṣṭaḥ na hi tat pratikṣepa sādhanāni kānicid yāni naḥ enam upalīyante yathā ayam tat sādhana sambhave api asya viśeṣaḥ tathā anyasya api syāt iti anabhiniveśaḥ eva yuktaḥ yasya pramāṇa saṃvādi vacanam saḥ artha vid yadi na hi atyanta parokṣeṣu pramāṇasya asti sambhavaḥ 
PVSV_165,22–165,26	 syāt etat na vayam puruṣa prāmāṇyāt kasyacid vyākhyānam abhiniviṣṭāḥ kim tarhi pramāṇa antara saṃvādāt bahuṣu api vyākhyātṛṣu yaḥ pramāṇam pratyakṣaḥ ādikam saṃsyandayati saḥ anumanyate tat na atīndriyeṣu adṛṣṭaḥ ādiṣu pramāṇa antara avṛtteḥ tat asambhavāt eva hi āgamaḥ tat pratipatti artham upayācyate 
PVSV_165,27–166,4	 anyathā sati api tasmin pramāṇa antara avṛttau apratipatteḥ tatas ca kevalāt artha pratipatteḥ asādhanam eva āgamaḥ syāt kevalāt anyatas api atīndriyeṣu apratipattiḥ iti ced katham atīndriyaḥ ca nāma pratyakṣaḥ ādi viṣayaḥ ca te punar sva viṣaye api āgamam apekṣye eva sādhakāḥ ced anāgamāt dhūmaḥ ādeḥ agni ādi pratyayaḥ na syāt 
PVSV_166,5–166,12	 na vai pravṛttaḥ āgame pramāṇa antaram anviṣyate kim tarhi saḥ eva āgama pravṛttiḥ na jñāyate iti ced svayam samarthasya prasādhane asya tat āgamaḥ upadhānam kam atiśayam puṣṇāti asamartham tu āgama pravṛttim api naḥ eva sādhayiṣyati sā ca atīndriya artha sambaddhā āgama pravṛttiḥ atīndriyā katham anyena siddhāḥ anyat ca evam āgama lakṣaṇam syāt tathā hi yasya pramāṇa saṃvādi vacanam tat kṛtam vacaḥ saḥ āgamaḥ iti prāptam nirarthāḥ apauruṣeya tā 
PVSV_166,13–166,19	 tulye api āgama vāde pramāṇa balāt āgamasya kvacid āgama tve pramāṇa saṃvādaḥ vacanānām āgama lakṣaṇam syāt na apuruṣa kriyā tasyāḥ sarve artheṣu tulya tve api pramāṇa abādhanāt pratipatteḥ tat bhāve api anyatra pramāṇa asaṃvādinī aniṣṭa tvāt kim ca yadi atyanta parokṣe arthe anāgama jñāna sambhavaḥ atīndriya artha vid kaścid asti iti abhimatam bhavet 
PVSV_166,20–167,1	 yadi āgama anapekṣam jñāna ayāthātathyam puruṣasya iṣyate parokṣe arthe santi puruṣāḥ atīndriya artha dṛśaḥ iti iṣṭam syāt pratyakṣa pūrvakānām pramāṇānām atat darśane asambhavāt pratyakṣa pramāṇam āgamaḥ pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ tu pratyakṣam anvākarṣati iti na puruṣa atiśayaḥ nivāryaḥ syāt tasmāt na asti atīndriyeṣu pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ atas eva āgamasya artha viśeṣa vṛtteḥ aparijñānāt ayam jaiminiḥ anyaḥ vā svayam rāgaḥ ādimān na artham vetti vedasya na anyatas na vedayati vedaḥ api veda arthasya kutas gatiḥ 
PVSV_167,2–167,10	 sarve eva hi puruṣaḥ anatikrānta doṣa viplavaḥ tam atīndriyam artha viśeṣa pratiniyamam vyākhyātāḥ na svayam vetti na api enam anyaḥ vedayati tasya api tulya prasaṅga tvāt na hi andhena ākṛśyamāṇaḥ andhaḥ panthānam pratipadyate na api svayam vedaḥ sva artham vivṛṇoti upadeśa vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt tat ayam aparijñāta arthaḥ śabda gaḍuḥ evam śalya bhūtaḥ asat darśana snāyu vinibaddhaḥ duruddharaḥ duḥkham āsayati tena agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti śrutau khādet śva māṃsam iti eṣa na arthaḥ iti atra kā pramā 
PVSV_167,11–167,15	 kvacid api arthe pratyāsatti viprakarṣa rahitasya agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti ādi vākyasya bhūta viśeṣe yathā abhimatam ghṛtaḥ ādi prakṣipet iti ayam arthaḥ na punar śva māṃsam khādet iti na atiśayam paśyāmaḥ nanu ayam sarvatra samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ parokṣa daiśikānām vacanānām artham yathā abhiprāyam idānīntanāḥ 
PVSV_167,16–167,20	 kim samanuyanti āhosvit viparyayam iti na upadeṣṭuḥ sve abhiprāya prakāśanena sampradāya sambhavāt na hi ayam adaiśikānām śabdānām sambhavati loka pratyāyana abhiprāyaḥ ca bruvāṇaḥ lokaḥ saṃketa prasiddhim anupālayati iti tatas api tat artha siddhiḥ syāt na apauruṣeyāṇām śabdānām tatra kasyacid 
PVSV_167,21–167,25	 sami iha abhāvāt api ca nyāyam eva anupālayantaḥ paṇḍitāḥ heyaḥ upādeya tat āśrayeṣu saṃghaṭante na tu pravāda mātreṇa iti na samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ tat ca yathāvasaram pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ nanu kaścid loka saṃniveśaḥ ādiḥ ayukti viṣayaḥ api sambhāvanīya puruṣa vacanāt arthaḥ pratipadyate na apratyayāt na hi kvacid 
PVSV_167,26–168,8	 askhalitaḥ iti sarvam tathā vyabhicāra darśanāt tat pravṛtteḥ avisaṃvādena vyāpti asiddheḥ ca agatyā ca idam āgama lakṣaṇam iṣṭam na atas niścayaḥ tat na pramāṇam āgamaḥ iti api uktam apauruṣeyānām śabdānām artha jñānam na sampradāyāt na yukteḥ na lokāt iti tatra apratipattiḥ nyāyyāḥ tatra api prasiddhaḥ loka vādaḥ ced pratipatti hetuḥ tatra kaḥ atīndriya artha dṛś aneka artheṣu śabdeṣu yena arthaḥ ayam vivecitaḥ 
PVSV_168,9–168,13	 na hi ayam loka vyavahāraḥ apauruṣeyāt śabdaḥ artha sambandhāt kim tarhi samayāt sva śāstra kāra samayāt pāṇinīyaḥ ādi vyavahāra vat upadeśa apekṣaṇāt na hi apauruṣeye tasmin upadeśaḥ yuktaḥ tasya kenacid ajñānāt atīndriya tvāt aindriyaka tve svayam pratipatti prasaṅgāt rūpaḥ ādi vat upadeśe ca puruṣāṇām 
PVSV_168,14–168,18	 svatantrāṇām yathā tattvam upadeśena avisaṃvādasya asiddheḥ anāśvāsaḥ veda vat tat vyākhyānam api apauruṣeyam sampradāya avicchedāt āgatam tatas artha siddhiḥ iti ced tasya api śabdaḥ ātmaka tve tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ katham asya arthaḥ viditaḥ iti puruṣaḥ hi svayam samitānām śabdānām artham śṛṅga grāhikayā api tāvat 
PVSV_168,19–168,23	 abudham bodhayet iti asti pauruṣeyānām śabdānām artha gatau upāyaḥ apauruṣeyaḥ tu śabdaḥ naḥ evam karoti na ca asya kaścid kvacid sambandha niyamam jñātum īśaḥ iti apratipattiḥ eva tat arthasya api ca vedaḥ tat vyākhyānam vā puruṣeṇa puruṣāya upadiśyamānam anaṣṭa sampradāyam eva anuvartate iti atra api samayaḥ 
PVSV_168,24–169,1	 śaraṇam āgama bhraṃśa kāriṇām āhopuruṣikayā tat darśana vidveṣeṇa vā tat pratipanna khalīkārāya dhūrta vyasanena anyatas vā kutaścid kāraṇāt anyathā racanaḥ adarśanāt api ca atra bhavān svam eva mukha varṇam sva vāda anurāgāt nūnam vismṛtavān puruṣaḥ rāgaḥ ādibhiḥ upaplutaḥ anṛtam api brūyāt iti na asya 
PVSV_169,2–169,6	 vacanam pramāṇam iti tat iha api kim na pratyavekṣyate sambhavati na vā iti saḥ eva upadiśan upaplavāt vedam veda artham vā anyathā api upadiśet iti śrūyante hi kaiścid puruṣaiḥ utsannaḥ uddhṛtāni śākhāḥ antarāṇi idānīm api kānicid virala adhyetṛkāṇi tadvat pracura adhyetṛkāṇām api kasmiṃścid kāle kathaṃcid 
PVSV_169,7–169,11	 saṃhāra sambhavāt punar sambhāvita puruṣa pratyayāt pracuratā upagamana sambhāvanā asambhavāt teṣām ca punar pratānayitṛṛṇām kadācid adhīta vismṛta adhyanānām anyeṣām vā sambhāvanā bhraṃśa bhayaḥ ādinā anyathā upadeśa sambhavāt tat pratyayāt ca tat bhaktānām avicāreṇa pratipatteḥ bahuṣu adhyetṛṣu 
PVSV_169,12–169,16	 sambhāvitāt puruṣāt bahulam pratipatti darśanāt tatas api kathaṃcid vipralambha sambhavāt kim ca parimita vyākhyātṛ puruṣa paraṃparām eva ca atra bhavatām api śṛṇumaḥ tatra kaścid dviṣṭā jña dhūrtānām anyatamaḥ syāt api iti anāśvāsaḥ tasmāt na apauruṣeyāt vyākhyānāt na api sāmayikāt loka vyavahārāt 
PVSV_169,17–169,21	 veda artha siddhiḥ asāmayika tve api nānā arthānām śabdānām vyavahāre darśanāt kasyacid aprasiddha arthasya aprasiddhasya vā punar vyutpatti darśanena sarvatra tat āśaṅkāḥ anivṛtteḥ sarveṣām yathārtha niyoge api avaiguṇyena yathā samayam prati iti jananāt iṣṭa aniṣṭayoḥ aviśeṣāt aviśiṣṭānām sarve artheṣu ekam artham 
PVSV_169,22–169,27	 atyakṣa saṃyogam anatyakṣa darśini puruṣa sāmānye kaḥ vivecayet yatas lokāt pratītiḥ syāt api ca svayam api ayam na sarvatra prasiddhim anusarati yasmāt svargaḥ urvaśī ādi śabdaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ arūḍha artha vācakaḥ anena eva nirvarṇyamānaḥ manuṣya atiśāyi puruṣa viśeṣa niketaḥ atimānuṣa sukha adhiṣṭhānaḥ nānā upakaraṇaḥ svargaḥ tat nivāsiny 
PVSV_169,28–169,32	 apsarāḥ urvaśī nāma iti lokaḥ vādaḥ tam anādṛtya anyām eva artha kalpanām ayam kurvāṇaḥ śabda antareṣu katham prasiddhim pramāṇayet tatra avirodhāt abhyupagamaḥ iti ced na atra api atīndriye virodha asiddheḥ anyatra api avirodhasya duranvaya tvāt viruddhām api agnihotrāt svarga avāptim māndyāt ayam na lakṣayet 
PVSV_169,33–170,4	 api virodha avirodhau ca bādhaka sādhaka pramāṇa vṛttī te ca atyakṣe na abhimate tat katham tat vaśāt pratītiḥ na ca vacana vṛtteḥ eva avirodhaḥ anyatra api prasaṅgāt apauruṣeyaḥ āgamaḥ tasya pravādāt artha siddhiḥ tatra punar virodha cintāyām anāśvāsaḥ āgame syāt sati api tasmin atatha abhāvāt arthasya apramāṇa 
PVSV_170,5–170,12	 vṛtteḥ anyasya api śaṅkanīya tvāt yat uktam agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti atra śva māṃsa bhakṣaṇa deśanā vikalpaḥ bhavatu iti sa na bhavati pradeśa antareṣu tathā tasya carcanāt na tasya artha aparijñānāt pradeśa antareṣu api tathāvidha artha kalpanāyāḥ anivārya tvāt yadi hi kvacid vidita arthaḥ ayam apauruṣeyaḥ śabda rāśiḥ syāt tadā tatas artha pratītiḥ syāt te tu bāhulye api andhāḥ eva sarve iti yatheṣṭam praṇīyante tasmāt śabda antareṣu tādṛkṣu tādṛśī eva astu kalpanā 
PVSV_170,13–171,3	 yādṛśī agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti asya vākyasya api ca prasiddhiḥ ca nṛṇām vādaḥ pramāṇam sa ca naḥ iṣyate tatas ca bhūyas artha gatiḥ kim etat dviṣṭa kāmitam na prasiddhiḥ nāma anyāḥ anyatra jana pravādāt te ca sarve janāḥ rāgaḥ ādi avidyā aparīta tvāt asambhāvanīya yāthātathya vacanāḥ tat eṣām pravādaḥ na pramāṇam na hi kasyacid api samyak pratipatteḥ abhāve bāhulyam artha vat bhavati pāraśīka mātṛ mithyā cāra vat teṣām eva puruṣāṇām vacanāt punar parokṣa artha sampratipattiḥ iti katham tat eva yugapad dveṣyam ca kāmyam ca atha prasiddhim ullaṅghya kalpane na nibandhanam prasiddheḥ apramāṇa tvāt tat grahe kim nibandhanam 
PVSV_171,5–171,17	 prāpta pratilomanena anyatra pravṛttiḥ guṇa doṣa sandarśanena yuktāḥ iti prasiddheḥ anvayaḥ iti ced na prāpteḥ pramāṇa vṛtti lakṣaṇa tvāt yat kiṃcana grahaṇam hi prasiddhim apramāṇayataḥ tat mukhena pratītiḥ nyāyāt prāpti pratiṣedhāt tulyā sva para vikalpayoḥ ubhayathā api vṛttiḥ iti kaḥ prasiddhau anurodhaḥ api ca iyam utpāditā prasiddhyai eva śaṅkā śabdaḥ artha niścaye yasmāt nānā artha vṛtti tvam śabdānām tatra dṛśyate na prasiddheḥ ekaḥ artha niścayaḥ śabdānām tatas eva śaṅkā utpatteḥ nānā arthāḥ hi śabdāḥ loke dṛśyante loka vādaḥ ca pratītiḥ atas eva nānā arthāḥ iti tatas ekaḥ artha niyamaḥ na yuktaḥ anyathā asambhava abhāvāt nānā śakteḥ svayam dhvaneḥ avaśyam śaṅkayā bhāvyam niyāmakam apaśyatām 
PVSV_171,18–171,26	 iti antaraślokaḥ tasmāt avidita artha vibhāgeṣu śabdeṣu ekam artham atyakṣa saṃyogam anālambana samāropam viniścitya vyācakṣāṇaḥ jaiminiḥ tat vyājena svam eva matam āha iti na tīrthakara antarāt asya viśeṣam paśyāmaḥ tathā hi tat artha vacana vyāpāra śūnyasya tat samāropeṇa abhidhānam na sva vacanam atiśete tat kāriṇā kevalam mithyā vinīta tā eva ātmanaḥ samuddyotitā syāt tathā hi eṣa sthāṇuḥ ayam mārgaḥ iti vakti iti kaścana anyaḥ svayam bravīmi iti tayoḥ bhedaḥ parikṣyatām 
PVSV_172,1–172,9	 nirabhiprāya vyāpāra vacane sthāṇau samāropya upadiśataḥ svatantrasya vā svayam vacanaḥ upagame na kaścid viśeṣaḥ anyatra jaḍasya pratipatti māndyāt api ca ekaḥ artha niyame sati enam jaiminiḥ jānīyāt saḥ eva śabdasya sarvatra yogyasya ekaḥ artha dyotane niyamaḥ kutas na hi śabdasya kaścid arthaḥ svabhāva niyataḥ sarvatra yogya tvāt ayogya tve ca tat apracyuteḥ avidheyasya puruṣāṇām kvacid upanayana apanayana asambhavāt jñātāḥ vai atīndriyāḥ kena vivakṣā vacanāt ṛte 
PVSV_172,10–172,18	 puruṣa praṇīte hi śabde kayācid vivakṣayā sa tām kadācid kvacid nivedayet api iti vivakṣā pūrvakānām śabdānām artha niyamaḥ pratīyeta api apauruṣeye tu vidyamānaḥ api artha niyamaḥ katham vijñeyaḥ svabhāva bhedasya abhāvāt sati vā pratyakṣasya svayam prati iti prasaṅgāt apratyakṣe api kenacid jñātum aśakya tvāt na ca asti kaścid viśeṣaḥ sarve śabdāḥ hi sarve artha pratyāsatti viprakarṣa rahitāḥ tatas teṣām vivakṣā niyame hetuḥ saṃketaḥ tat prakāśanaḥ apauruṣeye sā na asti tasya sā ekārtha tā kutas 
PVSV_172,19–172,23	 vivakṣayā hi śabdaḥ arthe niyamyate na svabhāvataḥ tasya kvacid apratibandhena sarvatra tulya tvāt yatra api pratibandhaḥ tat abhidhāna niyama abhāvāt sarve śabdaiḥ karaṇānām abhidhāna prasaṅgāt tasmāt vivakṣā prakāśanāya abhiprāya nivedana lakṣaṇaḥ saṃketaḥ kriyate apauruṣeye tu na vivakṣā na saṃketaḥ 
PVSV_172,24–173,1	 kasyacid abhiprāya abhāvāt iti na niyamaḥ na tat jñānam svabhāva niyame anyatra na yojyeta tayā punar yadi saṃketa nirapekṣaḥ svabhāvataḥ eva artheṣu śabdaḥ nilīnaḥ syāt uktam atra apratibandhāt aniyamaḥ iti api ca svābhāvike vācya vācaka bhāve na punar vivakṣayā yatheṣṭam niyujyeta saṃketaḥ ca nirarthaḥ syāt 
PVSV_173,2–173,7	 na hi svabhāva bhedaḥ indriya gamyaḥ sva pratītau paribhāṣā ādikam apekṣate nīlaḥ ādi bheda vat tat apekṣa pratītayaḥ tu na vastu svabhāvāḥ kim tarhi sāmayikā rāja cihnaḥ ādi vat yaḥ ca sāmayikaḥ sa svabhāva niyataḥ ayuktaḥ tasya icchā vṛtteḥ atas eva saṃketāt svabhāva viśeṣasya vyaktau ca niyamaḥ kutas 
PVSV_173,8–173,15	 svaḥ icchā vṛttiḥ saṃketaḥ saḥ iha eva kartum śakyate na anyatra iti naḥ uparodhaḥ asti sa ca puruṣaiḥ sve icchayā kriyamāṇaḥ tam eva svabhāvam vyanakti na anyam iti na niyamaḥ asti yatra svātantryam icchāyāḥ niyamaḥ nāma tatra kaḥ dyotayet tena saṃketaḥ naḥ iṣṭām eva asya yogyatām iti antaraślokaḥ yasmāt kila īdṛśam satyam yathā agniḥ śīta nodanaḥ vākyam vedaḥ eka deśa tvāt anyat api aparaḥ abravīt 
PVSV_173,16–173,21	 anyaḥ tu apauruṣeyam āgama lakṣaṇam parityajya anyathā prāmāṇyam vedasya sādhayitu kāmaḥ prāha avitathāni veda vākyāni yatra apratipattiḥ vedaḥ eka deśa tvāt yathā agniḥ himasya bheṣajam iti ādi vākyam iti tasya idam rasa vat tulya rūpa tvāt eka bhāṇḍe ca pāka vat śeṣavat vyabhicāri tvāt kṣiptam nyāya vidā īdṛśam 
PVSV_173,22–173,26	 svayam īdṛśam ācāryeṇa anumānam naiyāyika śeṣavat anumāna vyabhicāram udbhāvayatā tulya rūpa tayā phalānām tulya rasa sādhana vat ekaḥ sthālī antargamāt dṛṣṭa vat adṛṣṭa taṇḍula pāka sādhana vat ca asādhanam uktam tat asādhana tva nyāyaḥ ca pūrvam eva uktaḥ uktam ca idam āgama lakṣaṇam asmābhiḥ tat tu 
PVSV_173,27–174,8	 sarvasya śakya vicārasya viṣayasya yathāsvam pramāṇena vidhi pratiṣedha viśuddhau na antarīyaka tva abhāve api śabdānām artheṣu varam saṃśayitasya vṛttiḥ tatra kadācid avisaṃvāda sambhavāt na tu anyatra dṛṣṭa pramāṇe uparodhasya puruṣasya pravṛttiḥ iti yaḥ punar prākṛta viṣayasya vahneḥ śīta pratighāta sāmarthyasya abhidhānam satya artham upadarśya sarvam satya artham āha śāstram śakya paricchede api viṣaye pramāṇa virodhāt bahutaram ayuktam api nityasya puṃsaḥ kartṛ tvam nityān bhāvān atīndriyān aindriyān viṣamam hetum bhāvānām viṣamām sthitim 
PVSV_174,9–174,18	 nivṛttim ca pramāṇābhyām anyat vā vyasta gocaram viruddham āgama apekṣeṇa anumānena vā vadat virodham asamādhāya śāstra artham ca apradarśya saḥ satya artham pratijānānaḥ jayet dhārṣṭyena bandhakīm apracyuta anutpanna pūrva apara rūpaḥ pumān kartā krameṇa karmaṇām karma phalānām ca bhoktā samavāyi kāraṇa adhiṣṭhāna bhāvaḥ ādinā iti āha vedaḥ tat ca ayuktam iti āvedita prāyam nitya tvam ca keṣāṃcid bhāvānām akṣaṇikasya vastu dharma atikramāt ayuktam apratyakṣāni eva hi sāmānyaḥ ādīni pratyakṣāni janma sthiti 
PVSV_174,19–174,23	 nivṛttīḥ ca viṣamāḥ padārthānām anādheya viśeṣasya prāk akartuḥ para apekṣayā janaka tvam niṣpatteḥ akārya rūpasya āśraya vaśena sthānam kāraṇāt ca vināśa iti ādikam anyat api pratyakṣa anumānābhyām prasiddhi viparyayam āgama āśrayeṇa ca anumānena bādhitam agnihotraḥ ādeḥ pāpa śodhana sāmarthya ādikam tasya 
PVSV_174,24–174,28	 evaṃvādinaḥ vedasya sarvatra śāstra śarīre pramāṇa virodham apratisamādhāya sambandha anuguṇaḥ upāya puruṣa artha abhidhānāni ca śāstra dharmān apradarśya atyanta prasiddha viṣaya satya abhidhāna mātreṇa prajñā prakarṣa duravagaha gahane api niratyayatām sādhayitu kāmaḥ bandhakīm api prāgalbhyena vijayate kācid kila 
PVSV_174,29–175,6	 bandhakī svayam svāminā vipratipatti sthāne dṛṣṭvā upālabdhāḥ sā tam pratyuvāca paśyata mātar puruṣasya vaiparītyam mayi dharma patnyām pratyayam akṛtvā ātmīyayoḥ naḥ itaraḥ abhidhānayoḥ jala budbudayoḥ karoti tena jaratkāṇena grāmya kāṣṭha hārakeṇa prārthitāḥ api na saṃgatāḥ rūpa guṇa anurāgena kila mantri mukhya dārakam kāmaye aham iti evaṃjātīyakam etat api vahneḥ śīta pratīkāra vacanena dṛṣṭa pramāṇa virodhasya api atyanta parokṣe arthe avisaṃvāda anumānam sidhyet pramāṇam yadi evam apramāṇam atha iha kim na hi ekam na asti satya artham puruṣe bahu bhāṣiṇi 
PVSV_175,7–175,12	 yathā idam ati duṣkaram atyanta satya abhidhānam tathā atyanta asatya abhidhānam api tatra ekasya vacanasya kathaṃcid saṃvādena aviśiṣṭasya tat vacana rāśeḥ tathā abhāve na kaścid puruṣaḥ anāptaḥ syāt api ca na ayam svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā vastūnām vaktari dhvaniḥ na ca tat vyatiriktasya vidyate avyabhicāritā 
PVSV_175,13–175,20	 na tāvat etat vacanam vācyānām svabhāvaḥ na api eṣām kāryam tat abhāve api vaktuḥ vivakṣā mātreṇa bhāvāt na ca anyaḥ kaścid kasyacid avyabhicārī vyabhicāre ca tatas anyathā api tat sambhavāt tat bhāvāt tat pratītiḥ ayuktā pravṛttiḥ vācakānām ca vācya dṛṣṭi kṛtā iti ced syāt etat kāryam eva vacanam vācakasya vācya darśana vṛtteḥ evam sati paraspara viruddha arthā katham ekatra sā bhavet 
PVSV_175,21–175,26	 yadi eṣa pratiniyamaḥ vācyam vastu antareṇa śabdaḥ na pravartate iti bhinneṣu pravādeṣu ekatra vastuni viruddha svabhāvaḥ upasaṃhāreṇa vacana vṛttiḥ na syāt na hi ayam sambhavaḥ asti ekaḥ śabdaḥ niṣparyāyam nityaḥ ca syāt anityaḥ ca iti vastubhiḥ naḥ āgamāḥ tena kathaṃcid na antarīyakāḥ pratipattuḥ prasidhyanti kutas tebhyaḥ artha niścayaḥ 
PVSV_175,27–176,2	 āgamam pramāṇam tat ādarśita artha pratipattaye ajñaḥ janaḥ samanveṣate samadhigata yāthātathyānām upadeśa anapekṣaṇāt ajñasya ca atīndriya guṇa puruṣa vivecane asāmarthyāt vacanānām samīhita artha sattām antareṇa api vṛttim paśyataḥ bhavitavyam eva adṛṣṭa vyabhicāra vacasām api puruṣāṇām vāci śaṅkayā kim yathārthā 
PVSV_176,3–176,16	 na vā iti tena na yuktam anena kasyacid vacanena kiṃcid niścetum tasmāt na tat nivṛttyā api bhāva abhāvaḥ prasidhyati yat uktam sarva viṣaya tvāt āgamasya sati vastuni avisaṃvādena asya vṛtteḥ tat nivṛtti lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ abhāvam sādhayati iti tat asya sarva viṣaya tve api vastu antareṇa āvṛttau syāt tat ca na asti tatas pratipattu kāmasya asiddhiḥ iti uktam tena asaṃniścaya phalāḥ anupalabdhiḥ na sidhyate tasmāt na pramāṇa traya nivṛttau api viprakṛṣṭeṣu abhāva niścayaḥ veda prāmāṇyam kasyacid kartṛ vādaḥ snāne dharmaḥ icchā jāti vāda avalepaḥ santāpaḥ ārambhaḥ pāpa hānāya ca iti dhvasta prajñāne pañca liṅgāni jāḍye
